cclxiij ¶how lāde englōde fyrſt named albion ād encheſon ſo named ther noble lāde surre noble myghti kīg mā grete renome men called diocliſian well worthely hym gouerned ruled thurgh noble chiualrie conquered landes hym ſo almoſt kynges world entēdant hit befell thus thys dyocleſian ſpouſed gentill damyſell wōder fair emes doughter ād men called hyr labana ſhe loued hȳ reſō wolde ſo gate vpon xxxiij doughtres whiche eldeſt men called albine thees damiſelles whā comē vnto age bicomen ſo fayre wōder wherfor dyocliſian anon̄ let make ſomaunce commaūded lrēs alle kinges helden hȳ ſhold come certaȳ day hyr lrēs cōteyned make ryall feſte whyche day thider comē brought wyt hem amyrallis prince duke ād noble chyualrye feſt rially arayed ther lyued en ioye myrthe ynough wōder wit befell thus thys dyocliſian thought marie doughtres amōg kinges tho ſolēpnite punctel ſo ſpaken ād ded albyne eldeſt doughter hir ſuſtres richely maried vnto xxxiij kinges lordes grete honour power ſolēpnite whan ſolempnyte done every king toke wyf ād lad hē owne contre ther made hē quenes befell thus afterward dame albyne bycome ſo ſtoute ſo ſterne ſhe tolde lytel pry lorde hym ſcorne ād deſpit wolde done wyll ſhe wolde haue hyr owne wil diuerſe mater hyr ſuſtres euerichone bere hē ſo euel ayēſt hyr lordes wō der wyt aſmoch̄ hē thought hyr huſbondes nought ſo hye ꝑage comen hyr fadre kinges hyr lordes wolde haue caſtiſed fayr ſpeche beheſtes alſo yeftes warned hem fayr maner vpon loue frēdſhip ſholde amē de lyther condycyons nought dydden hyr owne alle thyng hem lyked power wherfor xxxiij kynges vpō tyme often tymes beten hyr wife wēd wolde haue amēded tacches hir wikked thewes ſuche condicions fair ſpech̄ warnyng dydden alle wers betynges eftſones mochel wers wherfore kyng yt wedded albyne wrote tacches condicions hys wyfe albyne ſent letter diocliſian hyr fadre whā kinges herde albynes lord ſent letter dyocliſiā anone ſent lettres enſealed hyr ſeales condycyons tacches hyr wyfes alſo whan noble kȳg dyocliſian ſaw herd ſo many complayntes hys doughtres ſore aſhamed became wō der angrye wroth toward hys doughtres ād thought night day might amē de ſo myſded anone ſent lrēs vnto ye xxxiij kȳges ſhold come hȳ bringe hem hir wife euerichone certaȳ day wolde ther caſtyſe wikkedneſſe yf might maner wyſe kīges camen alle day tyme tho ſette bytwene hȳ kyng diocliſian vnderfeng hem moche honour made ſolempne feeſt alle vnder lordſhip thridde day ſolempnite noble kyng diocliſian ſent hys xxxiij doughtres ſhold come ād ſpeke wyth chābre whan come hir fadre ſpake vnto hem hyr wikkedneſſe ād hir crueltie diſpytouſly hem reproued vndernam punctel hem ſaid yf wold chaſtyſed ſhulde loue leſe euermore ladyes herdē thys becamē moch̄ abaſſhed gretly aſhamyd fadre ſayd wold make alle amēdes ſo departed owt hyr fadres chambre dame albyne eldeſt ſuſter lad hem alle hyr chābre made voyde alle therȳne ſo lyue amōge hē ſhe hyr ſuſtres tho ſayd albine fayr ſuſtres well knowē kȳg fadre v hath reproued ſhamed deſpyſed encheſō make v obediēt vnto oure houſbōdes certes ſhal j neuer while yt j lyue ſyth come hyer kynges blode thā mȳ huſbōde whā ſhe thꝰ ſayd hir ſuſtrē ſaid ye ſame tho ſayd albyne j wote wel fayre ſuſtres yt huſbōdes haue playned vnto fadre vpō v wherfor hath v thus foule reproued deſpyſed wherfore ſuſtres counſeyll thys night whan huſbondes ben̄ bedde wyth owne aſſent cuttē hir throtes may bene pee hem ād better mowe doo thȳge vnder fadres power elles anone ladyes conſented graunted counſeyll whan nyght comē lordes ladyes went bedde ād anone hir lordes ſlepe cutte hir huſbōdes throtes ſo ſlowen hem whenne diocliſian kȳg fadre herd thȳg become hugely wroth ayēſt doughtres anon̄ wold hem haue brent· alle baron ād lordes surre counceylled ſo ſuche ſterneſſe hys ownes doughtres ſholde voide lād hem euermore ſo neuer ſhold come ayen̄ ſo dyde diocliſiā fadre anoue commaunded hem gone ſhip delyuered hem vytailles half yere whan done ſuſtren wēt ſhip ſayled forth ſee bytoke alle hyr frēdes appolyn hir god ſo lōge ſaylled ſee tyll laſt came ād arryued yle wilderneſſe whan dame albyne come londe hir ſuſtres albyne went forth owt ſhip ſayd hyr othyr ſuſtres aſmoche ſayd ſhe oldeſt ſuſter thys companye fyrſt land haue taken ād moch̄ name albyne wyll lō de called albyon mȳ owne name ād anon̄ hir ſuſtrē graū ted hyr wyt good wyl tho went alle ſuſtres owt ſhippe tokē land albyō hyr ſuſter called ther wente vp ād downe fonde nether man ne woman ne child wilde beſtes diuerſe kȳdes when̄ hir vytailles diſpended hem faylled fedde hem wyt herbes frutes ſeſon yere ſo leued beſt myght ād token fleſſh̄ dyuerſes beſtes bicame wonder fat ād ſo deſired mannys companye mannys kynde hem failled hete woxen wō der coragious kynde ſo deſyred mannis cōpanie ony othir ſolace mirthe· whan deuel perceyued went dyuerſe cōtreyes nomme body eyr likynge nature ſhad men ād come lande albyon lay wymen ſhad nature vpon hem ꝯceyued brought forth geants whych̄ men kalled gogmagog lā gherigan ſo nēpned dyuerſe name ād maner came forth ād borne horryble geants albyō dwelled caues hulles hyr lō de albion hem lyked vnto tyme brute arryued ād came totneſſe ī yle albyon ther brute conquered ſconfyted geants aboue ſayd ¶here endeth prolog albyon tho ile herkene brute goten ſlowe fyrſt hys moder afterward hys fader conquered albyon nēpned bretaygne hys owne name kalled englōd name engiſt saxonie capitulo primo ther noble cyte grete troye noble king ād man grete power kalled eneas whan cyte troye loſt ād deſtroyed thurgh heem grece eneas wyt hys meyne fledde thēs come lumbardie tho lorde gouernour lōde king called latyne othir kyng kalled turocelyne ſtrongely werred vpon king latyne often tymes dyd hym moch̄ harme whē kīg herde eneas comē vnderfeng hȳ wyth mochel honour hym helde moch̄ herde hȳ wiſt well noble kinght ād worthy body ād dedes eneas helpe king latyne werre ſhortly telle ſo well worthely dyd ſlowe turocelyne diſcomfyted hȳ peple whan thys done kyng latyne yaf londe turocelynis eneas mariage lauyne doughter mooſt fayre creature mā wiſt ſo lyued gedre ioye myrthe hir lyfes tyme wedded wyfe vpō hir begate ſone called silueyne thys sylueyne whā coude ſome reſon man vnwytyng fadre ayenſt acqueynted damiſell coſȳ leuine kȳg latynes doughter quene eneas wyfe brought damiſell childe ād whan aſcamus fadre wiſt anone let enquere wyſeſt maiſtres greteſt clerkes child ye damiſell ſhold bring forth anſwerd ſeyd ſhe ſhold bryng forth ſone ſholde quelle bothe fadre ād moder ād ſo dyd moder deyed berȳg hȳ ad whā child borne fadre let calle hȳ brute maiſtres ſayd ſhold moche harme ſorwe many diuerſe place ād ſhold come grete honour worſhip kyng aſcamꝰ deyde whā god wolde ſilueyne ſone receyued ye land made hȳ wonderlich̄ wel beloued amōge peple brute yt ſilueynus ſone xv yere olde went vpō daye wyt fadre pley ſolace brute ſhold ſhete vnto hert arwe myſhapped glaced ſo brute quelled fadre brute dryuen owt land helde hȳ grece capitulo ſecundo myſchance befalle peple lāde made ſorwe ynough ſore ā gred ād encheſon therof dryuen brute oute lande wolde ſuffre amōges hē ſaugh muſt abide went fro then grece ād ther fonde vijm men lygnage kynryd troye comē grete blode ſtorie telleth men wymen ād chyldrē whiche holden throldome bondage kȳg pādras grece deth achylles bitraied ſlayne troye brute wonder fayr man ſtronge ād hughe hys age glad chere ſē blant alſo worthy body ād wel beloued amonge peple king pādras herde ſpeke hys goodneſſe cōdicyons anone made hȳ dwelle wyth ſo brute bicome wonder pryue moch̄ beloued wt king ſo longe tyme brute dwelled wyth kyng ye laſt troye brute ſpaken gydre kynred lygnage acqueyntaūce ād ther pleyned hem vnto brute hyr ſorwe hyr boundage many ſhames kyng pandras hem done brute ſaidē vpon time ye lord owr lygnage ād ſtrōg man myghty ye capiteyn lorde wyll bycome yowr men cōmaū dements done alle maner thȳ ge ād bringe ye v oute wrecchedneſſe bondage fight kyng thurgh grace grete god ſhal hȳ ouercome ſhal make kyng lande yow done homage yow ſhull holde euermore brut tho grete pite hyr bondage brought preuely went hȳ kīges court tho troye went ād put hē wodes mōtaignes hem helde ſent vnto kȳg pandras ſholde yeue hē leue ſauelych̄ wēte owt lāde wold lēger dwelle hys bōdage kyng pādras wax tho ſore annoied ſwore wolde ſlee hē euerichone ād ordeyned gret power went towardes hem fyght· brute men māly hem defended fierſly foughten quelled ye kȳges mē none hē eſcaped tokē kȳg hȳ helde pryſō ordeyned coū ſeyl bitwene hē might done somme ſayd ſhold put deth ſomme ſayd ſhold exiled oute lande ſomme ſayd ſhold brent tho ſpake wyſe knight called mē pry ſayd brute ād troye yf kyng pandras wolde yelde haue hys lyfe coūſeyll yeue vnto brute duke ſouerayngne doughter gennogē wyfe mariage hyr hōderd ſhippes wel arayed treſour gold ād ſyluer corne wyne moch̄ nedeth haue thīg go owte land punctel ordeyne v lande elles wer fore ne none owr kynred comen v ſhall neuer haue pee lād amonges hē grece haue ſlayne many hyr knightes frēdes euer werre ād cōtake ſholde ben̄ amonges v brute tho alle folke cōſented well cō ſeyll thys thyng tolden kyng pandras therfor haue hys lyfe graūted moche axed anone yaf vnto brute gennogē hys doughter wyfe c ſhippes wyt moche hē nedeth alle vytailles ordeyned brute tho toke hys wyfe men forſoke lād grece wentē hem vnto 〈◊〉 haddē wynde weder camē thridde day ile called lorgers brute anon̄ ſente men lande aſpie maner cōtre fondē olde cyte vaſted ād forlet therinne nether mā ne woman ne thyng dwellȳg ād middel cyte fondē olde tēple fayre lady called dyane ye goddeſſe camen ayen̄ vnto brute tolde ſeyn fondē counceilled hȳ gone done ſacrefice vnto dame dyane ſhe wont yeue anſwer thyng euer man praied hyr ād namely vnto honoured wt ſacrefice brute wēt jmage ſayd dyane noble goddeſſe lady thing haſt might thy power wyndes water wodes feldes alle thynges ye world alle maner beſtes ther ben̄ yow make prayer ye counceylle telle ād place ſhall maye haue ād fynde couenable dwellyng ād peple ād whan ſhal haue fonden thys coūceill ſhall make honour yow well fayre temple noble wherȳne ye ſhal euermore ben honowred whan done hys prayer goddeſſe dyane anſwerde hȳ maner brute ſayd ſhe go euen forth thy wey ouer ye ſee īto fraū ce toward weſt ther ye ſhall fȳde ile kalled albyō yle bycompaſſet wyt ſee punctel man may come ther ben̄ ſhippes lāde wont geāts nowo ſo wylderneſſe punctel forſayde land deſtynyed ād ordeyned peple ¶how vaillaūt knight coryn became brute men kyng goffars diſcomfyted capitulo iij whan brute herde thys āſwere diane goddeſſe anone let ancres wynde vp ſayled hygh̄ ſee ād whan hys men ſaylled xx dayes moo fonden faſt beſide coſt ſee thouſād men lygnage ād kynred troye hyr ſoueraigne ād hyr maiſtre kalled coryn whan brute wiſte whennes tho vnderfeng hem wyth moch̄ joye ſhyppes ād lad hē forth wyth hym thys coryn tho become brute men̄ dyd feaulte homage ſo ſo longe ſaylled forth ſee tyll camen gaſconye· anone arryued hauē lyrgers ād ther dwelled viij dayes hē reſtē hyr ſaylles amēde ther nede thyſe tydȳges ſone camen kyng goffar punctel lord lande mochel folke ſtrange lande arryued hys land hauen lirgers wherfore ſore angred anoyed camen arryued lande wythoute leue anone ordeyned hȳ grete power dryuen owte ād deſtroye brute wyth peple kyng goffar diſcomfyted alle hys folke hym ſelf fledde fraunce ſeke helpe ād ſocour tyme regned fraunce xij kynges xj kynges aſſembled grete power helpe goffar fyght ayenſt brute goffar dwelled hem fraunce halfe yere brute mene tyme hys companye deſtroyed alle lād gaſconie let take alle treſour goffar hath let bringe ſhippes brute fonde land fayre place moche couenable made fayre ād ſtronge caſtel whan alle thing doū kyng goffar came fro fraunce xj kynges wyth hym broughtē xxm men fyght ayēſt brut companye brute vijm ccc men neuertheles two hoſtes metē gedre brute folk thurgh helpe ſelf turyn coſyn coryn wel ād manly hym deffended foughtē ſo ī lytel time quelled frenſhmē two thouſād moo tho lyue fledde way bataill turȳ brute coſyn ſlayn ād brut let burye worthely whā ſpace leyſer caſtell made tho let calle caſtell tour ye name turyne buryed ād yet thys day ther noble cyte called tour whan kyng goffar wyſte turyn dede came ayen hys men yaf ſtrō ge bataill vnto brute brute men ſo wery fyghtyng myght lenger endure māgre hiſe brute went caſtell wyth alle men ād made yates faſt ſaue hym ſelfe take counſeyll amonges hem beſt brute coryn toke counceill ordeyned coryn preueli ſholde go owte hyde hym wode ther bi tyl morne mornyng whan kȳg brute ſholde fyght wyt hys enemyes coryn ſhold come folke owne ſyde ſlee doo harme might mornyng dawenyng brute went owte caſtell faught vaylliauntly hys enemyes ād fierſly defended hem wythyn lytel tyme brute folke ſlew viijc kyng goffars men tho came coryn fro buſſhement ſmote grounde ād hys companye wolde ſtonde abyde ſo kyng goffart folke diſcomfited begonne faſt flee brute coryn hyr companye ferſely hem purſued quelyd mo theyr fleddyng dyden bataille maner vaillaūt kyng brute victorye hys ennemyes neuertheles made moch̄ ſorowe coſyn thurȳ ſlayn̄ othir alſo hys men loſt bataille ther ſlayn hys men vij c xv whyche let nobely burye ye caſtell tour ther buryed turyn hys coſyn ¶how king brute arryued totteneſſe ile albyon bataille bytwene coryn gogmagog capitulo quarto alle thys thing done brute wolde lenger ther dwelle fyghte ne moo leſe hys peple kynghts goffarus peple myght euery day encreſſe moo moo brute peple laſſen ād therfore toke alle hys men ād wēt vnto ſee ād wynd ād weder wylle fyfthe daye afterward arryued ī hauen totteneſſe camen jle albyon ther fō de thei nethir man nethir womā ſtorye telleth ye geāts dwelled hylles ād caues brute ſawe lōde fayre ād lyking good alſo ād hys folke goddeſſe dyane hym behyght tho kīg brute wonder glad ād ryght wel content ād lete aſſemble vpō day alle hys folcke make ſolempne ſacrefyce grete feſt honowr reuerence dyane ye goddeſſe thurgh who counſeyll comen good fayre lād whan hyr ſolempnyte made vpon day ſate mete ther camen vpon hem ſodenly xxx geants quelled brute men xxx brute hys men anone ſturtē vp foughten wyth geants quelled hē euerychō one geant maiſtre alle called gogmagog ſtronger hyer geāts ād brute kept ſaued hys lyf encheſon ſhold wreſtell wyt coryn coryn greter hyer brute men frō gerdelſtede vpward gogmagog corȳ vndertoke wraſtlyn ynfere▪ ſo gedre wraſtled longe tyme laſt gogmagog geant held coryn ſo faſte brack two rybbes hys ſyde wherfore vaylliaūt knight coryn ſore angry toke tho gogmagog geant bytwene hys armes kaſt downe vpon roche ſo gogmagog brak peces ſo deyed euyll deth therfore ye place called yet vnto day ſaulte gogmagog ād tho yaf brute alle contre coryn coryn kalled hys name cornewaille hys men kalled cornewailles ād ſo ſhull men cōtre ben̄ called euermore contre dwelled coryn men made townes ād howſes inhabyted land hyr wylle brute made london kalled thys lande bretaigne ſcotland albyne walys cambir capitulo quinto brute men wentē forth ſawen aboute ī diuerſe place wher might fynde good place couenable thei might make cite folke ye laſt camen fayr ryuer kalled thamys brute begā make fair cyte let calle newe troye mynde remēbraūce ye grete troye which̄ place hir lygnage comē brute let fall downe wodes let crye ſowe lādes ād done mowe mede ſuſtenaūce peple punctel departed lād hem ſo euerychon certaȳ place dwelle vpō ād brute let calle thys lande bretaigne owne name folk let calle breton brute goten wyfe geunogen thre ſoens worthy deedes fyrſt kalled lotrȳ ſecōd albanak thred cāber brute bare corone ye cite newe troye xx yere time cite made ther made lawes bretōs holdē thys noble kyng brute wonderly well beloued among alle men peple brute ſones alſo loued wonderly well gedre whē king brute ſought alle ye londe lēgthe brede fonde lande joyned bretaign̄ north ād land yaf brute albanack ſone let kalle albanye hys name kalled scotlād brute fond othre contree toward weſt yaf camber hys ſone let calle camber name ād nowe kalled wales▪ whā brute regned xx yere ſayd deyed cyte newe troye hys ſone hym entryd wyt mochel honour lotryn brute ſone crownyd king wyt mochel ſolempnite alle lande bretaigne whā crownyd albanack camber two bretheren went ayen hyr owne contre lyued mykel honour lotryn brother regned kȳg gouerned land wel wyſely good man wonder well beloued alle hys land befell ſo albanack lotryns brother dwelled hys owne lande wyt mochel honour worſhyp gouerned hys lād wyſely thenne cam kyng humbar hunlād wyt grete power arriued ī albayne wolde haue cōquered land began werre vpō albanack hȳ quelled bataille whā albanak ſlayne folck ye land fled vnto lotryn told kīg bretaigne brother ſlayne prayed hȳ helpe auenge brother deth lotrine anon̄ let aſſemble alle bretōs kēt douer derewent north folk ſouthfolck keftefen lyndeſſey aſſembled ſped faſt ward ennemies yeue hē bataille lotryne ſent cāber brother ſhold come al ſo hȳ alle power might make • hȳ helpe ſo dyd good ſo comē gedres toke wey preuelich ſech̄ hū bar wher might hym fynde ſo betell hūbar beſides water grete ryuer wyt folk hȳ diſpotre tho came lotryne cāber brother hyr folk ſodēly er ony wiſt whan hūbar ſaw hȳ come ſore adrad aſ moche men wiſt ād alſo vnarmed ād anone hūbar drede lept water drēched hȳ ſelfe ſo died men alle ſlayne ſo none eſcaped· ād therfore water called hū bar euermore ſhall called thus encheſon kyng humbar therinne drēched lotryne wente hys ſhippes toke goold ſyluer moche fand vnto hym ſelfe ād othir pilfre yaf vnto othir folke hooſt founden one ſhippes fayre damyſell kyng humbars doughter kalled eſtilde whan kyng lotryne ſawe hyr toke hyr hȳ hyr fayrneſſe ouertaken wyt loue wolde haue wedded hyr tydȳges came coryn anone thought auenge vpon lotrin moch̄ lotryne made couenāt ſpouſe corines doughter kalled guē tolen coryn haſte wente vnto newe troye ād thus ſayd kyng lotryne nowe certes ſayd ye rewarde full euell alle paynes ſuffred haue many tymes kyng brute fadre therfore wyll nowe auenge vpon yow ād drewe owt ſwerd hyghe wolde haue ſlayne kyng lotryne damiſell wente bytwēne hem made hem accorded maner kyng lotryne ſholde ſpouſe guentolen whiche corynes doughter ād ſo lotryne dyde neuertheles ſpouſed guentolen corines doughtyr preuelych̄ came eſtrilde brought hyr chylde gate hyr fayre doughter which̄ called abrā hit befell anone corine deyed anone ded kyng lotryne forſake guentolen hys owne wyfe made eſtrilde quene hys royaulme guētolen wente thēs cornewaille ſeyſed • le londe hyr handes punctel moch̄ ſhe hir faders heir ād vnderfong feaultres homage men land ād aſſembled grete hooſt grete power ben vpon lotryne auenged hyr lord came hym yaf ſtrōg bataylle ther lotryn ſlayne men diſcomfited xv yere regne guentolen let take eſtrild abrā hyr doughter ād lete bynde bothe hā de fete ād caſt hem water ſo drenched wher fore water euermore called abram· name ye damiſel eſtrildis doughter engliſſhmen calleth water ſeuerne walſhmen calle abram day gwentelon let crowne hyr quene londe ād gouerned land full well wyſely vnto tyme madan hyr ſone lotryne beget vpon hir xx winter age myght king ſo quene regnyd xv yere ād tho let ſhe hir ſone crowne regned gouerned land well ād honorabely ſhe went cornuwaille ād ther ſhe dwelled hyr lyfes tyme ¶of kyng madan regned pee hys lyfes tyme· ād menpris maulyn ſones menpris ſlewe maulyn brother ād wulfes drow hym peces capitulo ſexto whan vaylliaunt kȳg madan regned xxx yere· deyed lyeth newe cyte troye punctel two ſones whyche owne called menprys men kalled maulyn thyſe two brother hir fadres deth ſtryuen faſt lande mēprys encheſon eldeſt ſone wolde gladli haue lāde punctel maulyn wolde graunte ne ſuffre hym ſo token day loue accorde day mēpris let quelle brother thurgh treſon hym ſelf afterward helde londe ād anone let crowne hym kȳg regned ād bicame ſo lither man deſtroied alle men hys londe laſt became ſo wikked ſo lecherous forſoke hys owne wyf vſed ſynne ſodome wherfore almighty god wroth vpon hȳ toke vengeaunce day wēt wode hountyng loſte folke went allone vp ād downe crieng hys men ād ther came wulfes drowe peces regned xxiiij yere whā hys peple wiſt dede punctel made ioye ynough anone made ebrac ſon kyng ād regned moche honour ¶of kyng ebrack conquered fraūce bygate xx ſones xxiij doughtres cap vij ebrac regned lx yere ſtrōge man myghty ebrac thurgh hys myght grete helpe hys brytons conquerd fraunce ād wan ther ſo moche gold ſyluer whā came ayen lande made made cyte canterbury wynceſtre regned xiij yere ād deyed lyeth wyncheſtre ¶of king bladud ludibras ſone regned good man nygromancer capitulo xi lud ludibras regned bladud ſone grete nygromancer thurgh hys craft nygromancye made meruailloꝰ hothe bathe geſt tellyth̄ regned xxi yere lyeth newe troye ¶of kyng leyr anſwere iōgeſt doughter gracyouſly maryed kyng fraunce capitulo xij kyng bladud regned leir ſone thys leyr made towne lyceſtre let calle towne name gouerned towne wel nobely thys kyng leyr iij doughteres fyrſt called gonorill ſecond rygan thridde doughter called cordeill ād iongeſt doughter faireſt ād beſt condicyōs kyng hyr fadre became olde man wold hys doughtres maryed er deyde fyrſt thought aſſaye whiche hem loued hym moſt ād beſt ſhe whiche loued hȳ beſt ſhold beſt ben̄ maryed axed fyrſte moche ſhe hym loued ſhe anſwerd ſaid better thā hyr owne lyfe nowe certes ſayd fadre grete loue tho axed ſecōd doughter moche ſhe hym loued ſhe ſayd ād paſſȳg alle creature ye worlde bi trouth ſayd ye fadre may axe tho axed ye thridde doughter moche ſhe loued certes fadre ſayd ſhe ſuſters haue tolde yow gloſing wordes forſothe ſhall telle trouth j loue moch̄ j ought loue fadre ād bryng yow certayn loue yow ſhal yow telle ye bene worth ye loued kyng hyr fadre wende ſhe ſcorned become wonder wroth ād ſwore heuen erthe ſhe ſholde neuer haue good doughters loued hȳ ſo moch̄ ſholde ben̄ wel auaūced maried ye fyrſt doughter maried managles kīg ſcotlād ſecond maried hanemos erle cornualle ſo ordeyned ſpake bitwene hē ſholde departe reaulme bytwene hem two deth kȳg leyr hyr fadre ſo cordeyl yongeſt doughter ſhold thyng haue land· cordeyll wonder fayre ſo good condicyōs maners kyng fraūce agāpe herde hyr ſpeke ād ſente kȳg leir hyr fadre haue hir vnto wyfe praied hȳ therof kyng leir hir fadre ſent hȳ word departed lō de vnto ij doughtres ād ſaid lande wherwyth hir marie whan agāpe herde anſwer ſente anon̄ leir ſaid axed nothȳg hyr onely hir clothyng hyr anone kȳg leir ſent hyr ouer ſee kyng fraunce receyued hyr moche worſhip wyt moch̄ ſolempnite ſpouſed hir made hyr quene fraunce ¶how kyng leir driuē owte hys land thurgh hys folye cordeill hys yōgeſt doughter helpe hym hys nede capitulo xiij thꝰ fel afterward two eldelſt doughtres wolde abyde tyll leir hyr fadre dede werred vpon hym while lyued moche ſorwe ſhame hȳd dyd wherfore benōmen hȳ holy royaulme bitwene hem ordeined one hē ſhold haue kyng leir ſoiorne lyfe tyme xl knyghtes ſquyers might worſhuply go ride whidder wolde cōtre hē lyked pley ſolace managles kyng scotlād kīg leir hym maner aboue ſayd half yere wer paſſed corneil eldelſt doughter ād quene scotland ſo anuoyet hȳ peple anone ſhe ād hir lorde ſpake gedre wherfore knyghtes half hys ſquyers hȳ gone mo left xxx whā don̄ leir began make moche ſorwe encheſon eſtate empeired mē hȳ ſcorne deſpyte euer befor wherfore wiſt ye laſt thought wold go cornewaille rygan othir doughter whan comen erle wyf leires doughter welcomed hym wyth moche ioye dwelled wyt xxx knyghtes ſquiers dwelled ther ſcarſely xij monthes doughter hȳ wery ād companye hir lorde ſhe hȳ ſcorne deſpite ſo frō xxx· knyghtes broughtē vnto x afterward v ſo ther left moo tho made ſorowe ynough ād ſaid ſore wepyng allas euer cam̄ londe ſayd yet ben better haue dwelled wt fyrſt doughter anon̄ wēt thēnes fyrſt doughter anone ſhe hym ſaw come ſhe ſwore alle goddes ād bi moch̄ ſhe might yt ſhold haue mo wt hī one knyght· wolde ther abide tho begā leir ayen̄ wepe made moch̄ ſorowe ſayd tho ala haue longelyued ſorwe meſchyef falle poure ſom time riche haue frende ne kyn yt woll good whā riche men honoured worſhipped euery man hath ſcorne deſpyte wote wel cordeil yongeſte doughter ſaid trouth whan ſhe ſayd moch j ſo moche ſhold ben̄ beloued ād alle j good tho beloued ād honoured richeſſe two doughters gloſed tho nowe ſette lytell pry ſoth tolde cordeill wolde byleue ne vnderſtande therfor j let hyr go fro thing ſette lyttell pry j wote neuer ſyth yt two doughters thus haue diſceyued j ſomoch̄ loued nowe muſt nedes ſech̄ hir othir lād lightly let gone fro wytoute rewarde yeftes ſhe ſayd ſhe loued moch̄ ſhe ought loue hir fadre alle maner reſon tho ſholde haue axed hyr ād ſo fayre beheftes thurgh fals ſpeche ij eldeſt doughters diſceyued thys maner leir lōg time began make mone laſt ſhope hȳ ſee paſſed ouer fraū ce aſked ād aſpied wher quene might fondē mē told hȳ wher ſhe ād whā cam̄ cyte ther ſhe preuely ſēt ſquyer vnto ye quene telle hir hir fader comen hyr gret nedes whā ſquyer came quen̄ tolde hyr euery dele hyr ſuſters beghȳnyng vnto ye ende cordeill quene anon̄ toke gold ſyluer plente toke ye ſquyer coūſeille ſhold gon̄ bere vnto hir fadre ſhold go certaȳ cite araye waſſhe thā come ayen̄ hir bringe hȳ honeſt cōpanye knightes x • atte leſt wt meyne then̄ ſhold ſende hyr lord king ſaye yt comen ſpeke wt doughtir ſeen ſo dyd whan king ye quene herde camen wt mochel honour receyued kyng fraūce tho let ſende thurgh royaume ꝯmaū ded alle men ſholde hȳ entendaund kȳg leir quenes fadre alle maner thyng ſelf whā kȳg leyr dwelled ther moneth tolde king ye quene doughtyr hys ij eldeſt doughtres ſerued agāpe anone let ordeyne grete hooſt ſend bretaygne wt leir quenes fader conquere land ayen̄ kȳgdō cordeyll alſo came wyt hyr fadre bretaigne haue ye royaume hyr fadres deth went ſhip paſſed ſee came bretaigne foughtē felon hē ſcōfyted quelled tho land ayen̄ lyued thre yere helde royaume pee afterward deyed cordeill hys doughter hȳ let ēburye mikel honour lyceſtre ¶howe morgan conedage neveus cordeyl werred vpon hir put hir pryſō cap xiiij whan king leir dede· cordeil yōgeſt doughter helde land v yere mene time deyed hir lord agampe kyng fraunce ād deth ſhe left vydue tho came morgā conedage cordeyl ſuſtre ſones hyr enymite moche aunte ſholde haue lande bytwene hē ordeyned grete power vpon hir werred gretly ād neuer reſt tyl hir taken put hir vn deth▪ tho morgā conedage ſeyſed alle land departed bytwene hem helden xij yere whā ye xij yere gon̄ ther began bitwene hym grete debate ſo yt werred ſtrōgli togedre eueri hȳ dyd othir moche diſeſe morgan wold haue lande fro beyonde hūbar conedage helde came ayēſt hȳ wyt ſtrōge power ſo yt morgā durſt abyde fled away wale conedage purſued hī toke hī queld tho came conedage ayen ſeyſed lāde hāde helde regned xxxiij yere tho deyed lyeth newe troye ¶how reygnold conedages ſone regned aftir fadre time rayned blood thre dayes tokenyng grete deth capitulo xv conedage regned reygnold hys ſone wiſe knight herdy curtois wel nobeli gouerned lād wōder well made hym beloued alle maner folcke ī tyme rayned blode laſted thre dayes god wold ſone ther came grete deth peple deyde without nōbre wherfore man might ſkape tyll almighty god therof toke mercy pite tho began ceſe reignold regned xxij yere dyed lyeth york ¶how gorbodyan regned pee reygnoldes ſone capitulo xvi reygnold regned gorbodiā ſone xv yere ād dyed lyeth york gorbodyan ij ſones one ſlowe haue herytage ād ydoine hir moder quelled wherfor lād deſtroyed cap xvij gorbodyā dede hys ij ſones becamen ſtoute prowde▪ euer warred gedre ye lād one called ferre othir porres ferres wold haue lād othir wold ſuffre hȳ ferres felōs hert thought thurgh treſon ſlee brother preuely wēt fraūce ther abode wt king syward tyl vpō time came ayen̄ fought wyt brother ferres happed hȳ euell· ſlayne fyrſt whā ydome hir moder wiſt porres dede ſhe made grete ſorow encheſon ſhe loued hȳ thā ād thought hȳ quelle preuely preuely ſhe came hyr ſone vpō night wyt two knyues ther cutte ſhe throte body alſo ī ſmale peces herd euer ſuch̄ kurſed moder quelled wyt hyr owne hādes hyr owne ſone lōge time cam reproue ſhame moder encheſon owne ſone murdrid othir· ſo ſhe loſt hē iiij kinges courtoiſly helde bretaigne ben̄ hir name cap xviij whan two bretheren ſo dede lefte behynd hē nethir ſone ne doughter ne none kynred might haue heritage moch̄ ſtrēgeſt men dryuē ſcōfyted ye febleſt tokē hyr lā de ſo euery contrey grete werre ſtryfe vnder thaȳ amōg alle othir thȳges ther amōges hē cōtre ouercame othir ſtrēgth̄ might token alle lādes euery thaȳ toke certaȳ contre ꝯtre let kalle hȳ king one hē called scater ād kyng ſcotland ād othir called dawailliere kȳg loegers alle lād lotrinꝰ brute ſone thridde called rudac kīg walys yt iiij called cloten punctel ād kyng cornewaille clotē ſhold haue lande reſō ther man wiſt non̄ ſo rightfull heyr ſtrēgheſt ſet lytell bi hē leſſe eſtate therfor clotē nomore lād among hē cornewaylle ¶of kȳg donebāt clotes ſone wōne lād capitulo xix clotē ſone called donebāt deth fadre became herdy man fayr curtois ſo paſſed ye kȳ ge britaigne fraūce mā hede worthyneſſe anon̄ knight wiſt wel whā fader lyued moſt rightfull heyr alle lād ſhold haue reſon kīges yt ſtrēgth̄ benōme hȳ lād afterward donebant ordeyned power fyrſt conquered ye lande loegiers wolde haue ꝯquered scotland walys scater cam̄ men yaf hȳ bataill ād rudac cam̄ ayē walſhmen helpe befell ſo rudak queled ſcater alſo plaȳ bataill ſo donebant victorye cōquered lāde wel maintened pee quiete neuer ſo wel maintened donebant fyrſt kyng euer wered crowne golde bretaigne capitulo xx thys donebant let make hȳ croune golde wered ye crowne vpō hys hede neuer kyng dyd ordeyned ſtatut man done neuer ſo moch̄ harme yf might come yt tēple mā ſhold hȳ miſdo gon̄ therin ſauf pee ād go ꝯtrey hȳ lyked mā ſet hōde vpō hȳ thā ſhold leſe lyfe donebant made towne malmeſbury towne ye vyſe ād whā regned wel wortheli xl yere deyed lyeth newe troye ¶how brenne belȳ departed bitwene thaȳ ye lād deth donebāt hir fadre werre capitulo xxi doneband dede ſones departed land bitwene hē hir fader ordeyned ſo belȳ hys eldeſt ſone lāde thys half humbar brother brēne lād frō humbar vnto ſcotland moch̄ belyn beſt part brēne therfore wroth wolde lād belyn brother wold graūte hī wherfor cōtak werre aroſe bytwene hē ij brēne yonger brother might ne ſtrengthe ayēs belȳ ād therfor brēne thurgh cōſeyl folck went fro thēs norwey ye kyng olſinges praied hȳ helpe ſocour conquer ye lād vpon belyn hys brother vpō couenant wolde haue doughter wyfe kīg olſinges hym graunted belyn anone brother norwey ſeiſed hys hāde ye lande northūberland ād toke alle caſtelles let hem araye ād kepe coſtes ſee brenne ſhold arryue ſyde take kīg olſinges lete aſſēble grete hoſt delyuerd doughtyr brēne hȳ neceſſarie thys damiſell samye longe tyme loued kīg called gutlagh· hȳ ſhe tolde hyr coūſell brēne ſhold haue hir hir lede wt hȳ euermore ſo ſhold leſe hir wtoute ſhe might forſake delyuered frō brēne ād whā gutlagh herd thys tidȳg lay aſpye brē ne wt many ſhippes might haue ſo ye ij fletes mettē gedre fougtē lōg time ſo brēne ſhippes turned ayen̄ diſcōfyted kȳg gutlagh toke ſamie put hir ī ſhippe brēne ſhamefulli fled then̄s mā diſcōfyted gutlagh wolde haue gon īto owne cō tre cam vpō hȳ grete tēpeſt v dayes laſtyd ſo tēpeſt driuē bretaigne wyt iv ſhippes ād mo tho kept coſtes ye ſee token gutlagh famye folke hē preſented belyn belyn put hē pryſon ¶how belyn drofe oute hys lande kyng gutlagh dēmarke samye ca xxij hit longe ye brēne came ayen̄ grete nauye ſēte hys brother belȳ ſhold yelde ayen̄ hys land wyf folke caſtelles elles wold deſtroye lāde belȳ drade thīg menace wold thing deſyre wherfor brē ne came wyth folk ād fought belyn brenne diſcōfyted folke ſlayne hȳ ſelf fledde xij men fraunce belyn brennes brother went yorke toke coūſeyl might king gutlagh kȳg gutlagh profred become hys man holde hys lāde hȳ yeldȳg yere thouſand pounde ſiluer euer ād ſikerneſſe couenaunts behold gutlagh ſhold brȳg good hoſtages ſhold done homage folke yet ſhold ſwere vpon boke yt theſe couenāts ſhold neuer ben̄ broke ne falſed belyn tho counſeyl lordes folke graūted hȳ axyng ſo gutlagh became man ād belyn vnderfeng hȳ homage othe writyng ſame couenāts vpō theſe couenāts king gutlagh nōme ſamye folke ād went thēs turned ayen denmarck euermore couenants holden truage paied tyll tyme honelos king denmark alſo thys lāde thurgh wyf gildeburgh ſpouſed· ſhe right heir lande punctel belȳ dwelled pee worſhipfully helde amōg barōs made iiij real weyes one frō eſt weſt kalled watlyngſtrete frō north vnto ſouth called jkelmeſtrete ij othir weyes made ī boſſȳge thurgh oute lāde called toſſe othir foſſedike maī tened wel ye good lawes donebant hys fadre made ordeyned ī time ſaid howe accord made bitwene brēne belȳ thurgh cornewen hir moder ca xxiij brēne belynus brother lōg time dwelled traūce ther cōquered grete lordſhip mariage duke bourgoyn̄ thurgh doughter duke fewȳ ſpouſed right heyr lande brēne ordeyned grete power hys folk alſo fraū ce came thys lande fyght wyth kyng belȳ hys brother belyn came alſo ayenſt hym grete power breton wolde haue yeuen hȳ batayll theyr moder cornewenne tho lyued herd yt one brother wolde haue deſtroied ād went bytwene hyr ſones hem made accorded moche payne ſo laſt ye two bretheren michell blys went gedre grete troye nowe called londō ther dwelled yere ād toke theyre coūſeil gone conquere fraunce ſo thei dydē brent townes deſtroyed land length̄ brede kyng fraūce yaf hȳ batayll power ouer comen yaf truage vnto belyn brother wenten forth rome cōquered rome lūbardye germanye toke homage ād feaulte erles baron othir thei camen lande bretaigne ād dwelled breton ioye ād reſt tho made brēne ye towne briſtowe ſyth went ouer owne lordſhip ther dwelled hys lyfe ād belyn dwelled newe troye ther made fayre gate kalled belyngeſgate owne name whan thys belyn regned nobely xj yere dyed ād lyeth newe troye kyng cormbatrꝰ quelled kyng dēmarc encheſō wold paye hī truage capitulo xxiiij thys belȳ regned ſone cormbatrus good man worthy ād ye king • dēmarke wolde paye hȳ hys truage ſay pounde ſworne oth pay • alſo writyng recorded belȳ fadre • wherfore euell payed thys kyng cormbatrꝰ aſſēbled grete hooſt brytons went dēmarke ſlow kȳg gut • ath brought lād ſubiectyō newe toke folke feaultes homage went ayen̄ lād ād came forth orkeney fōde xxx ſhippes full men woman beſides koſt ſee ye king axed thei erle maiſtyr hem courtoyſly āſwerd vnto ye kȳg ſayd exiled oute ſpaigne ſo thei trauailled half yere ād ſee wytē yf thei might fynde king lō de hē wolde haue pyte mercy yeue hē lāde contre wher might dwelle haue reſt ād become liege men hȳ wolde don̄ homage feaulte while lyued ād heyres hȳ hȳ ād hys heires holden lande ād whan kȳg thys herde pyte hē yafe hē ile al wilderneſſe ther yt nomā dwellyng ſaufe onely wilde beſtes ād erle thanked moch̄ kȳg became man dyd hī homage feaulte toke folk ād went ſame jle erle called irlamall· therfor let brother gadred grete hooſt gydre breton yafe bataylle emperour claudiꝰ quelled romayns grete plente emꝑour knight kalled hamō ſawe peple faſt ſlayn̄ preuelich̄ kaſt way owne armes toke armes dede breton ād armed hym wyt armure came bataill kyng ſayd maner syr ye good hert goddis loue romaȳs ben̄ enemyes anone ſhal ſlayne diſcōfyted euerychon ye kīg yaf kepe ne reward ſpech̄ encheſon armes vpō wende ben breton traytour euer helde next kyng preuely vnder ye ſhuldres armes ſmote ye king dede ād fell doū erthe whā armager ſawe brother dede punctel caſte away armes toke brother armes came ī ye bataill amonge breton bad hem hertely fyght faſtely downe romayns armes thei wendē ben king gynder erſt ſlayn̄ wiſt then̄ gon breton hertely fight quelled ye romains ſo laſt ye emperour forſake felde fledde faſte might folke cyte wyncheſtre fals traytour hamō queld kyng began anon̄ faſte fle haſt might armager kȳges brother purſued full ferſeiy ferſe herte▪ drofe hȳ vnto water ther toke anone ſmote both̄ hādes hede foot hewe bodi peces caſt hȳ water wherfore water called hamonus hauē afterward ther made fayre towne yet ſtā deth kalled ſoupthanptō ād afterward armager wēt wȳ cheſtre ſeke claudius ceſar emperour ther armager toke claudiꝰ ye emperour coūſeyll romains hȳ left lyue made pee wyt armager maner ye ſhal ſaye claudiꝰ emꝑour ſhold yeue armager gennen fayr doughter haue wyfe ſo lād fro tyme afterward ſhold emperours power rome vpō ſuche couenaūt yt neuer afterward none emperour rome ſhold take non̄ othir truage lād feaulte punctel ſo accorded vpon couenant claudiꝰ ceſar ſent rome doughter gennen whā ſhe comen claudiꝰ ceſar yaf hyr armager wyf armager ſpouſed hyr lō moche ſolempnite mirthe tho armager crouned made king bretaigne ¶of kyng armager who time ſaint petre preched anthiochie othir apoſtoles diuerſe contreyes ca xl kīg armager regned well worthely lāde gouerned claudius ceſar remembraunce accord reuerence ād honour doughter made lande fayre towne fayre caſtel let calle toune name clauceſtren nowe kalled glouceſtre whan don̄ emperowr toke leue went ayen̄ rome armager tho king gouerned land wel nobely lyfes tyme ād armager gote ſone wyfe kalled weſtmer whyles thys king armager regned ſaȳt petre preched anthyoche ād ther made noble chyrch̄ which̄ ſate firſt dwelled vij yere ād wēt rome made pope tyll nero emperour let hym martre ād tho preched opēly alle apoſtles diuerſe lādes ryght fayth whā armager regned xxiiij yere deyed lyeth londō howe kyng weſtmer yaf berynger iland forlet ther berynger made towne berewyke capitulo xli thys armager regned ſone weſtmer good man worthly well gouerned lande hit befell ſo tydynge came day kyng rodryck gaſconye comē land wyt grete nōbre peple dwelyng ſtaineſmore ād whan kyng weſtmer herde thyſe tydynges let aſſemble grete hooſt bretōs came kyng rodryck yaf hȳ bataill ād kyng weſtmer queld rodryck wyt owne hādes plaine bataill whan kyng rodrykes men ſawe hir lord dede yolden hym vnto ye kȳg weſtmer bicamē hys men euermore yaf hȳ contre forletē wheryn myght dwelle thydder went dwelled hyr lyfes tyme ixc men hem mo lefte bataille hyr gouerneur ād prince kalled berynger anon̄ began towne make might therȳne dwelle haue reſtorte punctel let kalle towne berewik vpō twede dwelled bycame riche woman amōges hem bretōs wold yeue hyr doughtres ſtrangers wherfore wēt ouer ſee irland brought hȳ woman ſpouſed thaȳ men koude vnderſtande lāgages ne ſpeche woman ād therfore ſpaken gedre ſcottes afterward thurgh changyng hir langages alle fraunce called ſcottes ſo ſhullē folke contre ben̄ kalled euermore kyng weſtmer let arere ſtone entryng weſtmerland ther ſlayn king roderyck· ther begā fyrſt howſing capitulo xlij bataill aboue ſaid roderyk dede kyng weſtmer remēbraūce hys victorie lete arere ther beſides wey grete ſtone yet hit ſtant euermore ſhall ſtande let graue ſtone lrēs thus ſayd kyng weſtmer bretaigne quelde place roderyk enemye waſtmer fyrſt man made townes hous englōd ſtone begȳneth weſtmerlād weſtmer let calle aft owne name whā weſtmer ſo don̄ dwelled lyfes time contre weſtmerlād condicyons well gouerned lande alle men loue pee hys lyfe neuer cō tak debate ne werre bretaigne regned king pee lyfes tyme ād whā ben̄ kyng xi yere dyed lyeth yorke kȳg lucie regned coill fadre good man becam criſten ca xliiij kȳg coil regned lucye ſone yt good mā god ye peple ſēt rome apoſtle eulē tre tho pope ſayd wolde become cryſtē man receyue baptiſme ye name god torne right beleue eulē tre ſēt two legatys called pagan elybayne thys land baptyſed king mayne wēt fro toune towne baptyſed peple till lande baptyſed clvj yere ye incarnacion lord • hū criſt king made tho ij erche biſſhoppes cāterburye york othir many biſſhoppes yet ben ī lād whā thees ij legatys baptyſed ye land ordeyned preſtes baptiſe child make ſacramēt ād went ayen̄ rome ye kȳg dwelled lāde regned grete lād wold ſuffre othir kȳg liued werre debate amōges hem l yere wtout kȳg befel afterward grete prince came fro rome land men called ſeuerie nought werre ſaue ye right rome natheles dwelled half yere ī lād yt ye bretōs ne quelled hē whā rome wyſt seuerye ſo ſlayne ſent grete lord land mē kalled allec ſtrōg mā myghty body· dwelled land long tyme dyd moch̄ ſorwe bretōs ſo aftyr pure malice choſen hem kyng amonges hem men kalled aſtlepades ād aſſembled grete hooſt breton went londō ſech̄ allec fō den queld hym alle hys felaws one mē kalled walon defended hȳ ferſely fought longe breton laſt diſcomfyted breton nomme hī boundē handes foot kaſt hȳ water wherfore water called afterward walbroke tho regned aſtlepades quyete tyl one erles men kalled coill made fayr town ayens ye kynges wyll let kalle town colcheſtre name wherfore kyng full wroth ād thought deſtroye erle ād began werre vpon brought grete power yaf batail erle erle defended hȳ ferſely power ād ſlowe king hym ſelf bataille tho coill crowned made kyng land coil regned gouerned royaulme wel nobely noble man wel beloued amōg bretōs whā rome herden aſtlepades ſlayne wonder glad ſent grete prynce romayns whiche kalled conſtaūce came kyng coyll chalēge ye truage wont payed rome kīg āſwerde wel wyſely ſayd wold paye rome reſon wolde good wyll ſo accorded wythoute contak thei dwelled gedre loue kyng coill yaf hys doughter eleyne conſtāce haue hir ſpouſe whyche fayr wyſe good wel lettred conſtāce ſpouſed hyr moch̄ honour ād befell ſone afterward king coyll deyed yere hys regne xiij ād lyeth colcheſtre entiered king conſtance romaȳ whiche choſen kīg deth coyll moche yt ſpouſed eleyn whyche kȳg coyles doughter capitulo xlvi kyng coyl cō ſtance made kyng crowned moche ſpouſed king coyles doughter whiche heir lande whiche conſtāce regned well wortheli gouerned lande begate wyf eleyn ſone called cō ſtantyne kyng bare trewe fayth truely dyd hem rome lyfe whan regned xv yere dyed lyeth york ¶how conſtantyne king conſtances ſone ſone ſaint eleyn gouerned ruled lande emꝑour rome capitulo xlvij kȳg cōſtāce regned conſtantine ſone ād ſone ſeint eleyne yt fonde holy croſſe holy lande conſtantyne became emperour rome hit befell ſo tyme ther emperour rome ſarazyne tyrant called maxencyus whiche put deth beleued god ād deſtroyed holy chirch̄ hys power ſlew cryſten men might fȳde amōg let martre ſaint kateryne ād many othir criſten peple drede deth fleddē camen lande king conſtantine tolde ſorwe maxence dyd criſtiēte wherfore conſtātyne grete pyte made moch̄ ſorowe aſſē bled grete hoſt grete power went ouer rome toke ye cyte quelled ther myſbeleue might finde tho made emperour ād good man gouerned hȳ ſo wel alle lādes hym attēdaūt ben vnd er gouernaill deuel tyrant maxence tyme ye lā de grece herde thys tydynge then̄ became wode ſodenly dyed ſo ended hys lyfe whan cōſtantine went fro land rome toke hym moder eleyne mochel wyſedome ſhe coude othir grete lordes yt moſt loued· one called hoell called taberne thridde morhin ād toke alle lande kepe vnto erle cornewaille called octauiā anon̄ octauyan wiſt hys lord dwellȳg rome ſeiſed alle land hys hand therwith dyd wyl among high̄ lowe helde hym kyng whan tydinge came conſtātyne emperour wonder wroth toward ye erle octauyan ſente taberne wt xijm men deſtroye erle falſeneſſe ād arryued porteſmouth whan octauyan wiſte aſſembled grete power breton diſcō fyted taberne taberne fledde then scotland ordeyned grete power came ayen̄ land othir tyme yeue bataille octauiā whē octauyā herde telle aſſē bled grete power cam̄ towardes taberne moche might ſo two hoſtes mettē vpon ſteineſmore ſtrōgeli ſmoten gydre tho octauyan diſcōfited fledde then norwey taberne ſeyſed alle land hādes townes caſtelles aſmoch̄ thei ther ſith octauiā came ayen̄ fro norwey wyt grete power ſeyſed ayen̄ lande hande ād drofe owt romains tho made king regned maruniā ye emperours coſyn rome ſpouſed octauians doughter made kyng capitulo xlviij kyng octauyan gouerned land wel nobely non̄ heir ſauf doughtyr yōge child loued aſmoch̄ lyfe ād moche ſeke point deth myght lenger regne wold haue made one neveus haue ben̄ kȳg which̄ noble knyght ſtrōg man whiche called conan meriedok ād ſhold haue kept kīges doughtyr haue maried hir whā tyme ben̄ lordes lande wolde ſuffre yaf hir coūſeill maried ſōme hygh̄ mā honour thā might ſhe haue hir luſt take coūſeil ye emꝑour conſtātine hir lord coūſeill thei accorded choſe tho cador cornewaill wēte ye emꝑour thys meſſage toke wey went rome tolde ye emperour tyding well wyſely emꝑour ſent lande hī owne coſyn vncles ſone noble knight ſtronge called maxymian ſpouſed octauianus doughtyr crowned kȳg lande maximian emꝑours coſyn cōquered almorican yaf conāmeriedok cap xlix king maxymiā bicame ſo ryall thought cō quere land amorycan grete rycheſſe herde telle yt ther lande ſo ne lefte man worthineſſe knight ſquier ne none othir man ne toke wyt grete domage land left home behynd hī mā kepe lande toke hem hym fro land xxx thouſād knyghtes doubthy mennys bodyes wēt ouer lande amorican ther ſlewe king whiche called imball conquered alle lāde whā ſo done kalled conā ſaid· moch̄ kȳg octauyan haue made king bretaigne thurgh ye lette deſtrobled ye kȳg yeue land amorican make therof kȳg moche ye ben breton men alſo become fro bretaigne lād haue ſame name ād nomore kalled amoricā ſhal called lyttel bretaigne lād fro whēs ye ben comen ſhall called mochel bretaigne ād ſo ſhal mē knowe one bretaign̄ fro conan moriedok thāked hī frendeli ſo made kȳg littel bretaigne whā al maximian went thēs rome tho made emperour conſtantyne conan meriedok dwelled littel bretaigne mochel honour let ordeyne ijm plougmē lāde erye land harwe ād ſawe feſſed hē richely moche kȳg conan ne none hys knyghtes peple wolde take wife nacyon fraūce ſēt tho grete bretaigne ye erle cornewaille men called dyonothe ſhold cheſe thurgh owt alle lande xjm maydens ſaye viij mene peple thre thouſād greteſt lordes ſholde hem ſpouſe whē dionothe vnderfounge cōmaūdemēt let ſeche thurgh ye grete bretaygne many nombre came man durſt withſtonde commaūdements moche alle lād taken hymward kepe done thing hem good lyked whan alle maydēs aſſembled let hem come hym londō let ordeyne hē ſhippes haſtely aſmoch̄ hē nedeth ye vyage toke owne doughtere called vrſula faireſt creature man wiſt ād wold haue ſent hyr kȳg conan ſhold haue ſpouſed hir made hir quene land ſhe anone made preuely god vowe chaſtite hyr fadre wiſte ne man elles lyuing vpon erthe vrſula xim maidēs cōpanye wēt toward lyttell bretaigne martred coleyne cap l vrſula cheſe hyr companie xi maidēs ſhe ladye ād maiſtreſſe alle wente ſhip one tyme ye water yt called tamyſe ꝯmaū ded hyr kyn alle hyr frendes almyghty god ād ſailled toward lyttell bretaigne comē ye hygh̄ ſee ſtrō ge tēpeſte aroſe goddis wille vrſula wyt hyr ſhippes hyr ꝯpanye dryuē toward hundlād thurgh tempeſt arryued hauē cyte coleyne kȳg ye lād called gowan tho ye cite whā wiſt tyding ſo many fayr maidēs ther arryued toke elga brother houſhold hym went ſhyppes ſeē fayre companye whan ſaw hem ſo fayre companye wold haue ouer fayne hē betake fro hem hyr maydēhode vrſula good mayd coūſeilled prayed warned thought hem hir felawes ſhold defende hē hir myght rather ſuffre deth ſuffre hir body defowled ſo alle maydens became ſo ſtedfaſt god thei hē defended grace ſo none hem power done hē ſhame wherfore kīg gowan ſore anoyed wroth let ſlee hem euerychone ād ſo alle maydenes martred loue god lyen coleyne ¶how kȳg gowan came deſtroye lād mā grete power kalled gracyan deffended land capitulo lj whā kīg gowā ſarezȳ called brother elga ſayd hȳ ſhold go cō quere ye lād fayr maydēs borne ordeyned tho grete power pechitet denmark orkoney norwey thei came lande brēt townes ſlewe folck caſt downe chyrches houſes religiō robbed lād lēght brede put deth alle wolde forſake right beleue criſtēdome moch̄ ther ſoueraigne might hē helpe kȳg maxymian takē wyt hȳ alle ye worthy men goon cōquere littel bretaign̄· ſame time ye telle ſeynt albone martred thurgh ye wode tyrant dyocliſiā ſame place abbye made ſeint albone whyles yt paynyme cōuerted hī god thurgh predicacyon clerk wyſe man called antybell herburghed night howſe thys incarnacyon jeſu criſt ccxxvi yere mē ſhal vnderſtāde ſaȳt albone ſuffred martyrdome ſeynt edmond martred ād therfore ſeȳt albone called fyrſt martyr englond thys gowannes brother folk ſaraſynes wēt thurgh oute land deſtroyed thīg fonden thing ne ſpared whan tydȳg cam̄ rome kyng gowan bigonne deſtroye thys land emperour rome ſēt ſtrong man ād grete power called graciā wyt xxiiij men wel fyghtyng caſt owt saraſenes owt land alle arryued porte mouthe maximian might come hym ſelfe moch̄ choſen emperour deth conſtātinꝰ ſaīt elynes ſone whan gracyā arryued hoſt let aſpie preuely wher kīg gowā might fondē ād came vpō hem ſodēly lay hir beddes diſcomfited ſlew hem hyr beddes euery chō non̄ hem eſcaped ſauf gowan fled moche ſorowe hys contre sone aftir maximian ſlayne rome thurgh treſon whan gracyan wiſt tydyng let crowne hȳ ſelf kyng lande ¶howe gracyan made ſelf kyng whan maximiā ſlaȳ afterward ye breton queld wikkedneſſe c lij gracyā whā began regne became ſo wikked ſterne ſo moch̄ dyd ye bretōs thei ſlowe hȳ amōges hē tho ye kȳg gowan vnderſtōd gracyā ſlayne downe deth aſſēbled grete power came ayen̄ lād erſ • don̄ harme tho dyd moch̄ tho deſtroyed alle thys lāde criſtē peple moche bretaign̄ ſo man ſo herdie nempne god ſo dyd anon̄ put ſtrōge deth biſſhop londō tho called goſſeleȳ eſcaped wēte thēs thē rome ſeche ſocour helpe deſtroye ſarrazenes yt deſtroyed land romaȳs ſaydē thei ſo ofte anoyed hir ſending folke bretaigne helpe ye bretōs wolde ſo done ſo ye biſſhop goſſeleyne went thēs withoute ſocour helpe tho went kȳg lytell bretaigne kalled aldroye ād thridde king gowā meriedoke ſayd biſſhop prayed thys kyng aldroye helpe ſocour kīg grete pyte hys herte whan herde biſſhop fledde criſten men ſlayne grete bretaigne thurgh paynyms ſarazenes graunted hym conſtantyne brother helpe hȳ wyt power folke hym dyd araye hors armure ſhippes alle thīg hem nedeth vyage whan thyng redy called biſſhop hȳ ſaid punctel take helpe ſocour cō ſtātyn̄ brother vpon thys couenant god yeue grace paynymes ſarazenes ſhende diſcōfyte ye make hȳ kȳg biſſhop graunted hȳ good wille conſtantyne biſſhop toke leue king aldroye betok hem god ād delyuerd thaym xij men wēte hyr ſhippes ſailled toward grete bretaigne arryued toteneſſe whā breton herde tydynges hē came ſocour ſtrō gely holpen ordeyned hē hughe nombre peple cam̄ hē moch̄ honour gowā anon̄ wiſt tydynges aſſembled ſarazenes came ayenſt hem yafe hem bataille conſtantyne ſlow owne handes alle ſarazenes diſcomfyted ſlayne non̄ eſcaped conuerted vnto god cōſtantyne kynges brother lytel bretaign̄ crowned kȳg mochel bretaigne worthyneſſe capitulo liij annone bataylle went lōdō crouned ther conſtātyne made hȳ king lande ād biſſhop goſſelyne ſette croune hede anoyted falleth king ben̄ tho began criſtēdome king cōſtātine whan crowned anone ſpouſed hys wyfe thurgh ye counſeyll breton begate thre ſones hir fyrſte called conſtance· othir aurelambros thridde vter conſtāce eldeſt brother whā came age made hī mō ke wynceſtre conſtātyne hyr fadre ſlayne thurgh treſon befell tyme pehite came hȳ vpon day meſſage ſaid wolde ſpeke preuely kyng counſeyl king let voyde chābre ye men yt wythȳne ther abode mo king pehyte mad • cōtenaū ce though wolde haue ſpoke king ere ther queld hȳ longe knyfe went ſecretly oute chābre othir chābre ſo laſt mā wiſt become whā ye kīges meyne wiſt hir lord ſo ded made ſo moche ſorwe yt wiſt doo hys two ſones anrilābros ād vter werē ſo yō ge yt none hē might kȳg· ye thridde brother mōke wī ceſtre ſayd vortyger erle weſtſexe thought preuely herte queyntyſe kyng punctel went wincheſtre ther conſtance monke ſaid cōſtā ce fader dede yowr two bretheren ben̄ wyt goſſeleyne biſſhop lōdō noryſſhe ben ſo yonge none hem may king wherfor ·j coū ſeyll ye forſake habyt come ſhal ſo breton ye ſhall made kyng ¶of conſtance kyng cōſtantynꝰ ſone mōk wyncheſtre made king hys faders deth counſeyll vortyger yt erle weſtſexe moche aurylambros vter hys two brother yonge age vortyger let ſlee hȳ kyng hym ſelfe ca liiij thys vortyger coūceylled thys conſtāce ſo moche tyll forſoke habyte went hȳ anone afterward crowned made kȳg aſſent bretōs kyng conſtaūce whan crowned made kīg wiſt ne knewe lytel ye world ne cowde thȳg aparteigned kyng made vortyger chief maiſtre counſeillier ād yaf alle power ordeyne aſmoche royaulme aparteigned ſelfe thing entermedled onely bare name kyng whan vortyger ſawe ye land ward gouernaille owne wyl thought pryue treſon ād ſlee conſtaunce king might ſelfe ben̄ crowned made king regne let ſende c knyghtes pehites worthieſt alle land helde thaym dwelle wyt hȳ kepars bodi wold wente thurgh lād ordeyne thynges aparteigned kȳg vortyger honoured ſo moche hōdred knightes ſo moche yafe thaym gold ſyluer ād ſo ryche iewelles robe hors othir thȳges plē te wherfore helde moch̄ lord dydē kȳg vortyger tolde hē yf might kȳg • ye thurgh treſon wolde make richeſt lande ye laſt thurgh grete yeftes yeue largely cryed thurgh ye contre vortiger better worthy kyng cōſtaū ce wherfore vortyger made ſemblaūt ben̄ wroth departed then fro court ſaid muſt gon̄ elles whidder thī ge done ād ſo traitour ſayd encheſon yt ſhold ſlee ſay conſtance whan vortiger gone befel ſone ye hō dred knightes pehites broken dores kinges chābre ād ther ſlowē ſmoten heed bare vortiger ther dwelled vortiger ſaw heed wepte ful tē derly wyth hys eye notheles full glad deth anone let take hondred knightes pehites bynde hir hādes behynde lede londō ād dāpned deth fals traitours anone alle breton ye lāde cōmune aſſent crouned vortiger made hȳ king lande ¶how wardeyns two child kepe cōſtātynes ſones ladde hem lytel bretaygne treſon falſeneſſe vortyger capitulo lv kyng vortyger whā crouned thei two childrē keping aurylābros vter thurgh ordināce goſſeleyne biſſhop lōdō hys deth durſt dwelle lāde ye child lad hē kȳg litell bretaigne aſmoche tho wiſt ye treſon vortiger tho made king thurgh whō cō ſtance hir brother ſlaȳ wherfore hondred knightes pehytes put deth bare ye blame vortyger wiſt therof ne nothir ther conſented ſo kepars two child dred leſt vortiger wold put hē deth thurgh hys treſon falſeneſſe hyr brother beforne therfore lad ouer littel bretaigne kīg thaym receyued mochel honour lete hem noryſſhe ther dwelled tyll becamen fayre knightes ſtronge fers thought auenged vpon deth cōſtāce hyr brother whā ſawe hir time ād ſo dyd ye ſhall telle afterward hit longe tydinges ne came ouer ſee kynred hondred knyghtes pehites dampned put deth vortiger lāde therfore wō derly wroth ſworē wolde ben̄ auēged hir kynnes deth camen thys land wyt grete power ād robbed many place queld dyd alle ſorwe myght whā vortyger wiſt made moche ſorwe ſore anoyed place tydynges came aurilābros vter brother ordeyned ād aſſēbled grete hoſt come mochel bretaign̄ ſaye lāde ben̄ auenged vpō conſtance hir brother deth one halfe ād othir brought ī ſo moch̄ ſorwe ne wiſt whidder gon̄ engiſt xj thouſand men came lāde whō vortyger yafe place kalled thong caſtell capitulo lvi ſone ſorwe tydynge came vortiger grete nauye ſtrā giers arryued contre kēt wiſt whēs thei ne wherfore thei comē lād kȳg ſente anone meſſagier thidder ſōme hē ſholde come ſpeke wyt hȳ wyt folke axed contre wolde gon ther two bretherē maiſtres prīces ſtrong cōpanye one kalled engiſt ād othyr horſſe· engiſt went king tolde encheſon wherfore arryued lād ſaid syr bene contre called saxonie lande ermanie wher yn ſo moche ſorwe peple ſo moche lāde may hē ſuſteyne maiſtres prince haue lande gouerne rule maken comen hem men woman bolde ben amonge hem fyght beſt may trauaille dyuerſe landes ſo ſhall hem yeue hors harnaye armure alle thyng hem nedeth ſhall ſaye hem go othir cōtre wher mowe lyue hir aunceſtres dyd beforne hē therfore syre king yf ye haue ought companye come lande wyth good well wyll ſerue lande helpe kepe defende enemyes yf ye • aue nede whā vortiger herde tydinge ſayd wolde glad • hem withold vpon couenant 〈◊〉 might delyuere hys land enemyes wolde yeue hem reſonable lōdes wher ſho • dwelle euermore engiſt thā ked goodly maner companye xjm ſhold dwelle king vortiger ād ſo moche dyd thurgh boldeneſſe delyured land clene hys ennemyes tho prayed engyſt kyng ſo moche lād myght make hym cyte hym meyne kyng anſwerde done without coūſeyll hys bretōs thē ne engyſt prayed hym eſtſones moche lande place myght compoſe wyth thonge ſkynne wervpon might make hī maner dwelle kyng graunted hym freely tho nomme engyſt bully ſkynne cut ſmale might thwōge roūde ther compaſed moche lande made vpon fayr caſtell whē caſtell made let kalle ye thwoncaſtell moche place marked thonge ¶of romewen engiſtes doughtyr kīg vortyger ſpouſed hir hir beaute capitulo lvij whā caſtell mad full well arayed engyſt ſent letter cō tre came hondred ſhippes fylled wyth ſtronge man bolde fyghtyng batailles ād ſhold bryng hem romewē hys doughter ye fayreſt creature man might ſee whan peple comen ſente toke hem caſtell moche ioye ād ſelfe vpon day wente vnto king prayed hym ther worthely wolde come ſe newe maner made ī place compaſſed thonge ſkynne kyng anone graūted freely hym wente thydder ād wel payed caſtell fayr werke ād gedre ther eten dronken wyt mochel ioye whan night came king vortyger ſhold gon̄ chambre take ther nyghtes reſte romewē engiſtes doughter came wt coupe gold hyr handes ād kneled king ſaid hī waiſſaille ye kīg wiſt mene ne ſhold āſwere moche hym ſelfe ne none hys breton yet coude none englyſh ſpekē ne vnderſtond • ſpoken tho ſame langages breton yet done neuertheles latiner tolde ye kīg fulle vnderſtanding ther waiſſaille ād ſhold āſwere drȳke haille firſt tyme waſſaille drinkhaille came vp land tyme vnto time wel vſed lāde king vortyger ſawe fairneſſe romewen armes layd aboute hir necke ſwetely kyſſed hir anone right anamered vpon hir deſyred haue hir wyfe ād aſked engiſt hir fadre engyſt graunted vpō thys couenāt king ſhold yeue alle contre kent might dwelle theryn ād peple kyng graunted preuely wyt good anone ſpouſed damyſell which̄ moche cōfuſion ſelfe therfore alle breton became ſo wroth encheſō ſpouſed woman myſheleue wherfor went frō thing toke kepe ne helpe thīg don̄ ¶how vortymer vortigers ſone made kȳg engiſt dryuē owte vortimer ſlayne cap lviij engiſt wēt kēt ſeiſed lād ī hys hād men ād bicame lyttell whill ſo grete poer ſo moch̄ peple yt men wiſt lyttel tyme whiche kinges men which̄ engiſt men wherfor bretaigne drede ſaid amōg hē ne toke othir counſeill betwene hē land ſhold betraied thurgh engyſt peple vortiger ye king bigotē firſt wife iij ſones firſt called vortimer ye ij catagrē thridde paſſēt breton alle bi one aſſent choſen vortimer hir lord ſoueraine hir coūcellier euery bataille crowned hȳ made hȳ king wolde ſuffre vortiger lenger regne encheſon aliā ce bitwene engiſt hȳ breton ordeyned grete hoſt driue oute engiſt ād cōpanie lande yafe thre batailles firſt kent ther lorde ſecōd tetforde thridde ſhire kalled nycoll bataille hem met catagrē horſſe engiſtes brother ſo eche hem ſlewe moche contre yeuē lōg horne thurgh vortyger tho ſpouſed hys coſin ther made fair caſtell men called horne caſtell owne name vortimer ſo anoyed brother deth catagrē dede ſuche maner wherfore anone let felle ye caſtel groū • de ne leſt night ne day tyll dryuē owt engiſt peple lande ād whan engiſt driuen away romewen doughtyr made ſorwe ynowe queyntely ſpake hē next king vortymer pryuyeſt hym ſo moche ſhe yaf yeſtes enpoiſened deyed lō iiij yere hys regne ād ther lyeth breton choſē othir tyme vortiger theyre kyng engyſt came ayen̄ thys lande foughten gedre capitulo lix vortemers deth breton bi hir ꝯmune aſſent eſtſones made vortiger hir king vpon couenant yt ſhold neuer ſuffre engiſt ne none eſtſones comen land whā done romewen ye quene preuely ſēte letter engiſt ſhe ēpoiſened vortymer vortyger hir lord ayen̄ bare crowne regned ſhold come land well arayed moche peple auenge vpon breton wynne lād ayene whā engiſt herde tidinge made grete ioye apparailled hym haſtely xv thouſand men yt doubgthy euery batayll came thys land whā vortiger herd telle engyſt ayen̄ comē grete power land aſſembled breton wente ayenſt engiſt haue yeuen bataill ād folke engiſt drad hȳ ſore breton diſcōfyted beforne driuen owte wt ſtrengthe wherfore engiſt prayed loue day ād ſaid comen lande fight haue lāde ayen̄ might accorde breton hem haue grace kȳg vortiger thurgh coūceyll hys bretōs graū ted loue day ād thus ordeyned thurgh breton ſame loue day ſhold ben̄ holde faſt beſyde salyſbury vpō hyll engiſt ſhold come thidder wyt iiijc knightes withoute moo king many ye wyſeſt lande day kyng came coū ſeyll ordeyned engiſt warned knightes preuely hem cōmaūded euery hem ſhold put longe knyf hoſe whan ſaid fayre ſyres nowe tyme ſpeke loue pee euery man anon̄ ſhold drewe knyfe ſlee bretō ſo quelled thouſand lxi knyghtes moche ſorowe many hem eſcaped ād ye king vortiger ſelfe tho taken lad thongcaſtell put pryſon ſōme engyſtes men wolde kyng ben brent quyke ād vortiger haue lyfe graūted hem aſmoche wolde axe yaue vp alle landes townes caſtelles cytees burghes engyſt hys folke ād alle brytons fledde then wale helde ſtille engyſt wente thurgh lande ſeiſed alle hāde wyt fraū chiſes euery place let kaſt downe chyrches howſes relygyone deſtroyed criſtē dome thurgh lande let chā ge name land noman ſo hardy y• tyme calle lande bretaign̄ calle engiſteſland departed land men made ther vij kȳges ſtrēghte land bretōs ſhold neuer come therȳ firſt kingdome kēt ther engiſt ſelfe regned lord maiſtre ouer alle othir othir kȳg ſouthſexe nowe called chicheſſtre iij king weſtſex iiij kyng hadde eeſtſexe v kyng eſtāgyll called nortfolk southfok merchemerich̄ yt ſaye erldome nychol vj leiceſtreſhire northm̄ptonſhire hertford huntȳgdone vij oxūford glouſtre wincheſtre warrewyk ād derbyſhyre vortiger wēt wale begā caſtell wolde ſtande wytout mortier tē pred blode c lx whā engiſt departed lāde maner bitwene men delyuered vortiger pryſon ād ſuffred freely gone whidder wolde nōme hys wey went wale ther hys breton dwelled moche lād ſtrōg wykked winne engiſt neuer came ther ne knewe neuer land vortiger helde hȳ ther breton ared coū ceyl beſt done yaf coūceyll make ſtronge caſtell might ſelf therynne kepe ād defende nede werkmen anone begannen werke caſtell vpō ye hylle breigh certes thus befel ye werke maſons made day fell downe night wyſt myght ben̄ therof king ſore anoyed chaūce wiſt done wherfore ſent wyleſt clerkes alſo alle lerned men thurgh oute wale might fondē ſholde telle wherfore foundament ſo failled vnder werke ſholde hym telle thyng beſt done punctel whan thieſe clerkes ād wyſe maiſtres longe tyme ſtudied ſayden king ſhulde done ſeke chylde borne woman neuer man done childe ſholde ſlee tempre hys blode mortier werke ſo ſholde werke euer endure withoute ende howe kyng lete ſeche merlȳ thurgh alle wale ſpeke wyt hym capitulo lxi whan king herde cōmaūded hys meſſagiers anone wēte thurgh oute alle wale ſeke ye childe yf might hym fynde ſhold bringe hym forth hē vnto him· recorded witneſſe thys thynge delyuered hē lrēs thei ne deſtroubled man ne lette tho meſſagiers wente thēs ſpedde ſo faſt came towne yt kalled karmardyne ād thei paſſed forth hir waye fonden two chyldrē xiiij yere age chydȳg gydre wt haſty wordes one hem ſaid othir done bat ſayd ye done wronge chydde ſtryfe ye haue ne wit ne reſon haue certes merlȳ ſaid ye child wit ne yowr reſon make force men telle cōmuneli· ye haue thing god almighty ſyth ye neuer fadre euery man knoweth well moder meſſagyers king vortyger whā herdē ſtryfe bytwene ye two chyldren axed hem ſtōdē beſydes hem whēs merlyn borne alſo noriſſhed folke hē tolde grete gentyll woman bare karmardyne called adhan neuer man might wite might chyldes fadre whan kynges meſſagiers herdē tydīg wē ten anone wardeyne towne tolde hȳ kynges wyll· lrē ſhewed hȳ wherfor comē thydder merlyn moder anon̄ ſēt fore ye wardeyne towne commaunded hem ſholde gon̄ kyng ordeyned meſſagiers merlyn moder wente then camen fore kȳg vnderfonge wyt mochel honour kȳg axed lady yf ye childe hyr ſone begate lady anſwerde full tēderli wepȳg ād ſaid ſhe neuer companye man wordely ſyre kyng quod ſhe yōge mayden fadres chābre grete lygnage ī companye oftē tymes wōt playe ſolace beleft allone chambre wold gon owte brennyng ſō ne vpon time ther came fayre bacheler entred chambre ther allone came wiſte neuer ne yet wote j dores faſt barred wyt dyd game loue ne might ne power deffende fro ofte cam forſaid maner ſo begate thys chylde neuer might wyt ¶of anſwere merlȳ wher king axed hys werke might ſtande begonne ner proue cap lxij whā merlȳ herde moder ſayd ſpak kȳg thys maner syre begotē axe ye fallyth nought ne non̄ othir wyte telle encheſō wherfor brought wherfore ye haue ſent certes ſaid king wyſe counceilliers haue don̄ vnderſtōde ye mortier werke j haue begōne behoued tempred blode foū dament ſhall faill euermore syr ſayd merlyn wyll ye ſlee blood tempre therwith mortier ye ſayde kyng elles neuer ſhall caſtell ſtade counceilliers done vnderſtōde tho āſwerde merlyn kȳg ſaid syr let hem come byfore wyſe coūceilliers wyll proue ſay wel ne trewly wiſe maiſtres comen merlyn axed hē blode encheſon make werke ſtand endure wyſe abaſſhed coude anſwere merlyn tho ſaid kȳg syr ſhal telle yow thēcheſon wherfore werke thus failleth ād may ſtande ther vnder ye montaigne ther ye haue begonne towre grete ponde water bothome water ther ben two dragōs one white reed fyghten gydre ayēſt ye dygge ſo depe tyll mē comen ponde ād yowr men take away water oute ye ſhall ſe dragon haue tolde gedre fyght ayēſt werk encheſon certes wherfore y• foundament failleth kȳg anone let dygge vnder tyll thei camē pōde let done away water ther fonden two dragon merlyn tolde which̄ egrely foughten gydre whyte dragon egrely aſſailled rede layd hym ſo ſtrōgely might endure withdrewe reſted ſame caue whyle reſted went ād aſſailled reed dragon angrely helde ſo ſore myght ayēſt hym endure withdrowe ād reſt came ayen̄ whyte dragō ſtrō geli fought reed dragon bote hym euell hȳ ouercam̄ fleigh thēs nomore came ayene ſygnyfycacion two dragōs bottom ponde foughtē gedre capitulo lxiij king vortiger men ſawe thys bataill grete meruaille praied merlyn telle hym might betokē syre ſayd merlyn ſhall telle yow rede dragon betokeneth yowr ſelf whyte betokeneth ye folk saxone fyrſt ye toke helde lande fyghten ayēſt yow yow haue driuen enchaſed ye breton lygnage ouercamē hem ād drouē hem away ſythen comyng ayen saxōs recoured lād held euer dryuen owt breton dyd wt lād hir wyll deſtroyed criſtēdome thurgh lā de ye firſt ioye wyt hir comȳg turned grete domage ſorwe ij bretheren conſtāce kīg whiche ye let ſlee punctel ſhulle come beforn̄ moneth paſſed wyt grete power lytell bretaigne ſhull auenge deth hyr brother ſhull brenne yow firſt ſorwe ād ſhul ſlee grete partie saxon ſhull owt dryue remanaūt ye lād therfore abide ye lē ger make caſtell ne none werke anone goo elles yowr lyfe ſaue god bitake trouth j haue ſaid yow thyng ſhall befall vnderſtōdeth well aurylābros ſhal king ſhal enpoyeſēd lyttel tyme regne ¶of kyng aurilambros howe purſued vortyger engiſt howe dydden capitulo lxiiij merlyn moder departed fro king turned ayen karmardyne ſo tyding came ye breton aurylambros vter brother arriued totteneſſe grete hooſt breton anone aſſembled hē went receyued aurilābros vter wit grete nobyleſſe lad hem london punctel ād crowned ther aurilambros ād made kȳg dyden homage axed wher vortyger kyng might fonden wold ben auenged brother deth ād wolde werre vpon paynyms thei told hȳ vortyger whale ād ſo ladde thydderward vortyger wyſt well bretheren came cōquere hȳ flew then caſtelll yt kalled gerneth ſtode vpon hygh̄ montaigne ther helde hym aurilambros vter brother hir folk beſieged caſtell full longe tyme caſtell ſtronge wel arayed laſt caſt therin wylde fire brent hows men ād hir araye moche withȳ ye caſtel ſo vortiger brēt amonge alle ſo deyed moch̄ ſorwe tho engyſt kent regned ther herde tyding anone fledde ād wold haue gone scotland haue ſocour aurilambros men met hȳ northcontre yafe hym bataille engiſt men hem defended while might folke diſconfyted ſlayne otta ſone fley yorke aurilābros hym folowed egrely otta littel whyle ayēſt ſtode· afterward putte mercy aurilambros vnderfenge men yafe contre galewey scotland ther dwelled kȳg aurilābros went thurgh owt ye lāde put away name engiſteſ land engiſt name called tho let calle ayen̄ grete bretaigne let make ayen̄ chyrches howſes relygion caſtelles cytees ād burges townes whych̄ ſaxons deſtroyed came londō ād let make walles cyte whiche engiſt folk caſt downe bretōs led hym monthe anbrian wher ſome tyme hows relygyō tho deſtroyed thurgh paynymes wher knight called anbri ſō tyme founder ye hous therfore hyll called ye mont briā called ambreſbury ſhal euermore ¶how aurylābros dyd redreſſe land grete bretaygne deſtroyed thurgh ſaxōs capitulo lxv king aurylābros let amēd redreſſe hous amleſbury therȳ put moke ther nō ne lyttell frō ye place called saliſbury ther tho ſaxons kyllyd bretōs engiſt ſholde haue made loue day which̄ time ther ſlaine • lxi knightes thurgh treſon engiſt kīg therof grete pyte • thought make minde hem monument ſtone might ēdure ye worldes ende thys thyng toke hir coūſeil therof beſt done tho ſpake king biſſhop london called ternekȳ ſholde enquyre merlyn cowde beſte telle thyng myght beſt made merlȳ ſought fondē came kyng kīg tolde hys monument yt wold haue made tho anſwerde merlyn kyng ſaide ben grete ſtones jrland lōge vpon hyll kyliā men kalled geants karoll yf place ben̄ ſhold endure euer remēbraunce knightes ben entered throuth̄ ſayd king hard ſtones lād jrland soth ſaid merlȳ • landes bene ſuche geants ſet hem grete good hem ſelfe eueri time woūded maner hurte▪ weſſhē ſtones hote water ād weſſhe hem ſelf ther anone hole breton wentē ſeche grete ſtones irland capitulo lxvi whan bretōs herde thys thing wēt ād ſwore among hē wolde gone ſeche ſtones nomme hem vter kȳ ge brother ben hir cheueteyne xvm men merlyn coūceylled hem gon̄ irlād ād ſo dydē whan kȳg irlād called gwillomer herd tell ſtraūgiers arryued lāde aſſēbled grete power fought ayenſt hē folk diſcōfyted bretōs wente forth tyll camē ye monte kylian clemed vnto ye mōte whā ſaugh̄ ſtones ye maner thei ſtodē thei grete mervaille ſayd bytwene hē mā ſholde remene ſtrength̄ ne engyne ſo hughe ād ſo lōge merlȳ thurgh craft queȳtiſe remened hē brought hē hir ſhippes came ayen̄ land merlȳ ſette ſtones yt kȳg wold haue hē ſet hē ye ſame maner ſtodē irlād whā kȳg ſaugh yt made thā ked merlȳ rychely hȳ rewarded owne wille place kalled ſtōheuge euermore paſſēt vortigers ſone ye kȳg guillomer cam̄ lād traitour called coppa ēpoiſened king aurilābros ca lxvij men ſhall vnderſtōde paſſāt vortyger ſone liued ye ſame tyme came thys lāde wyth grete power ād arryued north contre wolde ben̄ auēged fadres deth vortyger ſtrongely truſted vpon cō panye brought hȳ owt lande germayne conquered alle north contre vnto york whē king aurylābros herd aſſembled grete hooſt brytons went fyght hȳ peple diſcōfyted paſſent eſkaped then wyth ſome folke fled thēs irland ād came kȳg guillomer prayed helpe ſocour kyng graunted hȳ wyt good wyll ād ſaide wold helpe vpō couenāt ſelfe muſt gone you▪ alle power bretaigne wolde auenge vpō bretōs rather lande camē token ſtones ſtrēth̄ called geants karoll kȳg guillomer let ordeyne hys ſhyppes wente ſee xv thowſand men arryued wale begōne robbe moch̄ ſorwe done hit befell ſo kȳg aurilambros lay ſeke wȳcheſtre might helpe ſelf ſent name vter brother grete power helpe wale ād thydderward wente moch̄ might king irlād paſſent herd telle aurylābros ſeke hē both̄ came ſarazen which̄ called coppa ſaid sire dwelle ye pee wyt hooſt behote yow thurgh queyntyſe ſhal ſlee kȳg aurylābros ſeke ye ſo ſaid paſſēt ſhal yow rycheli auaūce traitour coppa put vpon habyt relygyon let ſhaue brode crowne came kȳges court ād ſayde wolde hele kȳg maladie tho ſaid ye traitour ye king syr ben good confort ſhal yeue ſuche medicine ye ſhall ſwete anone right luſtē ſlepe haue good reſt ād traytour yaf hȳ ſuche poyſon ſlept anone ryght ād deyed ſlepȳg traitour ſaid wold gone owte felde tyl wer awaked ſo eſcaped away mā ſuſpectyon encheſon habbyt clothed alſo brode croune whā kinges men wiſten dede moche ſorwefully ſoughtē faſt traitour might fynde hȳ coppa turned ayene ye hooſt fro whēs comen yt whā aurilābros dede ye mornȳg ſterne ſeyne wt clere light bought beme ſeyn̄ thē hede orryble dragon cap lxviij whā kīg aurilābros thus dede wincheſtre morne dede aboute ye time prime ther ſeyne grete ſterre clere ye beme ye ſterre brighter thā ſonne ye bought ye beē appered dragōs hede • oute mouth came ij grete lightes bryght fyre brēnȳg yt one beme ſaw toward fraūce ſtraught ouer ye ſee thidderward owt beem came vij bemes full clere longe light fyre thys ſterre ſeyn̄ many man none hē wiſt betokened vter yt kȳges brother ī walys wt hoſt bretōs ſawe ſterre ye grete light yaf wōdred ther gretly might betokē let calle merlȳ praied hȳ telle might betokē ¶of ye betokenȳg ye ſterre cap lxix merlyn ſaw ye ſterre behelde hȳ lōge time fithenes quoke ād wept tenderly ād ſayd allas allas ſo noble kȳg worthy dede j vnderſtāde aurilābros brother ēpoiſoned • j ſee wel ſterre ſelf betokeneth ye heed ye dragō ſeyne ye bought ye beē ſelf yt ſhal kȳg regne bi ye beē ſtond towardes ye eſt vnderſtōdē ye ſhal gete ſone yt ſhal conquere fraūce lādes bē longȳg ye croune fraūce ſhal worthier kȳg honour euer aūceſtres beē ſtryght toward irland betokened ye ſhall getē doughtir ſhal quene jrland vij bemes betokened punctel ye ſhal haue vij ſones euery hē ſhall kȳg regne wyt mochel honour abyde ye lē ger goo yeue bataill enemyes fight wyt hē boldely ye ſhal ouercome hē haue victorie vter thāked hertely merlȳ toke hys men went toward hys enemyes foughten gedre dedely ſo diſcōfyted ennemies deſtroyed hym ſelf quelled paſſēt vortigers ſone breton queld gwillomer yt king irlād men vter anon̄ aftir bataill toke way toward wȳcheſtre done enburye aurylābros king yt hys brother tho body brought ſtōhēge wyt mochel honour made remēbraūce ye bretōs ſlayn̄ thurgh treſon engiſt ſame day ſhold haue beū accorded ād ſame place beryed aurylābros ſecōde yere regne wyt worſhip myght belōgē ſuch̄ kȳg who ſowle god haue mercy ¶of vter pendragon wher kalled ſo ye ſhall ouertakē wyt ye grete loue jgerne ye erles cornewaill wyfe c lxx deth aurylā bros vter brother crowned regned well worthely remēbraūce dragon lyked let make ij dragon thurgh coū ſeill breton one bore beforne hȳ whēne wēt bataille abyde wyncheſtre byſſhoppes chyrche encheſon called euer vter pē dagron otta engyſtes ſone commended lyttell vter made newe kyng ayēſt hȳ began meve werre ordeyned grete cōpanye hys frēdes kȳne offa brother yt take lād frō hūber vnto york thei york helde ſtrongely ayenſt hē wold ſuffre hem come towne nothir yelde cyte hem· beſieged towne anone right yafe ther ſtrō ge aſſaulte cyte hē kepte well ſtrōgly whā vter herde therof came thydder grete power helpe reſeue toune put awey ſiege yafe ſtrōge bataill ād otta cōpanye hē deffended well might laſt diſcōfyted ye moſt part hē queld otta offa takē put pryſon lōdō vter hȳ ſelf dwelled yorke ād went lō eſter ſuyng wolde crowned holde ſolempne feſt let ſompne hys erles barōs thei ſhold come feſt ād thei wyfes ſhold bringe hem alſo feſt thei camē kynges commaūdement commaūded feſt rychely holden worthely ſettē mete werē eſtate ſo erle gorloys cornewaille jgerne wyfe ſeten alther next king kīg ſawe fairneſſe ladi ſhe rauiſſhed hir beaulte ād ofte made hir nyce ſemblaūt lokyng lawghyng ſo laſt erle perceyued pryue lokyng lawghyng loue bytwene hem aroos vp frō table wroth̄ toke wyfe called knightes went thēs wrath withoute takȳg leue king king anone ſent ſhold come ayē go thēs deſpyte hȳ ye erle wold come ayē maner wyſe wherfore king full wroth wrath̄ deffied dedely enemye erle went then cornewaylle wyf caſtel tȳ tagell kyng let ordeyne grete hooſt ād came cornewaille deſtroye erle myght put hym ſuche caſtell ſtronge wel arayed tyntagell wold yelde hȳ king kȳg anone beſieged caſtel dwelled xv dayes neuer might ſpede euer thought vpon jgerne vpon hir laid ſo moche bone nyſt doū laſt called hȳ knight called vlfyn which̄ pryue hȳ told hȳ coūſeyll axed hym beſt done syre ſayd dothe ſend merlyn kan telle yow beſt coū ſeyl man lyuing merlyn anone ſent came ye king king told hym hys wyll syr ſaid merlȳ ſhal done ſo moch̄ thurgh craft j yt ſhall make yow come nyght caſtell tyntagel ye ſhal haue lady ¶how vter bigate igerne yt erles wyf cornewaill kyng arthour capi lxxi merlyn thurgh crafte cowde changed kȳ ge figure lykeneſſe erle vlfen garlois chambirlayne vnto figure iurdan erles chābyrlayne ſo eche hem trāſfigured othir lykeneſſe whā merlyn ſo done ſayd kȳg syr mowe ye goo ſodenly caſtel tyntagel axe entrie haue wyll king toke preuely hooſt gouerne lede knight moch̄ loued ād toke way toward ye caſtel vlfyn chāberlayne merlyn whan came thydder portier wēd ben owne lord whan tyme cam̄ go bedde king went bedde igerne erles wyf dyd wyt hir wille bygate vpon hir ſone called arthur vpō morne noble myghty king toke leue lady ād went ayen̄ hys hooſt ye ſame night kīg lay bi jgerne bedde wyt erles wyf kinges knightes men yauen ſtronge aſſault caſtel erle men manly hē deffē ded laſt befell ſo ſame aſſaulte erle ſelf ſlayne caſtel taken kyng anone turned ayē tyntagel ſpouſed igerne wyth mochel honour made hyr quene ſone tyme came ſhe ſhold deliuered bere chylde ſone whiche kalled arthour gate hir doughtir whiche kalled amya whā ſhe came age ſhe wa • nobely maryed noble baron which̄ kalled aloth lord leon whan vter longe tyme regned ther came vpon grete ſekeneſſe ſorwe ye mene time thei kepe otta engiſtes ſone offa hys brother tho pryſon let hem gone owt grete yeftes hē yaf wente hem whā two bretherē eſcaped ād came ayen̄ hir owne contre ordeyned hem grete hooſt grete power begonne werre vpon king kyng vter choſe alot kepe land bretaigne whyles ſeke moche might helpe hȳ ſelf ſekeneſſe capitulo lxxij aſmoche kȳg vter ſeke myght helpe hȳ ſelf ordeined alot ſone eleyꝑ yt tho choſen wardeyne ād chiueteyne folke anon̄ hys breton aſſēbled grete hoſt yafe bataille otta ād hys folke otta laſt diſcōfyted hit befell thꝰ afterward bretōs indignacyon aloth wolde
