hym ben̄ attendaunt wherfor kīg anoyed wonder ſore let hī putte horſe litter ȳ ye hoſt amonges folke lad hȳ veroloyne tho fayre cyte ther ſeȳt albone martred cite deſtroyed paynim thydder ſente otta offa ād hyr peple dwelled towne let make faſt yates ther helde hem kīg came beſieged hē made ſtrō ge aſſaulte yt therȳ manly hem defended kyng let ordeyne gonne hys engynes breke walles ād ſo ſtronge thīg myght hem myſdoo otta hys peple grete deſpite kīg lyggyng lyttier hem beſieged tokē counſeyll amonges hem ryſe vp morwe ād come owte yeue bataille vnto king ſo dyden bataill bothe otta offa ſlayne al • e ye eſcaped fled ſcotland made colegryne hir chyuetayne saxon alyue eſcaped fro bataill broughten ayen̄ grete ſtrength̄ amonges hem ſaidē kyng vter dede thei ſhold wel conquere land amōges hem thoughtē enpoiſen̄ ye king ordeyned men done dede yaf hē yeftes grete plente don̄ thing ordeyned hem thidderward ther kyng dwellȳg clothed hē poure habites better ſpedde hyr lyther purpoſe neuertheles alle falſeneſſe queȳtyſe might neuer come ſo nygh̄ kȳg ſo laſt aſpied king drāke none licour onely water clere welle ther nyghe beſydes ād thees fals traytour vpon daye preuely wente welle put therin poyſon ſo water enpoyſened anone king dronke ye water begā ſwelle ſone deyed many drōkē water deydē alſo anone falſeneſſe aſpied folke towne let ſtoppe ye welle euermore whē king dede hys folke bere stonhēge wyth grete ſolempnite byſſhops barōs yt enburyed hȳ beſide aurylambros brother turned ayen̄ euerychō let ſendē aftyr arthour hys ſone made king ye lād moche reuerēce aftir faders deth ye xvij yere regne ¶how arthour ſone vter crowned hys faders deth drofe colegryne saxon cheldryck almaygne owt thys lād c lxxiij whan arthur made king ye lād punctel yonge age xv yere faire bolde doubty body meke folke good courtoys ād large ſpēdyng made hȳ well beloued among alle men ther nede whan begā regne ſwore ſaxōs neuer ſholden haue pee ne reſt tyll dryuen thaȳ owte lād aſſēbled grete hooſt fought colegrine tyme otta dede ſaxons mayntened colegryne diſcōfyted fledde vnto yorke toke toune ther helde hī kȳg beſieged towne might ſpede towne ſo ſtronge withynne kepte ye towne wel orpedly mene tyme colegrine let towne bladulf fled hī ſelfe cheldryke king almaigne haue ſocour king aſſembled grete power came arryued ſcotland wyt vc ſhippes· arthour wiſt thys tydyng power ne ſtrēgth̄ ynough fight ayēs childrike let ben ſiege wente londō ſente anone lrēs ye kȳg littel bretaignn̄ called hoell neveu ſuſtres ſone ſhold come hī wyt power might aſſēbled grete hooſt arryued ſouthm̄ptō whā artur yt wiſte glad wēt ayēſt hȳ receiued hȳ moch̄ honour ſo ye ij hoſtes hē aſſēbled tokē hir way nycol yt cheldryck beſieged yet takē camē vpō childrik vpō peple er thei jt wiſt ther hē egrely aſſailled king cheldryk ād meyny defended hē māly hyr power kȳg arthur mē queld ſo many ſaxōs neuer er ſayne ſuche ſlaughter ād cheldryk men left lyue fledden awaye arthour hē purſued drofe hē wode might ferthir paſſe cheldryk ād men ſawe wel thei brought moche dyſeſe yoldē hem arthur maner ſhold take hir hors hir armures ſuffre thaȳ go fote hir ſhippes ſo ſholde gon̄ ī owne lāde neuer come agayn land vpon aſſuraūce thȳg yauē hȳ good hoſtages arthur bi coūſeyll hys men graunted thȳg receiued hoſtages vpō ye wēt hir ſhippes whan ye ſee hir mynde chaunged deuell wolde retourned hyr nauye came ayen̄ land arryued totteneſſe wēt hir ſhippes toke ye lād clene robbed ſlewē moch̄ peple token armure might fynde ſo wēt forth tyll camē bathe men towne ſhittē faſt hir yates wolde ſuffre hē come wyth towne deffended hē wel orpedly ayens hē howe arthour yafe bataill ſaxons whan camē ayē beſieged towne bathe ād hem ouercame cap lxxiiij whan arthour herde thys tydinge let hāge anon̄ hoſtages lefte hoel bretaigne neveu kepe marche toward scotland half peple hȳ ſelfe wē te helpe reſkew ye towne bathe whan came thydder punctel yaf ſtrōge bataill cheldrik killyd moſt peple man might ſtond ne endure vnder ſtroke ſwerd ād ther bothe ſlayne colegryne ād bladulf brother cheldrik fledde thēs wolde haue gone hys ſhippes arthur wiſt toke xm knightes cador erle cornewaill lete ſtoppe comȳg ſelf wē te toward marche ſcotlād meſſagiers told hī ye ſcottes beſieged hoell bretaigne ther lay ſeke therfore haſted thydder ward cador purſued cheldryk toke hī er might come ſhippes queld cheldryke hys peple whan cador done thys voyage haſted hym ayen̄ faſte might towardes artur fonde ſcotlād ther reſeued hoell bretaigne ſcottes al ferre moūref punctel ther held hem artur hem purſued fled then limoigne cō tre lx jles grete plēte briddes grete plente egles wont crye fyght gedres ād make grete noyſe whā folk come robbe land werren moche thei myght ſo dyden ye scottes grete rauennours ſo token myght fynde lād lymoigne without ſparȳg ther thei charged ayen̄ folke scotlād wente king artur axed merlyn auentures vj laſte kynges regne englond howe land ſhold ende capitulo lxxv sire ſayd merlyn yere incarnacyō jeſu criſte mccxv ſhall come lambe owte wincheſtre ſhal haue whyte thonge trewe lippes ſhall haue writē herte holyneſſe lā ſhal make many goddes houſes ſhall haue pee moſt part hys lyfe ſhall make one faireſt place world hys tyme ſhall fully made ende ye ēde lyfe wolf ſtraūg land ſhall moche harme ſorwe thurgh werre ye ende ye lābe ſhal maiſter thurgh helpe rede fox ſhal come nortweſt hȳ ſhall ouercome wulf wolf ſhal deye water· ād aftir tyme lābe ſhal lyue ne ſhal deye ſede thā ſhal ſtraunge land ye land ſhal withoute gouerneur litell whyle tyme ſhal come dragon melled mercy eke wyth wodeneſſe ſhall haue berd goot ſhall yeue ī englond ſadewe ſhall kepe land colde hete ād owne foot ſhal ſette wyke ye londō ſhal enbrace inhabitacyons ād ſhall open mouth toward walys· tremblyng hydour mouthe hys eres ſhal ſtrech̄ toward many inhabitacions ād contreys breth ſhall full ſwete ſtraunge lande time ſhal ryuers renne wt blode rayne ād ſhal make place lād walles ſhulle don̄ moche harme vnto ſeed tyme then̄e ſhal ther come peple owt northweſt regne ſhal lad thurgh owt wikked hare ye dragō ſhal don̄ crowne kyng whyche afterward ſhal flee ouer ſee wythout comyng ayen drede dragō tyme ſonne ſhal rede bloode men thā ſhal ſee thurgh al world whiche ſhal betoken grete peſtilence deth folk thurgh dent ſwerde peple ſhal bē fadreles tyl time dragō ſhal deye thurgh hare ſhal mewe ayenſt werre vnto end lyfe which̄ yt ſhal fully ben ended hys time dragon ſhall hold tyme beſt body alle world ſhall deye beſydes march ſtraunge lande ād land ſhal dwelle fadreles without good gouernour men ſhal wepe deth ile ſcheppey vnto hauē marcyll wherfor allas ſhall commune ſonge fadreles folke ſhull ouerlyuen hys land deſtroyed thys dragon ſhall come goot owt kar which̄ ſhall haue horne berde ſyluer ther ſhall come noſtrell domp ſhal betoken hunger ſorwe ād grete deth peple punctel moche lāde begynnyng regne ſhall waſted goot ſhal go fraunce ſhall opene flour hys lyfe deth ¶in time ther ſhal aryſe egle ī cornewaille ſhal haue tethres golde pride ſhal wythout pere lā de ſhal deſpyſe lordes • blode ād ſhal flee ſhamefully bere gauerſech ſhull made brigges men vpon coſtes ſee ād ſtones ſhull fall fro caſtelles many townes ſhull made playne tyme ſhal ſeme bere ſhal brenne ād bataill ſhal don̄ vpon ye armes ye ſee feld ordeyned ſheld ād bataill ſhal deye many white hedes wherfor batayll ſhall called white bataill forſayd bere ſhall done goot moche harme ād ſhal come ſouthweſt blood ſhall goot leſe moche hys lande tyll tyme ſhendſhyp ſhal hym ouercome ſhal clothe lyon ſkynne • ſhal vailliauntly wynne haſt loſt therto peple ſhall come owt northweſt which̄ ſhal make goot ſore drad thā ſhal auenge hym hys ennemyes thurgh counſeyll twoo owles whyche fyrſt ſhull ben̄ paryll bene vn done olde owle ſhall wēte certayne tyme therafter ſhall come ayene land thiſe two owles ſhall grete harm̄ many ād ſo ſhal coū ſeylle goot ſhall arere werre ayēſt forſayd bere· laſt goot owles ſhall come burton vp trēt ſhull wente ouer ād drede bere ſhall flee ſwan fro companye burton toward north ād ther thei ſhull ben̄ hard ſhour ſwan ſhall ſlayne ſorwe bere taken beheded alther next neſt ſhal ſtō de vpon brokē brygge whō ſonne ſhall caſt hir bemes ād many ſhall hȳ ſeke vertu fro hī ſhal come jn ſame ſhal deye ſorwe ād care peple lād ſo many lādes ſhull ben̄ hȳ bolder afterward two owles ſhulle doo moch̄ harme forſaid flour delyſe ſhull hyr lede diſtreſſe ſo yt ſhe ſhall paſſe ouer fraū ce make pee bytwene goot flour delyſe ther ſhe ſhall dwelle tyll tyme hyr ſeed ſhal come ſeche hir ād ſhull hem clothe grace ſhull ſeche two owles ād ſhull put hem deſpytous deth ſhall goot ben̄ brought dyſeſe grete anguyſſhe ād ſorwe ſhall lyue alle hys lyfes tyme thys goot ſhall come oute vyndeſore bore ſhall haue hede white lyon herte ād pytous lokyng vyſage ſhal reſte ſeke men breſt ſhall ſtanchyng therſt hē ben̄ therſt worde ſhal goſpel beryng ſhal meke lambe ¶in firſt yere regne ſhal haue grete payne iuſtifye hem ben̄ vntrewe tyme ſhall lād multiplyed wt alien bere thurgh fierſneſſe herte ſhall haue ſhall make wolfe become lambes ſhal called thurgh owt world boor holyneſſe ferſeneſſe nobyleſſe ād mekeneſſe ſhall done meſurably ſhall haue don̄ vnto burgh̄ jeruſalē ſhall whette hys teth vnto yates parys vpon fowre lādes spaigne ſhal tremble drede gaſcoyne ſhal ſwete fraunce ſhal put wynge hys grete taille ſhall reſte englond ſoftely almaigne ſhal quake drede hȳ boor ſhal yeue two mātelles ij tounes englond ſhal made ryuer renne blood ād brayne ſhall made many medewes red ād h̄e ſhall gete moche aunceſtres dyden ād er ſhal dede ſhal bere thre crownes ſhall put land grete ſubiectyon ſhall releued hys tyme thys boor dede doughtyneſſe ſhal entered coloigne land ſhal thā fullfylled alle good boor ſhall come lābe ſhal haue foot leed hede bra hert loppe ſwynes ſkyn ād harde hys tyme lād ſhall pee fyrſt yere regne ſhal make cyte ye world ſhall ſpeke therof lambe ſhal leſe tyme grete part hys lāde thurgh hydous wolf ſhal recoure yeue lord ſhip egle landes ād egle ſhal well gouerne tyl tyme pryde ſhall hym ouergone allas ſorowe ſhal deye brother fuered ſhal lāde fall forſaid lābe whiche ſhal gouerne land pee hys lyfes tyme punctel ſhal deye lāde ful fylled maner good lābe ſhal come molde warpe kurſed goddes mouthe caytyfe coward hare ſhall haue elderly ſkyne gote vengeaunce ſhall fall vpon hym ſynne fyrſt yere regne ſhal haue alle good grete plente lande toward alſo land ſhal haue grete preyſing tyll tyme ſhall ſuffre peple lyue moche pride withoute chaſtiſȳg wher god wyll wroth ſhall aryſe vp dragon north whiche ſhall fulfers ād ſhall mewe werre ayenſt forſaid molde warpe ſhall yeue hȳ bataill vpon ſtone dragon ſhall gadre ayene hys companye wolfe ſhal com̄ owt weſt begynne werre ayēſt forſaid molde warpe hys ſyde ſo ſhall dragon bynde hyr taylles gedre ſhal come lyon owte irland whiche alſo ſhall falle companye hem ſhal trē ble land thā ſhall called englond aſpen leef ¶and tyme ſhullē caſtelles felled downe vpon thamyſe ſhal ſeme ſhe neuer ſhal flothe bodyes ſhull falle dede theryn fowre chyef flodes englond ſhull renne bloode grete drede ſhull anguyſſhe ſhal arryſen ther molde warpe ſhal flee ād dragō lyon wolfe ſhull hē dryue away lande ſhall withoute hem molde warpe ſhal haue maner ne power ſauf onely ſhippe wher ſhall mowe flee wente ād ſhall gon̄ lande whan ſee withdrawe ſhal yeue thridde part lande haue fourth̄ part pee reſt ſhal lyue ſorwe lyfes tyme hys tyme hote bathe ſhullē becomen colde ād ſhall molde warpe deye auētourſly allas ſorowe ſhal draȳt flode ſee ſeed ſhal become fadreles ſtraunge lād euermore ſhal land departed thre partyes ſaye wolfe dragō lyon ſo ſhall euermore ſhal lād kalled land conqueſte ſo ſhullē righful heires englond ende arthour ouercame gwillomere king irland scotes becamē men capitulo lxxv whā guillomer king irland tydȳ ge kyng arthur entred glaſtenbury ordeyned grete power ire men came ſee ire peple ſo came ſcotland ouer ſee arryued faſte ther kȳg arthour hooſt anone wiſte therof wente towardes hem ād yafe hē bataill ouercame hē anone right gwillomer fledde wyt men ayen̄ irlād whā diſconfyture done arthour turned hym ayene ther yt place ther lefte ſcottes wolde haue hē ſlayne biſſhoppes abbotes othir folke contre ladyes wyth opēhede came kȳg arthour creyd mercy ſaidē gentyll king mighty haue mercy pyte v ſelfe ben right lawe hold mayntē criſtēdom̄ full grete diſhonour ſholde kylle hem byleue almyghty god ye don̄ goddes loue haue mercy ād pyte v ſuffre v lyue haue moche ſorwe payne saxōs haue many tyme thurgh lāde paſſed ynowe often tymes haue done v ſorwe dyſeſe caſtelles haue taken beſtes ſlayne eten moche harme haue v don̄ ye wolde v quelle non̄ honour kȳg quelle hem cryen mercy ye haue v ynowgh̄ ouercome ād loue god ſuffre v lyue haue mercy cryſten peple byleuen criſt ye whan king arthour herde ſorwe pyte hem ād yaf hem hyr lyfe fyll done foot becamē liegemē ād toke hē homage aftyr kyng arthour turned ayen̄ wyth hys hooſt came yorke abode duryng vyage tho yaf loegers aloth ſpouſed hys ſuſter othir yeftes grete plē te tho gawen coſin yonge age alle hys men hym ſerued hys werke yaf ryche yeftes thāked hem moche hyr good ſeruyce ¶how kyng arthour ſpouſed gūnore gūnores coſȳ erle cornewaille cō querede gwillomer irland capitulo lxxvij whā arthur brought land pee reſt ād goode ſtate reſt euery cōtre tho toke wedded wyf whiche called gunnor made hir quene ād fayre lady gentyll cador erle cornewaill longe tyme noryſſhed chā bre owne coſyn neuer childe gedre ād neuertheles kyng arthur loued hir wonder well derely anone wȳter paſſed let aſſemble grete hooſt alle hys baron ſayd wolde wē te irlād cōquere ye lād taryed longe ne paſſed ouer irlāde gwillomer king let aſſemble grete hoſt yaf bataill kȳg arthur gwillomer diſcōfyted yolde hȳ kȳg arthur bicame man hȳ dyd feaulte homage hȳ helde land fro tyme forward paſſed kīg arthur furthermore cōquered gutland iſland toke homage folke lōde ther dwelled xij yere ī pee regned ioye myrthe werred maner man ne mā vpō hym bicame ſo courtoys large ſo honorable emperours court rome ne none thurgh ye world accompted king arthour mā wiſt ne non̄ ſo well preiſed therfore beſt knightes alle maner lōdes came hī dwelle ād receiued hē good wyll reuerē ce· ād knightes ſo good mā knewe werſt ād therfore kȳg arthur made roū de table whā thei ſholde ſytten mete ſhull alyche hir euen lyk ſerued table none might make awaunt one wer hyer thā othir ād king arthur table breton frēſſh men norman flemȳges bourgouners mauſers lotherms alle landes halfe monthe gorye alſo hys lande bretaigne grete lāde cornewayille walys irland ſcotland ſhorteli telle alle landes wolden worſhip chyualrye ſeche punctel camen king arthoures court ¶how king arthour came fraunce conquerd land froll romayne hym queld capi lxxvij hit befell kȳg arthur thurgh counſeyll hys barōs lordes wold gon̄ conquere fraūce tho cleped galle thurgh romaīs helde lāde hir power hyr lordſhip romaȳs take lād noble knyght ād worthy body kalled frolle whā wiſt arthur came ordeined hoſt grete power fought wyt king folke diſcomfyted thennes fled vnto parys entred towne ād cloſed faſt yates whā arthour wyſt froll gone paris· purſued cam̄ thydder hȳ beſieged cyte ſo ſtrōge well arayed thei withyn defended hem wel ād manly king arthour dwelled moneth ther ſo moch̄ peple cyte vytailles faylled ſo grete hūger bicame amō ge hem deyden wonder thykke cyte hunger camen frolle praied hȳ ben̄ accorded kȳg arthur haue pee wolde yelde hym ād towne alſo froll ſaw lenger ne might holde towne ayenſt hir wylle truſt gretly vpon hys owne ſtrength̄ ſent kyng arthour ſhold come fight wyth hym body body ſo ſhold departe fraūce bitwene hem two kyng arthour anone graūted ād wolde non̄ peple ſhold vndertoke hym vpon morwe bothe camen well armed aboute cyte paris grene felde ther ſhold fyght anone ſmytten gedres ſo fyerſly ſo well foughtē bothe ſydes man cowde deme better hem ſo befell frolle yaf arthur ſuche ſtroke kneled grownde wolde nolde frolle withdrowe ſwerde wounded king arthour forhede blood fell downe eyē face arthur anone ſterte vp hertely whan felte hym hurt man ſemed almoſt wode toke tabourne goode ſwerd drewe vpon hygh̄ yafe frolle ſuche ſtroke therwith clafe heed downe ſholdres ſo yt helme might warrant ſo fyll anon̄ dede place cyte made grete ſorowe frolle neuertheles anon̄ yolde hē kȳg arthur ye towne alſo becamē men dydē hȳ homage feaulte vnderfēge hē toke hē good hoſtages king arthur went forth wyth hooſt cōquered angiē angiers gaſcoigne pehyto nauerne bourgoigne barry lotherne turȳ puthiers othir lād fraūce conquered holych̄ ād whan conquered takē hōmages feaultes turned ayen̄ paris ther dwelled lōg tyme ordeyned pee lōg tyme ouer cōtrey thurgh alle fraūce whā pee made ouer thurgh hys noble knighthood alſo hys owne worthyneſſe man ſo grete lord durſt meve werre ayēſt hȳ nothir aryſe make land fraūce quyte pee dwelled ix yere· ād dyde many grete wondres reproued many proude man ād lyther tyraunt hē chaſtyſed hyr deſeruyng kyng arthur auaūced men trauailled ī ſeruyce capitulo lxxix afterward befel thꝰ eſtrē ther helde feſt paris rychely began auaūce knightes hir ſeruyce holpen conqueſt yafe styward called kay angyē angiers beddeler brother yaf normandye tho called nēſtrie holdyne chābirlayn̄ yaf flaūdree māce dorell coſyn yaf boloigne ād richard nevew yaf pō tyf othir yaf large landes fee aftyr yt eſtate whā arthour thꝰ hys knightes feffed auerill next ſewȳg came ayen̄ britaigne owne lād aftir whytſontyde next ſewȳg bi coū ſeil barōs wold crouned king glomergō helde ſolēpne feſt let ſompne kynges erles baron ſholde come thidder euerichone punctel ſcater kȳg scotlād cadwre king ſouthwales gwillomer king northwales maded king irland malgamꝰ king gutland achilles king iſeland aloth kyng denmarck gone king norwey hell hys coſyn kȳg dorkeney cador king lyttell bretaigne norwyth erle cornewaill maurā erle glouceſtre gwerdon erle wyncheſtre boellerle hertford vrtegy erle oxūford curſall erle bathe ionas erle cheſtre enerall erle dorcheſtre kymare erle ſaliſbury waloth erle cāterbury iugerne erle chicheſtre arall erle leiceſtre ād erle warwyke many othir rych̄ lordes breton alſo ther cam mo yt ſay dippon donan gēnes many othir nēpned feſte many fair feſt kȳg arthur hold beforne neuer none ſuche ne ſo ſolempne laſtid xv· dayes mochel honour myrthe ¶of letter ſent frō cyte rome pryde kīg arthour ca lxxx iij day kīg arthur ſate mete amōges kīges amōg hē ſetten feſt· forne hē came xij eldren men age richely arayed courtouſly ſalued kīg ſaid camen frō rome ſent meſſagiers fro emperour toke hȳ lettre thꝰ moche vnderſtōde gretly v mervaylleth arthure thow art one ſo hardy yen thi hede make open werre cōtake ayens v rome owen worlde deme thow haſt neuer yet beforne tyme proued ne aſſayed ſtrēgth̄ ye romains therfore thou ſhalt lyttell tyme iuliꝰ ceſar conquerd lād bretaign̄ toke ther truage oure folk haue longe thurgh thy pride thou witholdeſt wherfore commaunde thou yelde ayen̄ yet haſt thou foly done thou haſt ſlayne frolle baron fraunce wrō ge therfore alle commune rome warnen commaū de vpon lyue lyme thou haſt rome amēdes make thy myſdedes thou haſt done ād yt ſo thou come nought ſhull paſſe hylle ioye ſtrengthe ſhull ſeke wher euer thou may fonden thou ſhalt haue fote lād thȳ owne ne ſhall deſtroye afterward wyth thy body ſhull don̄ wille whā lrē rad men herd ā noyed alle ſolempnite bretōs wolde haue ſlain̄ meſſagiers kȳg wolde ſuffre hem ād ſayd ye meſſagiers ſholde haue none harme mowe reſon none deſerue commaunded hem worſhipfully ſerued mete toke coūſeyll kinges erles baron anſwere might beſt yeue ayen̄ meſſagiers coū ceylled onys ſhold aſſēble grete hooſt ād power lādes which̄ lordſhip manly auenge hȳ vpō emperour deſpyte ſent ſuche letter thei ſworē bi god bi name ſhold hym purſwe brenne moche might ſaydē nold neuer faill kȳg arthour rather dede let wryte lettre ſende ye emꝑour bi ſame meſſagiers maner bolde anſwere king arthour ſend emperoure rome ye romaīs ca lxxxi vnderſtondeth amonges yow rome kyng arthour bretaigne freely hold ſhal hold ād rome haſteli yeue truage axen truage conſtātyne which̄ eleynes ſone emperour rome ād honour ther longed maxymian kyng conquered fraūce almaigne paſſed mounth yoye conquered lū bardye ād thyſe two myne aunceſtres helden j ſhal haue thurgh goddes wylle ye reuerence arthur dyd emperours meſſagiers rome capit lxxxij whan lrē made enſealed kȳg arthur meſſagiers yafe grete yeftes ād meſſagiers toke hyr leue went thēs came court rome ayeū tolde emperour worthely vnderfongē whyche ryalle cōpanye ſerue hī rialli ſeruid thā ye ēꝑour kyng lyuing worlde whan emperour ſeyne lettre herde therȳ ſaw arthur wolde ruled aftyr hym let aſſēble ordeyne hugh̄ hoſt deſtroye kyng arthur myght kȳg arthur touchȳg power partye ordeyned power knightes rownde table ¶of kynges lordes camē helpe kyng arthur ayēſt emꝑour ca lxxxiij king scotlād irlād gutlād dē marke almaign̄ euery hē men duc normādye gaſcoyne flaūdres pehyto boloygne iiij gerȳ chartres x hoell bretaign̄ xij m▪ hym ſelf hys owne lād xij alebreſtriers archiers othir folk foot mā hē cowde nōbre whē alle redy wente then̄e kyng arthour toke hys lād gunnore wyf kepe one hys neuews wy knyght hardy kalled mordred trewe ye ſhal afterward kȳg arthur toke reaulme mordred ſauf onely ye croune ād kȳg arthur nōme hys hooſt wēt ſouthamptō ſhippes brought folk aſſembled dydē hē ſee good wynd wether wille ād alſo ſone myght arriued harfleet went hir ſhippes ſpradden contre kȳg arthour fought wyt geaūte ſpaigne called dynabus queld eleyne kyng hoelles coſyn lyttel bretaigne cap· lxxxiiij kȳg arthur dwelled contre littel men ne tolde hym comen grete geaūt spaigne rauiſſhed ye fair eleyne coſin hoell bretaigne brought hir vpon hyll kalled moūte ſeȳt bernard ther man cōtre ſo bolde ne ſo hardy durſt wt fight ner come nere place geaunt dwelled called dinabꝰ moche ſorwe dyd contre whā king arthour herde tyding kalled key bedewere commaūded hem go preuely ād eſpie wher geant might fonden camen riuage ther men ſholde gon̄ ye mounte encloſed aboute water yet euer ſhall ſaw brēnȳg fire vpon hylle ther alſo othir hille nye thervpō othir fire brēning· key bedewere camen next hille fondē widewe opēhede ſittȳg beſides tōbe ſore wepȳg grete ſorwe made ofte ſhe ſaid eleyne eleyne key bedewere • ed hir wherfor ſhe made ſo moche ſorwe lay ye tōbe ſaid ſhe ſorwe miſauēture faire lordes ſeke ye geant may yowe finde ye worth anone dede bene ſtille good wyfe ſayd therof dyſmay ye telle v ſoth thou makeſt ſo moch̄ ſorwe wepȳg syres ſaid ſhe damiſell yt noriſſhed wt breſt which̄ mē called eleyne yt nece hoell kȳg bretaigne lyeth ye bodi tō yt betakē noriſſh̄ ther came deuel geāt rauiſſhed hir alſo lad v both̄ way wolde haue forlain̄ maide yt ſo yōge tēdre age ſhe might ſuffre ſo grete ſo hugh̄ ye geāt punctel come woned certis wil quelle both̄ therfore faſt wēt ye hē ne wherfor ſaid go ye hēnes certis ſires ſaid ſhe eleyne dede geant made abide don̄ haūte muſt nedes ſuffre god wote good leuer dede hȳ dele ſo moche payne haue whā forlyeth whan key bedewere herde al womā tolde turned ayen̄ came kȳg arthour tolde hym ſeyne herde arthour anone toke hē loth wēte preuely bi night none hooſt wiſt came morū erly geant faught wyt hȳ ſtrōgely laſte ſlowe hȳ arthur bad bedewere ſmyte hys heed brȳg ye hooſt ſhewe hem wonder ſo grete ſo hugh̄ whā camen ayen̄ ye hooſt toldē wherfor ben̄ owte ſhewed hem heed ād euery man glad ād joyefull worthy dede ye kyng arthur done which̄ hir lord ād hoell full ſorwefull hys nece ſo loſte aft whā ſpace let make fayre chapelle lady ouer eleyns tombe ¶how kyng arthour yafe bataille emperour· which̄ bataill emperour ſlayne capit lxxxv arthour ād peple tydȳg emperour aſſembled grete power wel ſarazīs paynyms cryſten men wher nombre lxxx hors men fote men arthour peple ordeyned faſt forth hyr way toward ye emperour paſſed normādye fraūce vnto bourgoigne wold euen haue gon̄ hooſt men tolde hȳ emperours hoſt wold come lucie emperour ād hooſt begȳnȳg auguſt remeved fro rome cam forth ye right way ward ye hooſt kīg arthur eſpyes comen ſaydē yf arthur wolde ſhold fynde ther faſt emperour thei ſaid emperour ſo grete power wt hȳ kynges lāde • paynyms ynfere ād alſo criſtē peple nere grete folye kīg arthur mete wyt hȳ eſpies tolde emꝑour v men vi ayens owne hyſe king arthour bolde hardy thyng hym diſmayed ād ſayd gowe boldely goddes name ayēs romaȳs wt hȳ lede ſaraſins paynyms maner truſt haue god oneli vpon hyr ſtrēgth̄ gowe ſech̄ hem ſharpely ye name almyghty god ſlewe paynyms cryſtē men ben hē deſtroye criſtē men god ſhal v helpe haue right ād therfore haue truſt god ſo ye enemyes criſtendome god mowe dede deſtroied ād men mowe recorde worthyneſſe knygthode whā kȳg arthour thꝰ ſaid cryed hygh̄ voys god fader almighty wurſhipped thy name withouten end amē graū te v grace well don̄ deſtroye enemy ben̄ ayēſt cryſtendome name fadre ſone holy goſt amen god yeue hȳ neuer grace ne worſhip world ne mercy haue day ſhal feynte wel ſmyte egrely ſo roden ſoftely ordeyned wȳges wel wiſely emperour herd telle kīg arthur ād folke redy arayed fight wyt hȳ thydder came ordeyned hys wȳges beſt maner might ād truſt vpō ſtrengthe thā god almyghty ſeȳ afterward whā ye two hooſtes mettē gedre emperour loſt ſo moch̄ folk alſo dyd kīg arthur ſo many ſlayn̄ well one ſide othir grete pyte ſe wit jn bataill ſlayne thurgh king arthur v kȳges paynȳs othir wōder moche peple kīg arthures men foughtē ſo wel romaīs ād paynyms ſtrēgthe withſtonde thā xx ſhepes ayēs v wolfe befell batayll wonder hard longe durȳg owne ſyde ye emperour amonge hē ſlaine mā wiſt ſoth hȳ ſlowe kyng arthour let enburie knyghtes loſt bataill ād ſēt emperours body rome ſlayne bataille capitulo lxxxvi whan romaȳs wiſt yt emperour dede thei forſoke felde paynȳs alſo kȳg arthur hē chaced till night ād ſo many hē queld wonder telie tho turned kȳg arthour ayē tho night ād thāked god victorye ye morne let loke ſee felde knightes loſte ſay burel erle maūt bedewere kay ligiers erle boloign̄ vrtegj erle baar aloth erle wȳcheſtre curſale erle cheſtre holdē erle flaūdres thees ye grete lordes king arthour loſt bataille amonge grete knyghtes ād ſome let entier abbeyes bi contre ſomme let borne hyr owne cō tre ād emptrours body let take put vpon beer ād ſent rome ſēt ſaye romains bretaigne fraū ce whiche helde othir truage wold non̄ pay· axed hȳ othir truage right ſuche truage wold hē paye king let bere key kenē owne caſtel entered ligier borne boloigne ther lord ād holden borne flaundres ther entered alle let entiere mochel honour abbeyes howſes religyō ye contre ther dede arthour ſelfe ſoiourned ſame yere bourgoigne wyt hooſt ād thought ſame yere folewyng paſſe ye mounthe ioye haue gone rome take cyte haue put romayns ſubiectyon wykked tyraunt mordred hȳ lete ye ſhall ¶how mordred traytour kyng arthour toke hys land kepe hys caſtelles ād helde ayenſt hym capitulo lxxxvij whan king arthour taken mordred reaulme kepe gon̄ ayens emperour rome ād paſſed ſee mordred anone toke homage feautes hem lāde wolde haue lāde owne vſe toke caſtelles aboute ād let hē araye falſeneſſe dyd grete wrōge ayens lawe criſtēdom toke hys owne emes wyfe traitour ſhold ordeyned hym grete hooſt ayēſt arthur comīg holde lāde ayenſt hȳ wt ſtrēgth̄ euermore ſlee kȳg arthur yf might ſend ſee land lette aſſemble painyms cryſten peple ſend ſaxones danoys helpe hym alſo mordred ſēt cheldryck done men come hȳ owte saxoyne worthy duke promyſed hym brought hȳ moch̄ peple wold graūte bretaigne euermore ye lād frō beyōde humber vn scotlād lande engiſt vortigers yift whē ſpouſed hys doughtyr cheldryk came grete ſtrēgth̄ power peple mordred aſſē bled alſo ī halfe xlm ſtronge knightes nede ¶how arthour enchaſed mordred traitour ād ſlayne alſo kyng arthour wounded deth capitulo lxxxviij whan thys tydynge came kȳg arthur ther burgoyne full ſore anoyed ād toke alle fraūce hoell kepe wyt halnēdel men prayed hȳ wolde kepe tyl came ayen ſelfe wolde went bretaigne auenge vpon mordred traitour forth went hys way ād came wytſand made hys men gone ſhippes hȳ ſelf wolde haue arryued ſādewith brought hȳ hoſt fraū ce alſo owne lāde er might come lande hys peple comē oute ſhippes mordred comen wyt alle power yafe ſtrōge bataille ſo kȳg arthur loſt many man er might comē londe gawē nevew ſlayne anguyſſhel helde scotland many wherof kyng arthour full ſory comen land mordred might ayēſt hem endure anon̄ diſcōfyted fledde thēs ſame nyght hys men vpon morne cam̄ londō cyte wold ſuffre hȳ come frō then fled wyncheſtre ther helde hym peple hȳ came kyng arthour let take body gawen coſyn ād body anguiſſell let hē borne ſcotlāt hyr owne contre entered anon̄ kȳg arthur toke wey deſtroie mordred fled fro thēs īto cornewaill quene gūmore yt kȳg arthours wyf tho ſoiourned yorke punctel herd yt mordred fled thēs might endure ayens kȳg arthur ſore adrad grete doubte wiſt beſt done ſhe wiſt wel hir lord kȳg arthur wold neuer hir haue mercy grete ſhame ſhe don̄ toke hir way preuely iiij men withoute mo came katlione ſhe dwelled hir lyfe ſhe neuer ſeyne amonge folke hyr lyfe durȳg arthur wiſt mordred fledde cornewaill let ſent men scotlād northūberlād vn hūbar let aſſēble folk withoute nōbre camen fro thēs cornewaill ſeche purſwe mordred mordred aſſēbled hȳ alle folk cornewaille peple without nōbre wyſt arthur comȳg ād leuer deye take chaūſe thā ferther flee abode yaf hard bataille king arthour peple ſo ſo moch̄ peple ſlayne half ād othir mā wiſte better partie ſo befell laſt morded ſlayne folke ād good cheualrie king arthour gadred noryſſhed dyuerſe lā de alſo noble knyghtes roūde table ſo moche preyſed thurgh owt alle world ſlayne arthour ſelfe wounded deth let hȳ borne lytier ſurgyē heled woundes yet bretōs ſuppoſē lyued othir lād ſhall come yet conquere bretaign̄ certes propoſicye merlyn ſayd deth ſhall doubtous ſayd ſoth· men ther yet haue doubte ſhullē euer men ſaith men wyt whether lyueth dede arthur borne auyone xxij yere regne incarnacyon owr lord iheſu criſt vc xlvi yere king arthour delyuered royaulme conſtantyn ye ſone cador nephew capitulo lxxxix whan kyng arthour wyſt myght lenger regne let come beforne hȳ conſtātyne cadors ſone erle cornewaill coſȳ hȳ betoke reaulme ſaid bad therof kȳg tyll came ayen̄ aſmoch̄ non̄ heir body begoten grete harm̄ ſo noble king ſo doubty child bodi begotē alle thȳg god wyl haue don̄ muſt don̄ who name bleſſhed withoute ende amē kȳg conſtātyne werred mordredes two ſones capitulo xc thys conſtātyne noble knight worthy body ye ij ſones mordred begoten grete enuye cōſtātine tho crowned king ſo begonne mene werre ayens hȳ punctel aſſē bled grete hooſt hē fore mordred bene dryuen away dyde moche ſorwe thurgh land one brother ordeyned lō take cyte wincheſtre cōſtātyne came london ſlew hȳ wēt wȳcheſtre ſlow hȳ alſo ēnemies dede whā cōſtātine regned iiij yere deyed lyeth lōdō kȳges adelbright ād edelf ca xcj affter kȳg cōſtātines deth ther ij kȳges bretaigne one called adelbright danoys helde cōtre northfolk ſouth fol othir hight edel bretō punctel helde nychol lȳdeſey ye land vnto hūbar thiſe ij kȳges faſt werred gydre accorded loued gedre borne owne body kīg edel ſuſtre kalled orewē ne yafe hir thurgh grete frēdſhyp king adelbright wyfe begate hir doughter kalled argentyll ye thridde yere came vpō hym ſtronge ſekeneſſe nedes muſt deye ſent kyng edelf brother lawe ſhold come ſpeke hym cam̄ wyt good tho prayed king ād coniured alſo name god▪ dede ſhold take argē tyl doughtyr lāde kept hyr well noriſſhe hyr hys chambre whā ſhe age ſhe ſhold maryed ſtrōgieſt worthieſt man might fynde ſhold yelde vp hyr ſād ayene edel graū ted· othe confermed hys prayer whan adelbryght dede entered edell toke damyſell argentil noriſſhed hir chambre ſhe became fayreſt creature myght lyue man fynde kyng edel maried damyſell knaue kychene capitulo xcij kīg edell vncle damyſel argentill bethought howe might falſely haue ye land nece euermore falſely ayēſt othe thought deceyue damiſell marye hyr knaue hys kychē kalled curan bicame ye worthieſt ſtrengiſt man bodi man wyſt lande tho lyued hym thought hyr ſhenfully haue maryed haue hir lād afterward clene deceyuyd curā hauelockes ſone· which̄ king kyrkelane denmarke curan conquered wyfes lād ſlewe kīg edelf wife vncle hyr land othir place telled openly regned thre yere saxon danoys hȳ kylled grete harme bretaigne breton bare ſtonhenge hȳ enburyed wt mochel honour ¶of kyng conam ca xciij thys curan regned conam coſyn which̄ wonder prowde knight regned coude haue maner loue euer medelȳg peple ād toke vncle wt werre quelled ij child ſaxones werred ayenſt ofte time hē ouercame laſt ſo pee lyfes tyme regned xiiij yere deyed lyeth london ¶of kyng cortyfād gurmō de camē thurgh paynȳs bretaigne cap xciiij conam regned coſȳ cortyf byhated peple man beloued cortyf loſt bretaigne thurgh werre tyme felle grete myſchief bretaigne criſtēdome deſtroyed alle breton dryuē owte ād lāde loſt wythoute recouerȳg afterward left ye lād ſaxōs ye afterward ſhal tyme paynym̄ yt called gurmōd ye kȳges ſone dauffrykes paynȳs folke reaulme fadre kȳg ſauf bequath yave brother ſaid neuer ſholde kīg might gete ād conquere reaulme ſtraūge cōtre bold right ſtrōge bodi▪ hȳ profecyed merlyn ſaid ſhold wolfe ſee let aſſē ble paynyms withoute nōbre ād let appareill ſhippes ād went many londes toke homage ād feautes many ſo went ſee conbuered many dyuerſe lādes ſo came jrlād cōquered lād oftentymes werryd vpō bretōs breton vpō hem ofte wōnē ofte loſten ād yaue hoſtages bretōs ſo thei ſente gurmonde ther irlād ſhold come bretaign̄ helpe ayēſt ye bretōs helpe hem delyuer land hē wolde gladly holde hir lord paynyme alſo paynyms ye bretōs criſtē wel ought thē helpe ſo one lawe whā gurmōd herd prayer haſted hȳ moche might arryued scotland came northūberlād ſaxons dwel • ȳg ād cōfermed couenaūts bitwene hem made bi othes hoſtages bere hȳ trewe fayth holde hȳ lorde paye truage yere tho began ſaxons affrycās deſtroye robbe brēne townes deſtroye thing aſmoch̄ myght ſpared nethir man woman ne childe lered ne lewde alle quelled caſt downe townes caſtelles ād chirches ſo put ye lād grete deſtructyon alle thei might fleen punctel fledde then well pore ryche biſſhoppes abbotes chanons alle grete ſmale sōme littel bretaigne ād ſomme cornewaille alle ſhippes might haue kyng gurmond drofe kyng cortyfe chicheſtre queld bretōs queȳ tiſe gete towne cap xcv cortife kȳg fley then chycheſtre tho goode cyte ād well ſtronge ther helde hȳ xx dayes thys gurmond beſieged cyte ſo ſtronge might gete cite maner engyn might don̄ tho bethought vpō grete queȳtiſe brenne toune made engȳs glewe nettes tokē peces tunder fire boūde ſparwers fete afterward let hem flee punctel anone right fley logged hē towne ther hir neſtes inſtakkes euiſſing houſes fire began tēde brent towne whan breton ſaw euery ſyde hyed hem owte faught anone ſlayne diſcōfyted ād while bataill dured kyng preuely hyd hȳ ſtale awaye walles ād men wyſt neuer wher became ſo towne chicheſtre taken deſtroyed went gurmond deſtroyed cytees townes yt neuer afterward made ayen ſeȳ yet many place thys land cleped england name engiſt ād many kȳges made ye land capitulo xcvi whan gurmond deſtroyed alle lād thurgh oute yafe ye lōde saxos anone toke wyth good wille ſaxons lōg tyme deſyred moche engyſtes kȳrede firſt alle land bretaigne tho let hem kalled engliſhmē encheſon engiſtes name lād let kalle england hir lāgage folke ben kalled engliſſhmē moche ī time called engiſtes land whā cōquered vortyger eſpouſed doughter tyme brute came fyrſt englād lād called bretaigne· ād folke breton ſyth tyme gurmōd eftſones conquered yaf vnto ſaxons anone right chaūged name ſayd whan gurmōd paſſed ouer fraū ce conquered many landes ād deſtroyed cryſten peple came ye ſaxōs dwelled land ād begonne faſt inhabite hir owne wylle wold haue made new kȳ ge lordes myght neuer aſſenten haue onely kȳg hem entendaūt ther fore made many kynges dyuerſe ſhyres engiſtes time firſt kyngdome kent ſouthſexe thridde weſtſexe iiij eſtſexe v northūberland vj eſtangle· ſaye northfolk ſouthfolk vij merchenorth erldom nichol hūtyngdone herford glouceſtre wyncheſtre warrewyk ād derby ſo departed ye engliſſh englond vij party befell kynges werred ofte tyme gedre euer ſtrengeſt benōme hī febleſt ſo long tyme nad kȳg crouned amonges hem ne cryſten man tho amonges hem ne criſtēdome nothir paynyms tyll ſaint gregorye pope rome ſeyn child nacion englād ye cyte rome wō der fayre creature ād grete deſyre hem beholde axed marchauntz whēnes nacion mē told hȳ englōd ād engliſſhe called peple englōd paynȳs beleued vpon god allas ſaid ſeȳt gregorie wel mowe called engliſſhe haue ye vyſages angeles ād therfore wel ought criſtē thys encheſon ſeȳt gregorie ſent ſeȳt auguſtin englād xl good men good lyfe holi men preche teche conuert englyſſh peple hē turne god vi yere ſeint gregorie bene pope ſaye incarnacyō lord jeſu criſt v clxxxvij yere cronicles telleth ſeynt auguſtyn baptyſed cōuerted king adelbright made ye biſſhoppes felawes capit xcvij whan ſeint auguſtin firſt came englād arryued ile tenet ſo paſſed forth ād came caūterbury ther ſoiourned kȳg adelbright kent lignage engiſt vnderfeng ſeint auguſtin hys felawes wyth moche honour yaf hȳ hē neded ferther yaf hȳ faire place nowe called abbey ſeint auguſtȳs which̄ place lyeth hē ſelf ſhrined king adelbright good mā wt good wil herd ſeint auguſtīs p̄dicaciōs ād yafe hē leue preche thurgh lād kent torne cōuerte hī alle peple might ād befell ſo afterward thurgh goddes grace littell tyme ye king adelbright hē ſelf conuerted god ād peple land baptiſed mene time peple hē turned god ſeint auguſtin came roucheſtre preched goddes word paynyms therfore ſkorned caſt hȳ reight tailles ſo al mantell honged ful reigh tailles deſpyte thei caſt hym gutes reighes fyſſhe punctel wherfor good man ſeint auguſtyn ſore anoyed greued prayed god childrē ſhold borne afterward ī cite roucheſtre moſt haue tailles whan ye king wyſt herde vēgeaū ce fall thurgh ſeins auguſtyns prayer let make hous ī honour almyghty god wheryn woman ſhold deliuered hyr chyldren brugges ende punctel which̄ hous yet womē ye cyte ben̄ delyuered childrē whā ſeȳt gregorie herde telle engliſſhmen turned god ād conuerted ſente ſeint auguſtyn palione biſſhop called paulyn made prymat ād erchebiſſhop englād yaf hī power make ordeyne biſſhoppes land ād anone auguſtyn pallione dignite erchibiſſhoppe made ij biſſhoppes hys felaws came hȳ fro rome one called mellyt dwelled londō called iuſtyn held dignyte roucheſtre biſſhop mellit tho wēt preche eſtexe baptyſed kyng contre kalled sicwith king adelbrightes coſyn ſuſtres ſone ād iuſtin wēt preche ſouthſexe turned moche peple god ſeynt auguſtin went ſelf prechȳg thurgh england ¶how ſeint auguſtyn went wale breton nold nat obedyent erchebiſſhop canterbury capit xcviij whā englād baptyſed turned god ſeȳt auguſtyn went land breton kepe hē fro engliſſhmē ſeyne jn wale fonde mōkes abbeyes vij biſſhoppes breton deſyred allway cryſten peple ſeint auguſtyn cōuerted ſaid biſſhoppes legat rome pmat england ſhold alle reſon obedyent wyt englyſſhemen ſaidē noldē erchibyſſhop carlyon ād ſaid nold neuer maner thyng ben obedyēt engliſſhmē ye engliſſhmen ſayd ben aduerſaires enemyes haue dryuē v owt owne contre ben criſten men euer haue ben̄ engliſſhmen haue euer ben paynȳs nowe late ben conuerted seint auguſtyn might hē none anſwere haue otherwyſe ſaydē aꝑtely nold neuer hem obeye hȳ ne pope rome ſeīt auguſtyn turned ayen ye kyng adelbright king kēt told hȳ thys folk wold man obedyēt erchebiſſhop karlyon whan kīg herde ſore annoyed ſaid wold hē deſtroye ſent olfride kȳg northūberland hys frend ſhold come hym wyt alle power might ſhold mete hȳ leiceſtre punctel ād thēs wold gon̄ wale deſtroye erchebiſſhop carlyon refuſed ſeynt auguſtin kyng adelbright kȳg olfride queld brecmale kyng breton helde contre leiceſtre capi xcix hit befel ſo ther king breton helde contre leiceſtre contre aboute named brecmale breton herde telle two englyſſhe kynges wold mete ther leiceſtre wente walys let ordeyne power fight thees two kȳges lyttell avaylled folk ſlayne ſelf fled loſt landes euermore theſe two kynges adelbright olfryd dwelled whyle leiceſtre departed landes amōges hē token homage feautes folk contre ther wentē ward wale wale herd telle ye diſcomfyture brecmale hath leiceſtre wonder • ore adrad two kynges ād anone choſe amonges hem good men holy heremytes mō kes preſtres ād othir folk grete plente wenten baarfoot wollwerd haue mercy two kynges kȳ ge ſo ſterne ſo wikked • old neuer ſpeke wyth hem queld hem euerichō allas ſorowe ne ſpared hē nomore wolf doth ſhepes punctel ſmotē hedes euerychon ſo alle martred hem camen vnderſtō de v hōdred xl afterward two kynges went fro thēs bangore quelle alle might fynde ye breton whan bretōs herdē aſſembled ordeyned hir power fight wyt hem tho barō wale called bledrik cornewaill ſom tyme lord denouſhyre ye kȳg adelbright driuen wale yeue bataille bataill kȳg aldelbright ſlayne eldryf wounded ſore forſoke felde moſt part peple ſlayn eldrif fled northūberland owne land afterward ye peple leyceſtre ſhire made ſtrēgthe cadewan brecynalis ſone kyng leiceſtre regned nobely grete honour ¶how cadewan kyng leiceſtre elfryd king nortū berland frendes debate afterward bitwene edwyn cadwalȳ bothe hyr ſones capit c bataill don̄ breton aſſembled hem went camen vnto leiceſtre made cadwā brecinalis ſone kīg leiceſtre contre ād toke homage feautes folk contre aſſembled grete hooſt ſaid wolde gone northū berland deſtroye kyng elfrid ſlee yf might whā comen thydder frendes went ſo bitwene hem made hē accorded manere elfryd ſhold hold alle londe frō hūbar vnto scotland cadewā ſhold haue alle land ſyde hūber vnto ſouth punctel became good frendes hys lyfes duryng ād loued gedre two brethrē elfride ſone kalled edwyn ād held lād northūberlād fadres deth· fader holde hys lyfes time cadewā ſone called cadwalyn helde fadres lād helde whyles lyfe ād loued gedre bretheren loue laſt bitwene hē onely two yere began debate bitwen̄ hē lyther enuyous coſin cadwalyne yt called bryeny ſo thei aſſembled grete hoſt both̄ partyes ye laſt befell cadwalyn diſcomfited edwȳ purſued drofe fro place place ſo laſt fley irlād deſtroyed land kaſt downe caſtelles brēt maners departed cadwalyns land amōge hys frendes long tyme came cadwalyn ayen̄ irland wt ſtrōg power plaine bataill quelled edwyne frēdſhippes nameli thaym witheld lādes thurgh edwynes yefte ¶how king oſwald queld thurgh kȳg cadwalyn peanda oſwy ſeīt oſwaldes brother regned queld peanda capitulo cj whan edwyne ſlaine offris ſone vndertoke werre ayenſt cadwalyn eme ſo offrys deyde duryng werre deth offrys tho regned gentill criſten man moche loued god almighty land northūberlād herytage called oſwold kȳg lād moche frend edwyne helde grete part land cadwalȳ ſame cadwalȳ werred vpon hȳ drofe hȳ toward scotland whē cadwalȳ ſawe wold ferther hym purſwe toke ſomme folke peāda brother lawe ād praied purſwe oſwald tyll take ſlayne cadwalȳ turned home ayene whan oſwald herd tydyng cadwalyn turned hom ayen wold lē ger flee abode peāda yafe bataille peāda diſcomfyted fled ād came ayen̄ cadwalȳ ſaid wold neuer holde ony foot lond hȳ ſo wold auē ge oſwold cadwalyn let aſſemble grete hooſt fight oſwold ſo peada came vnto northūberlād yaue bataill vnto oſwold ſame bataille oſwold ſlayne hede ſmyte ētered abbey bardeney whyche place god hath wrought many fayr myracle ther elles anone oſwy brother ſeiſed hys hād lād • oſwaldes folck northūberland loued wonder wel helde hyr lord men hys kyn worthy ynough wold haue departed lōd werred gedre • ād moche nat ſtrōg ynough camē peāda prayed helpe ſocour ād promyſed lōd largely vpon couenant wolde gyde help counceill peā da herd hyre prayer ſo ſpake king cadwalyn ſhold ordeyne grete hooſt· ād faſt ordeyn̄ northūberland fighte oſwy ād oſwy meke man moche loued pee charyte prayed peanda loue pee proferd gold ſyluer grete pleī te peāda ſo proud nolde graunte hym pee maner thīg thīg wold wyt hȳ fighte ſo ye laſte ther ſet day bataill oſwyne truſt vpon god peanda truſtyd vpon pryd vpon hooſt gedre ſmoten egrely peanda anone diſcomfited ſlayne ye jncarnacyon lord iheſu criſt vjc lv yere oſwyn regned tho xxviij yere ād king called oſwyn peanda coſyn werred vpō kyng oſwy foughten gedre oſwy victorie oſwȳ diſcomfyted ſlaine lyeth tēnemouth kyng cadewaldre yt cadewaleynes ſone regned aftir fadre laſte kyng breton capitulo cij deth cadwaleȳ regned hys ſone cadwaladre well nobely moder ſuſter kyng peanda whan regned xij yere fell grete ſekeneſſe then̄e ſo grete diſcord bytwene ye lordes land euery weried vpon othir yet tyme ther fell ſo grete derth ſcarcite corne vytailles thys •• nd man might goo thre day iiij fro towne towne yt ſhold nat fynde bye gold ne ſyluer brede wyne ne none othir vytaille wher man myght lyue onely peple lyued bi rote herbes othir lyuyng none ſo moche failled aboute fiſſhes wilde beſtes alle thȳg ſo yet thys myſauenture ther fell ſo grete mortalite peſtilence amonge peple corrupcyon eir lyuȳg peple ne ſuffyſed burye ye dede body deydē ſo ſodēli grete ſmale lord ād ſeruaunt etyng goyng ſpekyng ſo neuer herd ſodeyne deth among peple which̄ wende goū burie dede body wyt ſame dede body buried yt might flee fleddē forſoke hir lō de houſes wel grete hūger ſcarcite corn̄ vitailles ye horrible mortalite peſtilēce lād wentē othir lādes ſaue hir liues left ye lād deſert waſt ſo yt ther man trauaille tille ye lōd ne ere ne ſowe ſo ye land bareyne cornes othir fruites defaulte tilierſ thys myſauenture dured xj yere moo man myght ere ne ſowe ¶how cadwaldre went owt land littel bretaigne cadwaladre ſaw grete hunger mortalite peſtilence lond poure faylling cornes othir vitailles folke periſſhed ſaw alſo mooſt partie hys lād waſted voide peple appareilled hem folke left lyue paſſed ouer lyttel bretaigne wyt littel nauye vnto kīg alayne moche loued coſyn fadre moche loued time ſailled ſee made grete lamē tacyō ſo dydē ſaydē dediſti no dn̄e tan quam oues eſcarum gētibꝰ diſperſiſti no began cadwaldre cōpleyne folke pytouſly ſaid allas ſaid v wrecches caytyfs punctel owr grete ſȳnes which̄ wolde amende v whyle ſpace repētaunce comē vpō v myſauenture which̄ chaceth v oute owne reaulm̄ propre ſoyle fro owt whiche ſomtime romains ſcottes saxon ne dane might exilen v avaylleth nowe v tyme oft fithes haue gotē many othir lā de ſith wylle god abyde dwelle owr owne lande god werray jugge alle thȳg knoweth done made ſech̄ wolde ceſe owr ſȳ ne ād enemy ne myght v ne lignage exylen fro reaulme wolde amend v folyes ād ſene propr • defaultes therfore ſhewed v wrath wull chaſtiſe v myſdedes sith v doth without bataill ſtrength enemyes bi grete cōpanyes wrecchedly leue owre owne reaulme propre land turne agayn ye romains turne agayn ye ſcottes turne agayn ye ſa • ōs turne agayn̄ ye fraunſoys ſheweth bretaygne deſert whiche power myght neuer make deſert ne yet yowre power hath put v exill onely power ye king almyghty haue ofte offended bi folyes whyche wolde leue vnto ye tyme tyll chaſtiſed v bi dyuȳ power amōge wordes lamētacion kyng cadwaladre made folk thei arryued littell bretaigne came ye king alayne ſaid king receyued wyt ioye made hī ſerued wondre nobely dwelled longe time ēgliſſh peple lefte lyue eſcaped grete hūger mortalite lyued beſt wyſe might moche peple ſpronge came hem ſent saxoyn̄ borne hir frē de men woman childrē reſtore ye cytees peple othir tounes voide peple trauailie tellē erthe whan saxon herden tyding thei camen land wondre thikke grete companye logged ād herberwed hem ſelf ye cōtre wolden fonde man hem lette ne withſtonde ſo woxen multiplied gretly vſed cuſtomes contrees wher thei comē lawes langages hir owne land changed name cytees townes caſtelles burghes yaf hem name called hem thei kalled helden cō tree baronage lordſhippes tree maner breton tyme compaſſed hem among othir cōpanies came fro germayne ī lād came noble quene kalled sexburga wyt men woman withoute nombre arriued cōtre northumberland toke land albyone cornewaylle hyr hyr folke none might letten hem deſolat voide peple fewe poure breton lefthe moūtaignes wodes vn tyll tyme fro tyme forth loſte breton thys reaulme dayes engliſſh peple begā regne departed land bitwene hem ād thei made many kynges aboute diuerſe partyes lōd ben̄ deuiſed fyrſt weſtſex ſeconde merchenrich̄ thridde eſtangle fourth̄ kent fyfthe ſouthſex alle thees regned land cadwaladre paſſed owte land dwelled lyttell bretaigne wyt kyng aleyne hys coſyn ād trewe frēde punctel whā lōge dwelled knowing mortalite peſtilence ouer paſſed lōde repleniſſhed aliene peple thought turne ayene owne lande praied kȳg aleyne hys coſyn ſocour ād helpe myght reſtored hys propre reaulme fyrſt dignyte kyng aleyne graunted hys prayer wyt good dyd apparailen hȳ take hys way viage lande prayed god almyghty deuoutly wolde make hȳ demonſtracyon yf yt hys prayer land pleſaūce none agayn wyl god almyghty wolde thȳg don̄ whā thus deuoutly made prayer voys fro heuē ſaid bad hȳ leue iourney way englond ād ſhold go pope rome ſo wylle almighty god breton ſhulde nomore regne bretaigne ne neuer recoure land vnto ye tyme prophecye merlyn ſayd fullylled ſholde neuer ben̄ vnto ye tyme comen reliques body ſhull ben̄ brought fro rome tranſlated bretaygne whan relyques othir ſaintes haue ben̄ hyd perſecucyon paynyme folke ſhull fondē opēly ſhewed ſhall recoure hyr land ayene whiche haue ſo longe tyme loſt thurgh hyr grete ſȳnes whā cadwaldre herde thys anſwere mervailleth gretly 〈◊〉 tolde king aleyne thā kȳg aleyne dyd ſent clergye londe made hem brynge ſtories profecyes merlyn sybille hadde ſaid hir prophecyes whā knewe prophecye feſtome prophecyed regle ād ꝓphecies accorded dyuyne anſwere cadwaladre herd counſeylled hym leue peple navie ſubmitte hȳ ye diſpoſicyō god done āgele hȳ cō contre bytwene kynges mā might wyt lāde wēt abbotes pryours men relygyon wrytten lyves dedes kynges long euery regned who cōtre maner eueri kīg deyed biſſhoppes alſo ther made grete bokes let euer englōd kyng northūberlād oſbryght forlay ye wyfe buerne bocard thurgh ſtrēgth aftyr buerne conquered king power ſtrength̄ capitulo ciij thus befel ſame tyme ther kyng northūberland called oſbright ſoiourned yorke kyng wēt vpon daye wode hȳ refreſſhe ād diſporte whē came ayene went preueli good mannes houſes which̄ called buerne good man place gon̄ tyme ſee often time woned aſpie awaite theues robbours often tymes woned come ye land robbe brenne ād ſlee lady buernes wife wonder fayre woman ād welcomed kyng mochel honour worthely hȳ ſerued thing whan king etē toke lady bi hand lad hyr chābre ād ſaid wolde ſpeke wyt hyr coūceil folke frō chābre made avoide ſauf onely ladi lady wiſt wherfor dyd tyll done wt hir wille whan don̄ dede turned ayen̄ york lady left wōder ſore wepȳg dede done whā hir lord comen home ſawe hyr wepe ſuche ſorwe make axed hyr ſhe don̄ ſhe made ſuch̄ ſorwe syr ſaid ſhe queȳ tely falſely kīg oſbright done ſhame vylayne ayēſt tolde hȳ trouthe ye king hir forlayne wyt ſtrēgth̄ wher fore ſhe ſaid ſhe leuer deye thā lyue fair • eef ſtyll ſayd ayenſt ſtrength̄ febleneſſe littell worth therfore ſhalt thou neuer laſſe loued namely thow haſt told trewthe ād almyghty god graunte lyfe ſhal yow well auenge thys buerne grete man myghty lord beloued grete frendes let ſende ye greteſt lordes lande hē made cōplaint ye deſpyte king done ſaid wold bē auēged ſo euer alle hys frendes counceilled graūted hȳ therto went ward york ther king buerne toke meyne came ye king king hȳ ſawe kalled hȳ curtouſly buerne bi name buerne anſwerde ſayd syr yow deffye ād yelde vp feautes homage londes moch̄ haue holde yow ſo fro tyme foreward wyl neuer thȳg hold ſo departed kȳg withoute ſpeche abiding toke leue frendes went denmarke cōplayned gordryne tolde hym grete deſpyte forſayde king oſbright hym done wyfe prayed ſocour helpe hym auenge whan king godryne dēmarke danois herde pleȳte buerne prayer made wonder glad hert aſmoche might fynd cauſe gone englond werre vpon engliſſhmen alſo auēge buerne deſpite kyng done hys wyfe aſmoch̄ buerne ſibbe king dēmarke anone let ordeyne grete hooſt men let prepare ſhippes aſmoche nede viage whan alle hooſt redy ye kȳg made ij bretheren cheuytains noble knightes bolde one called hungar ād othir hubba danoys toke yorke ād quelled king oſbright afterward king elle capitulo ciiij whan thing redy two bretheren toke leue king gordryn went toward ye ſee wente englond faſte myght ſpede buerne ſo wel conforted faſt hyed ye danoys ben̄ arryued northcōtre comen thurgh oute holderneſſe deſtroied ye contre brent tounes ād robbed folke ād quelled myght taken tyll camen york whan king oſbryght ſaw hem come toke hys peple came owt cyte faught wyth hem foyſon ayens hem moche peple ſlayne bothe party kȳg oſbright hȳ ſelfe ther ſlayn̄ cyte anone take ād danois wentē theryn ther alſo othir king northumberland buernes frēdes choſen helde kyng called elle moch̄ wold kȳg oſbright bene entendaunt deſpyte done buerne hyr coſyn hit befell thꝰ kȳg elle gon̄ wode diſporte venyſon ſomdell take ſate ye wode mete knight ſaid haue well ſped moch̄ veniſon takē wt worde ther came man ſaid jf ye moche venyſon haue wonnen hondred tymes ſo moch̄ ther ayens ye haue loſt contre danoys haue getē take cite yorke punctel ayēs yowe ſhull hold neuer ye ſhull come theryn ſoth haue ſlayne king oſbright whā king elle theſe wordes herde let aſſemble folk ye cōtre ordeyned ye power might haue· wold haue gete towne york wyt ſtrēgthe danoys camen owte anone ād yafe bataille queld king mooſt partie men brought hȳ ſame place ther ſlayne ſhall euer kalled ellecroſt place littel yorke tho abode danoys neuer tyll conquered northumberland contre made wardeyns went ferther land token nothyngam ther dwelled wynter dyden ſorwe might whā ſomer tyme cam̄ remeued nothyngam camen nychol lȳ deſey holād mā myght hem withſtōde ſo moche power ſtrength̄ ¶how ſeynt edmond king martred cap cv ſo ferre danois paſſed contre vn contre euer brennyng robbȳg deſtroied might tyll camen vn thetford contre foundē cryſten kyng moche loued god ād werkes kalled edmōd kīg northfolk ſouthfolk ſeynt edmond king ordeined moche folk might fought danoys folk diſcomfyted king ſelfe dryuen vnto ye caſtell framelyngham danoys hym purſued camē vnto ye ſame caſtel whā kīg edmōd ſawe ye caſtel might hē witſtond came ayēs hē whō ye danoys firſt ſpekē anon̄ axed hȳ wher kīg edmōd nowe ſoth ſayd whan caſtel ther king whā went caſtel went oute alſo ād whethir ſhall eſcape deye goddes wyll muſt whā ſeȳt edmōd nēpned god bi wiſtē well ſelf anone hubba hūbar tokē ād ſaid ſholde god forſake criſten lawe many hȳ beforne ſeint edmond ſaid nold neuer rather wolde ſuffre ye deth goddes loue lawes kepe tho toke king edmōd boūde hī vnto tree ād made hir archiers hȳ ſhete arewes tyll yt bodi ſtikked ful arowes vrchone full prikkes paynes yt wold neuer god forſake ye ſame payne turment deyeth betoke hys ſowle god ād whā ſawen dede thei ſmyten hede maner ſeint edmond martred ¶how hubba hū gar tokē toune redyng ca cvj whā ſeȳt edmōd martred hūgar ād hubba went thēs wyt hir danoys vnto redȳge ād went thidderward brē de townes citees quelled cryſten peple wold god forſake caſt downe chyrches camen redȳge toke ye toune ther helde hem tyll yt kyng edelf weſtſex came thidder wt power take ye towne tho camē oute ye danois yeue bataill kȳg edelf ād bataill queld erle ye danoys called cydrake vpō morwe came ye kȳg elred brother alured wt ſtrōge power grete hooſt kȳg edelf came ayen̄ foughtē daye bataill ye danoys camē tho oute fight wt hem bataille wonder ſtronge many man ther ſlayn̄ ye danoys day ye victorye king eldred hys brother alured day diſcomfyted fourth̄ day afterward ye danoys ēgliſſhmē foughtē gedre othir tyme vpō ekeldēne ther ſlayn̄ kyng dēmarke yt called rafȳg iiij erles grete power day ye danoys ſhame thei driuen vnto engliſfelde ād xv day danoys engliſſhmē foughtē othir tyme rafȳg engliſſhmen diſcōfyted· then danoys called roynt wēt redȳg wt hooſt deſtroyed myght take king eldred fought hym ſore wounded werfore deyed ād regned v yere lyeth wonburne ¶of king alured danoys tyme praied mercy muſt goū land capitulo cvij deth eldred regned brother alured dolfynes kalled tho wentē danoys •• embled hem wente ſeche alured tho ye newe king southſex foundē wiltone littel peple notheles faught hem laſt fledde then felde went weſtſex ād ordeyned ſo moche peple hys owne reaulme alſo othir· ſo tyll ſtronge hooſt ſo danois power ayens hym ſtō de came london hooſt ther danois ſoiourned ther wolde • haue foughten hem ye danoys durſt fyghte praird pee muſt gon̄ ayen̄ vnto hir owne contre neuermore england come ayen harme done vpon couenant ſhold yeue hȳ plegge good hoſtages ſuche ye engliſſhmen wold axen hubba hungar quelled chipenham danoys brought hyr kyng king capitu cviij ſame day danoys departed frō lō ſo faſt rodē both̄ nyght daye neuer toke reſt goyng tyll camē vnto exceſtre token toune helde hem whan king alured herd tydīg anon̄ let take hoſtages wēt then exceſtre alle power whē ye danoys herd telle comīg wenten fro then weſtſexe camen chippenham ther didē moche harme contre thei robbed folke brought hem pryſon kȳg alured hem purſued came vpō hem ferſely hem aſſailled ād ſlayne hubba hungar brother ād buerne bocard thys bataill moche folk ſlayne wel one ſide gree felde leſt danoys moche kyng came littell company king haſted hym moche might wende ayene whan danoys foundē hubba dody dede entered made vpon grete logge let kalle hubbeſ • owe ſo called day place kalled denēſhire baron ſomerſet wyllſtſhire dorſet herd tell hir kīg diſcomfyted· ād ordeyned alle power myghten haue camen kyng ther thanked god fonden leyue wend danoys hym ſlayne tho toke counſeill king barōs thei wolde gon̄ ſeche danoys hem fyghten ād ſo riddē nyght hem ſeche camē morwe aboute pryme abyngdon ther danoys king tho alured baron aſſembled ād aſſailled danoys egrely yaf hē ſtrong bataill danoys nobely put hem lōge time man wiſt whethir partye yt mooſt peple ſlayne thus befell god wolde ye kȳg alured victore mochel honour danoys ſo driuen ne wiſt whyther torne xv dayes king hem purſwed wille glad ād fayne thei ſpeken pee accord token good hoſtages ād ſaid nold neuer vp hym werre ne debate arere ād ouer behyght kȳg alured wolde gon̄ bring hyr owne king vnto hir kyng ſhold baptiſed vpon condycion noble vaylliaūt kȳg alured graunted hem lyfe lymme ſaid hem ſhold gone hir king fetche certayn daye comen ayen̄ hem ſette ſo wente thei faſt forth camen ayen̄ hyr day aſſigned ād alle danoys brought hir king thaȳ kyng alured anone let hem ben̄ baptyſed hir name chāged king danoys kalled athelſton xxx felawes name chāged alſo othir baptiſed ryght beleue punctel thys done weſtmynſtre tyme kyng alured helde kyng athelſtone alle danoys xij dayes ſoioure mochel ſolempnyte ād yafe hem grete yeftes baptiſed ſo departed whan don̄ tho good kyng alured eſe ād yt hys enemyes ouercomen turned ryght beleue almyghty god danois gon̄ wyth gurmond fraunce camen ayen̄ englond deth kyng alured capitulo cix thꝰ befell afterward danoys northūberlād paynyms camē grete ſtrēgth̄ huge hooſt fraunce vnderſtode wyt hē wēt fraunce wyth gurmond auffryke whan cōquered englōd yafe vnto ſaxons tho camē fro fraū ce arryued kēt ſēt northūberland ſhold comē hem whan two hooſtes comē aſſembled anon̄ went deſtroye cryſten peple englōd fro place place dyden moch̄ ſorwe hit befel thus almyghty god wold hard chaūce englond· good kyng alured woned abate danois deide mene tyme kīg alured regned xxx yere good kīg ben̄ ād coude well chaſtyſe enemy good clere let make many bokes boke engliſſh̄ auentures kynges batailles ben done lond ād manj othir bokes geſtes let hem wryte gret wyſedome good lernȳg thurgh which̄ boke many man may hī amend wyll hem rede vpō loke vpon who ſoule almighty god haue mercy kyng alured lyeth wyncheſtre▪ ¶of kȳg edward kȳg alured ſone capit cx alured regned edward ſone which̄ good man wyſe wōder curtois danois dyd moche ſorwe lond hir power encreſced began wexe frō day day danoys camē ofte theyr companyes land whā king ſaw might better done nōme trewes wyth hem graū ted hem pee notheles truwes dured nat longe danois ne begonne ſtrongely werre vpō englyſſhmē dyd hem moch̄ ſorwe wherfore kīg edward dyd aſſemble grete hooſt fyght hem ād tho deyed kīg edward whā god wolde thys kyng edward regned xxiiij yere lyeth wȳ cheſtre beſides fadre kyng adelſton edmonde eldred ād edwyne brother capitulo cxi edward regned adelſton ſone whā regned iiij yere helde bataille ayenſt danoys drofe kyng gaufride kȳg danois hys hooſt vnto ſee ād reſted scotlād avoyed ſtrongeli contre yere thei cū berlād ſcottes weſtmerland begonne werre vpō king athelſton yaf hem ſo ſtronge bataille quelled ſo many hem man coude telle nombre hē ād ne regned thre yere regned xxv yere· lyeth malmeſbury thys adelſton regned hys brother edmond aſmoche king adelſton ſone edmond worthy knight doughty man body noble knight ī thridde yere king wēt ouer hūbar whiche place fonde ij kȳges danoys one called enelaf othir regnaut ād king edmond drofe hē both̄ land went ād toke grete prey cumberland edmōd ne regned vij yere lyeth glaſtenbury edmond regned eldrede brother avenged edward fadre hys ennemyes hȳ quelled ād ſeyſed northumberland hand made ſcottes abowe meke vnto ſecō de yere regned came arnalaf gwyrā kȳg denmarke ſeiſed northumberland helde lōde two yere came kyng eldred drofe hym land ād kȳg eldred noble mā good who goodneſſe ſeȳt dunſtō preched kyng eldred regned xi yere ād lyeth wȳcheſtre eldred edwyne ſone edmōd brother regned ād lyther mā toward god ād peple hated folk owne land loued ād honoured ſtraūge men ſette littel holy chirch̄ ād toke holy chyrch̄ treſour mighte haue grete ſhame vylanie ſelfe peryll ſowle therfore god wolde nat ſhold regne lenger iiij yere deyed lyeth wȳcheſtre kȳg edgar regned aboue kinges scotland ād wale ād begylled thurgh taking wyfe capitulo cxij thys kyng edwyne regned edgare brother man moch̄ loued god pee holy chyrch̄ alſo worthy lord bolde ſtronge mighty mayntened ryght well land pee thys kyng edgar lord kyng aboue kynges scotland walys tyme arthour gone neuer ſithē kyng hys power noble kīg edgar ſeȳt edwardes fadre whā edgares wyfe dede yt ſeint edwardes moder ētered herde ſpeke fairneſſe eſtrilde orga • u doughtir baron denē ſhire ſo faire woman men ſpekē therof called knyghtes yt moch̄ loued truſted vpon told hym go ſaid noble barō orgar denēſhire ſee hys doughter ſo fair men ſpeken ſothes haue hir wyfe knight yt called edelwold wēt forth waye came ladi whan ſaw hir ſo fayr thought haue hir ſelfe wyfe ther ſpake orgar hir fadre orgar olde man moo childrē onely hir ſaw edelwold faire yonge knight worthy ryche wel kȳg thought doughter ſhold wel maryed wel beſet vpon hȳ graūted hȳ doughter yf good lord kȳg wold ꝯſente ther edelwold came ayen̄ king told hȳ ſhe fair ynowe vpon ſee ſhe wō der lothly tho anſwered kīg ſaid toke littel charge syre ſaid edelwold tho hir fadres heir nat rych̄ landes ye wold conſente graūte muſt hir haue thā ſhold j rych̄ ynowe goddes name ſayd king cōſent ther edelwold thanked tho moch̄ king went ayen̄ denē ſhire ſpouſed ye damiſell contre dwelled thꝰ befel vpon tyme tolde counſeyll thing vnto wyfe howe maner begylled lord ye kīg wolde haue hir wyfe ād anone ſhe wiſt ſhe loued hȳ neuer afterward ſhe don̄ beforne lady conceyued ſone whan tyme child ſhold borne edelwold came king prayed haue ſone fouſton kīg hȳ graū ted let calle hym edgar aftir owne name whan don̄ thought yt ſure ynowe ye king ſhuld take wyfe aſmoch̄ lord ioly man amerous ¶how kyng edgar wedded fayre eſtrylde deth edelwold yt edelwold deyed capitulo centeſimo xiij thꝰ befell alle men kyng edgarys court tho ſpeken ſaiden thys knyght edelwold rychely auawnced thurgh mariage wyf yet thei ſaid avaūced hō derfeld ſpouſed fayreſt womā euer ſeyne kyng herde ſpeke ſomoch̄ hir beaute thought edelwold hȳ deceyued begylled thought preuely ī hert wold gone denēſhire hū te hert hynde ād othir wilde beſtes ſholde ſe lady er departed thēnes lady dwellȳg maner beſides foreſt king wold hunte ye maner herburwed al ye night whā tyme came king ſhold ſope axed goſſyp godſone edelwold made hyr come kȳg notheles myght haue bene ſhe ſholde haue comen hys ſighte wyll lady welcomed king ſwetely kiſſed toke hir hande tho next hȳ ſette ſo ſoped gedre tho cuſtome vſage thys land whan man dronke vnto othir punctel drynker ſhold ſey waſſaill othir ſhold anſwere drynkehaille thus dyd kȳg lady many tymes alſo kyſt ech̄ othir ſope whā tyme gone bedde kȳg wēte vnto bed hertely thȳkȳg vpō lady fairneſſe tho ouercomen hir loue thought ſhold deye wyll hyr vpon morne kyng aroos wēt foreſt diſporte hertes hyndes alle wilde beſtes hertes grete plente ladi ſent ofte wente ſolacen ſpeken ladj while dwelled ī cōtre ye kȳg remeved thēnes thought myght beſt delyuer edelwold wyfe hȳ fyrſt deceyued king anone viij dayes let ordeine parlament saleſbury hys baronage counceill haue ordeyne contree northūberland might beſt ben̄ kept danoys camen ther deſtroye land edelwold came alſo vnto kȳ ge parlamēt king ſent hī yorke keper cōtre thus befel men knewe hym ſlowe hȳ wey anone kyng herde dede let ſende lady eſtryld ſhe ſhold come cyte londō ben wedded kȳg grete ſolempnite worſhip held ſolempne feſt weryd crowne golde ād quene weryd alſo othir ſeint dunſton morwe came vnto king chambre fonde kyng bedde ād quene alſo ynfere ſeīt dunſton axed ſhe king anſwerde quene eſtrilde erchebiſſhop ſeint dunſtō ſaid grete wrong ayenſt goddes wylle take woman wyfe who child take fouſtoun̄ quene word neuer loued ſeynt dunſton notheles good man warned thaim foly lete warnȳg availled littell ye loue bitwene hem ſo moch̄ king begate vpon woman ſone kalled eldred tho chylde vi yere olde kyng hys fadre deyed ye time regned xvij yere lyeth glaſtenbury ſeynt edward martyr eſtrild hys stepmoder lete hym quelle make eldred hyr owne ſone kyng capitulo centeſimo xiiij edgard regned edward ſone begotē firſt wyfe wel nobely gouerned lande full alle maner goodneſſe lad full holy lyfe aboue alle thīg loued good holy chyrche quene eſtrild hys ſtepmoder let hym ſlee encheſō make hir owne ſone eldred king thus ſlayne afterward ye ſhull hit befell thꝰ daye kyng edward went wode playe ſouth contre beſides towne kalled warham which̄ foreſt grete plente hertes hȳdes ben̄ hym pleye thought vpon brother eldred whiche moder quene place nigh̄ foreſt thought gon̄ thydder viſite ād ſee brother toke hȳ lyttel meyne went hȳ tho toward ſtepmoders houſe ī time ſoiourned ye caſtel corfe ād rode thikkeneſſe wode aſpie hys game jt befell ſo went amys ād loſt meyne came laſt came owte wode then̄e loked aboute ſawe ther faſt beſides maner stepmoder dwelled ād thyddderward went allon̄ anon̄ told ye quene edward kyng comen allone wythoute companye therfor ſhe made yoye ynowe thought hys mynde ſhe might don̄ ſlain̄ preuely ſhe myght anone preuelich̄ ſhe called hir one knightes whō ſhe told moche hir coūſeill bitwen̄ hem camen ye kīg ād courtouſly hē receyued king told comen hir viſite alſo ſpeke wyt eldred brother quene many tymes thanked hȳ prayed wold abyde wyt hir night kyng ſaide myght ayene wolde wente vnto folke might hem fynde whan quene ſawe wold nat abyde ſhe praied hȳ wold one drinke graunted hir anon̄ drinke came quene dranke vnto kȳg kīg toke ye cuppe ſet mouth mene tyme while yt dranke knight wt quene knife ſmote euē king vnto herte fyll downe dede hys palfray vnto erthe quene dede yaf knight gold ſyluer grete plente othir richeſſe ynowe knight anon̄ thys don̄ wente hȳ ouer ſee ſo eſcaped oute land whan kyng edward thus martred hit ye yere jncarnacyō lord ieſu criſt ix clxxx yere regned xij yere halfe lyeth glaſtenbury king eldred ye kīg swyne denmarke helde englond eldred ſeint edwardes brother nat beloued reaulme therfore fledde normādie capitulo centeſiō xv king edward regned eldred brother ſeynt dunſton crouned hym king ſeynt dunſtō dyed ſone afterward foryeue quene hir treſpace eſtrild ēcheſō ſhe cauſe king edward deth ād ſeȳt dunſton hir aſſoyled ād penaunce hir enioyned ſhe • yued chaſte lyf clene kȳg eldred wedded engliſſh woman ād hir begate edmond irenſide ād othir ſone called edwyne deyed quene hir modre tyme came englād swyn king dē marke chalenge conquer hys aunceſtres tyme ſo conquered • ȳg good erle cutbert lyndeſ • peple northū berland ād mooſt grete lordes england helde wyth swyne kyng denmark moch̄ loued kȳg eldred encheſon hys good brother edward ſlayne falſely encheſon hȳ therfore man ſette littel wherfore kyng swyne wille toke alle land eldred king fledde tho normandie ſo ſpake duke rychard duke yaf ſuſter emma wyfe vpō whyche begate two ſones one called alured othir edward whā swyn conquered lād regned nobely lyued xv yere deyed lyeth yorke ¶how king eldred came ayene normādye knoght danoys regned werre bitwene edmond irē ſide capitu cxvi deth swyne yt danoys knoght ſone dwelled ī englōd wolde haue kȳg tho came ayen̄ eldred oute normandye moche peple wt ſtrō ge meyne knoght durſt abyde fley then dēmarke kȳg eldred ayen̄ reaulme helde ſo grete lordſhip began deſtroye thaī helpen swyn danoys ayenſt afterward came ayen̄ knoght frō dēmarke grete power ſo king eldred durſt wyth fight fledde fro then london punctel ther helde tho came knoght beſieged ſo long tyll king eldred deyed ye cyte london lyeth ſeȳt paulus regned ix iere kyng knoght cap cxvij deth thys eldred knoght danoys began tho regne· edmond jrenſide kīg eldredis ſone firſt wife ordeyned grete hooſt began werre vpon king knoght ſo dyd many tymes ofte werre ſo ſtronge ād ſo hard wōder wyte quene ēme dwelled tho weſtmynſtre grete drede hir two ſones ye werre alured edward leſt thei ſhold defoilled miſdone thurgh werre wher fore ſhe ſente hē ouer ſee normādye ye duke rychard hir vncle ther dwelled ſaufte pee longe time thys edmond jrenſide knoght werred ſtrōgely gedre laſt thei accorded maner thei ſhold depart reaulme bitwen̄ hē ſo dydē becamē good frendes ſo wel loued becamē ſworne bretherē ād ſo wel loued gedre bretheren geten body one modery borne king edmōd jrenſide traitourſly ſlayn̄ thurgh traitour called edrick ſtratton capit cxviij tho regned kȳg edmōd irenſide knoght danoys thꝰ befel afterward ſame yere accorded ād ſo moche loued gedre wherfor falſe thef traitour ēuye vnto loue bytwene hē frendſhip who name eldryk ſtraton· grete lord edmond jrēſides mā helde lāde notheles thought betraie lord ād make knoght king land intent richely ben̄ avaūced hȳ wel beloued wherfore prayed hys lord edmond jrenſide vpō day eten dwelle kȳg courtouſly graūted came hys prayer mete king ſerued ryally dyuerſe mete drinkes ād whā night came ſhold go bedde king toke owne meyne wente chābre loked aboute ſaw wōder fayr jmage wel made ſemblant archier wyth bowe bent hond bowe fyne arwe kȳg edmōd went tho nerre beholde better might ben̄ anon̄ arwe ſmote thurgh bodi ther king ſlowē engyn made quelle owne lord traitourſly whā king edmond thus dede ſlain̄ regned x yere peple made grete ſorwe bodi bere vnto glaſtēbury hȳ ētered fals traitour edrik anone went ye quene king edmondes wyfe ye wiſt hir lordes deth anone nōme hir hir two ſones fayre yonge hir lord vpon hir gote owne called edward edwyne lad hem bothe hȳ lōdō toke hem kyng knoght y• ſhold wyt hē wille tolde que •• tely quelled king edmond encheſon loue hȳ ſo kȳg knoght englond hys power holy might haue ¶o thow fals traitour haſt thou trew brother ſlayn̄ encheſon man moſt loued world mȳ hede ſhal thy trauaille rewarde well thow haſt deſerued anon̄ let hȳ take bȳd hō de foot maner traitour let caſt hī thamyſe maner falſe traitour ended lyfe kyng nomme ye two child toke hē abbot weſtmynſter warde kepe till wiſt beſt hem done kyng knoght ſent kyng edmondes ſones bothe denmarke flee ſaued capitulo cxix hit bebell ſone afterward kȳg knoght al lande hande ſpouſed quene emme thurgh conſent baronage ſhe fayre woman yt eldredis wyfe duke ſuſter normandie leued gedre moche loue reſon wolde king axed vpon day coū ſeyll quene beſt done wyt ſones edmōd irēſides syr ſaid ſhe right heires lād lyuen wyl doo moche ſorwe werre ād therfore let ſent hem ſtraunge land ferre ſomme man may hem defoille deſtroie kīg anone let calle danoys called walgar commaū ded ſhold lede ij child denmarke ſo ordeyn̄ hem neuer herde moo tydinges hem syr ſaid walgar gladly cōmaū dement ſhall done toke two child led hem den marke ād moch̄ ſaw two chyldren wonder faire alſo meke hē grete pyte routh wold hē ſlee led hē kyng hū gerj noryce walgar wel knowen kīg ād wel beloued▪ anone kyng axed whens chyldren walgare told ād ſaid right heires englōd ther men wold hem deſtroye therfore ſyr becomen mercy helpe ſeche ſoth mowe lyuen men ſhull becomen yow ſhull holde hir land kyng hungery hem vnderfenge mochel honour lete hē worthely kepte thus befell afterward edwyne yonge brother deyed edward elder drother liued fair man ſtronge large body gētyl curtoys ꝯdiciōs men hȳ loued thys edward cronycles called amonges engliſſhmen edward oute lawe made knight kinges doughter hungery ſo moche hȳ loued goodneſſe ād fairneſſe ſhe made called hym hyr derling kyng hir fadre perceyued wel loue bitwene hē two none heir doughter ād kyng vouched hys doughter man wel dyd hī ſhe loued hir yaf hir vnto hy • • ith good edward hir ſpouſed moch̄ honour king hongerye ſent baronage made ſolempne feſt ryche weddyng ād made men vnderſtonde ſhold king whā dede therfor maden grete ioye tidinge full glad thys edward begate vpon lady ſone yt called edgar belyng ād afterward doughtere called margarete aft er ward quene scotland king scotlād called mancholyn ſhe doughter called maude quene englond thurgh kȳg henry firſt ſone conquerour hir wedded ād begate hir doughtir yt called maude aft empreſſe almaigne maude came kȳg englōd vnto day kalled hē ry empreſſes ſone yet edward doughter bi wife kalled criſtian ſhe nonne kyng knoght proude man conquered norwey became afterward meke milde capitulo cxx haue ye herde edmondes ſones irē ſide kīg knoght wē de bene dede commaunded walgare punctel knoght hys hand englond denmarke went norwey lād conquere kyng lande called elaf came peple wende lande well haue kept defended ād ſo faught tyll laſt ſlayne bataille tho knoght nōme land hys hande whan cōquered norwey takē feautes ād homage ther came ayen̄ englōd helde ſelfe ſo grete lord hȳ thought world hys pere man became ſo proude hauten grete wonder ſo befel vpō day herd meſſe weſmynſtre wolde haue gone palays wawes ye thamyſe ſo ſwyftely ayēſt camē mooſt touched hys fette tho ſaid kȳg wt proude hert commaūde water turne ayen̄ elles ſhal make turne wawes commaundemēt wold ſpare flowed ouer hye ād kīg ſo proude hert wold flee water abode ſtille water bete water ſmale yerde helde honde commaunded water ſholde wēte ferther al commaundement water wolde ceſe euer wax hyghe ſo king vete ſtode ye water whan ſaw abyde ther lōg water wolde thing don̄ commaūdement tho ſone withdrowe hȳ tho ſtode vpon ſtone helde hondes high̄ ſaid wordes heryng peple god maketh ſee thꝰ aryſe hygh̄ king kinges mightes moſt caytyf man dedely may neuer deye· alle thing doth cō maūdement obediēt ye god praye warrant knowelech̄ caityf feble poer therfore wyll go rome wythoute lettyng wykkedneſſe punyſſhe amende god j clayme land hold non̄ othir anon̄ hardeknoght brother ī none othir maner might auenged thys kyng hardeknoght ſo large yeuer mete drīke table ſette euery day thre time full ryall mete drynkes hys owne meyne camen vnto court rychely nomā danoys though neuer ſo grete man amōges hē ſhold neuer king englond ye deſpite yt ye danoys don̄ engliſſhmē euer beforne hand ſo ye engliſſhmen danoys hapetē mete vpō brygge ye engliſſhmē ād counſeill ſenten vnto normādye ſeche two bretherē alured ād edward dwellȳg duke rychard eme • entēt crowne alured elder brother hym make kīg ēglōd thīg make ende erles baron made hir oth̄ goodneſſe kyng edward full mercy ād pyte ād thought wold go ayen̄ englōd ſeche haue grace hym might haue lād ayen pee arayed moch̄ myght put toward ſee ād came englōd lōdō kyng tyme alle lordes englond helde parlament godewyne ſent hem frendes ād mooſt gretteſt lordes land prayed hē ſech̄ kynges grace ād wold pee land graunte hys enemy ladden hȳ king ſeche grace anone king hȳ ſaw appelled treſon deth alured brother theſe wordes vnto hȳ ſaid traitour godwyne yt appelle thow haſt betraied ſlayn̄ brother alured certes ſir ſaid godwyne ſaue grace pee lordſhip j neuer hȳ betraied ne ſlew therfore put reward court fair lordes ſayd king ye bien liege erles baron land ben aſſembled full well ye haue herd mȳ appelle āſwere alſo godwyne therfore j wyll ye award right erles barōs tho drowē hem gedre done award bi hem ſelfe ād ſo thei ſpekē dyuerſely amonges hem ſomme ſaid neuer alience bi homage ſermēt ſeruyce ne lordſhyp bytwene godwyne alured whyche thing might drawe laſt deviſed demed ſhold put kynges mercj gedres tho ſpake erle leuerich couētre good man god ye world told reſō maner ſayd erle godewyne beſt frended man englōd king well might bene gain ſaid withoute coūceill godewyne alured neuer put deth wherfor award touching part hȳ ſelf ſone euery v xij erles ben̄ frendes wente king charged moche gold ſyluer mowe bere bytwene handes praye kīg foryeue euell erle godewyne ād receyue homage lād yelde ayen̄ alle accorded vnto award camē maner aboue ſaid euery hem gold ād ſyluer moche might bere bitwene hyr handes king ſaydē ye forme maner hyr accord hir award king wolde nat hem gayn ſaye moche ordeined graū ted confermed ſo erle godewyne accorded wyt king· ayene land afterward bere hȳ ſo wel ſo wiſely king loued wonder moch̄ wyth hȳ full pryue within littel tyme kȳg loued hȳ ſomoche ſpouſed edwyne hys doughter made hir quene notheles king wife lyued euer chaſtite clēneſſe body withouthe fleſſhli dede doȳg wyt wyfe ād q̄ne
