thys maner whā ſeynt edward dede mā falſely forſwore let croune hȳ kīg englōd falſely brak couenant made wt duke william wherfore duke wonder wroth ād ſwore wolde vpō ben̄ auēged euer might come therof anon̄ duk william let aſſēble grete hooſt came englōd auēge hȳ vpon harold conquere ye lād might ſame yere harold crouned harolde hareſtrēge kyng denmarke arryued ſcotlād thought haue ben̄ king englōd came tho englōd quelled robbed deſtroyed might tyll cam yorke ther quelled many mē armes· thouſand c preſtes whā tidȳge came king aſſembled ſtrōg power went fight wyt harold dēmarke wyt owne hōd hȳ quelled danoys diſcō fyted ād tho left lyue moch̄ ſorwe fleddē thēs hir ſhippes thus kȳg harold englōd quelled kyng harold dēmarke ¶how williā baſtard duke normādye came englōd quelled kȳg harold capitulo cxxxij whā bataill done harold became ſo proud wold thing ꝑt wt peple thyng goten held toward ſelf wherfore mooſt partie peple wroth frō hȳ departed ſo yt wt hȳ left mo ſoudyours vpon day ſate mete meſſagier came hȳ ād ſayd william baſtard duke normādye arryued englond grete hooſt taken al lād aboute haſtynge alſo myned caſtell whā kīg herd tydinge went thidder wyt lyttell peple wt haſt might littel peple wt left whan cam̄ thidder ordeyned mē yeue bataille duke william duk axed theſe iij thinges wold haue doughter wyfe made ſwore othe ād behight wold holde land hȳ truage· wold determine thīg thurgh bataill harold proude mā ſtoute ād truſtyd wonder moche vpon hys ſtrength̄ faught duke hys peple harold men diſcomfyted bataill ād ſelf ther ſlayne ād thys bataille ended tonbrigge ſeconde yere hys regne vpon ſeint calixtes day lyeth walthā kyng william baſtard gouerned well wyſely werre bitwene ād king fraūce ca cxxxiij whā william baſtard duke normandye cō quered land· vpon criſtmaſſe day tho next ſwynge let croune hī king weſtmȳ ſter worthy king yaf engliſſhmen largeli lōdes knightes afterward went ſtrife werre wyt duke william king williā ordeyned hȳ toward scotland men bothe bi land ſee deſtroye kyng mancolȳ accorded kȳg ſcotland became man helde lād kȳg william receyued homage came ayen̄ englōd whan king william king xvij yere maude quene deyed whō king william begoten many fair child ſeyne robert curthuſe willyam le rous rychard alſo whiche deyde hēry beauclerk ād maude alſo whiche ye erles wyfe boleynes othir foure doughteres wyfes deth began ther grete debate bytwen̄ hȳ kyng fraūce philippe laſt thei accorded tho dwelled kyng englōd lād normādye man werred alſo vpon man longe tyme king fraunce ſaid vpon day ſkorne kyng wylliam king wylliam longe tyme lyued chilhed longe time reſted hȳ thys worde came kyng englond ther lay normādye rouen ād word euyll payd ryght wroth toward kinge fraunce ſwore god whan aryſe gyſin wold lyghte thowſand candeles kȳg fraunce anone let aſſemble grete hooſt normandye alſo englyſſhmen ād begynnyng herueſt came fraūce brend townes ther came thurgh cōtre robbed ād dyd euell might thurghoute fraunce laſte brēde cyte mā dos· commaunded peple bere ſtrawe moche might brenne hȳ ſelf helpe therto might wyt good wylle grete hete fyre whiche ſo grete ād ye ſunne yt tho wonder hoot ſtuffed hȳ ſelfe became felle grete ſekeneſſe whan ſawe ſo ſtronge ſeke ordeyned aſſygned normā dye vnto robert curthous hys ſone englond william rous bequath henry beauclerk treſour tho thus done vnderfenge ſacramēts holy chyrche ād deyde xxij yere hys regne ād lyeth caan normandye ¶of kyng wylliam rous wylliā baſtardes ſone deſtroyed townes houſes religyon make newe foreſt capitulo cxxxiiij williā baſtard regned ſone wil • iam row william wōder contraryous man god holy chyrche ād let amende make towne cardeys paynyms deſtroyed thys king williā deſtroyed ye holy chirche poſceſſions part might hē fynde ther ſo grete debate bytwene hȳ erchebyſſhop canterbury ancelme encheſon vndernāme hym hys wykkedneſſe deſtroied holy chyrch̄ encheſon ther king wylliam bare grete wrath ād cauſe exylled hym owte lande erchebiſſhop tho wēt courte rome dwelled • ope kyng made newe foreſt caſt deſtroyed xxvi tounes ād lxxx houſes religyō make foreſt lenger bredder became wonder glad proude wode ād foreſt wilde beſtys yt therȳ mervaill wyt ſo men kalled hȳ keper wodes paſtures ād lēger lyued wikked became both̄ god holy chirche men king let make grete hall weſtmynſter ſo vpon day witſonday helde therin firſt feſte ād loked aboute ſaid halle littel haluendel laſt became ſo cōtrarious thing pleſed god diſpleſed hym alle thyng god loued hated dedely ād ſo befell dremed met vpō night lyttel er yt deyed let blode bled grete quantyte blode ſtreme blode lept hygh̄ toward heuen c vethemen clerneſſe day tourned derkeneſſe firmament alſo whan awoke grete drede ſo ne wiſt done tolde hys dreme meyny counſeill ād ſaid grete drede ſuppoſed hym ſome myſchaunce come ſeconde nyght monke dremed houſhold kyng went chyrch̄ moche peple ſo proude deſpiſed peple wyth ād toke ymage crucifixe ſhamefully bote wyt teth crucifixe mekely ſuffrid dyd kyng wode man rent armes crucifixe ād caſt vnder hys fete defowled threwe brode grete flamme fyre came crucifix mouth which̄ dreme many man grete mervaille ¶the good man dremed thys dreme told knyght tho mooſt pryue king alle men forſayde knyght kalled hamundes ſone ād tolde dreme kyng ſayd ſhold betoken thyng thā good neuertheles kȳg herd laughed ād ſette lyttel therof thought wold gone hūte pleye foreſt ād men hym counſeilled ſhold nat day ne maner thing come ye wode ſo bode home mete anon̄ eten mā myght hym lette nolde gone ye wode haue diſporte ſo befell one hys knightes whyche kalled walter tyrell wolde haue ſhot hert ād arwe glanced vpō braunce trough miſauenture ſmote king hert ſo fell downe dede ye grounde withoute worde ſpekȳg ſo ended lyfe ād grete wonder day deyde let ferme ye erchebiſſhop rich̄ canterburj xij abbeyes alſo ād euer dyd grete deſtructyon ye holy chirch̄ thurgh wrong full takyng axinges man durſt ſay yt wolde haue don̄ hys lytherneſſe wolde neuer withdrawe nothyr amēde lyfe therfore god wolde ſuffre lēger regne hys wykkedneſſe ben̄ king xiij yere vj wekes ād lyeth weſtmynſtre kȳg henry beauclerke williā rous brother debate bitwene ād robbert curthouſe brother capitulo centeſimo xxxv whā williā rous dede henri beauclerke brother made kīg encheſon williā rous child begoten body henry beauclerke crouned king london iiij daye hys brother dede ſaye v day auguſt anone ancelmꝰ erchebyſſhop canterbury court rome herd wylliam rous dede came ayen̄ englond kyng beauclerk welcomed mochel honour firſt yere king hē ri crouned ſpouſed maude margaretes doughter quene scotlād ye erchebyſſhop ancelme canterbury wedded hē kyng begate vpon wyfe ij ſones doughter ſaye williā richard maude ād maude empreſſe almaigne ſeconde yere regne hys brother robert curthouſe duke normandye came wyt hugh̄ meyne englond chalēge ye lāde thurgh coūſeill ye wyſe men lande accorded maner ye king ſholde yeue duke brother thouſand pounde euery yere which̄ hem lengeſt lyued ſholde ben̄ others heir ſo bitwen̄ hem ſhold debate ne ſtrife whan thus accorded duke went home ayen̄ normandie ye kȳg regned iiij yere ther arroos grete debate bitwene hym erchebiſſhop canterbury ancelme cauſe erchebiſſhop wolde graunte hī take taliage chirches hys wille therfore eftſones ye erchebiſſhop wēt ouer ſee court rome ther dwelled pope ſame yere duke normādie came englond ſpeke wt hys brother amonge othir thȳ ge duke normādye foryafe king hys brother forſaid thouſand poūde bi yere ſholde pay hī good loue duke wēt tho ayen̄ normādye whan ij yere gon̄ thurgh enticemēt deuell lyther men grete debate aroſe bitwen̄ kīg duke ſo kīg thurgh counſeyll went ouer ſee normādye whan kyng englōd comē normādye alle ye grete lordes normandye turned kyng englōd held • n ayens duke hyr owne lord hym forſoke ād kyng hem yelded ād alle good caſtelles ād tounes normādye ād ſone duke taken lad wyth kȳg englond ād king let put duke pryſon ād vēgeaūce god whē duke holy lād god yafe ſuche might honowr ther wherfore choſen ben̄ kȳg iheruſalem ād wolde nat forſoke ād therfor ſent hym ſhame deſpyte put ī hys brother pryſon tho ſeyſed king henry normandye hande ād helde hys lyfes tyme ſame yere came biſſhop auncelme court rome englōd ayen̄ kyng accorded yere next comyng ther began grete debate bytwene kyng philip fraūce kyng hēry englōd wher fore kyng hēry wēt normā dye werre ryght ſtronge bytwene hē two tho deyed kȳg fraūce ād lowys hys ſone made kyng anone faders deth ād tho wēt kyng hēry ayen̄ englōd punctel maried maude hys doughter hēry emperour almaigne debate bitwene kyng lowys fraunce kȳg henry englōd kȳg henryes two ſones loſt hygh ſee capitulo cxxxvj whenne kyng henry ben̄ kȳg xvij yere grete debate arroos bytwene kyng lowys fraunce ād kȳg henry englōd encheſon kyng ſent normādye hys mē ſholde ben̄ helpȳg ye erle bloyes mochel might werre ayēſt kyng fraūce· redy vnto wold ben vnto hyr owne lord ēcheſon erle ſpouſed hys ſuſtre dame maude whiche encheſon kȳg lowys kyng fraūce dyd moche ſorwe normādye wherfor kyng englond wonder wrothe grete haſte wēt ouer ſee wyt grete power came normādye defende land werre bytwene hem laſted two yere tyll laſt two foughten gedre ye kīg lowys diſcō fyted vneth ſcaped way wt moche peyne ād moſte part hys men taken kīg dyd wyth hem hem lyked ād ſomme hem let go freely ād ſomme let put deth afterward two kynges accorded whan kyng hēry holy lād normandye ſcōfyted hys enemyes fraunce turned ayen̄ englōd mochel honowr hys two ſones william ād rychard wolde come hyr fadre went ſee grete cō panye peple er thei might come lōde ſhip come ayēs roche brake pecys drownyd theryn ſauf man ye ſame ſhippe which̄ eſkaped ſeȳt katerynes daye thees ye name hem drownyd ſaye wylliam kynges ſone rychard hys brother erle cheſtre octonell hys brother geiffrey rydell walter emucry godfrey erchedeken kynges doughter counteſſe perſes kynges nece counteſſe cheſtre ād many whan kyng henry ād othir lordes arryued englond herde thiſe tydynges made ſorwe ynowe hyr myrthe ioye turned mornȳg ſorwe maude empreſſe came ayen̄ englond ād ſhe wedded geyffroy erle angeoy capitulo cxxxvij whan two yere gone erle dwelled kīg erle went tho kȳg began werre vpon hym dyd moche harme land normandye punctel toke wyt ſtrength̄ ſtrōge caſtell ther dwelled yere tho came hym tydyng henry emperour almaigne yt whiche ſpouſed maude doughter dede ſhe dwelled lēger almaigne ye ſhe wolde come ayene normandye hir fadre whan ſhe come hȳ nōme hyr tho came ayen̄ englond· made engliſſhmē make othe feaute vnto empreſſe ād fyrſt man made othe william erchebiſſhop canterbury othir king dauid scotland hym erles barōs englōd alſo noble mā ye erle angoy worthy knight ſent king englond wolde graunte hym haue doughter ſpouſe maude empereſſe encheſon hir fadre wiſt noble man kȳg graunted hȳ conſented therto tho toke doughter ladde hyr normandye ād came noble knight erle gaufryde ād ſpouſed forſaid maude mochel honour erle begate vpon hyr ſone called henry empreſſes ſone whan don̄ king henry dwelled yere normandye ād lō ge time grevons ſekeneſſe toke wher thurgh deyed kyng henry regned xxxv yere iiij monthes ād deyed ſaid normandye ād hert entered grete chyrche owr lady rouen ād body brought mochel honour englond entered redȳg abbey which̄ abbey begynner foundour stephane kynge henry ſuſtres ſone made kyng england capitulo cxxxviij kȳg henry firſt made king nepheu ſuſtres ſone stephē erle boloigne anone herde tidȳg vncles deth paſſed ſee ād came englond thurgh coū ſeyll ād ſtrength̄ helpe many grete lordes englond ayēs hyr othe made maude empreſſe tokē reaulme let crowne ſtephen kyng land ād erchebyſſhop william canterburj firſt made ye oth feaute vnto maude ēpreſſe ſet croune vpō king ſtephenes hede hȳ anoynted biſſhoppe rogier salyſbury mayntened kynges partye moch̄ myght firſt yere king ſtephē began regne aſſembled grete hooſt went hȳ toward ſcotland haue werre vpō ye king ſcotlād came ayēs pee good maner ād truſtyd made hī none homage moch̄ made homage vnto empereſſe maude iiij yere regne maude empreſſe came englōd tho began debate bitwene kȳg stephen maude empreſſe maude wente vnto cyte nichol king hir beſieged longe tyme might ſpede ſo well cyte kepte defended ād ye cyte queyntely eſcaped away withoute maner harme· ād tho toke king cyte dwelled theryn tyll candellmeſſe tho came barōs helde wt empreſſe ſaye erle randulfe cheſtre erle robert glouceſtre hugh̄ bygot robert morley brought hem ſtronge power faughtē king yafe grete bataill which̄ bataille kyng stephen taken ſette priſon caſtel briſtowe maude empereſſe went fro wyncheſtre vnto oxē ford ād ſhe eſcaped wallynford ſorwe diſeſe ſhe capitulo cxxxix whēne kyng takē brought warde caſtell briſtowe maude empreſſe anon̄ made lady englond alle men helde hyr lady lande kent helde wt king stephenes wyfe ād alſo william pree ād reteune helpe hem helde werre ayēſt maude empreſſe anon̄ king scotland came hem hugh̄ nombre peple tho went ynfere vnto wyncheſtre empreſſe punctel ād wolde haue taken hir erle glouceſtre came power ād foughte hem empereſſe mene bataille dured eſcaped fro then ād wente vnto oxenford ſhe helde hir ī ſame bataille erle glowceſtre diſcomfyted taken wyt hȳ alſo many grete lordes delyuerance ſo king stephen delyuered oute pryſon whan delyuered oute pryſon went thēs oxenford beſieged empreſſe which̄ tho oxēford ſiege endured fro mychelmaſſe vnto ſeynt andrewes ryde empreſſe let tho cloth hir white lynnen cloth encheſon ſhe wold nat knowē ſame tyme moche ſnowe ſo ſhe eſcaped thamyſe hem away hyr ennemyes fro thēs ſhe went wallīgford ther ſhe helde hir ād king wold haue beſieged hir punctel ſo moche don̄ erle randolfe cheſtre hugh bigot ſtrongely werred vpon euery place ne wiſt whyther turne erle glowceſtre halpe hem power gaufryde erle angeoy yafe vp vnto henry ye empreſſes ſone normandye capitulo cxl kȳg wēt vnto wylton wolde haue made caſtel tho cam̄ hī ye erle glouceſtre ſtronge power ād almoſt takē king ye kīg eſcaped moch̄ peyne william martel take who delyuerāce yafe vnto erle glouceſtre ye good caſtell ſhirborne take whan don̄ erle robert kinges enemyes wente faringdone ād begonne ther make ſtronge caſtell king came thidder ſtronge power drofe hem thēs ſame yere erle randolfe cheſtre accorded wyt king came court commaūdemēt erle wende ſaufely come kȳg anone let take put priſon muſt neuer thīg come oute till yelde vnto king ye caſtell nychol whyche toke king ſtrēgth̄ xv yere regne gaufryde erle angeoy yafe vp vnto henry ſone normandye ād yere next ſued deyde erle gaufryde ād henrj ſone tho anon̄ turned ayen̄ angeoy ād made erle mochel honour men land hȳ diden feaute homage moſt partie land tho hēry empreſſes ſone erle angoye duke normā die ſame yere made diuorce bitwene ye king fraū ce quene wyfe yt right heir gaſcoygne ēcheſon knowē proued ſybbe nyghe blode tho ſpouſed hir henri empreſſes ſone angeoy ād duk normandye duke gaſcoygn̄ xviij yere thys king stephen hēry came englond ſtronge power holde helpe ayēſt henry empreſſes ſone iiij yere regne put vnto owne lordſhip ye kīg walys ſame yere whan kyng scotland owne hōde ſeyn cyte carlylle caſtell banburgh punctel newe caſtell vpō tyne hys fadre normandye capitulo cxlij ye coronacyon kīg henry ſone king hēry empreſſes ſone went ouer normādie punctel ād let marye eleniore doughter dolphyne king almaigne ye vij yere erchebiſſhop ſeint thomas ben̄ outelawed kyng fraunce made kyng ſeynt thomas accorded tho came thomas erchebiſſhop canterbury ayene hys owne chyrch̄ accorde made begynnyng aduent ād afterward quelled martred v day criſtmaſſe tho next came kyng henry thought vpon ſeynt thomas erchebiſſhop vpō criſtmaſſe day ſate mete punctel ſaid thiſe wordes good knight hȳ many day paſſed auenged vpon ye erchebiſſhop thomas anon̄ syr williā bretō syr hugh̄ morvile syr williā cracy ād ſir reynout fitz vrſe beres ſone ī ēgliſſh preuely went vnto ſee camē englond chyrch̄ cā terbury ther martred ſeȳt benettes greteſt lordes englond ariſen ayenſt king henry fadre laſt god wold cōquered enemy kȳg fraūce accorded ād tho ſent henry fadre ſpecialy vnto king fraūce praied hym hertely hys loue wold ſend hȳ bi lettres name hē begonnē werre vpō kȳg fraū ce ſent ayen̄ bi letter name hem begōnen werre firſt iohan hys ſone rychard brother henry ſone newe kyng· tho hēry kyng wonder wroth curſed time euer hē begate werre dured hēry ſone deyed ſore repētȳg miſdede moſt ſorwe made onj man cauſe ſeȳt thomas deth canterbury praied fadre moche ſorwe hert mercy hys treſpas fadre foryafe ād grete pyte deyed xxxvi yere regne· lyeth redyng criſten loſt holy lād forſaid kȳges time thurgh fals criſten man became ſarazene cap cxliij while kȳg hēry empreſſes ſone lyued regned grete bataill holy lād bytwene cryſtē men ſarazenes ye cryſtē mē ther quelled thurgh grete treſon erle tyrp • wolde haue wife quene iheruſalem ſome tyme baldewines wife ſhe forſoke toke hyr lord knight worthi man kalled ſir emꝑches wherfore erle tyrpe wroth wēt anone right ye soladyne ſoudan babiloigne became ſarazene man▪ ād forſoke criſtendomme criſten lawe criſtē men wiſt nat dedes wende haue grete helpe hȳ wonet haue whan camē bataille fals criſtē man turned vnto ye ſaraſēs forſoke owne naciōs ſo ye criſten men ther quelled ſarazens thus cryſten men ſlayne ād put horrible deth cite iheruſalem deſtroyed holy croſſe borne way· kȳg fraunce let hē croſſe go holy land amōges hem wente rychard king henry ſone king fraū ce toke croſſe erche biſſhop tour toke nat vyage time encheſon let othyr maner wayes nedes done ād whan kyng henry fadre regned xxxv yere v monthes iiij dayes deyed lyeth foū tenerard kyng rychard conquered holy lande criſten men loſt capitulo cxliiij king henry regned rychard ſone ſtrōge man worthy alſo bolde crouned weſtmynſter ye erchebiſſhop baldewyne caunterbury iiij day septēbre ſecōde yere regne kȳg rychard ſelfe baldewyne erchebiſſhop canterbury hubert biſſhop saliſbury randulphe erle glouceſtre othyr many lordes englond went holy land vyage deyde erchebiſſhop canterbury king rychard wente forth reſted nat till came way vnto cipers toke cypre wyth grete force ſythen kyng rychard wēte forth toward holy land gate moch̄ criſtē men hadden loſt conquered ye lād ayen̄ thurgh grete might ſauf onely holy croſſe whā kīg richard came toune acre gete cite grete debate aroſe bitwene ye king fraunce ſo ye kȳg fraū ce went ayen̄ fraūce wroth toward king rychard er king richard went ayen̄ toke ye cyte acre whā taken dwelled cyte whyle came tidynges ye erle johan oxūford brother wolde haue ſeiſed englōd normandye alſo wolde croune king ye lād whan king rychard herde thys tiding wēt ayen̄ toward englōd ſpede might duke oſtriche met toke brought emperour almaign̄ emperour brought pryſon afterward deliured hugh̄ raū ſon̄ ſaye hounderd thouſand poūd which̄ raunſone payed eche othir chaliſe englond molte ād made money alle mō kes ordre ciſteaulx yauē hir bokes don̄ hem ſelle laſt pope ſēt auctoryte enioȳ ed biſſhoppes englond kyng wolde vnderfonge pryour caū terbury ād hys mōkes ſhold don̄ generall enterdytynge thurgh land englond graūted full power fowre biſſhoppes pronounce enterdytȳg nede firſt biſſhop wylliam londō othir biſſhop euſtace ely thridde biſſhop walter wyncheſtre ād iiij biſſhop giles herford theſe fowre byſſhoppes prayed ye kyng knelȳg hir knee ād ſore wepyng wolde done pope commaūdemāt ſhewed hym billes enterdytȳg prayer thei might praye wolde conſente therto whā theſe fowre biſſhoppes ſawe wēt kȳg moch̄ ſorowe ye morne ānuncyacion owr lady pronoūced generall enterdytyng thurgh owte englōd ſo chyrch̄ dores ſhit key ād othir faſtenȳg ād walles ād whan enterdytyng pronoūced kyng began wex oute meſure ād nō vnto honde poſceſſions fowre biſſhoppes ād clergye thurgh oute lande ād ordeyned mē kepe ye clerkis myght haue hir lyuing wherfore biſſhoppes curſed hem put ſhold medle holy chyrche goodes ayens wyll hē hem owed whā kīg wolde nat ceſe malyce maner thyng foure biſſhoppes fore ſaid went ouer ſee wēt biſſhop caūterburj told hym alle thȳg ecchebiſſhop hem ſaid ſhold gon̄ ayen̄ caūterbury wold come thidder hem elles wold ſent thydder certaȳ perſones hys ſtede ſhold done moche ſelf whā ye biſſhoppes herde turned ayen̄ englōd camē vnto cāterbury tydȳge came ye kȳg biſſhoppes comē ayen̄ caū terbury hȳ ſelfe myght nat comē thidder ye tyme ſent thidder biſſhoppes erles abbotes trete wyt hē kȳg ſhold vnderfōge erchebiſſhop stephē ye pryour ye mōkes caūterbury ſhold neuer ye time thȳg take ye holy chyrch̄ ayēs ye hē owed ye goodes ye kīg ſhold make full amēdes hē whō goodes takē ye holi chirch̄ ſhold haue fraūchiſes ferforth ſeīt edwardes tyme cōfeſſour stephen langeton came englond thurgh pope cōmaūdement went agayn cap cxlviij whā fourme accord thꝰ ordeyned apair endētures ād put ſeales vnto one part camē kȳ ge name put ſeales othir part endētures iiij biſhoppes aboue ſaid toke part endētures hem othir part endentures thei bare hem ſhewe king whan king ſawe fourme vnderſtōde held full wel paied maner thing ordeyned ſauȳg touchȳg reſtitucyō ye goodes make ayene thyng wolde nat accorde ſo ſent word axē ye iiij biſſhoppes thei ſhold don̄ owte ād put away one point reſtitucion āſwered yt nold don̄ ony word owt tho ſent king erbiſhop bi iiij biſſhoppes ſhold come canterbury ſpeke hȳ ſent vnto hȳ ſaufcōduyt vnder plegges ſeyne juſtices gillebert peyntewyne willyam de la brener iohā lefirz hugh̄ hir cōduyt ſaufely ſhold come gone ayen̄ maner erchebiſſhopp stephen came canterbury whan erchebiſſhop comen king came chilham ād wolde come nerrer cāterburj time ſent treſorer ye biſſhop wȳcheſtre ſholde done owt endētures clauſe reſtituciō make ye goodes erchebiſſhop made oth wold neuer don̄ anj word therof ne chaū ge biſſhoppes ſpoken ordeined tho went erchebiſſhop ayene rome withoute doyng kȳg iohan tho wrother euer let make cō mune crie thurghoute englōd holy chyrch̄ rente ād went ouer ſee thei ſhold come ayen̄ englōd certaȳ day elles thei ſhold leſe hyr rente euermore cōmaunded eueri ſhirrefe thurgh oute englād· thei ſhold enquyre biſſhop abbot pryour p̄lats holy chyrch fro day afterward receyued maundemēt come fro pope ſhold take body brȳge thei ſhold take kinges hōde hir landes holy chyrch̄ whiche yeuen man bi erchebiſſhop stephen bi priour caunterbury tyme electyon erchebyſſhop punctel commaūded wodes ye erchebiſſhoppes ſhold caſt downe vnto ye grounde ſolde king iohan deſtroyed ordre ciſteaux capi cxlix ſame tyme iryſſhmē begōne werre vpon kyng iohan king johā ordeyned hȳ wē te irlād hugh̄ taxe thurgh oute englōd ſay xxxvm mark ſent thurgh englōd monkes ordre ciſteaux ſhold helpe vi marck ſyluer anſwered ād ſaid durſt nothing wythoute hyr abbot ciſteaux wherfore kyng johan came irland dyd hem ſo moch̄ ſorwe care thei nyſt abyde toke ſo moch̄ raūſone euerj houſe hem ſomme mounted ix mccc mark ſo clene loſt deſtroyed· voided hir houſes ād hir landes thurgh oute englond abbot wauerley drad ſo moch̄ menace forſoke alle abbey went thēs preuely ordeyned hȳ ouer ſee hous ciſteaux whā tyding came pope king don̄ ſo moch̄ malice tho king ward ful wroth ſent two legatz vnto king owne caled pandolfe othir durāt thei ſhold warne kīg pope name ſhold ceſe perſecuciō dyd vnto holy chyrch̄ amende wrōge treſpaſſe done erchebiſſhop canterbury ād pryour vnto monkes canterbury clergye englōd ſhold reſtore goodes ayen̄ takē hem ayens hir elles thei ſhold kurſe kȳg bi name thyng conferme pope toke hē lrēs billis patentz ¶theſe two legatz camen englōd wentē kyng northamptō ther helde parlamēt ād full curtouſly hym ſalued ſaiden syr ben come fro pope rome pee holy chyrch̄ punctel ye land amend amoneſte yow firſt ye popis halfe ye make ful reſtituciō goodes ye haue rauiſſhed holy chyrche land ye vnderfenge ſtephen erchebiſſhop cāterbury dignite▪ pryour canterbury monkes ye yelde ayen̄ vnto erchebiſſhop hys landes rente withoute holdȳg yet ouer ye ſuch̄ reſtituciō make holy chirch̄ ſhall holde hir paī ed tho āſwered king touchyng pryour mōkes cāterbury ye haue ſayd wil gladly thȳg ye wyll ordeine touchȳg erchebiſſhop ſhall telle yow myn hert hit lithe erchebiſſhop leve biſſhoprich̄ pope thā hī wol pray vpon auenture ſholde lyke ſome othir biſſhoprye yeue englōd vpō cō dicyon wol hym receyue vnderfōge notheles englōd erchebyſſhop yf abyde ſhal neuer haue ſo good ſaufconduyt ſhall taken tho ſaid pandolfe vnto king holy chirche neuer wonet diſcharge erchebiſſhop withoute cauſe reſonable euer ſhe wonet chaſtiſe prȳces yt god holy chirch̄ inobediant quod ye king manace ye nay ſayde pandolf ye opēly haue tolde ſtandeth herte yow telle pope wille thus ſtand yt hath holy interdited accurſed wrōges ye haue done holy chirch̄ ād ye clergye ād aſmoch̄ ye dwelle beth wille abyde malyce ād wille come none amādement ye ſhall vnderſtonde fro time afterward ſentence vpon yow yeuē holdeth ſtede ſtrength̄ vpō thaȳ yow haue cōmuned time whethir thei ben̄ erles baron knightes othir ſo euer ben̄ hem aſſoille ſaufly vnto thys day fro time afterward cōdicion euer hem accurſe wyt yow comen· ſo ſentēce vpon hē openly ſpecialy aſſoill quytly erles baron knightes othir maner men hir ſeruices homage feautes thei ſhold vnto yow don̄ tidinge cōferme yeue pleyne power biſſhop wyncheſtre biſſhop northewhiche ſame power yeue scotland biſſhoppes roucheſtre saliſbury ād wailis yeue ye ſame power biſſhoppes ſeint dauid landalf ſeint aſſe ouer ſende thurgh cryſtendome biſſhoppes beyonde ſee thei ſhal done accurſe alle thaȳ helpeth yow coūceill yeueth yow maner nede ye haue don̄ partie world aſſoille hem aſo ye auctoryte pope cōmaū de hē alſo yow werre hȳ enemye holy chirch̄ tho āſwerde kīg mowe ye done tho anſwered pandolfe ſeyne yow verbo dei ye ne none heire ye haue neuer daye may crowned tho ſaid king bi almighty god j wiſt thȳg er ye came mi lād ye brought ſuche tiding ſhold haue made yow ryde holy yere tho āſwerde pandolfe full well wende firſt comȳg ye wold haue ben̄ obedyent god holy chirch haue fulfilled pope commaūdement haue ſhewed pronoūced ye pope wille charged therwyth ye haue ſaid ye wiſt ye cauſe comyng ye wolde haue made v ryde holy yere punctel ād well ye might haue ſayd ye wold haue take holy yere reſpyte bi pope leue ſuffre deth ye cowde ordeyne ſhul nat ſpare telle yow holy pope meſſage wille charged pādolfe delyuered clerk falſed coūterfeted kȳges money kȳg ſelfe capi cl anone tho commaū ded kȳg ſherews bailifs northāpton ye kinges p̄ſence thei ſhold bringe forth ye priſō ners might ben̄ don̄ vnto deth pādolf encheſon king wende wold haue gayne ſayd hir dedes cauſe deth thynge ſpoken afore whā priſōners comē kȳg kyng cōmaūded ſome hanged ſome ben̄ drawe ād ſome drawe hir eyen oute hir hede amōge clerk falſed kinges money king cōmaū ded ſhold hāged whē pādolfe herde cōmaūdemēt king ſtert hȳ vp ſmertly anon̄ axed boke cādell ād wold haue curſed alle hē ſet vpō clerk ony hōde pādolfe hī ſelf went ſeche croſſe kȳg folowed delyuered clerk hōde ſhold don̄ wyt hȳ euer wold thꝰ clerk delyuered went thēs pādolf felawe durant wēt fro ye kȳg iohan came ayen̄ pope rome told hȳ kȳg johā wolde nat amēde euer abide ſo accurſed notheles ye pope graūted ye yere thurgh oute ēglōd mē might ſing maſſes couenable chirches make goddes body yeue ſike mē paſſe ſhold oute world alſo men myght chriſtē child ouer whā pope wiſt ſawe kyng wolde nat bē vnder ye rule gouernaūce holy chyrche maner thing pope ſēt king fraū ce remiſſyō ſynnes ſholde take wyth hym alle power might wente englond deſtroye kyng iohan whan tyding came kȳg iohā tho ſore annoyed ſore drad leſt ſho • de leſe reaulme ſelf don̄ deth tho ſent ye pope meſſagiers ſaid wold ben̄ iuſtifyed come maundemēt thīges wolde mak ſatiſfactyon maner men pope ordenaūce tho ſēt pope ayen̄ englond pā dolf othir meſſagiers camen canterbury ther king abode xiij day may kȳg made oth ſtand ye pope ordenance pādolf legat ī maner thīges which̄ accuſed ſhold make full reſtitucion alle men holy chyrch̄ religyon goodes takē hem ayens hir ād alle ye grete lordes englōd ſwore vpō boke ād holydome yf king wolde nat holde oth ſaydē wolde make holde ſtrēgth̄ tho put kȳg court rome pope· tho yaf vp reaulme englond irlād alſo hys heires euermore ſhold come ſo king iohan heires ſholde take two reaulmes pope hand· ſhold holde tho two royaumes ye pope ferme payng euery yere vnto ye court rome thouſād mark ſiluer tho toke kȳg crowne hede ād ſet knee thes wordes ſayd herȳg grete lordes englond reſegne vp crowne reaulme englōd pope hond innocēt iij put holy mercy ordenaūce tho vnderfē ge pandolfe croune kyng iohan ād kept v dayes ſeyſin takȳg two reaulmes englond irland confermed maner thynges bi chartre foloweth letter obligatorie kīg iohan made vn court rome wherfor petres pēs bene gadred thurgh oute alle englād ca cli cryſtē peple thurgh oute worlde dwellyng iohan grate god kyng englond gretȳg vniuerſite knowyng aſmoche haue greued ād offended god owr moder chyrch̄ rome aſmoche haue nede merci lord iheſu chriſt may nothyng ſo worthy offre competant ſatiſfactyon make god holy chirch̄ owne body reaulmes englōd irland grace god deſyre mek v loue hī meked hȳ deth croſſe thurgh counſeil noble erles baron offren freely graunte god apoſtles ſeynt petre ſeint paule modre chirch̄ rome ād owr holy fadre pope jnnocent thridde pope cometh hym reaulme patronage chyrches englond irland hir appertenaūces remiſſyon ſynnes helpe helthe kyn ſowles ād criſten ſowles ſo tyme afterward woll receyue holde modre chyrche rome fee ferme doyng feaulte holy fadre pope innocent thridde pope comen hī maner aboue ſaid preſence ye wyſe mā pandolfe pope ſubdekene maken liege homage ī pope preſence hym ſhull don̄ maner thȳ ge aboue ſaid therto bȳ den v alle comen v heires euermore withoute gayne ſeyeng pope ād eke ward chyrches vacaunt tokē thȳ ge euer laſt wyll ꝯferme ordeyne ſpecialle rētes forſaid reaulme ſauȳg ſeīt petres pen thing ye moder chyrche rome payeng yere thouſand mark syluer ij termes ye yere maner cuſtomes ſhold done forſaid reaulmes ſeyne mychalmaſſe eſtren ſeyn̄ vij c marc englōd ccc mark irland ſauyng v heyres iuſtices ād othir fraū chiſes othir realtes apperteygneth crowne theſe thȳges ben̄ ſaid wylle ferme ſtable withouten ende oblygacyō ſucceſſours ād heires ī maner bē boūd owre heyres thurgh preſumpcyō falle point ayēſt theſe thȳ ge aboue ſaid warned wull nat amende ſhal leſe forſayd reaulme euermore thys chartre oblygacyō owr warrant euermore ferme ſtable withoute gayn ſayeng ſhull fro daye afterward trewe god moder chyrche rome pope innocēt thridde alle thaȳ cometh hym ād reaulmes englōd ād irland ſhull maynten̄ trewly maner point ayēs maner mē bi owr power thurgh goddes helpe clerkes outelawed owt englōd came ayen̄ kȳg iohā aſſoilled capitulo clij whāne thys chartre made enſealed kȳg vnderfēge ayen̄ croune pandolfes hande ād ſent anon̄ vnto erchebiſſhop stephen hys othir clerkys lewd men exilled oute land ſholde come ayen̄ englōd ād haue ayen̄ hir landes hir rente wold make reſtitucyon goodes taken hem ayens hir king ſelfe tho pādolfe erles baron went tho vnto wȳceſtre ayēs erchebiſſhop stephē whā come kyng went ayēs hym fell downe hys fete ſayd fair ſire ye wellcome crye yow mercy encheſon haue treſpaſſed ayens erchebiſſhop toke hȳ vp tho armes kyſſed hȳ courtouſly oftetymes lad dore ſeynt swytynes chyrch̄ hōde aſſoilled hym ſentēce hym reconceilled god ād holy chyrche ād ſeȳt margaretes day erchebilſhop anon̄ wēt ſing maſſe punctel king offred maſſe mark gold whā maſſe done went vnderfonge alle hir lādes withoute maner gayne ſayeng daye made myrthe ioye ynowe yet ēterdytyng releſed encheſon ye pope ſet ēterditȳg ſhold ben̄ vndoune tyll kyng made full reſtitucyon goodes take ye holi chyrch̄ alſo hym ſelf ſhold done homage ye pope certayne legat ſhold ſende englōd tho toke pādolfe leue king biſſhop went ayen̄ rome londō tour hī yolde ſame time pope ſēt englōd legat called swalo king iohā ne deth capit clv ſame tyme •• pe ſent englōd legat yt kalled swalo preſt cardynall rome maynten̄ kȳg iohā ne cauſe ayens ye barōs englond barōs hath ſo huge part helpe thurgh lowys ye kinges ſone fraūce kȳg iohan wiſt nat whydder turne gone ſo fell wolde haue gon̄ nycholl went thidderward cam̄ abbey ſwyneſhede▪ abode twoo dayes ſat ye mete • axed mōk howſe moche lofe worth ſete hym vpon table mōke ſaid lofe worth halpeny ſayd tho king grete chepe brede nowe quod kyng may lyue ſuc • lofe ſhalbe worthy c ſhillyng halfe yere gon̄ whan ſaid word moch̄ thought ofte ſyghed toke ete brede ſaid god worde haue ſpoken ſhall bene ſoth monke ſtode ye kyng thys worde full ſory hert thought rather wolde hȳ ſelfe ſuffre pitouſe deth • rather ordeyne therfore ſome maner remedie • anone monke went abbot ſhryuē hym tolde abbot kȳg hath ſayd prayed abbot aſſoille hȳ wolde yeue kīg ſuch̄ vaſſaille englōd ſhold glad therof ioyeful tho wēt monke gardeyne fonde grete tode theryn toke hir vp put hir cuppe ād prykked tode thurgh wyth broche many tymes tyll venime came oute euery ſides ye cuppe tho toke ye cuppe fylled wyth good alle brought kyng knelyng ſayd syr quod vaſſaille nevyr dayes youre lyfe ne dronke ye ſuch̄ cuppe begȳ ne monke quod kȳg monke drāke grete draught ād toke kȳg cuppe kȳg alſo dranke grete draught ſette downe cuppe mō ke anone ryght went ye fermorie ther deyed forthwyth̄ who ſowle god haue mercy am̄ v mōkes ſing ſowle ſpecyaly ſhulen whyles abbey ſtād kȳg aros vp anone full euyll eaſe cōmaunded remeue table axed aftyr monke men told hȳ dede wōbe broken ſunder kȳg herde thys commaūded truſſe nought bely begā ſo ſwelle drȳ ke yt drāke deyed iohā whā regned xvij yere v monthes v day deide caſtell newerke ād hys body buryed wȳcheſtre ¶of kyng henry thrydde crownyd glouceſtre capitulo c lvi aftyr thys king iohā regned henry ſone ſone anone legate enterdited walys encheſō helde wt baron englōd alſo thaȳ holpē yafe coūceill meue werre ayens newe kȳg hē ry kurſyd hem begynnyng put ſentēce kī ge ſone fraūce lowys notheles ſame lowys wolde nat ſpare werre wēt anone toke caſtel berkāſted caſtell herford frō day aftyrward baron dyd ſo moche harme thurghoute englōd principaly frēſhmen comen wyt king lowys wherfore grete lordes common peple englōd let hē croice dryue lowys hys cō panye oute englōd ſomme baron alſo frēſh men gone vnto ye cite nychole token cyte ād helde kȳg lowys profyt thydder came king henryes men wyt grete power ſeye erle randolfe cheſtre williā erle marchall williā brener erle feriers many lordes hem yafen bataill vnto lowys men ād ſlayne ye erle perch ād lowys men foulle diſcōfyted taken serle erle wȳcheſtre hūfrey de bowne erle herford ād robert ſone walter many begonne werre ayens ye kīg taken ād lad vnto kīg hēry king iohānes ſone wha tydyng ſcōfiture came vnto lowys kynges ſone fraūce removed then wēt vnto london let ſhit yates faſt cyte anone aftyr kȳg ſent burgeis lō ſhold yelde hē vnto cite alſo wolde hem graūte fraūchiſes euer wont haue wolde conferme hem hys grete newe chartre vndyr grete ſeall ſame time grete lord which̄ called euſtace monke came oute fraūce grete companye lordes wolde haue comen englond haue holpē lowys kinges ſone fraū ce hubert borugh ād v porte wt viij ſhippes tho mette hem hygh̄ ſee ād aſſaylled hem egrely ād ouercame hem ſtrengthe ſmoten euſtache monkes heed ād tokē alſo x grete lordes fraū ce put hem pryſon quelled almoſt men camē hem ād anone drenched ſhippes ſee ¶how lowys turned ayen̄ fraūce cōfirmacyō kyng iohannes chartre capitulo clvij lowys herde thys tydyng drad ſore dede loſte let ordeyne ſpeke bitwen̄ kyng lowys legat swalo thurgh erchebyſſhop cā terbury thurgh othyr grete lordes pryſonners one halfe othir ſhold delyuered ād gon̄ quyte lowys hīſelfe hī mochel honour ſame tyme gyllebert clarēce erle glouceſtre ye ward alſo forſayd simond thurgh cōmaundement kyng henri wente grete hert encheſon ſaid gyllebert foole coūceill wherfore ordeined hȳ ſo held hym kȳg henrj ſaterdaye next myddes auguſt ſyr edward kynges ſone diſcomfyted ſir symond demoūfort kenilword ye grete lordes takē ſeye baldewyn̄ wake william mounchenſie ād many othir caſtell vnto kīg maner ſelf alle othir within caſtell ſhold haue hir lyfe ād lymme aſmoche thyng theryn hors harnays iiij dayes reſpyte delyuer clenly caſtell hem ſelfe maner thīg within caſtell▪ lewelyne ād ſaid wold ſende h̄is doughtyr ſo ſent aymer brother aftyr damyſell lewelȳ arrayed ſhippes doughtyr ſir aymer ād thayre companye ſhold goo hyr ¶and lewelȳ dyd grete wrōge couenaūt aſſent baronage eſtre next ſewȳge kȳg ſent bi letter lewelȳ prynce walys ſhold come parlement lande holdyng walles ſtrength̄ letter obligatorye witneſſed tho lewelyn ſcorne deſpite kynges cō maundement pure wrath begā ayene werre vpō kȳg edward deſtroied lādes tho kȳg edward herde thys tydyng wex wōder wroth vnto lewelyn ād haſt aſſembled peple went hym toward walys werred ſo vpon lewelȳ prȳce tyll brought hȳ moche ſorwe diſeſe lewelȳ ſaw defence might nat auaille cam̄ ayene yelde hym kynges grace cryed hym mercy ād longe tyme knelyd ye kynges fete kyng hym pyte cōmaū falſeneſſe wherfore ſome hōged ſome drawen aftyrward honged kȳg ordeyned ye ſterlȳg halpeny ferthing ſhold gon̄ thurgh lād ꝯmaūded man fro yt day aftyrward yaf ne feffed hous religyō wyt lāde tenemēt wtoute ſpecyall leue ye kȳg dyd ſhold punyſſed kynges ye yift ſhold nought lōge aftir yt lewelȳ prynce walys thurgh ticemēt dauyd brother both̄ hir conſent thei thought diſheryte kȳg edward moch̄ might· ſo yt thurgh hē both̄ ye kīges pee brokē· ād whā kȳg edward herde anon̄ ſente baron northūberlād ſurreis alſo yt ſhold gon̄ take hyr vyage vpon traitours lewelȳ dauyd wōder hard werre tho hit wȳter walys whē othir cō tree ſomer lewelȳ let ordeyn̄ welaraye wt vytailles caſtell swādon theryn wyth hugh̄ nombre peple plente vytailles ſo king edward wiſt nat wher entre whan kȳges men perceyued alſo ſtrength walys let come ye ſee barge botes grete plākes many might ordeyne ād haue gon̄ forſaid caſtell swandone wyth men fote eke hors walſh men ſo moche peple ſo ſtronge thei dryuen ye englyſſhmē ayen̄ ſo ther ſo moch̄ prees peple turnyng ayen̄ charge berthen hem made barge bottes ſinke ther drē ched full many good knyght yt ſeye syr rogier gilford syr williā lȳdeſey ſir iohannes ſone ſir robert ād ſir rychard tanny hughe nōbre othir ād thurgh hyr owne folye yf hath good eſpies thei nat ben̄ harmed whā kȳg edward herd telle hys peple ſo drenched made ſorwe ynowe tho came ſir iohā veyſſye frō kyng aragon brought wt moch̄ folk bachiloers ād gaſcoynes ſowdiours dwellyng wyth forſayde ſir iohan veyſſye vnderfōge wage wyth hym withholde ād noble men fyght ād brent many townes quelled moche peple walſſhmē thei might taken wyth myght ſtrength̄ made ſtrōge aſſaulte caſtell swādon gete caſtell whā dauyd prȳ ce brother herd tydynge ordeyned flyght lewelȳ prȳce ſaw hys brother ſlowen ſore abaſſhed power hys werre mayntene ād ſo iewelyn began flee ād wende well haue eſkaped· morwe ſir rogyer mortiemer met hym onely x knyghtes ſet hym roūde aboute went ād ſmote hede preſented vnto kyng edward ād maner prynce walys taken hede ſmyten alle heyres diſherited euermore thrugh right full dome alle landes reaulme dauyd lewelynes brother prȳce walys put deth capitulo clxiiij dauyd prince brother walys thurgh pride wente haue ben̄ prynce walys aftyr hys brother deth vpon ſēt aftyr walſſhmen parlement dinbygh̄ ād folych̄ made walys aryſe ayens kyng began meue werre ayens began meve werre ayēs king dyd ſorwe diſeſe yt might power whē kīg edward herd thȳge ordeyned men purſwe vpō hym dauyd ferſely defēded tyll came towne ſeint morice ther dauid take fledde lad ye kȳg kyng commaūded ſhold hōged drawe ſmiten hede quartryd hȳ ſende hede londō ād fowre quartyers ſende iiij townes chief walys ſholde take example therof ben̄ ware aftyrward kyng edward let crie pee walys ſaiſed lāde hande· grete lordes left lyue came done feaute homage kȳg edward hir kȳde lord tho let kyng edward amende lawes walys defectife aftyr ſēt lordes walys letter patēt ſhold come hys parlament whā comē kyng ſaid hem full curtoiſly lordynges ye well come ād behoueth coūceil helpe wente gaſcoyn̄ amende treſpaces yt don̄ entrete pee bytwen̄ kyng aragon ād prince morey kynges liege men erles baron conſēted ād graūted therto tho made kyng edward redy wēt gaſcoyn̄ let amēde treſpaces hym done gaſcoyne ye debate bytwen̄ kyng aragon ād prynce morey ceſed made hem accorded whylle good kȳg edward quene elianore wyfe ī gaſcoyne good erle cornewaill made wardeyn̄ englond tyll edward came ayene tho enquered traitours cōgeted falſeneſſe ayens ād ech̄ hem vndyrfēge dome aftyr thei deſerued mene tyme while ye good kyng edward beyonde ſee don̄ hem make amēdes • ayens treſpaced fals thefe traitour kalled rys ap meriedoke begā make werre ayens kyng edward encheſon ſir spayne tiptot wrongfully greved diſeſed forſayd rys ap meriedok whē kȳg edward herd ſend hys letter ri ap meriedok ſhold begȳne make werre ſhold ī pee loue came ayene englond wold vndertake querell ād don̄ amēd myſdon̄ forſaid ri ap meriedoke deſpyſed ye kȳ ge cōmaundement ſpared done ſorwe myght kynges men englōd anone aftyr taken ād lad york drawen hanged hys felonye ¶of redreſſyng kȳg edward made iuſtyces ād hys clerkes thei don̄ hyr falſeneſſe drofe yewes owte englond vſery myſbeleue capitulo clxv whan kyng edward h̄ad dwellyd thre yere gaſcoyne wille came hym turne ayene englond tho come ayene punctel fonde ſo many plaȳtes made iuſtyces ād clerkes done ſo many wrō ge falſeneſſe wondyr whiche falſeneſſe syr thomas weilond kynges juſtyce forſwore englōd towre london falſeneſſe mē put vpon hȳ wherof atteynt ād proued fals anone aftyr kyng don̄ hys wyll iuſtyces tho let enquyre ād aſpye jewes deſceyued ād begylled hys peple thurgh ſȳne falſeneſſe vſerye ād let ordeyne pryve parlament amonge hys lordes ordeyned amōges hem iewes ſhold voide englond myſbeleue alſo hir fals vſerye dydē vnto criſten men ſpede make ende thys thyng communite englond yafe vnto kyng xv peny hyr goodes menable ſo werē iewes dryvē oute englond tho went iewes fraunce dwellyd thurgh leue kyng phelyp tho kȳg fraūce ¶how kyng edward ſeyſed lōde scotlād thurgh conſent graunt lordes ſcotland cap clxvi hit nat longe aftyr alyſander kyng scotland dede dauid erle huntȳgdone kynges brother scotland axed claymed kȳgdome scotland encheſon rightful heyre lande ſcotland many grete lordes scotland ſayden nay wherfore grete debate aroſe bytwene hem hyr frendes moch̄ wolde nat cō ſente coronacyon ye mene tyme ye forſayd dauid deyde ſo befell ſame dauyd thre doughtyrs whiche worthely maryed fyrſt doughtyr maried bailloll ſecōde brus thridde haſtȳges ye peuenes kynges archier nowe god ſo helpe nought thow ſpekeſt gold englōd wolde nat let gon̄ withoute cōmaūdement kyng edward tho lad kyng edward king wolde ſee cōmaūded lede hym way haue dome ¶how ſir hugh̄ ſpēcers ſone made kynges chamberlayne ye bataill mytone capitulo cxcij lōge aftyrward king ordeined parlament york ſir hugh̄ ſpē cer ſone made chamburlayne mene tyme whyle werre laſt kept pryſon baron herd thys thyng camen pounfret erle thomas ſoiourned told hī mortimer yelde hem kyng put hem grace ſiege tykhill capi cxcvi ſir thomas erle lancaſtre herde thei wonder wroth companye gretly diſcomfyted ād ordeyned hir power gedre beſieged caſtell tykhyll withynne ſo manly defēded hem ſelf baron might gete caſtel kyng herde caſtell beſieged ſwore god hys holy name ſiege ſholde remeved aſſembled hughe power peple went thydderward reſkewe caſtell power encreſed day day ¶whenne noble gentyl erle lancaſtre ād erle herford baron hyr companie herd thȳg aſſembled hir power wēt hem burton vp trent ād kepte brygge kyng ſhold nat paſſe ouer befell ſo ye x day moneth march̄ ye yere grace thowſand thre hondred xxi kyng ād ſpencer ſir aymer valaunce erle penbroke ſir iohan erle arundell ād hyr power wē ten ouer watyr diſcomfited erle thomas cō panye fledden vnto caſtell tutbery fro thennes wenten pounfret ād vyage deyed ſir rogier dā morie abbey tutbery ſame tyme erle thomas traitour hȳ kalled robert holand knight erle brought vp nought noryſſhed hȳ botelerie yeven thowſand mark land yere ſo moche loued hym myght don̄ erles court thing lyked bothe amonge hye lowe ſo quētely yt thefe bare hȳ ayēs lord yt truſtyd vpō hym thā vpon man lyve erle ordeyned lettres wēte ye erldome lancaſtre make mē aryſe helpe vyage· ſeye vc men armes fals traitour came ther maner men warne ne make ariſe helpe hys lorde whā traytour herde telle hys lorde diſcōfyted burtone fals thefe traitour ſtalle away ād robbed raueneſdale lordes men came fro ſcomfyture toke hem hors harneis quelled hem myght take tho came yelde hȳ vnto king good erle thomas wiſt ſo betraied ſore abaſſhed ſaid ſelfe almighty god quod might robert holād fynde hys hert betraye ſithen̄es haue loued hȳ ſo moch̄ god wele may mā ſee hym man may deceyue othir rather thā truſt mooſt vpon hath full euyl yelde godneſſe worſhip hȳ haue done thurgh kēdeneſſe haue j avaūced made hī high̄ frō lowe ād maketh go hygh̄ vnto lowe yet ſhall deye euyll deth ¶of ſcomfyture burbruge capitulo cxcvij good erle thomas lancaſtre humfrey de bohōne erle herford baron wyt hem toke coūceill bytwene hem frere prechours poūfret tho thought thomas vpon traitrie robert holād ſaid reproue allas holand hath betraied ay reed ſome euel ſhrede ād cōmune aſſent ſhold wente ye caſtell dū ſtāburgh whiche parteyneth erledome lancaſtre ād ſhold abyde tyll yt kyng foryeue hē hyr maletalent good erle thomas herde anſwered maner ſaide lordes quod gon̄ toward ye north northren men wyll ſeyne go toward ſcottes ſo ſhuld hold traitours cauſe diſtaunce bitwene kyng edward ād robert brus made kȳg ſcotlād therfore ſay touching ſelf wyll goo ferther north thā mȳ owne caſtell pownfrete whē ſir rogier clyford herde aroos vp anone wrath drowe ſwerde ſwore almyghty god ād holy name wolde gone wt hem ſholde dede ād wolde ſlee noble gentyll erle thomas lācaſtre ſore drad ſaid fair ſires wyll gon̄ yow whyder ſo euer ye lede tho went gedres north wyt hē vijc men armes ād camen burbrygge whā ſir andrew herkela north contre thurgh ordenaūce kyng kepe contre ſcotland herde tell thomas lācaſtre diſcomfited companie burton vpon trent ordeyned hȳ ſtronge power ād ſir symond ward alſo tho ſherewe york camē mette ye baron burbrygge anon̄ breke brigge made tree ſir thomas lancaſtre herde ſir andrewe herkela brought hym ſuch̄ power ſore adrad ād ſent ſir andrew herkela ſpake ſaide hym thys maner sir andrewe quod ye mowe wel vndyrſtōde lord kynge lad ād myſgouerned moch̄ fals coū ceille thurgh ſir hugh ſpēcer fadre ſir hugh̄ ſone ād ſir iohan erle arundell thurgh maiſter robert baldolke fals pylled clerke nowe kȳges court dwellȳg wherfor praye yow ye wolde come wyt v wyt power ye haue ordeyned ād helpe deſtroye venȳ englond traitours ben therinne wyll yeve vnto yow beſte part v erledomes· haue ād holde wyll make vnto yow othe wyll neuer done thyng withoute yowre coūceill ſo ye ſhalbe efte well wt v euer robert holand tho anſweryd ſir andrew herkela ād ſaid syr thomas wold don̄ ne conſente ther maner thyng ye myght yeue punctel withoute ye wille commaundement owr lord kynge ſholde ben̄ holde traytour evyrmore whan forſaid noble erle thomas lancaſtre ſawe nold yeue conſent vnto hym maner thyng syr andrewe ſayd wyll ye nowe nat conſent deſtroye venȳ reame conſent one word ſir andrew j telle thys yere gone ye ſhull ben̄ take holde traytour thā ye hold v nowe ād wers deth ye ſhall deye thā euyr deyed knight englōd vnderſtondeth well ye dede nevyr thyng ſorer ſhall yowe repent nowe goth ād dothe yow good lyketh wull put vnto mercy grace god ſo wēt fals traitour ſir andrewe herkela ī way fals traitour tyraunt fals forſworne mā thurgh noble erle lancaſtre vnderfeng armes cheualerie thurgh hym made knight tho might mē ſeē archyers drawe hem one ſyde othir ād knyghtes alſo fowghten gedre wonder ſore alſo among othir ſir humfrey de boughon erle herford worthy knyght • nō thurgh criſtendome ſtode faught hys enemy vpō brygge thief rybaude ſkulked vnder brigge ferſely ſpere ſmote noble knight fowndement ſo bowelles camē oute there· allas ſorwe ſlayne flour ſolace comfort alſo curteſye ſir rogier clyford noble knyght ſtode euyr ād fought well nobely hym defended worthy barō laſt ſore wownded hede ād ſir willyam sullayād syr rogier bernefeled ſlayne bataille whan ſir andrewe herkela ſawe ſir thomas men lā caſtre laſſed ſlaked anone companye camen gentyll knyght ſir thomas lancaſtre ſeyd yeld trai tour yeld gentyll erle āſwered tho ſayd nay lordes traitours none wyll nevyr v yelde whyles yt owr lyfes laſten leuer haue ſlayne ī trouthe thā yelde v yow ſir andrew ayene grad vpō ſir thomas cō panye yollyng wode wolfe ſaid yelde yow traitours taken yeld yow hygh̄ voys ſaide bethe ware ſyres none yow hardy vpon lyfe vpon lymme miſdone thomas body lancaſtre ād wyth worde good erle thomas went chapell ſayd knelyng vpō knee turned hys viſage towardes croſſe ſayd almyghty god yelde holy put thy mercy wyt vyleyns rybaudes • ept aboute hym euery ſyde tyraunts wode turmentours diſpoilled hym hys armure clothed hym robbe ray ſquyers lyuere forth lad hym vnto yorke water tho myght men ſeen moche ſorwe care gē tyll knightes fledden euery ſyde rybaudes vyleyns egrely hem diſcryed grad highe yelde yow traytours yelde yow yolden robbed boū den thevys allas ſhame deſpyte gentill ordre knyghthode bataylle lande tho wytoute lawe holy chyrch̄ tho reuerence thā bene bordelhows punctel bataille fadre ayens ſone· vncle ayens hys nephew ſomoche vnkendeneſſe neuer ſeyn englōd tyme amonge folk one nacyō kynrede pyte othyr· hungrie wolfe hath ſhepe wonder grete lordes englōd nat nacyon medled othir nacions ſeyne ſomme bretōs ſōme saxon ſomme danoys ſome pehites ſomme frenſhmen ſomme norman ſomme spaynardes ſomme romayns ſomme henaudes ſomme flemmynges othir dyuerſe nacyōs whiche nacyons accorded kynde blode englond ſo grete lordes ben̄ wedded englyſſh peple ſhold pee haue ben̄ reſte amōges hem withoute envye bataill ſir rogier cliford tak sir iohan mō bray ſir william tuchet sir william fit william many othir worthy knightes taken bataille ſir hughe dandell next daye taken put pryſon ſhold haue bene don̄ deth yf ſpouſed kynges nece erle gyllebertes ſuſter glouceſtre anon̄ ſir bartholomewe badeleſmere taken ſtowe park maner biſſhoppes lyncolne nephew many baron ād baneretz wherfore made moch̄ ſorwe thomas lācaſtre beheded poūfrete v baron honged drawen capitulo cxcviij nowe ſhall telle noble erle thomas lancaſtre whē taken brought york many cyte full glad punctel vpon hym cryed wyth hyghe voys ſir traitour ye arne wellcome bleſſed god ſhal ye haue reward longe time ye haue deſerued ād kaſt vpō many ſnowe balles many othyr reproues dyd hȳ· gentyll erle ſuffryd ſayd nothir oon ne othir ſame tyme kȳg herd ſame ſconfiture full glad haſt came pounfret ād ſir hughe ſpencer ſir hughe hys ſone punctel ſir iohan erle arundell ſir edmond wodeſtoke kinges brother erle kent ſir aymer valaunce erle panbroke maiſter robert baldock fals pyled clerck pryue dwelled kynges court▪ ād came thyder kȳg kyng entred caſtell ſir andrewe herkela fals tiraunt thurgh kynges commaundement toke gentyll erle thomas pounfrete pryſoned ī hys owne caſtell newe made· ſtode ayens abbey kyng edward· ſir hughe fadre ād ſone caſt thought ād maner good erle thomas lancaſtre ſholde dede wythoute iugement perys wherfore ordeyned thurgh kinges iuſtices kyng ſholde put vpon poyntes treſon ſo befell ye barre kynges iuſtyces bare hede thief fair halle withyn owne caſtel made therȳ many feſt riche eke poure ād theſe iuſtyces syr hugh̄ ſpē cer fadre aymer valaunce erle pēbrok ſir edmond wodeſtok erle kent ſir iohan bretaigne erle richemond ād ſir robert nalemethorpe iuſtyce ſir robert acoulped thys maner thomas fyrſt owr lord kyng thys court excludeth maner anſwere thomas lord ye kyng put vpō ye haue lāde ridē wyt baner diſplaied ayēſt pee traitour worde gentyll erle thoās wyt hygh̄ vois ſaid nay lordes ſoth bi ſeȳt thomas neuer traitour iuſtice ſaid ayen̄ thomas lord kīg put vpō ye haue robbed folk mordred peple thefe thomas king alſo put vpō yow diſcomfited peple wt folk owne reaume wherfore ye went fled ye wode outelawe alſo ye taken outelawe thomas traitour ye ſhul hōged reſō ye kīg foryeve iewes loue quene iſabel thoās reſon wolde alſo ye ſhold hōged kȳg hath foryeve yow yt cauſe lygnage thomas aſmoche ye take fleyng owtelawe kyng wyll youre hede ſhalbe ſmytten ye haue well deſerued anone doth hȳ owte preſence anone brȳg hym hys jugemēt whan gētyl knyght thomas herd theſe wordes wyth hyghe voys cryed ſore wepyng ſaid allas ſeynt thomas fayr fadre allas ſhall deed thus graū te nowe blyſſefull god āſwere avaylled hym thyng kurſed gaſcoynes put hȳ hydder thydder hym cryed hygh̄ voys god moſt dredfull wel knowē thyn open traitrye euyll deth ſhalt thow deye thou haſt wel deſervyd tho ſette vpō hys hede ſcorne olde chappelet rent torne nat worth halpeny ſette vpon leue white palfrey full vnſemelich ād eke bare olde bryddell horryble noyſe drouen owte ye caſtell toward deth caſt vpon hym many balles ſnowe turmentours lad hym oute ye caſtell tho ſaid pytouſe wordes handes helde vpon hyghe towardes hevē punctel kyng heuen yeve v mercy erthely kyng hath v forſake frere prechour wente hym oute caſtell tyll came place ended lyfe vnto whō ſhrofe lyfe gētyl erle helde frere wonder faſt bi clothes ſaid fayr fadre abyde wyth v tyll ded fleſh quaketh drede deth ſoth ſeye gē till erle ſette vpon knee turned toward eſt rybaulde kalled hygone moſtone ſet hāde vpon gentyll erle ſayd deſpyte syr traitour turne toward ſcottes thy foule deth vnderfong turned ward north noble gentill erle thomas anſweryd tho mylde voys ād ſayd fayrlordes ſhall don̄ wille worde frere went fro ſore wepyng anone ribaulde wēt ſmote hede xi kal apryll yere grace cccxxi allas euer ſuche gētyll blode ſhuld ben̄ done deth withoute cauſe reſon traytourſly kȳg coūceilled whē thurgh fals counceill ye ſpēcers ſuffred ſir thoās vncles ſone put ſuche deth ſo ben beheded ayens maner reſon grete pyte alſo ſuche noble kyng ſhold ben̄ deceyued ād myſgouerned thurgh ryght falſe counceill falſe ſpencers whiche mayntened thurgh loſ lerie ayens honour eke profyte punctel aftyrward ther fyll grete vengeaunce englōd encheſō forſaid thomas deth ¶when gentyll erle hys life paſſed pryour monkes pounfrete geten body ſir thomas kyng buryed hyghe auter ryght ſyde ſame day gentyll lord dede honged ād drawe ſame quarell pounfret sir william tuchet ſir william fitz willyā syr warreyne yſille ſir henry bradborne ſir willyam chenie barōs iohan page ſquyer ſone aftyr york drawē ād honged ſir rogier cliford sir johan monbray baron ſir goſſelm dauyll knight briſtowe drawe ād honged ſir henry wymyngton ād ſir henry mounfort baron glouceſtre drawe honged sir iohan giffard ſir william emelbrugge baron london honged ād drawe ſir henry tie baron wynchelſee ſir thomas colepepir knight wȳdeſore ſir fraūceis waldenham baron caūterbury drawe honged ſir bartholomewe badeleſmere ſir bartholomewe aſſhebourneham barōs kerdyfe walys ſir williā flemmȳg baron kyng edward went scotland hoūdred thouſand men armes might nat ſpede capi cxcix whan kyng edward englond brought ye floure cheualerye vnto hir deth thurgh counceyl ſir hugh̄ ſpencer fadre ſir hughe ſone became wode lyōne ſo euer ſpencers wolden haue done ſo well ye kȳg loued hē might don̄ wyt hym thynge wolde wherfor king yafe vnto ſir hugh̄ ſpencer fadre erledome wȳ cheſtre ſir andrewe herkela erledome cardoill p̄ iudice harmyng croune kīg edward tho th •• gh coūſeille ſpēcers diſherited hē ben̄ ayens querell wt thomas lācaſtre many othir diſherited alſo encheſō yt ſpēcer coueited haue hir lādes ſo thei wolde deſire wt wrō ge ayēs reſon tho made kȳg robert baldok fals piled clerke chaūceler englond thurgh counceyll forſayd ſpencers fals ribaud· coueytous ſo counceylled kyng moch kyng let taken tho hys owne ward goodes lordes wrongfully put deth owne hande well token ye goodes holy chyrche goodes withoute let hē put treſorye cyte london therof let hem kalled forfayts bi hyr coūceill kyng wrought evyrmore diſheryted hem goodes oughten thurgh hir counceyll lete arere talliage goodes englōd wherfore richeſt kyng euer england aftyr wylliam baſtard normandye conquered englōd yet thurgh counceyl hem hym ſemed ynowe made yet euery towne englond fynde man armes vpō hir owne coſtages gone werre vpon scottes enemyes wherfore kyng wente ſcotland wyt houndred thouſād men armes witſontyde yere owr lord iheſu criſt mccc ād xxij ſcottes went ād hyd hem mountaynes wodes caried englyſſhmen fro day day kyng might maner thyng hem fȳ de playne felde wherfor many englyſſhmen fewe vitailles hadden hunger deyden wonder faſt ſodenly goynge comynge ād namely tho ben̄ ayens thomas lancaſtre robed hys men vpon hys landes whenne kyng edward ſawe vitaylles failled hym tho wonder ſore diſcomforted encheſon alſo men deyed nought might ſpede ennemies ſo laſt came ayene englond anone came iames douglas alſo thomas randulph huge hoſt englond northumberland hem englyſſhmen dryuen owte englond camen robbed contre ād quelled peple alſo brent towne called nortallertone ād many othir townes vnto york king herde tidȳge let ſompne maner mē myghten trauaille ād ſo englyſſhmen met ſcottes abbey beigheland xv day mychelmaſſe ſame yere aboue ſaid englyſſhmen diſcomfyted ād ſcomfyture take ſir johan britaigne erle richemond helde contre erledome lancaſtre paied huge raunſone let gone went fraunce came nevyr aftyrwdrd ayene ſir andrewe herkkela taken ād put vnto deth erle cardoille capitulo ducenteſimo tyme ſir andrewe herkela newe made erle cardoille cauſe takē good erle thomas lācaſtre ordeyned thurgh ye kȳ ge commaūdement englōd bryng hym power yt might helpe hym ayens ſcottes ye abbey beigheland whā fals traitour gadred peple myght ſhold haue comē kyng vnto abbey beighelād fals traitour lad hem othir contre thurgh copelād thurgh erldome lācaſtre went thurgh cōtre robed queld folk might ād ferthermore ye fals traytour takē grete ſome gold ſiluer ſir iames dowglas ayens kyng englond helpyng holdyng wyth ſcottes who treſon kyng englond ſcomfyted beiheland er came thydder wherfor king toward wonder wroth let pryuely enquere contre aboute ſo mē enquered aſpied laſt trewth̄ founde ſought ād atteynt taken fals traitour noble erle thomas lancaſtre tolde er don̄ vnto deth takyng burbrygge hȳ ſaide yere don̄ ſhold take holde traitour ſo holy man ſaid wherfore kyng ſent pryuely syr anthoyn̄ lucy knight cōtrey cardoille ſholde take ſir andrewe herckela ād put hȳ vnto deth brynge thȳg vnto ende kyng ſent cōmiſſion ſo ſame andrewe taken cardoill led vnto barre ye maner erle worthely arayed ſwerd gurt aboute hȳ ād hoſed ſpored tho ſpake ſir anthoyne maner ſir andrewe quod kȳg put vpon aſmoch̄ thow haſt bene orped thy dedes ded vnto mochel honour made erle cardoill ād thow traitour vnto thy lord kȳg laddeſt hys peple cōtre ſhold haue holpe hȳ bataill beyghelād thow laddeſt thē away cōtre copelād thurgh erledome lancaſtre wherfore lord kyng ſcomfyted ſcottes thurgh thy treſon falſeneſſe ād yf thou haddeſt com̄ time maiſtiry thurgh treſon thow dydeſt grete ſome goold ſiluer thou vnderfēg iames douglas ſcote kynges enemye lord ye kynges wille ordre knyghthode whiche thow vndyrfeng thin honour worſhip vpō thy body brought nought thy eſtate vndone yt othir knightes lowe degre mowe beware whyche lorde hath avaunced hugely ī diuerſe contrees englōd mowe take example hir lord aftyrward trewly ſerue tho commaūded knave anone haue hys ſpores helys aftyr let breke ye ſwerde ouer hede whiche kyng yafe kepe defēde lande therwith made hī erle cardoil aftyr let hym vnclothe furred tabart hode furred cote gurdel don̄ ſir anthoyne ſaid vnto andrewe quod art thou knight knaue thy treſon ye kyng wille thou ſhalt hō ged drawe thy boweles taken owte thy body brent thy body quartred thyn hede ſmyten ſent vnto londō ther ſhall ſtonde vpō londō brugge thy fowre quarter ſhull ſēt fowre townes englond mowe chaſtyſed antoyne ſaid ſo done maner thynge laſt day octobre yere grace mccc xxij yere ſonne tho turned ī blode peple ſaw dured fro morne til xi clokke day ¶of ye miracle yt god wrought ſeynt thomas loue lācaſtre wherfore king let cloſe chyrche dores pryowre pounfret yt man ſholde come therȳ body offrē capitulo ccj ſone aftyr erle thomas lancaſtre martred preſt longe tyme bene blynde dremed hys ſlepyng ſhold gone vnto hylle ther good erle thomas lancaſtre don̄ vnto deth ſholde haue ſyght ayen̄ ſo dremed iij nightes ſewȳg ye preſte let tho lede ſame hylle came place martred deuoutely made ther prayer praied god ſeȳt thoās muſt haue ſight ayene whē hys prayer laid right honde vpon ſame place good man martred drope drye blode ſmale ſand cleued honde therwith ſtryked eyen anone thurgh myght god ſeȳt thomas lācaſtre ſight ayen̄ thanked tho almyghty god ād ſeint thomas whē miracle knowen amonge men peple came thydder euery ſyde ād kneled ād made hir praiers tō pryorie pounfrete praied holy martyr ſocour helpe god herde hir prayer alſo ther yōge chylde drē chyd welle towne pounfrete ād dede thre dayes thre nightes ād men camen ād laid dede childe vpon ſeynt thomas tombe holy martyr child aroſe deth life many man ſawe ād alſo moch̄ peple owte hir mynde god hath hē ſent hyr mynde ayene vertu holy martyr alſo god hath yeuen therto creples hyr goyng croked hir hō de hir foot blynde alſo hir ſighte ād many ſike folke hyr hele dyuerſe maladyes loue thys good martir alſo ryche man coundom gaſcoyne ſuche maladie right ſyde roted fyll way hym mē myght ſe lyuer alſo hert ſo ſtanke vnneth men myght come nye hym wherfore frē de wōdre ſory laſt almyghty god wolde praied ſeynt thomas lancaſtre wolde praye almyghty god pryſoner behit gon̄ poū frete don̄ hir pylgrymage vyſion next aftyr martyr ſeint thomas came vnto hȳ annoynted ouer hys ſike bodj therwith ye good mā awoke hole fleſh reſtored ayen̄ roted falle away myracle ye good man frēdes loued god ſeȳt thomas euyr aftyr good mā came englōd toke wt hȳ iiij felawes came pounfrete vnto holy martyr ād hir pilgrimage ye good man yt ſike came thyder nakyd ſauf brech̄ whē done turned home ayen̄ hyr cōtre tolde ye myracle wher ſo euer thei came alſo ij mē haue helyd ye mormall thurgh helpe yt holy martyr though yt euyll holyd īcurable whē ye ſpēcers herd god dyd ſuch myracles holy martyr wolde beleve ī maner wyſe ſaid opēly yt grete hereſye ſuch̄ vertu hȳ beleue whā ſir hugh̄ ſpēcer ſone ſawe doynge anon̄ ſent meſſagier frō poūfrete ther dwelled king edward tho crauene skyptō cauſe kyng ſhold vndon̄ pylgrimage ribaude ye meſſagier wēte toward kyng don̄ meſſage came hylle whyche good martyr done deth ſame place made hys ordure whā don̄ went toward kyng ſtronge flix came vpon er came york ſhedde bowles fondemēt whan ſir hugh̄ ſpencer herde thys tydyng ſome deel drad thought vndone pylgrimage might maner way kyng wente ād ſaide ſholde grete ſklaūdre thurgh oute criſtendome deth thomas lancaſtre yf ſuffred ye peple don̄ hir pylgrymage poū frete ſo counceilled kyng commaūded cloſſe church dores poūfrete which̄ chyrch̄ ye holy martyr ſeint thomas entered thus thei dyden ayens fraunchyſes ye holy chyrch̄ ſo fowr yere aftyr might pylgrime come vnto holy body encheſon monkes ſuffred men come honoure holy body ſeint thomas martyr thurgh counceill ſir hugh̄ ſpencer ſone thurgh coūceill alſo maiſtir robert baldok falſe pylled clerk kynges chaūceler kyng cōſentyd thei ſhold ſette hir wage punctel let make wardeins ouer hir owne good longe tyme· thurgh commaūdement forſaid ſir hugh̄ ſpencer xiiij gaſcoynes well armed kepte hylle ye good man ſeint thomas 〈◊〉 vnto hys deth ſo pilgryme might come bi yt way full well wende haue take cryſtes might power ye grete loo myracles ſhewed hys martyr ſeȳt thomas cryſtendome ād ſame tyme king made robert baldolke pyled clerke fals thurgh praier ſir hugh̄ ſpē cer ſone chaūcelere englōd ſame tyme ye caſtell walyngford yolden ayēs kyng thurgh priſoners yt withinne caſtell ſeȳt thoās quarell lācaſtre wherfore peple contre came tokē caſtell vpon forſayd pryſonners wherfore ſir johan golyngton knyght ſir edmond beche priſonners ſquyer kalled rogier walton take ād ſent kyng poūfrete ād done pryſon forſaid rogier ſent vnto york punctel drawe ād hanged anone ſir ro gier mortymer wigmore bra ke owte toure londō manere forſaid ſir ro gier herd ſhold drawe honged london morne ſeint laurence day day helde faire feſt ye toure lōdō ſir ſtephen ſegraue conſtable ye toure many grete men wyt whē ſhold ſope forſayd ſtephē ſent officiers toure came ſoped hym whē ſhold take hir leue hȳ ſquier called ſtephē full pryue wyth forſaid rogier thurgh coūceil yafe hem ſuch̄ dranke leſte hem ſlepē two dayes ij nightes mene tyme ſcaped away watyr ſaye tamyſe went ouer ſee helde fraūce wherfore kyng ſore annoyed tho put ſame ſtephē conſtablery ¶how quene iſabel went fraūce trete pee bitwene hir lord king englōd king fraūce hir brother capitulo ccij king wēt tho vnto lō ther thurgh coūceil ſir hugh̄ ſpēcer ye fadre ād ſone maiſtir robert baldok fals pyled clerk hys chaunceler let ſeiſe tho quenes lōdes owne honde alſo landes ſir edwardis hys ſone ſo put hir wage ayens maner reſon thurgh falſeneſſe ſpēcers whē kyng fraūce quene jſabelles brother herde falſeneſſe ſore annoyed ayēs kīg englōd fals counceillers wherfore ſent letter vnto kīg edward vnder ſeal yt ſhold come fraūce certaȳ day don̄ homage therto ſomened hȳ elles ſhold leſe gaſcoign̄ ſo ordeyned englōd thurgh ye kȳg coū ceill quene iſabel ſhold wēde fraūce trete pee bitwene hir lord hyr brother oliuer ynghā ſhold wēde gaſcoigne haue wt hȳ vijm men moo armes ben̄ ſene ſhall wardeyne gaſcoign̄ ſo ordeyned quene iſabell wēt tho ouer ſee came fraūce hyr went ſir aymer valaūce erle pēbroke yt ther mordred ſodēly priue ſege thurgh goddes vengeaūce one iuſtices conſented ſeȳt thomas deth lācaſtre wolde neuer repēte hȳ wykked dede time ſir oliuer ynghā wēt ouer gaſcoign̄ dyd moch̄ harme kȳg fraūce gate ayen̄ kȳg edward loſte▪ moch̄ therto ¶how king edward ſent ſir edward hys ſone eldeſt fraunce capi cc iij quene iſabel quarter yer̄ dwelled fraunce sir edward hyr eldeſt ſone ne axed leue wente fraūce ſpeke wt modre iſabell quene kyng fadre graūted hȳ wyt good ſayd hym go fayr ſone goodis bliſſyng myne ād thenke come ayen̄ haſtly thou might wēt ouer ſee came fraūce kȳg fraūce vncle vnderfēg hym mochel honour ſayd vnto faire ſone ye welcom ād cauſe fadre come homage ye duchye guyhēne aūceſtres went yeue yow yt lordſhipp holde heritage aunceſtres haue don̄ tofore yow wherfore called duke gwyhenne ¶how kyng exilled quene iſabell edward eldeſt ſone capitu cciiij whenne kyng edward englond herde telle howe kyng fraūce yeuen duchye gwyhēne vnto ſir edward ſone withoute cō ſent wille ſone vnderfonge duchye became wonder wroth ſente ſone lettre wyfe alſo ſhold come ayen̄ englond haſte myght quene iſabell ſir edward hir ſone woder ſore adrad kynges menace hys wrathe pryncipaly falſeneſſe ſpencers both̄ ye fadre ſone commaūdement wold come wherfore kyng edward ſore annoyed let make crye lō yf quene yſabell edward hir eldeſt ſone came englond ſhold bene holden enemyes reame englōd wold obeye ād come kynges cōmaūdement englond bothe exilled modre hir ſone quene iſabel herde thees tydynges ſhe ſore adrad ſhēt thurgh fals cō getyng ſpēcers wēt wt ye knyghtes exilled oute englond ſeynt thoās cauſe lācaſtre ſeye ſir rogier wygmore ſir williā truſſell ſir iohan cromwell ād many othir good knightes wherfor thei tokē hir coūceill ordeyned amō ge hē make mariage bytwene duke gwyhēne ye kȳ ge ſone englōd erles doughter henaude yt noble knight name ād doughty tyme yf thȳg myght brought aboute thā ſtode thei trouwȳg helpe god recouer hir herytage englond wherof put thurgh fals congettȳges ye ſpēcers kyng edward thurgh coū ceill ſpēcers ſent douſeperes fraūce ſhold helpe quene iſabel hyr ſone ſir edward exilled oute fraunce capitulo ccv whan kyng edward ſpēcers herde howe quene jſabell ſir edward hir ſone alied hem erle henaud oute exilled englōd encheſon thomas lācaſtre ſo ſory wiſte done wherfore ſir hugh̄ ſpēcer ſone ſaid vnto ſir hugh̄ fadre maner wyſe· fadre accurſed tyme coūceill euer ye conſented quene iſabell ſhold gon̄ vnto fraunce trete accord bytwene kyng englōd hir brother kȳg fraūce youre counceyll time ſoth wit failled j drede ſore leſt thurgh hyr hyr ſone ſhull ſhēt yf take better coū ceill fayre sire vnderſtondeth mervaillous felonye ād falſhede ſpēcers ymagined ād caſt priuely let fylle v bale wyt ſiluer ſomme amounted v thouſend pounde thei ſēt barelles ouer ſee preueli alyen kalled arnold ſpaigne brecour lō dō ſhold gon̄ ye douſeperes fraūce ſhold procure ſpeke kȳg fraunce quene iſabell hir ſone edward dryuen ād exilled oute fraūce amonge othir thȳges brought deth preuely thei might almyghty god wolde ſo arnold ye hye ſee takē zelāders met hym ſee toke hȳ lad hȳ hyr lord erle henaude moch̄ ioye made yt takyng ād laſt arnold preuely ſtale hȳ ſelf away fro thēs came london thys takȳg othir thȳges erle henaude ſaid ye quene iſabell dame maketh yow mery bene good chere ye rycher thā ye wend haue ben̄ ▪ take ye theſe v barelles full ſiluer ſent douzeperes fraūce quelle yow ſone edward thēketh haſtely wēte englōd taketh ye ſir iohan henaude brother vc mē armes many hē fraūce whō ye haue grete truſte grete deinte yow ſcorne ād almyghty god graū te yow grace ennemies ouercome quene iſabell ſent tho thurgh henaud flaūdres hir ſowdyours ordeyned hyr euery day wēte englōd ayene ſo ſhe hir cōpanye sir edmond wodeſtoke erle kēt ſir edwardes brother englond kyng edward let kepe coſtes ſee tried beſte men werre englond capitulo ccvi whenne kȳg edward herde telle quene iſabell edward hir ſone wolde come englond wyth many alien hem oute lawed oute englond hir rebelneſſe ſore adrad put downe leſe kyngdome wherfor ordeyned kepe hys redy whā outeheſe crie made purſwe take aliēs camē englond benymme hȳ londe put oute hys kyngdome ouer let crye thurgh hys patent lrēs euery place euery market englōd quene iſabell ſir edward herewych dydē capitulo ccvij quene iſabell ſir edward hir ſone duke guihēne ſir edward wodeboke erle kent ſir johā therles brother henaud hir men drad menace kyng ne traytours truſt goddys grace ād camē vnto herewich ſouthfolk xxiiij day septēbre yere grace mcccxxvi quene ād ſir edward hir ſone ſēt lrēs ye maire comminalte londō requyryng hē thei ſhold ben̄ helpīg quarel cauſe thei begōne ſeye deſtroye traitours ye reame none āſwere ſent agayne wherfor quene ſir edward hir ſone ſenten othir patēt letter vnder hyr ſeales tenour which̄ lettre folowed maner izabell grace god quene englōd lady irlād coūteſſe pountyf edward eldeſt ſone kȳg englōd duke gwihenne erle cheſtre ād poūtyf monſtroille maire ꝯminalte cyte london ſendeth gretȳg moche haue ye tyme ſēt yow lettres become thys lād wt good aray good maner honour profyte holy chirch right dere lord kyng ād reame might power kepe maynten̄ alle good folke forſayd reame holdē don̄ vpon prayen yow ye wolde ben̄ helpȳg v moche ye may quarel commune profyte reaume haue none āſwere ye forſaid lettres ne knowe yowr wille partye wherfore ſent yow agayne pray charge yow ye bere yow ſo ayens v haue cauſe greue ye ben̄ v helpyng mayes ye may ye may well openly knowen alle ben̄ comen wyth v thys reame thenken done thā alle thȳg lyked good ſhal commune proffyte alle reame onely deſtroye hugh ſpencer enemye alſo enemye alle reame englond ye well opēly knoweth wherfor praye yow charge yow ye ſayth ye owe owre lord kyng v yf ſaid hugh ſpēcer enemye come withinne power ye don̄ haſtely ben̄ takē herewych brought hyr companye ſir iohan henaud hym mē armes wythoute nombre wyt word syr hughe ſpēcer fadre ſpake ſayd thus kyng moſt wurſhypfull lord kyng englond mowe ye make good chere certeȳ ly ben̄ owres kȳg ſawe thys word confortable notheles ſorefull penſyf herte kyng yet fulfylleth hys mete ther came halle othir meſſagier ād ſayd quene iſabell arryued herewych beſyde yepſwych ſouthfolk syr hugh spencer fadre ſpake ſayd meſſauger maner telle ye haue ſeyne fayr frēde ſhe come ſtrē ghte certys ſire ſoth ſaye ſhe ne hyr companye vij hōdred men armes punctel wyth worde ſir hughe walſſhmen ayens quene iſabell edward hyr ſone fyght ſo purpoſe euerichō maiſtir waltier ſtapilton byſſhop exceſtre kynges treſorer beheded london capitulo ccviij ſame tyme kȳg edward ſore adrad leſt towr makȳg hys cloſſe vpon ryuer tamyſe· withoute temple bare hym faylled ſtone make therof ende wherfore commaūded men gon̄ ye chirche freres carmes token ſtone make therwith towre moche ſand morter ād olde robous left ād deſpyte biſſhopp done vnto holy chyrch̄ two ſquyers buryed ſand though thei ben̄ hoū de ther leyen xi wekes tyll quene iſabel ſent hir lettres commune ād prayed hem thei wold ſuffre graū te biſſhop myght takē owte place bene buryed exceſtre hys owne chyrche ſo hys two ſquyers buryed ſeynt clemens chyrch wytoute temple bare wonder though ye biſſhop deyed euell many townes ſhold made pleȳ ſayd ſoth̄ whā kȳg edward diſcomfited scotlād came tho ſouthward ye ſcottes beſieged caſtelles dyd hem moch̄ harme brent townes vnto hard erth̄ aft er ward merlȳ ſayd egle ſhold come cornewaille ſhold haue fetheres gold pryde ſhold haue piere ſhold deſpyſe lordes blood deye thurgh bere gauerſiſe prophecye ful well knowe ād fonde ſothe bi egle vnderſtōde ſir pier ſholde come vnto arme ſee burton vp trent ſhold wēde ouer drede bere ſholde flee ſwan companye vnto bury toward ye north thurgh vnkynde owtputter ſwan thā ſholde ſlaine ſorwe bere ſholde ſlayn̄ full nygh̄ owne neſt ſholde ſtōde vpon poūfrete· vpon ſōne ſhall ſhede bemes many folke ſhall ſeche mochel vertue ſaid full ſothe punctel good erle thoās lācaſtre borne ye northweſt coſyn kyng ſone vncle▪ lawe made ye king leſe moche lād which̄ purch̄aſed wylfully· till laſt king therof toke ſhame ſelf fylled cruelte▪ gate ayene loſte ād moche therto thurgh folke let aſſēble oute ye northweſt made ben̄ adrad auēged hȳ hys barōs thurgh coūceill ſir hughe ſpēcer fadre ād ſir hugh̄ ſone beforne outelawed ēglōd hir wykkedneſſe aft er ward came ayene englōd ſir hugh̄ ſpencer fadre oute fraū ce ſo moch̄ counceilled kyng ſhold werre vpon thoās lācaſtre ſo kyng ſpēcers erle arūdell ād hyr power met thomas lā caſtre burton vp trente hym diſcōfited ſir humfrey erle hereford cōpanie fleddē forſayd thoās hūfrey hir ꝯpanie burbrugge ſir andrewe herkela kalled vnkȳde outeputter alſo ſir ſymōd warde erle yorke came ād met wt thomas lācaſtre wyt huge companye hem ther croune ye kinges ſtate owt meſure ¶how ye pee made bitwene englyſſhmen ſcottes alſo iuſtyfyēg troillebaſtone capitulo ccxvii kȳg edward witſontyde ſecōd yere regne thurgh coūceill modyr ſir rogier
