crowne englond foryafe hē vnto ſcottes euyrmore chartre enſealed ferthermore endenture made ſcottes vnto kyng edward kyng hēryes ſone which̄ ēdēture called rageman whiche conteyned homage feautes fyrſt ye kȳg scotland prelats erles ād baron reaulme scotland hir ſeales ſet ther othir chartres remembraūces kyng edward baron ryght ī ye reame ſcotland foryeve hem ayene holy chyrch ād alſo ye blake croſſe ſcotland whyche good kyng edward conquered ſcotland brought oute abbey scone full precious relique▪ alſo ferther releſed ād foryafe alle landes barōs englōd ſcotland olde conqueſt pee holde ād laſt ſcottes bounde vnto king xxx thouſād pownde ſiluer paid withȳ thre yere ſeye euery yere xm pownde evyn porcyons ferthermore aboue thei ſpake bitwen̄ party aboue ſaid dauid driton̄tier robert bruſ ſone fals tiraunt traytour fals forſwore ayens othe aroſe ayens liege lord ye noble kȳg edward falſely made hȳ kyng ſcotlād age v yere ſo thurgh kurſed coūſeill dauyd ſpouſed berewyke dame iohā ye tour kyng edwardes ſuſter ye geeſt tellyth vpon mary magdalene day ye yere grace mccc xxviij ye grete harme empeirīg kȳges blod wherof yt gentyll lady come allas tyme punctel wonder moch̄ faire damyſel diſparged ſith ſhe maried ayēs cōmune aſſē te englōd fro tyme brute conquered albyon nempned lōde aftyr hys owne name britaigne nowe kalled englōd name engyſt ſo reaume scotland holden reaulme englond crowne bi feaute ād homage brute conquered land ād yafe albanak ſecond ſone kalled lande albayne aftyr owne name ſo heyres camen hȳ heldē brute heires kīges bretaigne feaute ād homage tyme vnto thys kȳg edward ye reame ſcotland holden reame englond feautes ſeruyces aboue ſaid cronycles englōd ſcotland beren witneſſe plenarly accurſed ye tyme parlemēt ordeined northamptō thurgh fals coūceyll falſely diſherited yet withyn age ād yet whan kȳg edward put downe royalte ēglōd yet men put hȳ oute feautes ſeruyces reaulme ſcotland ne fraunchiſes diſherited euermore notheles grete lordes englōd ayēs conferme pee tremes aboue ſaid ſauf quene iſabell kynges modyr edward biſſhop ely ād lord mortimer reſon lawe wolde fynall pee ſholde made bytwene hē wytoute cōmune aſſent englōd debate bitwene quen̄ iſabell ſir hēry erle lā caſtre leiceſtre ridȳg beford capi ccxvij whē forſaid dauid ſpouſed dame iohane tour ye toune berewyke ſaid ſcottes deſpyte ye englyſſhmē called dame johā coūteſſe make pee ye corwardyſe pee ordeyned ye kynges ꝑſone bare wyte blame wt wrō ge makȳg ye accorde don̄ thurgh quene ād rogier mortymer ād nat lōge aftyr ye quene iſabell ne toke hir owne hāde ye lordſhip poūfrete almoſt lādes value apperteyned croune ēglōd ſo yt kīg diſpēde vſes ād eſcheker quen̄ jſabell mortymer grete meyn̄ hir retenaū ce folowed euermore kȳ ge courte· wente toke ye kȳges pryſe hir peny worthes good ſhepe wherfor ye cō tre camē ynne ful ſore adrad almoſt deſtroied tho begone commynalte englond hate iſabell quene ſo moch̄ loued hyr ſhe came ayene purſwe fals traitours ſpencers fraūce ſame tyme fals traitour robert holand betraied lorde ſir thoās lancaſtre tho delyured owte pryſon▪ ād wonder pryue quene iſabell ād alſo rogier mortimer availled hym littell take michelmaſſe tho came next ſewyng rode toward quene jſabell lōdō ſir thoās wither ſmote hede beſides toune ſeynt albones ſir thomas dwelled tho wyt ſir hē ry erle lancaſtre put hydyng drede quene ſhe loued wonder moch̄ praied vnto kyng hȳ ſame thomas muſt ben̄ ex ••• ed oute englōd noble erle ſir henry lācaſtre ofte tymes herd cōmune clamour englyſſhmen diſeſes done englōd alſo dyuerſe wronges done amonge commune peple which̄ kȳg bare blame wronge na full yonge tēdre age thought good man don̄ away ſlake ſklaūdre kynges perſone migh̄t maner wyſe kyng therof nothȳg gylty wherfor peril •• th lymme ſo aſſembled retenaūces went ſpake vnto thē kynges honour alſo amēd eſtate ſir thomas brotherton erle marchall ſir edmōd wodeſtoke kynges vncles alſo men london made hir othe maȳten ī ſame querell hir cauſe thys kyng ſhold holde houſold ād hys meyny kyng ought done haue alſo ryalte quene iſabell ſhold delyuer oute hir honde kynges hō de maner lordſhyppes rente townes caſtelles apperteyned crowne englond othir quenes done hyr medle wyth none thynge alſo ſir rogier mortimer ſhold dwelle vpon owne landes whych̄ londes holpe diſherite moche peple ſo cōmune peple nat deſtroied thurgh hir wrongefull takyng alſo enquere ād kyng betraied falſely deceyued stanhope ād thurgh who coū ceyll ſcottes went away night kyng alſo thurgh who counceill ordenaūce made kynges coronacion put downe ſeyne king amendement helping reaume honour hȳ ſholde gouernyd ruled xij greteſt wyſeſt lordes ye reaume withoute hem ſholde nothing graunted ne done ne ſayd whiche couenaunts malycyouſly put downe fro kynge wherfor many harmes ſhames reproues haue falle vnto kyng reaume vndyrſtōd aſmoche edward ſomtyme kyng englond ordeyned aſſēt comynaulte playne parlement vndyr warde gouernaunce henry erle lancaſtre coſyn ſavacion body take owte caſtell kenilworth yt warde thurgh counſeill quene iſabell mortymer withoute conſente parlament toke lad hȳ nevyr non̄ kynred myght wyt hym ſpeke ne ſee ād traitourſly mordred who deth foul ſlaundre aroſe thurghoute cryſtendome done alſo treſour ſir edward carnarvan left many place englond ād walys waſted ād born̄ away withou te kyng edward ſone deſtructyon hym folk alſo who coū ſeil kyng yafe vp kīgdome ſcotland whyche reame kinges aūceſtres full ſore trauailled ſo dyd many noble man right deliured vnto dauid yt robert brus ſon̄ right right reaume world wiſt alſo chartres remembraūces ye ryght ſcotland take oute treſorie take vnto ſcottes ye kynges enemyes diſherithing ſucceſſours ād grete harme vnto liege grete reproue vnto ēglyſſhmē evyrmore alſo wherfor dam̄ iohan̄ tour kinges ſuſter edward diſparged maried vnto dauid robert ye brus ſone traitour enemye vnto englond thurgh who coūceill ſhe take enemyes hōdes oute englōd mene tyme ye good erle hēry lācaſtre ꝯpanie tokē coūceil theſe poyntes aboue ſaid myght ben̄ amended vnto ye worſhip king profyte proffyte alſo lieges· quene iſabell thurgh coniectȳg ſoutilte alſo mortimere let ordeyne parlement saliſbury ād ye ſam̄ parlemēt mortimer made erle marche ayens barōs englōd preiudice kyng crowne ſir iohā eltham ye kȳges brother gurt ſwerd cornewaill tho kalled erle cornewaille evyrmore quene iſabell ſo moch̄ procured ayēs hyr ſone king ſhe ye warde forſaid ſir edward ād hys lādes parlemēt erle lācaſtre wold come ordeyned alle hys power ayens quene iſabell mortymer men london ordeyned hem wyt vc men armes quene jſabell wiſt doyng ſhe ſwore bi god bi name full angreli euyll tyme thought vpon tho poyntes tho ſent quene iſabell ād mortimer hir retenue kynges retenue ſo yt ordeyned amō ge hem huge hoſte coūceilled kyng ſo vpon night roden xxiiij myle toward bedford ther erle lancaſtre companye thought haue deſtroyed night ſhe rode beſydes kyng hyr ſone knight armed drede deth done kȳg vnderſtonde erle henry lācaſtre companye wolde haue deſtroyed kyng counceill evyrmore wherfore kȳg ſomdelle towardes hevy annoyed punctel whan erle marchall ād erle kente kynges brother herden tydyng rydden ſo meſſage bitwene hem ye kȳg graunted pee erle hē ry lancaſtre certaȳ raū ſone xi pownde neuer paied aftirward theſe lordes helden wyth ſir henry lancaſtre ſir henry beaumount sir fouke fitzwaren ſir thomas rocelyn ſir wylliā truſſell ſyr thomas wither aboute hoūdred knightes moo hym conſentȳg exilled thurgh coūceill quene iſabell mortymer mortymer weited haue hir landes yf might thurgh maner coniectyng ſore couetous tho moch̄ hys wylle grete pyte kyng edward went ouer ſee homage vnto kyng fraunce duchye gwyhenne capitulo cc xix longe yt kīg fraūce thurgh coūceil douſeperes • ent kyng edward englōd ſhold come parys done homage reſon wolde duchye gwyhenne ſo thurgh coūceyll lordes kyng edward went ouer ſee aſcencion tyde came vnto parys thridde yere regne homage vnto kyng fraūce vnderfeng homage made moche ioye wurſhip whā kȳg edward made hys homage haſtely ſent fore englond thurgh quene iſabell modre anon̄ came ayene englond vpon witſonday withoute takyng leue kȳg fraūce wherfore wonder wroth ſir rogier mortimer bare prowdely ſo hye capi ccxx nowe ſhull ye ſir rogier mortymer wingmore deſired coueyted hygh̄ aſtate ſo kyng graūted hym called erle march̄ thurgh oute hys lordſhyp becam̄ ſo prowde ſo hauteyne wolde leſe forſake name aunceſtres euer befor ād encheſon let hem kalle erle marche non̄ cōmunes englōd durſt calle none othir name called ſo thurgh ye kinges crye men ſhold kalle erle marche mortymer bare hym tho ſo hanteyne ſo proude wonder wit alſo diſgyſed hȳ wondre riche clothes maner reſon ſhaping weryng wherof englyſſhmē grete wōdyr maner might cōtryue fynde ſuch̄ maner pryde ād ſaid amonges hem ꝯmunely pryde ſhold longe endure ſame time ſir geffrey mortimer yōg yt mortimer ſone let kalle kȳg folye ſo befell aftyrward dede ſo full pryde wrecchedneſſe yt helde rounde table walys men thyder wold come coūtrefeted maner doȳg kȳg arthures table opēly failled noble kȳg artur mooſt worthy lord renōme worlde time yet came neuer none ſuch̄ aftyr noble knightes criſtēdome dede armes loſed punctel dwelled wyt kȳg arthure helde hȳ wt theire lord yt well ſene cōquered bataille romayne yt kalled frolle gete hȳ reame fraūce quelled hȳ wt hōdes alſo faught wt geaūt called dynabus ād quelled rauiſſhed fayre eleyne yt kyng hoeles nece littel britaigne aftirward quelled bataill emꝑour rome yt called lucye aſſembled ayēs kȳg arthur fight ſo moch̄ peple romains phehis ād ſaraſyus man cowde hē nombre diſcōfyted hem ſtory hȳ telleth ſame tyme cōmune loo ſprong englōd thurgh coniectȳg ordenaūce freres prechours ſir edward carnarvan kyng edwardes fadre geeſt telleth ſayden lyue caſtel corfe wh̄erfor ye cōmunes moſt englond ſorwe drede whethyr ſo wyſtē traitourſly mortimer hī don̄ mordred edmond wodeſtoke erle kent kynges brother edward ca •• • uan beheded wȳcheſtre capitulo ccxxi vpon tyme befell ſo ſir edmōd wodeſtoke erle kent ſpake vnto pope iohan xxij avyuion̄ ſaid almighty god oftetymes don̄ thomas loue lācaſtre many grete miracle many men woman thurgh dyuerſe malady vndone vnto world thurgh praier thei brought vnto hir helthe ād ſo ſir edmōd praied pope hertely wolde graūte hī grace forſaid thomas myght tranſlatyd • ope ſaid nay ſhold trāſlated vnto time bettyr certefyed clergye englond ſent hir obedience thyng god don̄ loue thomas lācaſtre aftir ſuggeſtyon forſayd erle kent vnto hȳ made edmōd ſawe might ſpede hys purpoſe touchyng tranſlacyon praied coūceill touchyng ſir edward carnarvā brother· ſaid longe gone king englond thyng myght beſt done touching delyurance ſyth commune fame thurgh englond lyfe hole ſauf pope herde hym telle ſir edward lyve commaūded erle vpon benyſon ſhold helpe power might deliured owte pryſon ād ſaue hys body maner might breng thys thyng ende aſſoilled hȳ companye pena culpa tho helpe hys deliurance tho toke edmōd wodeſtoke leue pope came ayen englond whan ſir edmond comen ſomme freres preſchours came ād ſaid ſir edward hys brother yet liue caſtel corf vndyr kepyng ſir thomas gurnay tho ſped hȳ forſayd edmond faſt might till yt came vnto ye caſtell corfe ſpake ſo faire wyt iohan dauerill coneſtable ſame caſtell yafe hȳ rich̄ yeftes haue acquytaūce hȳ knowe hys coūceill thus befell forſaid ſir edmond prayed ſpicially telle hȳ preuely hys lord hys brother ſir edward yf lyued dede lyue prayed hym one haue ſight ſir iohā dauerill hygh̄ herted man full corage anſweryd ſhortely vnto ſir edmond▪ ſaid ſir edward hys brother hele vnder kepyng durſt ſhewe vnto man ſyth yt defended hȳ ye kinges halfe edward edwardes ſone carnarvā alſo thurgh cōmaūdemēt quen̄ iſabell kȳges modyr ſir rogier mortymer ſhold ſhewe hys body vnto maner man ye world ſauf onely vnto thaȳ vpon peine lyfe lymme diſherityng heyres euermore fals traytour falſely lyed hys warde take then lad vnto ye caſtell berkelee thurgh thomas garnay bi ꝯmaū dement mortimer till dede ſaid ſir edmond wodeſtoke wyſt thȳg edward brother dede whervpō toke lettre vnto forſaid ſir iohā praied hertely wolde take vnto kȳg edward brother worthi lord vnderfeng lrē hȳ behight hī meſſage wtoute maner faill wt ſir edmōd toke leue thēs ye forſaid iohan wēt tho own̄ cōtre lorſhypp kent there▪ anone johan wiſt ſir edmō gon̄ kent owne lordſhyp anon̄ wēt haſt might fro caſtell corfe came vnto ſir rogier mortimer toke hȳ lettre yt ſir edmōd wodeſtoke erle kent take hym cloſed enſealed wt owne ſeal whan ſir rogier vnderfēg lettre vncloſed ye lrē ſawe cōteyned theryn began rede wherof ye begȳ nȳg wurſhippes reuerēces wyt brother legaūce ſubiectione sir knight wurſhipfull ād dere brother yf yow pleſe praye hertely yt ye good confort ſhall ſo ordeyne yow ſone ye ſhull come oute pryſō delyured yt diſeſe yt ye ben great lorſhip ſhall vndreſtande haue cōſentȳg almoſt grete lordes englond wyt hyr apparaille ſaye wt armure treſour withoute nombre maynten̄ helpe quarell ferforth ye ſhull kyng ayene ye ād haue ſworn̄ vpō boke well prelate erles ād baron whē ſir rogier mortymer ſaw vnderſtode ye might ſtrength̄ letter punctel anone wrath hert gan ſwelle ād euyll hert bare toward ſir edmond erle kent ād ſo wyt haſte myght wente vnto dame iſabell quen̄ kȳges modre ſhewed hir sir edwardes lrē hys purpoſe coniectyd ād ordeyned put downe kīg edward wȳ deſore hir ſone ryalte ād kīgdome nowe certes ſir rogier quod quene hath ſir edmond done ſo fadre ſoule quod ſhe wull therof auenged yf god graunte lyfe ſhort tyme anone quene iſabel wente vnto kyng edward hir ſone parlemēt wȳcheſtre haue amē ded wronges treſpaces done amonge peple reaume tho toke ſhe ād ſhewed lettre ſir edmond wodeſtoke erle kēt made enſealed wt owne ſeal bad vpon hir benyſon ſhe ſhold auenged vpon hym vpon dedely enemye tho quene ſo wroth toward ſir edmond erle kent ād ceſyd never praye vnto hyr ſone tyll ſent haſt aftyr vpon kȳg ſent lettres ſir edmond wodeſtoke ſhold come ād ſpeke hym wȳcheſtre maner thing left whan ſyr edmond ſawe kyng ſent hȳ lettres enſealed haſted hȳ might tyll came wyncheſtre tho quene wiſt syr edmond come vnto wȳcheſtre anon̄ ſhe praied ſo faſt wēte vnto kyng edward hyr ſone syr edmond good erle areſtyd anone ād led vnto barre robert henaude coroner kynges houſhold aſſociated vnto hȳ ſir rogier mortimer tho ſpeke forſaid robert ād ſaid syr edmond erle kente ye ſhal vnderſtonde don̄ v wyte principaly vnto owr liege lord ſir edward kyng englond almighty god ſaue ād kepe ye hys dedely ennemye traitour alſo cōmune enemye vnto reaume ye haue bene aboute many day make preuy delyuerāce ſir edward ſom tyme kȳg englōd brother whiche put downe rialte cōmune aſſent lordes englond peſing owr lord kȳges aſtate alſo reaulme tho āſweryd good man ſaid ſoth ſir vnderſtonderſtondeth well neuer traytour kyng ne ye reame god ād world ferthermore kynges leue ſhal preue defende man owght tho ſayd mortimer ſir edmond ſo fer forth knowe yt may nat well gayneſaid ād p̄ſence ben̄ ſhalbe well prouyd hath fals mortimer ſam̄ lettre ſir edmond take ſyr iohan daueryll caſtell corff toke vnto kyng edward brother ſir edmōd wiſt ne ſuppoſed thing ſir iohan daueryll ben̄ ſo fals delyure hys lrē ſuche wyſe mortimer thought maner thing lettre ād ſaid ſir edmond ſhewed letter ſealyd axed knewe lettre ſeal ſir edmond loked theron avyſed longe printe ſeal might ſee lettre withȳ forth therȳ wiſt wel ſeall thought yt ſome letter bore grete charge thought thing lettre ād ſaid openly herȳg hem ye forſoth ſeall nat forſake loo quod mortimer sire ye heren hath ſaid knowelecheth lettre ſeal ye ſhul cōteyned theryn mortimere opened lettre foldē fore gedre red opȳli word word heryng hē all· whan letter red ſayd· • ſires ye haue herde wryten knowlegyd hys letter ſeal may go ther cryed yafe dome ſhold honged ād drawe heed ſmyt maner traytour hys heyres diſherited euermore ād ſo lad forth put priſō thys done quen̄ wiſt dampned wey lawe lyfe ād lymme heires diſherited euermore thrugh open knowlegyng pleyne court wherfor hē thought good forſaid ſir edmōd haſtly put deth withoute wityng ye kīg elles kyng lyghtely wolde foryeue hym deth thā ſhold turne hē moche ſorwe ſo empeched punctel anone quene thurgh coūceyll mortymer withoute othir coūceil ſent haſt baillyfs wȳcheſtre ſhold ſmite ſir edmondes hede wodeſtoke erle kent withoute maner abidȳg reſpite vp payne lyfe lymme ād ſhold haue none othir execucion cauſe tarieng natwithſtandyng iugemēt tho tokē baillifs ſir edmond oute pryſon lad hȳ beſides caſtell wyncheſtre made gonge fermer ſmyte hys hede none othir man durſt done ſo deyed ther allas tyme ſeye x day octobre thridde yere kȳg edwardes regne whan kyng wiſt therof wonder ſory louyd hī wel let entier frere minours wȳ cheſtre ¶of deth ſir rogier mortimer erle marche capitulo ccxxij ſo befell tyme ſir rogier mortimer erle march̄ ſo prowde ſo hauteyne helde lord reame pere ād tho became ſo couetous folowed dame iſabel quenes court kyng edwardes modyr beſete peny worthes wyt officiers ye quenes houſhold ſame maner kȳges officiers ād ſo made takȳg touchȳg vitailles alſo cariages dyd cauſe ſpēces gadre treſour ſo dyd wythoute nombre al might tho made hī wōdre ſecret wt ye quen̄ jſabel ſo moch̄ lorſhip retinue grete lordes englōd hȳ adrad whefore ye kyng hys coūceill toward hym angry ordeined amōge hē vndon̄ hym thurgh pure reſō lawe cauſe kȳg edward kynges fadre traytourſly thurgh hē mordred caſtel berkelee ſaid plenarli ye ccxvij chapitre boke ſome kīges coūceill loued ye mortimer told hym pryuete yt kȳg coūceill aboute frō day day hym ſhēd vndon̄ wherfor mortimer ſore ānoyed āgry ye deuel ayēs hē kȳ ge counceil ſaid yt wold ben̄ auēged ſo euer toke yt lōge afterward yt kȳg edward dame phelip hys wyfe dame jſabel kynges modre ſir rogier mortimer ne went vnto nothȳgham ther ſoiourne ſo befell quen̄ jſabell coūceill ye mortimer toke hir keyes yates caſtell nothinghā ſo yt man myght come nethyr ne oute night commaūdemēt mortimer neyther kyng ne non̄ coūceill yt tyme fell ſo yt mortimer malyce towardes kinges men pryncipally ayens hem hym accuſed king ye deth ſir edward hys fadre preuely coūceill take bitwen̄ quen̄ iſabell mortymer ye biſſhop lincoln ſir symōd bereford ſir hugh̄ ttrūpiton othyr pryue coūſeill vndon̄ hem accuſed mortymer vnto kīg fadres dethe treſon felonye wherfore tho kȳges coūceill whā wiſt mortymers caſtyng preuely came kȳg edward ād ſeydē mortymer wolde hē deſtroye cauſe thei accuſed kyng edwardes deth hys fadre praied hym wold maynten hē hir ryght theſe lordes purſwe quarell ſir wylliā moū tagu sir hūfrey de bogun sir willyā brother sir rouf ſtafford sir robert herford sir wylliā clinton syr iohā neuyll horueby many othyr hir conſent alle theſe ſworne vpō boke maynten̄ quarell moch̄ myght befell ſo aftyr ſir wylliam montagu ne none kȳges frēdes muſt ben̄ herburghed ī caſtel mortimer went token hyr herburghes dyuerſe place towne nothyngham ād tho ſore adrad lefte mortymer ſhold hem deſtroye haſt ther came vnto kīg edward syr wylliam mowntagu caſtel preuely told hym ne none hys coneſtable anſweryd ſaid kynges wille ſholde don̄ fulfylled moch̄ myght wolde nat ſpare maner dethe ād ſo ſwore ād made oth̄ tho ſayd forſayd ſir willyā moū tagu coneſtable herȳg hem helpyng vnto gracyouſly homage feautes scotlād wher put owte thurgh fals coūſeyll iſabell modre ād ſir rogier mortymer yt newe made erle marche capit ccxxiij ye haue herde lordes ſir iohan bailloll tyme pee ye ſcottes deſpyte hym called hym iohā turnelabard cauſe wolde offende ne treſpace ayens kȳg edward englond ſo forſoke reame scotland ſette therof littel pry ſir iohan lōge tyme dwelled fraunce baillol loued moch̄ ny ful pryue ſo iohan barnaby debate frenſhman ye toune dunpier ſo quelled hȳ went way might caſtell haue ſocour helpe lorde anone came officiers town̄ take iohan barnaby felō ſir edward lord halpe hym reſcued ād nigh̄t made wende owte caſtel punctel ād ſo went hys way ād came englond wythoute harme kyng fraūce ſaw ſir edward reſcued felō became wōder wroth ayens ſir edward anon̄ let hȳ areſtyd toke hande londe tho dwelled ſir edward pryſon vnto tyme yt ſir hēry beaumoūt came fraūce whych̄ henry ſō tyme erle angos scotland thurgh wyfe put oute forſaid pryue thought make deliurāee ſir edward baillols body might maner wiſe tho praied kȳg wolde graunte hem grace ſir edward baillols body vnto ye next parlement might liue wyt owne rētes men̄ tyme armes two thouſād archiers footman tho wē te ſhippe raueneſpore ſailled ſee till camen londe kynkehorne xij myle ſeint iohānes toune anone ſent oute hir ſhippes ayene ſhold nat hurte ne ēpired nethir man ſhold gon̄ ſhipp ayen̄ though thei nede· abide perilles flee▪ ſtonde rather ſuffre dethe flee maynten hir trewe quarell whā erle fiffe fers man ſtorne herd bailloll comen take lāde ſcotland came haſte kȳg horne x thouſand ſcottes diſtrouble ſhold nat come londe ſir edward bailloll companye diſcōfyted which̄ diſcō fiture ſir alizaūdre fetō quelled many othir erle fiffe tho ſory ful ylle ſhamed ſo littell companye diſcomfyted ſhamefully put hȳ cōpanye lyve flee tho came ſir edward bailloll toke contre aboute hym tyll came vnto ye abbey dū ſermelyne fownde vytailles hym hys folke amonge othir thȳges fonde chaūbre aboute v honderd grete ſtaues fyne oke longe pykes yren ſtelle toke hē delyured hē ye moſt ſtrengeſt men ꝯpanie anone wēt fro thēs loged hym felde ij myle ſeint iohānes towne ye burgeys toun̄ herd erle fiffe diſcō fyted thurgh ye bailloll ſore adrad brak brygges made ouer water erne ſo bailloll might gon̄ ouer wherfor logged hȳ night littell hede tok reſt ſaid vnto peple nowe fayre lordes ye knowe full well ben̄ nowe logged bitwen̄ enemy yf mowe v hampre ther bote deth̄ wherfor yf abyde nyght ſtyll thȳ ke ſhall turne v moche ſorwe harme power ſcottes may euery day wex ād encreſſe may ſo don̄ bene littell peple ayens hem wherfore pray loue almyghty god make v bolde hardy may myghtely take ſcottes nyght boldely werre vpon hem ād let v purſwe hem night trauailled thurgh v ād ſee hardyneſſe ſo othir ſcottes comen mete hem ſee hem ſo trauailled wery ſorer wull thei drad v fyght ād ferſly ſhull fyght wyt hē vpon hem purſwe ſo thurgh grace god almighty world ſhall ſpeke ye doughtyneſſe cheualrye ſyres vnderſtōdeth wel cōpanye comē wyth ſir erward bailloll graunted well vnto coūceil therof glad anone purſwed vpō ſcottes becomen wōder wery bailloll cōpanye ſore folowed hem dyd hē moch̄ ſorwe thurgh hir aſſaulte ſo yt might feble hem helpe ād littell peple tho ſaid ye ſcottes amonges hem befall ſo littell peple bailloll hath wynge don̄ v ſo moch̄ trauaille ſorwe certes ſemeth v wreccheth grace wōder ḡ cyous quarell certes ſhul ben̄ dede er may come hym v yelde ſith fadre ſette v pry amonge othir thinges ye bailloll paſſed watyr erne ſo ſir rogier swynerton̄ ſone fers angrj wente forth ſawe peple armes full well arayed forth wente vnto hem wyth hem fowghten quelled many wold abyde toke notheles ſame aſſaulte baillols men wende bene mooſt grete hooſte skotlande whan came morne gadred hē gedre rrſted hem whyle whyle englyſſhmen reſted hem noble baron thomas weſy alſo ye noble gentyll baron ſtafford pryked hyr horſes vp doune hylles kepe eſtres contre pryked vp downe ſaw grete hooſt good aray ordeyned thre wynges helmes ſheldes ſhynyng comyng vpon hem two ſayd lordes ſawe camē ayene vnto baillols folk wt grete haſt ſayd nowe loue god almyghty ben̄ good cō fort ye ſhall haue bataill anone ryght tho ſpake ſir fouke ſone gareyne worthy baron grete renomme dede armes syres lordynges vnderſtondeth well wull ſaye vnto yow haue ſeyn̄ many dyuerſe wynges well amō ge ſarazens jewes amonge ſcottes yet ſaw neuer tyme ferthe part wynge fyght therfore yf wyll abyde ennemyes ben ynowe fight ayens hē· yf good hert good wille fight wyt hem certes bene full fewe ayens companye ther loue god take vnto v good herte let v ben̄ bold thenke nether oure wyfes ne child cō quere hem bataille ād thurgh helpe lord god enemyes ſhull ouercome wyt came hoſte ſcottes toward hem full ferſly ayēs ſir edward bailloll iij batailles well araied armure ād wōder ferſly camen toward baillolls men ſir donald erle marchille ſawe ſaid robert brus ye ſone robert ye brus theſe wordes syr robert quod full ſore fortinketh myne hert yt thees folke bailloll hath brought ſhold deye wyt dynt ſcotteſſh ſwerd ſyth ben cryſten men well ben therfore thȳketh grete charite ſend vnto hem yelde hem vnto mercy grace raūſone hē thurgh grevous raunſone aſmoch̄ haue takē lād done ylle nowe certes quod ſir robert brus haue well perceyued thou art ennemye traitour vnto ſcotlād ſyth thow wilt conſente ſaue dedely enemyes haue don̄ v moche ſorwe ſhame nowe ſemeth wel ye ben hyr aſſēt certes robert quod ſir donald falſely ye lye j hir companye ne hir cōſent haſtely ye ſhul ſee fyght hem rather companye certes ſir robert ſaid j ſhal maugre thin heed aſſaille hē er thow prykedē hyr ſtedes ferſly vpon caſkemore wynges hem folewed rēche tho came ād mete bailloll companye hongyng bought ſtreit paſſage ſo faſt thei haſted hem vnto englyſſhmen ſo thouſendes fell ye groū de one vp yt othir hepe bothe hors ād man bailloll tho men mygthely ſtode ayens hem faſt quelled ſcottes vnto grounde many ſore wounded ſo longe tyll yt ſtoden vpon hem foyned hem hyr ſwerdes ād ſperes thurgh body ād ſo ſore trauaylled vpon hem till becamen full wery wiſt nat done ſcottes left lyve fleddē away ſaue hī ſelfe beſt maner might tho purſwed hē ſir edward bailloll men quelled hē tyll nyght fro then went vnto ſeint iohannes towne toke helde hem vitailled hē ſelfe hir owne wyll fō den ynowe wherwith make hē mery tho made bailloll hys men wounded gon̄ ſhipp wende englond hele hyr wowndes tyme ther flemmyng ſee ſtronge thefe robber called crabe flemmȳg driuen flaū dres wykkedneſſe ād therfore came ſcotland holde ſcottes moch̄ harme vnto englyſſhmen might crabbe met ye ſee ye baillols men woū ded ī bataille ſent ayen̄ englōd hele hyr woū de crabbe yafe vnto hem grete aſſaute wold haue quelled hē euerichon̄ engliſſhmen defended hem wel manly diſcomfyted crabbe cō ſcotlād ſo befell longe king scotland ne remeued came toune anaude toke dwellyng thyder came hȳ companye knightes ſtronge men worthy yelde hē vnto kyng bere hem ſo faire dede continaūce truſt moch̄ hem anon̄ traytours ſawe truſt moch̄ vpon hem ordeyned amonges hem fyfty companie ād wold haue quelled hir kīg thurgh grace almighty god brake thurgh wall hole chābre god wold aſcaped trecherie alle men quelled eſcapyd wt moch̄ drede vnto ye towne cardoill ther helde ſore annoyed befell ladyes eue conceptyō tho ſent kȳg edward bailloll kyng edward englond falſely traitourſly worde ſhold holde hȳ pee ſtille ye forſaid cite cardoylle till gadred power tho ordeyned kyng edward englond coū ceill london let gadre mē dyuerſe ſhires englōd redy wēte toward towne berewyke vp twede thyder came kȳg edward baillol ſcotland power beſieged towne made withowte towne fayre towne pauillons dyked hē aboute ſo drede ſcottes made many aſſaute gonne engynes toune wherwith deſtroyed many fayre howſes chyrches alſo bete downe vnto erthe grete ſtones ſpitouſely came oute gonne ād othir engynes· notheles ſcottes kepte well towne two kȳges might come therin lōge time notheles kȳges abyde ther ſo longe till thaȳ town̄ failled vitailles ād alſo ſo wery wakyng wiſten nat don̄ ye ſhul vndyrſtō de ſcottes ye towne berewyke thurgh commune coūceill hir aſſente let crye vpon walles toun̄ might haue pee englyſſhmen therof prai den king grace mercy praied hȳ trewes viij day vpon thys couenaunt yf reſcued ſide ye town̄ toward ſcotlād ſcottes withī viij dayes thei wold yelde hem vnto kȳg ād town̄ alſo holde thys couenaūt profred kyng xij hoſtages towne berewyke whē hoſtages delyured vnto king anone town̄ ſent vnto ye ſcottes told hem hyr ſorwe ād meſchief ſcottes camen tho preueli ouer ye watyr twede bought abbey ād ſir williā dyket tho ſtiward skotland many othir camen put hē grete peryll tyme hir lyfe thei camē ouer brigge brokē ye ſtones way many hir cōpanie drenched ye forſaid wylliā went ouer othir cōpanye came ſhippes englond quelled barge hull xvi men aftyr wēt īto towne berewyke ye watyr ſide wherfore ſcottes helde tho towne reſkued aſked hyr hoſtages ayen̄ kȳg englōd king ſent worde ayen̄ axed hoſtages wt wrōge ſith camē town̄ englōdes ſide ye couenaūt bitwen̄ towne ſhold reſkued ye halfe ſcotland anon̄ kȳg edward tho cōmaūded yelde town̄ wolde hange ye hoſtages ſcottes ſaid ye towne reſkued ynowe ther wold holde hē whā kyng edward ſawe yt ſcottes breke hir couenaūt thei made wōder wroth anone let take ſir thomas fitz willyā ſir alexandre ſetō wardeyne berewyk which̄ thomas perſon dūbare led theȳ alle othir hoſtages encheſō ſir alixaūdres fadre keper towne cō maūded euery day ij hoſtages towne ſhulde hanged tyll done vnto deth yf wolde yelde towne ſo ſhold teche hem breke hys couenauntes whā ye towne herde thees tydinges becamē wō der ſory ſentē kyng englond punctel wolde graūte hē viij dayes reſpite ſo bitwen̄ two hoūdred men armes ād xx men armes myght ſtrength̄ gon̄ bitwene hem towne berewyke hem vytaille town̄ muſt holde reſcued ſo xxi xxij ſlayne two hoūdred ſaid toune ſhold holde reſcued couenaūt holden ſent hym xij ye town̄ hoſtage kīg englōd graunted hē prayer ād toke hoſtages ſeynt margaretes euen yere grace mccc xxxij ſcottes came ferſely iiij wēges wel araied armes mete kȳg edward englōd edward king ſcotland wt hir power ād came faſt ād ſharpely ayens euē ſōge tyme ſame tyme flode berewyke watyr twede man myght wēte ouer hir hors foot watyr bytwen̄ two kynges reaume englond tyme abyden ye ſcottes othir ſide encheſon englyſſhmen ſhold haue ben̄ drownyd ſlayne aray ſcottes camen bataylles ayens two kynges englond ſcotlād vaūtward ſcotland theſe lordes capieulo ccxxiiij erle moryf james friſel symōd friſel waltier ſtyward reygnold theyne patrik grahā iohan le graūt iames cardoil patrike parkes robert caldecotes phelipp melledrum thoās gyllebert raufe wyſe man adā gurdone iohānes gramat robert boyde hugh̄ parke xl knyghtes newe dubbed ād vjc men armes iij commune ¶in fyrſt partie ye halfe bataille theſe lordes styward ſcotland erle mouref iames hys vncle punctel willyam douglas dauid kȳſdeſay· mancolyn flemmȳg william dunkau kamboke wyt xxx bachelers newe dubbed ſecond part bataill theſe lordes iames ſtiward cloden aleyn ſtyward williā abbrehyn williā moryce iohā fitz williā adam leinoſe walter fitz gillebert iohan cerlton robert walleham vijc mē armes ād xvijm commune ¶in thrydde part bataille ſcotlād theſe lordes erle marre erle roffe· erle ſtraherne erle ſotherl williā kyrkely iohan cambrō gillebert hay willyā rāſey williā prendegeſt kyrſtȳ harde williā gurdon arnold garde thomas dolphȳ xl knightes newe dubbed ixc men armes xvm cōmunes ¶in iiij warde bataill ſcotlād theſe lordes archehald dōglas erle leneuay alixaūdre le brus erle fif iohā cambel erle atheles robert lawecher william lonſtone iohā de labels· groos de ſherenlawe iohan de lȳdeſey alixaūdre de gray ingrā de vmfreville patryke de polleſworth dauid ye wymes michel scott williā lādy thomas de boy rogier de mortimer wyt xx bachelers newe dubbed ixc mē armes xviijm iiijc cō munes erle dūbare keper caſtell berewyke helped ſcottes l men armes ſir alixaūdre ſeton keper forſaid town̄ berewyke wyt hōdred men armes cō munes toune wyth iiij hō dred men armes wt hē viijc footmē ſōme erles lordes aboue ſayd ammoūteth lxvi ſomme bachelers newe dubbed ammoūteth hoūdred xl ſomme men armes ammoūteth mmmc ſomme cōmunes ammoūteth liijmcc ſō totall peple aboue ſaid ammounted lvimvijc xlv ād theſe lxv grete lordes laddē othir grete lordes aboue ſayd fowre batailles ſaid kȳg edward englōd edward kyng skotlād well apparailled folk foure bataylles fighte foot ayens hir enemy englyſh̄ minyſtrelles blewe trū pe pypes ād hydouſly aſcryed ſcottes tho euery englyſſh bataille two wȳ ge pry archiers whyche batalll ſhoten arewes ſo faſt ſo ſore scottes myght nat helpe hem ſelfe ſhoten ſcottes thowſandes grounde gon flee fro englyſſh men ſaue hir lyfe ¶and whan engliſſh̄ page ſawe ſcomfiture ād ſcottes fall faſt groūde priked hir mayſtres hors wyt ſpores kepe hē fro peryl ſet hir maiſtres force engliſſh men ſawe leptē hyr hors faſt purſued ſcottes abyden quelled doune right might mē ſee doughtyneſſe noble kyng edward men manly purſued ſcottes th̄at fledden drede myght men ſee many ſcottiſſh man caſt down̄ grownde dede· hyr baners diſplayed hakked pecys many good haberione ſtelle ī hir blode bathe many tyme ſcottes gadred company euermore diſcomfyted ſo befell god almyghty wolde ſcottes daye foyſon ne myght ayens englyſſhmen xx ſhepe ſholde haue ayens v wolfe ſo ſcottes diſcomfyted yet ſcottes wele v men ayens one englyſſhman bataille done halydonnehille beſides towne berewyke whyche bataille ſlayne ye ſcottes xxxvmvijc xij englyſſhmen onely xiiij footman victorye befel engliſſhmen ſeȳt margaretes eue yere ye incarnacyon lord iheſu criſt mcccxxxij yt doyng laſte englyſſh page toke pilfre ſcottes quelled euery mā might take withoute chalengyng men ſo gracious victorye kīg turned ayene vnto ſame ſiege berewyke whan beſieged ſaw herd king edward ſped yolden hym towne wyth caſtell morwe bataille don̄ ſeye ſeynt margaretes day kyng ordeyned sir edward baillol othir noble ād worthy men kepers ād gouernours ſcotland abſē ce hȳ ſelfe turned ayen̄ came englond victory moch̄ ioye wurſhip ād yere next ſewȳg ſaye yere incarnacion lord iheſu criſt mcccxxxiij kyng edward vij went ayen̄ ſcotlād wynter tyme which̄ viage caſtell kylbrigge ſcotland men wyt hȳ came recoured ayēs ſcottes wille one luſte ſame yere ſir edward baillol kyng ſcotlād helde parlement ſcotland wyt many noble lordes englond yt ſame parlement encheſon hir londes lordſhippes reaulme ſcotland heldē ſam̄ bailloll viij yere regne abowte feſt ſeȳt iohan baptiſt ſir edward baillol veray trewe kyng ſcotland herytage ād right lyne made hys homage feaute vnto kyng edward englond reame ſcotlād newe caſtell vpō tyne preſence many worthy lordes alſo cōmunes bothe reaume englond alſo ſcotlād anon̄ aftyr ſame yere kyng edward englond receyued duke bretaigne hys homage erledōme lordſhip richemond ſo folowyng yere hys regne mychelmaſſe kīg edward rood ſcotland ther faſt ſeint iohānes towne allmoſt wynter tyme helde cryſtmaſſe caſtell rokeſburgh ſame yere thurgh oute englond aboute ſeynt clementys tyde ye winter ther arroos ſuch̄ ſpryngyng wellyng vp water ād flodes both̄ ſee alſo freſſh̄ ryuers ſprynges ſee brynkes walkes ād coſtes breken vp men beſtes howſes ī many place namely lowe contrees wiolently ād ſodēly dreynt dryuē awey fruytes erthe thurgh cō tinuance habundaunce water ye ſee euermore aftyrward turned ſaltneſſe ſorweneſſe sauor x yere kȳg edwardes regne kȳg edward entred scottyſſh ſee aftyr mydſomer many ſcottes yafe bataill ouercame hem many treted ād bowed vnto hys pee thurgh doughtyneſſe mychelmaſſe thā next folowȳg erle morryf take edenburgh brought englōd put pryſon moneth iuyn̄ iuyll thā next folowyng xi yere hys regne appyred firmament bemed ſterre ye which̄ clerkes kalled ſtella comata ſterre ſeyne dyuerſe partyes ye firmamēt anon̄ folowed englond good ſhepe wonder grete plente chafre vitaille marchādyſe ther ayēs hōger ſcarcite meſchief nede money ſomoch̄ quarter whete londō ſold two ſhillyng good fat ox noble v good peious peny which̄ yere deyed ſir johan elthā erle cornewaille kyng edwardes brother lyeth weſtmynſter ¶how kyng edward made duchye erledome cornewaill alſo vj othir erles newe made ye fyrſt chalengȳg kȳgdome fraū ce capit ccxxv yere lord mccc xxxvij kīg edward xij ye moneth marche duryng parlemēt weſtmynſtre lent tyme kīg edward made erledome cornewaill duchye let calle duchye cornewaill which̄ duchie yaf vnto edward fyrſt ſone wyth erledome cheſtre alſo kȳg edward made ſame tyme vj othir erles ſeye ſir henri erle lancaſtres ſone erle leyceſtre william boghune erle northamptō williā mon̄ tagu erle salyſbury hugh̄ awdele erle glowceſtre robert vford erle sowthfolke williā clyton̄ erle hū tyngdone ſame yere ordeyned ye ſame parlement man ſhold cloth wrought oute englond cloth gold ſilke velvet damaſke latyn bā dekyn ne none ſuch̄ ne none wilde ware ne furre beyonde ſee ſuch̄ might ſpēd c pownde rent yere thys ordenaūce ſtatute lyttel effect thȳg holde ¶in xiij yere regne kyng edward wente ouer ſee braban wyth quen̄ philipp wyfe beryng chyld andewarpe dwelled yere trete wyt duke brabā eche othre allyed chalengyng kyngdome fraūce kȳg edward englond bi right inheritaunce aftyr deth karoll grete kȳg fraūce brother germayne quene iſabell kyng edwardes modyr apperteigned which̄ holden occupyed vnrightfully phelip valoys ye emes ſone kyng karoll which̄ duke ād hys forſaid thȳges othir therto belongyng wyt mē ād goodes kyng edward fonde redy vnto hȳ maden promyſed bitwene thaȳ ſeurte good fayth truſt aftyr kīg haſted englond ayen̄ left quen̄ ſtille behynde brakan xiiij yere hys regne whan ye lordes reame othir fallen parlement kalled aſſembled gedre ſame parlement holden london feſt ſeint hilarie kinges nedes put forth promoted touchȳg kȳgdome fraunce which̄ nedes ſped king axed ye fifthe part alle mevable goodes englōd wulles ix ſhefe euery corne ye fordes euery toun̄ wher ſuch̄ thīg ſhold taxed gadred ſhold anſwere kyng therof helde one luſt ād wherfor yf ſhall knowlech̄ veray trewth̄ ynner loue peple turned hate ād commune praiers kurſyng cauſe cōmune peple ſo ſtrongely greued alſo forſayd phelipp valoys fraūce gadred vnto grete hoſte deſtroyed hys partyes ād kȳgdome many kynges frendes englond townes caſtelles many othir hyr lorſhippes ād mani harmes ſhames deſpites dydē vnto quen̄ wherfor kȳg edward whē herde tidȳ ge ſtrongely meved therwith angred ſēte diuerſe lettres ouer ſee ye quen̄ frendes glading hē certefyēg hē wolde hȳ ſelfe haſte might anon̄ aftyr eſtre ſped thīg hym neded went ouer ſee ayen̄ who comȳg quen̄ frendes wondre glad made moche ioye enemy ayēs hȳ heldē maden moch̄ ſorwe ¶in ye ſame tyme kȳg thurgh coūceyl trew liege coūceil hys lordes ther preſent tokē kyng fraū ce name toke medled kȳ ge armes fraūce quartred armes englōd cō maunded forth hys coygne gold vndyr deſcriptiō wrytȳg ye name englōd fraū ce made beſt myght ſeye floryn̄ called ye noble pry vj ſhillyng viij pen ſterlinges halfe noble value iij ſhillynghes iiij pen ferthyng value xx pen kyng edward came sclus diſcōfyted power fraūce hauen capitulo ccxvi next yere ſay ye xv yere regne commaū ded let wryte chartres writtes othir letter date regne fraūce fyrſt thus doyng trauaillyng fraunce thurgh con̄ceill wrote prelate duke erles baron noble lordes contre ād alſo diuerſe cōmune peple diuerſe lettres maundemēts berȳgh date gandaune viij day februarye anone littell tyme came ayene englond wyt quen̄ chyldren ye ſame yere mydſomer eue • began ſaille toward fraunce ayene manly ſtyfly fille vpon phelip vajoys which̄ longe tyme lay gadred hī full grete meyne dyuerſe nacyons hauen sclus ād fowghten gedre kȳg fraūce hoſtes fro mydday vnto thridde hour morne which̄ bataill ſlayne xxxm men kinges companye fraūce many ſhippes kogges takē ād ſo thurgh goddes helpe ye victorie ād bere thēs glorious chiualrie ſame yere aboute ſeȳt james tide wytout ye yates ſeīt omers robert autheis wt men englond flaūdres bitterly faught ayens duke burgoygne frenſſhmrn which̄ bataill ſlayne take ye frēſſhmen xv baron lxxx knightes ſhippes barge takē vnto nōbre cc xxx ſame yere kyng makyng abydyng vpon ſiege turney erle henaude wyt engliſſh archiers madē aſſaute ye town̄ ſeint amēd ſlowe l knightes many othir ād alſo deſtroied town̄ ye xvj yere regn̄ folowyng wynter tyme ſame kȳg dwelled ſtill vpon forſaid ſiege ād ſent ofte englōd hys treſorier othir purneiours gold money ſhold ſent hym ther nede procuratours meſſagiers curſedly full flowly ſerued hȳ nede hȳ deceyued who defaute laches king toke trewes bitwen̄ hym kȳg fraū ce kyng full wo ſorwe ād ſhame hert drowe fro ſiege came britaigne· ther ſo grete ſtryfe vitaill loſt manj peple whē don̄ cam̄ dreſſed hī ouer ſee englond ward ſaylled toward englōd ye high̄ ſee ye moſte myſhappes ſtormes tēpeſtes thūdring lightnȳges fyll hȳ ye ſee whiche ſayd don̄ areiſed thurgh euyll ſpirites made bi ſorcery nygromācy hē fraū ce wherfor kynges hert full ſorwe anguyſſh weylyng ſighing ſaid vnto lady thys wyſe bleſſyd lady ſeīt marie cauſe euermore goyng fraūce alle thȳges wether fallē ioyefull lykyng wolde haue hē allewey turnyng englond ward thinges fallē vnprofytable ād harmefull neuyrthelater ſkapyng alle perilles ſee god wold came bi night tour londō ſame yere kīg held cryſtmaſſe meners ād ſent word scottes hys meſſagiers redy wold fight wt hem ſcottes wold abyde yt fledden ouer ſcottiſſh ſee ād hyd hē well might xvij yere hys regne abowte feſte cōuerſion ſeint paule kyng edward ſcotland ſawe skottes fledde came ayen̄ englōd littel befor lent turnement dunſtaple· which̄ turnement came yonge bachelerie cheualrie englond wyt many erles lordes whych̄ turnement kyng edward ſelfe preſēt next yere folowyng xviij yere hys regne hys parlement holden weſtmynſter quynzeme paſhe king edward ye thridde made edward hys fyrſt begoten ſone prynce walys xix yere regne anone aftyr ianiuer foreſayd ſame kyng edward let make full noble iouſtes grete feſtes place byrthe wyndeſore neuer none ſuch̄ ſeen ther which̄ feſt ryalte ij kinges two quenes ye prynce walys duke cornewaill x erles ix cownteſſes baron many burgeys whych̄ mighten lightely nombred dyuerſe landes beyonde ſee werē many ſtraūgiers ye ſame tyme whan iouſtes don̄ kyng edward made grete ſouper which̄ ordeyned fyrſt began rownde table ordeined ſtefaſted day forſaid rownde table holdē wyndeſore wytſon wyke euermore yerly ī tyme englyſſhmen ſo moch̄ han̄ ted cleued wodneſſe foly ſtrangers tyme comyng henawdres xviij yere paſſed ordeyned chawnged hem euery yere diuerſe ſhappes diſguyſyng clothyng lōge large wyde clothes deſtitut deſert frō olde honeſte ād good vſage othir time ſhort clothes ſtreite waſtyd bagged kyt euery ſide ſlatered botened ſleues tapites ſurcotes hodes ouer lōg ouermoch̄ hāgȳg ſothe ſhall ſaye lich tormauntours deueles hir clothȳg ād ſhoyng othir aray thā men woman nyfely yet paſſed men aray coriouſlaker ſo ſtreyt clothed let hange tailles ſowed bineth wythin hyr clothes hele hidde hir arſes ye which̄ diſguyſinges pryde pa • aduēture aft er ward brought forth cauſed many myſſhappes meſchief reame englōd xx yere kyng edward wēt ouer īto britaign̄ gaſcoigne who cōpanie wēt erle warrewyke ye erle ſouthfolk erle hūtȳgton ye erle arūdell many othir lordes ād ꝯmune peple grete multitude grete nauye cc xj ſhippes anone aftyr mydſomer auēge many wronges harmes hȳ don̄ phelipp valoys king fraūce ayēſt trewes hād graū ted· which̄ trewes falſely vntrewly cauellaciōs loſed ād diſquate ¶how king edward ſailed normādye arriued hogges grete hoſt ca cc xxvij xxi yere regn̄ kȳg edward thurgh coū ceill grete lordes reame englōd called ād gadred gedre parlement weſtmȳſter eſtrē ordeyned hī paſſe ouer ye ſee ayen̄ diſeſe deſtrouble rebelles fraūce nauye come gedre made redy wēt wt hugh̄ hoſt ye xij day iuyll ſailled normādye arryued hogges whā reſted hym vj dayes cauſe trauaillyng ſee haue oute men wyt hir neceſſaries oute hyr ſhippes wēt toward cadoun̄ brēnyng vaſtyng deſtroyng tounes yt fonde way xxvi day iuyll brigge cadony māly orpedli ſtrengthyd defēded wt normās ſtrōge bataille longe thurgh which̄ grete multitude peple ſlayn̄ ther take pryſoners ye erle ewe lord tākerwille c knightes men armes vjc footmē nombred ye towne ſubarbes vnto ye bare walles thing might bore caried owt robbed deſpoilled afterward king paſſyng forth cōtre aboute coūtre aboute brode xx mile vaſted maner thīg fōde whē phelip valoys ꝑceyued though faſt wt ſtronge hoſte wolde come nerre breke alle ye brigges beyōde ye watyr ſeyne fro rone vnto paris wyt ye haſt yt might ſoth noble kȳg edward whē came paris brigge fonde broken withȳ ij dayes let make ayen morwe aſſumptiō lady kȳg edward paſſed ouer ye watyr ſeyn̄ goȳg toward creſcy deſtroyed way tounes wt peple dwellȳg theryn feſt ſeȳt bartolomewe paſſed ouer ye water somme vnhurt wt hoſt neuer hand maner way ne paſſage wher ij ſlayn̄ hē letted hir paſſage ouer therfore ye xxvj day auguſt king edward feeld faſt creſey hauȳg iij batailles engliſſhmē coūtred ād met wt philip valoys hauyng wyt hȳ iiij batailles whych̄ leeſt paſſed gretli nōbre englyſſh peple whē thees ij hoſtes mettē gedre ther̄ fyll vpō hȳ king beme duke loreyne erles alſo flaū dres dalunſon bloys harecourt anmarle nevers many erles baron lordes knightes punctel men armes ye nōbre mvc xlij wtoute footman othyr men wel armed yt nothyng rekened vnvnglorious philippe withdrowe reſidue peple wherfore ſayd cōmune amōg owne peple noſtre beal ſoy retreyt ſeye fayr withdrawith thā king edward engliſſhmē thanked god almighty ſuch̄ victorie hir grete labour taken hem thyng nedefull hir ſuſtynaūce ſauyng hir lyfe drede hyr enemyes reſted hem full erly mornyng frenſſhmē wyt hughe hooſt came ayen̄ yeue bataille fyght wyt ye englyſſhmen whō mettē coūtredē erles warrewyke northāptō northfolk wyt hir cōpanye ſlowen two thouſand tokē many pryſoners gentills hem remanaunt ſame hoſt fledde iij myle thēs ye thridde day bataill kyng wēte caleys ward deſtroyng countre skotland wyt full grete multitude ſcottes came englōd nevilles croſſe aboute ſeȳt lucas day euāgeliſt hopȳg truſtyng haue fondē londe deſtytute voyde peple aſmoch̄ kȳg englōd beyōde ſee ſaufe mariner othir orped fyghtȳg men coūtre· diſparkled hem aſſhamed went home ayen hir owne coūtre amōg ther boyſtons ād ſtronge veſſel hir nauye ouerſailled engliſſhmen periſſhed dreynt which̄ ye ſtyward othir worthy grete men dēmark take pryſoners ād kyng englōd counceill pryſoned which̄ lordes dane afterward came ſoughten aboute haue gooddes loſt wele payed ne pleſyd anſwere herē turned homewardes ayen̄ leuȳg behȳde hem ynnes prevely wrytē ſcrowes wale yet ſhulld dane waſt wane thā happed ther englyſſh wryter wrote ayēs dane maner wyſe ſhul dane fet herbanes ſame time pier kyng spaigne kynges ſaye kyng naverne kyng malogre beyng menes wētē praied coūceill helpe ſir edward prince thurgh who coūceil whē vnderſtond hir article ād deſire required kynges lothe aſhamed ſay nay contrarie hē notheles gaſt leſt ſhold preiudyce ayens pope lōge time taried hem wold graūte conſent therto till bettyr coūceill avyſement good deliberaciō kyng edward getter hys fadre ¶but euery day continuell beſechinges many noble men requyred ād ſpoken wyth many prayer ſent made bytwene hem prynce edward ſent hys fadre bothe pleynynge letter alſo confortable conteinyng alle hyr mynyſtres ryght lybertees defende hir ennemyes euelles ther ayens bitterly puniſſhe deſtrouble rightes lybertees priueleges holy chyrche encreſe mayntene amende thȳges wrōgfully betakē withdrawe ce wher gete hem littell wurſhyp ād nauye ther huge ooſt frenſſhmen vpō chalkhull brigge ād othir hoſte alſo englyſſhmē faſte ſame brygge lōge tyme leyne many worthy men grete englyſſhmen ordeyned yafe coūceill fight ād yeve bataille frēſſhmē forſayd lordes wolde nothing conſent therto ne aſſent maner thynge ther anon̄ happed erle warrewyk came thidderward werre whā frenſſhmē herd coming er came fully lande left hir tē te pauillons hir vitailles fledden went away preuely whan erle comen land hys men went haſt toward normā dye deſtroyed ile caw thurgh dynt ſwerd ād thurgh fyre allas retournyng englond ward home ayen̄ caleys take wyt ſikeneſſe peſtilēce deied leuȳg behȳde hym aftyr hys dayes ſo noble knight orped armes whiche tyme regned ād werred ye orped knight ſir iohā hawkewode englyſſhmē borne hauȳg wyth gouernaūce whit companye fore nempned· whiche ſome tyme ayens holy chyrche ſome tyme ayens lordes werred ād ordeyned grete batailles therin cōtre dyd many mervaillous thynges aboute ye conuerſion ſeynt paule kyng whā ended done enthering axequyes wyt grete coſtes rialtes aboute ſepulture berieng quene phelypp wyfe helde parlement weſtmynſter whiche parlement axed clergie thre diſmes ſaye grete diſme paied thre yere durȳg clergie put ād wold graunte vnto eſtre next comyng graūted wele ī thre yere bi certeyn termes diſme ſhold paied alſo ye lay fee iijxviiies graunted king payed thre yeres ¶how ſir robert knolles wyth certeyne lordes reaume went ouer ſee fraunce hir gouernaūce capitulo ccxxxiiij xlv yere king edward begynnȳg kyng edward wyt vnwyſe counceyll vndiſcrete borewed grete ſomme gold prelatz lordes marchaūts othir riche men hys reaume ſeyng yt ſhold diſpended defendȳg holy chirche hys reaume ſaufwithȳ caſtell britaigne frēſſhmē ſawe men deuyded dyuerſe company place nat holdyng ne ſtrēgthyng hē gedres ought fyllē ferſely men moſte partye tokē hē ſlowē hē tho toke led wt hē priſoners ſame yere pope vrban came fro rome auion̄ encheſon cauſe yt ſhold accord make pee bitwen̄ kīg fraūce kȳg englond euermore allas begā hys tretes deyed wt ſikenes xxi day decēbre buried englyſſhmē flēmȳges punctel engliſſhmen victorie tokē xxv ſhippes charged wyt ſalt ſleyeng drenchȳg men theryn vnwytȳg hem cōtre redly moch̄ harme falle bycauſe therof ne pee accord ye ſonner bytwene hē made thys ſame yere frēſſhmē beſieged town̄ rochell wherfore erle pēbroke ſent gaſcoigne grete companie men armes deſtroye ſiege whych̄ paſſed ſee came ſauf hauen rochell whē hauen mouth might entre ſodēly came vpō hē ſtronge nauye spaigne which̄ ouercame tho ye englyſſhmen moch̄ blemyſſhyng hurtyng ſleyng many perſones moche englyſſhmē redy fyghte ne ware hē comīg vpō spaignardes alle englyſſhmē othir take ſlayne x hem woūded deth· hyr ſhippes brēt toke ye erle wyt huge treſoure ye reame englōd many othir noble men alſo mydſomer euen which̄ ſeīt etheldredes mayre lōdō william walworth ye tyme comen wt aldermē commune ye cyte came ſouthwerke knowe intēcyon theſe rebelles myſgouerned peple iake ſtrawe thā made oye feld peple accord ſhold come nere proclamacyō crye lordes ād mayre ye aldermē wyt cō minalte hauīg indignaciō couetyſe falſeneſſe hys fowle p̄ſūpcyon anon̄ williā walworth ye time beyng mayr drowe owt knyf ſlowe iak ſtrawe ād anon̄ right ther dyd ſmyte hede ſette vpō ſpere ſhafte ſo bere thurgh lōdō ād ſet hygh̄ vpō lōdō brigge anon̄ thees ryſers ād myſgouerned mē voide ād clene vaniſſhed nought ye kīg grete goodneſſe praier lordes made vj knightes good worthy men cyte londō ſaye williā walworth tyme mayre ſlowe iak ſtraw ſeconde nycholas brēbre thridde johan philiptot iiij nycholas twiford v robert laū de vj robert gayton kyng lordes ād knightes retourned ayen̄ vnto tour londō ther reſted tyll peple better ſeted ſette reſte pee proceſſe tyme myght gete ād take thes rebelles ryſers henge hem vpon nex galewes euery lorſhyp thurghoute reame englōd xl xxx x ād xij euer might geten takē party v yere kyng rychardes regne ye grete erthe quak▪ generally oute world ye woneſday witſonday yere lord mccclxxxxi wherof maner peple wer̄ ſore agaſt dred full longe tyme drede vengeaūce lord ſhewed dyd vj yere regne kȳg richard ſir hēry ſpencer biſſhop norwiche went wyth croiſerie ouer ſee ye coū tre flaūdres gate towne grauenyng ye toune broburgh dunkerk newport ād ther laded fraught • j ſhippes pelage haue come englond theſe ſhippes gooddes ye byſſhop norwych coūceil let brenne thees ſhippes wyt ye pelage ſame hauen hard aſſhes dunkerke done grete bataille bytwene flēmȳges englyſſhmē bataille ſlayne grete multitude flēmȳ ge huge nōbre wēt biſſhop retenwe vnto ypre beſeged longe tyme might goten ſo lefte ſiege came ayen̄ englōd englyſſhmē foull deſtroyed many deyed flixe ſame yere came quene anne englōd ſpouſed vnto kyng rychard hir fadre emperour almaigne kyng beme ād came duke taſſy vncle many worthy lordes knightes hyr cōtre beme duche toū ge hir reuerēce wurſhip ſir ſimōd beuerle worthy knight garter othir knightes ſquyers werē kynges embaſſatours brought hyre englond ſo forth lō dō peple cyte ſeye mayre ye alderman ād cōmunes riddē ayēs hyr welcome hyr euery man good aray euery crafte mynſtralſie beſt maner mete hir blakheth kent ſo brought hir vnto lōdō thurgh cyte ād ſo forth vnto weſtmynſtre vnto kȳges paleys ther ſhe ſpouſed vnto kyng rychard wel worthely abbey weſtmynſtre ther ſhe crowned quen̄ englōd hir frendes camen hir haddē grete yeftes werē well chered refreſſhed longe tyme abydē thys ſame yere bataille done kīges paleys weſtmynſtre certeyn poȳtes treſon bytwene ſir iohā anſley knight defendant ād carton ſquier appelaūt ſir iohā āſley ouercame carton made yelde withyn ye lyſtes punctel anon̄ carton deſpoilled harneys drawen oute lyſtes ſo forth tiborne honged falſeneſſe ye viij yere regne kyng rychard ſir edmōd lāgely erle cābrigge kȳges vncle wēte portyngale wyt fayre meyne mē armes archiers ſtrēgthyng helpyng kȳg portyngale ayens kyng spaygne power ther kyng portȳgale victorie enemy thurgh helpe cōfort englyſſhmē whē iourney done erle cā brygge came home ayē peple englōd haſte bleſſed god hys gracyous yifte am̄ ſame yere kyng richard helde cryſtmaſſe marche eltham ſame tyme kyng ermonye fledde owte hys owne land ād came englond haue ſocour helpe kyng ayens hys enemyes dryuen hȳ oute hys reame ſo h̄e brought vnto kyng elthā kyng helde hys ryall feſt criſtmaſſe owr kyng welcomed ād dyd moch̄ reuerence wurſhipp cōmaunded lordes make hȳ chere cowde beſought ye king grace helpe hys comfort nede myght brought ayene hys kyngdome lōde turkes deuoured deſtroied moſte part lōde thys cauſe fledde came thyder ſocour helpe kȳg then̄ hauyng pyte cōpaſſyon hys grete meſchief ād grevous diſeſe anone toke counceyll aſked beſt don̄ anſweryd ſaid yf lyked yeue good· well don̄ towchyng hys peple trauaylle ſo ferre oute landes grete jupardie ſo kyng yafe hȳ gold ſiluer many rycheſſes yeftes iewelles betaught god ſo paſſed ayene oute englōd ſame yere kyng rychard wyt ryall power went skotland werre vpon ſcottes falſeneſſe deſtructiō scottes don̄ vnto englyſſhmē march thā ſcottes came vnto kīg entrete wyt lordes trewes certeyne yeres ſo kīg coūceyll graūted hē trewes certeyne yeres vnto aſkyng kyng turned hī home ayen̄ englōd whan come vnto york punctel ther abode reſted hym ſir iohan holād erle kētes brother ſlow erles ſone stafford hys heir wyth dagar th̄e cyte york wherfor kīg ſore ameued greued remeued thēs came lōdō mayre alder men commune ſolempnite yt myght done ryden ayēs ye kīg brought ryally thurgh cyte ſo forth vnto weſtmynſter vnto owne paleys ye ix yere kȳg rychardes regne helde ꝑlement weſtmȳſter ther made two duke marqueyes v erles fyrſt yt made duke kinges vncle ſir edmond langlee erle cambrigge hȳ made duke york ¶and vncle ſir thomas wodeſtoke erle bukkyngham hym made duke glouceſtre ſir lyonevere erle oxūford hym made markeys dyueleyne henry bolyngbroke duke ſone lancaſtre hȳ made erle derby ſir edward ſone yorke hī made erle rutcelōd sir iohā holād erles brother kent made erle hūtȳgdō sir thomas monbray erle nothȳghā erle marchall englōd ſir mychell de la pole knyght hȳ made erle sowthfolk chaunceler englond erle marche ſame parlement holden weſtmȳſter playne ꝑlement among lordes cōmunes ꝓclamed erle marche heire apꝑant crowne englond kyng rychard which̄ erle marche wēt ouer ſee irland vnto lordſhippes londes erle marche erle vlſter irland right lyne herytage ther ye caſtell hys lay tyme ther came vpon grete multitude buſſhemētys wild iriſſhmen hȳ take deſtroye came owte ferſely hys caſtell hys peple ād mā ly faught wyt hem ther take hewe peces ther deyde who ſowle god haue mercy amen x yere kyng rychardes regne erle ot arundell went vnto ſee wyt grete nauye ſhippes enarmed mē armes good archiers camen brode ſee mette wyt hole flete camen wyt wyne laden rochel which̄ wyne enemyes goodes· ād ther nauye ſet vpon hem ād toke hem browght hem vnto dyuerſe porte ād hauenes englond ſome londō ther ye might haue tonne rochel wyne beſt xx ſhillīg ſterlynges ſo grete chepe wyne thurghoute reaume tyme thanked god almyghty v lordes aryſen rattecoſte brigge capit ccxli regne kyng rychard xi yere v lordes aryſē rattecort brigge deſtructyon rebelles tyme ye reame firſt v lordes syr thomas wodeſtoke kȳges vncle duke glouceſtre ſecōd ſir rychard erle arundell iij ſir rychard erle warrewyk ye iiij ſir hēry bolȳgbroke erle derby v ſir thoās mō bray erle nothȳghā theſe v lordes ſaw meſchyef myſgouernaūce ād falſeneſſe kȳges counceyll wherfore tyme chyef ye kynges coūceyll fleddē owte lād ouer ſee ſaye ſir aliſaūdre neuill ye erthebiſſhop york ſir robert leveer markeys deuelyn erle orēford ſir mychel de la po • le erle sowthfolk chaūcheler englōd theſe iij lordes wentē ouer ſee came neuer ayen̄ deyde thā theſe v lordes aboue ſayd maden ꝑlemēt weſtmȳſtre ther thei toke ſir robert trefiliam chef juſtyce ſir nycholl brēbre knyght cytezeyne lōdō ſir iohan ſalibury knyght ye kīges howſhold vſke ſergeaūt armes ād many mo othir peple werē take iugged vnto ye deth ye coū ceyll theſe v lordes hyr parlemēt weſtmȳſtre treſō put vpō hē drawen frō ye tour london thurghoute cyte ſo forth vnto tyburne ād ſhold hōged trothetes kut thus ſerued deyd ſame parlemēt weſtmynſtre ſir symōd beuerlee worthy knight garter punctel ſir iohan beauchamp knight ſtiward kynges howſhold ſir james berners iuged vnto deth lad fote toure hyll ād werē hyr hedes ſmyten many othir mo theſe v lordes ſame ꝑlement xij yere kyng rychardys regne let crye ordeyne generall iouſtes kalled turnemēt lordes knightes squyers jouſtes turnemēt holdē london ſmythfeld maner ſtraūgiers lōde coūtre euer thydder right welcome ād hem othir holdē open houſhold grete feſtes alſo grete yeftes yeuen maner ſtraūgiers kynges ſyde werē ſute hir cote hir armures ſheldes hors trappure white hertes wyt crownes aboute hir nekkes chaynes gold hauȳg thervpon crowne hauyng low hertes body whiche herte kynges lyuery yafe lordes lady knyghtes ſquyers knowe hys houſhold othir peple feſt comyng jouſtes xxiiij ladyes lad theſe xxiiij lordes gartes wyth cheynes gold ſame ſute hertes afore ſaid tour horſebak thurgh cite london ſmythfeld ther yt ye iouſtes ſhold holde feſtes iouſtes hold general thaym wold come land nacyon euer hold duryng xxiiij dayes kynges coſt thees xxiiij lordes āſwere maner peple wold come thyder thyder came erle ſeynt poule frawnce many othir worthy knyghtes wyth hȳ dyuerſe partyes full well araied oute holand ād henaud came ye lord oſtreuaūt duke ſone holand many othir worthy knyghtes hym holand full well arayed feſte iouſtes ended kīg thā ked theſe ſtraūgiers yafe hȳ many grete yeftes thā token hir leue kyng othir lordes ladyes wē tē home ayene hir owne cō tre grete loue ād moch̄ thāk xiij yere kyng rychardes regne ther bataill done kȳges paleys weſtmynſtre bytwene squyer nauerne kȳg rychard othir squyer kalled iohan walſſhe poyntes treſon thys nauerous put vpon walſſhmā nauerous ouercome yelde creaunt aduerſayre anon̄ deſpoiled armure drawe oute paleys tibourne ther honged hys falſeneſſe xiiij yere kīg rychardes regne ſir iohā gaūte duke lācaſtre wēt ouer ſee spaigne chalenge right wyfes title vnto croune ſpaign̄ wyt grete hoſt peple mē armes archiers wyt hym ducheſſe wyfe iij doughters ouer ſee ſpaign̄ grete laſt kīg spaigne began trete wt duke lācaſtre ād accorded gedre thurgh bothe counceill maner yt kȳg ſpaign̄ ſhold wedde duke doughter lācaſtre right heire spaigne ſhold yeve vnto duke lācaſtre goold ſiluer caſt grete wegges many othir iewelles many viij chariettes might carie euery yere lyfe duke lācaſtre ducheſſe wife xm mark gold which̄ gold ye auenture charge ſpaign̄ ſhold auēture brȳg yerely vnto bayone duke aſſignes ſurete made alſo duke lācaſtre maried othir doughters vnto ye kyng portingale ſame tyme whē don̄ thus came home ayē ēglōd good lady hys wyfe alſo many worthy mā vpō flix yt viage deyed xv yere king rychardes regn̄ helde criſtmaſſe march̄ wodeſtoke erle pēbroke yōg lord tēdre age wold lerne iouſte wt knight yt called ſir iohā ſeȳt johā ridē gedre parke wodeſtoke ād worthy erle pēbroke ſlayne wt othir knightes ſperes keſt frō hȳ whā cōpled thus good erle made ende therfor kȳg quen̄ made moch̄ ſorwe deth ī xvj yere kīg rychardes regn̄ johā hēde beyng yt time mayre lōdō punctel iohā walworth hēry vāner beyng ſherewes lōdō yt ſame time baker mā bare baſket horſbrede fleetſtrete toward hoſtre ther came yomā biſſhoppes ſaliſbury yt called romaȳ toke horſelofe owte baſket baker aſked hȳ dyd ſo· romaȳ turned ayen̄ brake baker hede neyghbours cam̄ oute wolde haue areſted thys romaȳ brake frō hē fledde vnto lordes place cōſtable wold haue hȳ ye biſſhoppes mē ſhet faſt yates kept place yt mā might entre thā moch̄ peple gadred thyder ſaid wold haue oute elles wolde brēne vp place withyn came mayre ſherewes wyth othir moche peple ceſſed malyce ye cōmunes made euery man go home hir howſes kepet pee romayns lord ye byſſhop saliſbury maiſtir johā walthā yt tyme treſorer englond went ſir thomas arundell erchebiſſhop york alſo chaū cheler englōd ther ye biſſhop made cōplaynt vnto ye chaū cheler vpon peple cyte lōdō thā theſe ij biſſhoppes grete malice venyaūce came vnto kyng wyndeſore made grete compleynt vpō ye mayre ſherewes anon̄ cyte afterward befor kyng coūceyll caſt vnto cyte grevous hert wōder grete malyce anon̄ ſodenly kȳg ſent ye mayre london two ſherewes ād came vnto hym vnto caſtell wyndeſore kȳg rebuked mayre ſherewes full foully offēce thei done ayēs officiers chambre london wherfore depoſed put owte mayre both̄ ſhrewes thys doū xiiij dayes afore feſte ſeȳt iohā baptiſt thā kyng kalled hȳ knyght yt called ſir edward delingryge made hȳ wardeyne gouernour cyte chambre lō ouer peple theryn ſo kept offyce iiij wekes cauſe ſo gentyll tendre cytezeins lō wherfor king depoſed hī made ſir baudewyne radȳgtō knight cōtroller kynges houſhold wardeyne gouernour chambre peple therin choſe vnto hȳ two worthy men cyte ſherewes hym gouerne kepe kynges lawe cite one kalled gillebert mawefeld othir thomas newenton ſherewes mayre ij ſherewes alle aldremen wyt worthy craftes londō wente foot vnto toure ād came oute conſtable towre yafe mayre ſherewes hyr othe charge thei ſhold haue take eſcheker weſtmynſtre kynges court hys iuſtyces baron eſcheker went home ayen̄ kȳg coūceil grete malyce deſpyte cyte londō remeued courtes weſtmȳſtre vnto cyte yorke ſaye chaūcelerie eſcheker kynges bēches commune place ād ther held theſe courtes lawe fro mydſomer ſeye· feſt ſeȳt johan baptiſt vnto feſt criſtmaſſe next ſewyng king coūceil ſaw profitable lōdon anon̄ remeued ayene vnto londō ſo weſtmynſtre grete eſe officyers ād avauntage king cō munes reame· whan peple londō ſaw knewe thees courtes come ayene ye kȳg peple alſo then̄ mayre alderman wyt chief commune cite let gadre grete ſomme gold ye cōmunes cyte ordeyned made grete ryalte ayēs comȳg london haue grace good lordſhip ād alſo hir libertees fraunchiſes graū ted vnto hem ayen̄ fore tyme hadde thā grete inſtaūce praier quen̄ anne othyr lordes lady kyng graūted hem grace ād done ſhene futhereie kyng withȳ two dayes aftyr came londō mayre londō ſherews aldermē worthy mē cyte afterward ridden ayens king good aray vnto heth ſide maner ſhene ſubmyttȳg hem hūbely mekely wyth maner obeiſſaūce vnto hym thei ought don̄ thus brought kyng quene lōdō ¶and kyng came forſayd yate brugge london preſented hym mylk white ſtede ſadled brydled trapped wt clothe gold rede parted gedre quene palfrey white ye ſame araye trapped wt white reed condytes london ronnē wyt white wyne both̄ white rede alle maner peple drynke bitwene ſeynt poweles croſſe cheep made ſtage ryall ſtanding vpon hygh̄ therynne many angel wyt dyuerſe melody ſonge angle came downe frō ye ſtage hygh̄ vyſe ſette crowne gold pight rych̄ perle ād precious ſtones vpon kynges hede ād othyr vpon quenes hede ſo cytezeyns brought ye king quen̄ vnto weſtmynſtre hyr paleys thā morne mayre ſherewes alderman londō camē vnto kyng paleys weſtmynſter preſented hȳ wt ij baſȳs ſiluer ouer gilt full coyned gold punctel ſomme xx c pownde prayeng hȳ hys hygh̄ mercy lordſhyp ſpicyall grace myght haue hys good loue wt ye libertees fraūchiſes lyke haue tymes lrēs patētz hys chartre confermed quen̄ ād othir worthy lordes ād lady fell knee beſought ye kȳg ḡce cōferme thȳg thā ye king toke vp quene graūted hyr hyr aſkyng thā thāked kyng quene wentē home ayen̄ ¶and xvi yere kyng rychardes regne certeyne lordes skotlād came englond gete wurſhyp foot armes theſe ye perſones erle marre chalenged erle marchall englond iouſte certeyne pointes horſebake ſharpe ſperes ryddē gedre two worthy knyghtes ād lordes certeyne courſes full chalenge scottyſſh erle made caſt both̄ hors man ād two rybbes broke wyt fall ſo borne home oute smythfeld hys yn withȳ littell tyme caryed hom̄ward lytier yorke ther deyde ſir willyam darell knyght banerer ſcotlād made othir chalēge wt ſir pier courteyne knyght kynges banerer englōd certeyne courſes horſbake ſame felde whē riddē certeȳ courſes ſaw might haue ye bettyr yafe ouer wold chalēge turned hys hors rode home hys own̄ loggȳg one cokkeborn̄ ſquier ſcotlād chalēged ſir nychol haworke knight certeī courſes wt ſharp ſperes horſbake ryddē v courſes gedre euery courſe ye ſcotte caſt downe both̄ hors mā thꝰ engliſſh lordes thāked god haddē felde ye xvij yere kīg richardes regne deide ye good gracious quen̄ anne yt wyfe kȳg rychard ye maner ſheū ī ſhire furre vpō witſōday thā ſhe brought lōdō ſo weſtmȳſtre ſhe beryed worthely entered beſide ſeint edwardes ſhryne who ſowle god haue mercy amē ¶how kīg richard ſpouſed dame iſabel kȳges doughter fraūce ye toune caleys brought hir englōd let hir crouned quen̄ ye abbey ſeint peter weſtmȳſtre ca ccxlij ye xx yere kīg richardes regne wēte hī ouer ſee vnto caleys wt duke erles lordes barōs many othir worthi ſquiers wt grete araye ꝯmune peple reame good araye appertyned ſuch̄ worthi kīg prīce nobley own̄ ꝑſone don̄ hȳ reuerēce obſeruaūce ouzt don̄ vnto hir liege lord mighty kȳg emꝑour ī owene abyde ād receyue worthy gracyous lady ſhold ben̄ hys wyfe yonge creature xix yere age dame iſabell kȳges doughter fraū ce many othir worthy lordes grete name bothe baron knyghtes wyt moch̄ othir peple camen vnto towne grauenyng ij duke fraūce one duke burgoigne duke barry yt wold ferther laſſe thā thei plegges hē thā kyng rychard delyured two plegges hem go ſauf ād come ſauf two worthy vncles duke glouceſtre duke yorke two wentē ouer ye watyr grauenȳg abydē ther plegges vnto ye tyme mariage feſte don̄ thees ij duke fraūce come ayen̄ vnto greuenȳg watyr thees two worty duke came ouer water grauenȳg ſo caleys wt hys wurſhipfull lady dame iſabell yt kīges doughter fraū ce ād hir came many worthi lord ladi knightes ſquyers beſt araye might metten meyne caleys ye whych̄ welcomed hyr hir meyne beſt honour reuerēce might ād ſo brought towne caleys ſhe receyued wyt ſolēpnyte ād wurſhip might done vnto ſuche lady brought hyr vnto kyng kyng toke hyr welcomed hyr ād hir fayre meyne made ſolempnyte myght done king coūceill aſked ye frēſſh lordes whethyr couenaūtes forewardes wyt compaſſyon ordeyned made bothe party ſhold trewly kepte holde bytwene hem ſaid ye ād ſworne toke hir charge vpon boke made hyr othe well trewely hold maner pointes couenaūts withowte contrdaictyō delaye maner wyſe punctel ſhe brought vnto ſeint nycholas chyrche caleys ſhe worthely wedded wt moſte ſolēpnyte kyng quen̄ myght erchebiſſhop biſſhoppes mynyſtres holy chyrch werē brought home vnto caſtell ſet mete ſerued maner delicaſie ryall metys drinkes plenteuoiſely maner ſtrāgiers othir creature warned yt feſte welcome grete halle tentes ſette vpon grene withowte caſtell receyue maner peple euery offyce redy ſerue hē thus worthy mariage ſolempnely done endeth ryalte· theſe two duke fraunce wyth hir peple token hyr leue kyng quene wenten ayen̄ grauenyng water frenſſh lordes ſeye two duke hyr meſone comen ouer ye watyr greuenyng metten euery toke leue othyr ſo departed owr lordes camen ayen caleys frenſſh lordes wente ouer watyr ſo home fraunce ayene anon̄ aftyr kyng made hym redy quene hys lordes ladyes hir peple hem camen ouer ſee englond ſo lō mayre ſhereues wyth alderman worthy commune ryddē ayens hem vnto blake heth ket metten wyth ye king quen̄ ād welcomed hem good aray euery man clothyng crafte mynyſtrelles fore hem ād ſo brought hem vnto ſeīt george barre ſowthwerke toke hyr leue punctel kyng quene rydden kenygton peple lō turned home ayen̄ turnyng ayene lōdō brygge ſomoch̄ preſſe peple bothe hors ād foot dede brygge xj perſones men womē chyldrē who ſowles almyghty god haue pyte mercy amen aftyrward quene browght vnto towre londō ſhe nyght morwe ſhe brought thurgh cyre lōdō ouer ſo forth vnto weſtmȳ ſtre ſhe crowned quene englond ſhe brought ayene kȳges paleys holde open ryalle feſt hyr coronacyō maner peple thyder came don̄ ſonday next aftyr feſte ſeynt clement xx yere kȳg rychardes regne ¶and thā xxv day auguſt next euell excitacion fals coūceill grete wrath malyce kȳg olde time vnto hys vncle ye good duke glouceſtre erle arundell erle warrewyke anon̄ kyng euell excytacyon euyll counceyll malyce late euenȳg ſame day aboue ſayd made hym redy ſtrength rode eſſex vnto toune chelmeſford ſo came place ſodenly good ſir thomas wodeſtoke gē till duke glowceſtre lay place than̄e good duke came welcome kȳg anon̄ kyng areſted good duke ſelfe hys owne body ſo lad downe ye watyr anon̄ put ſhyp anon̄ lad vnto caleys ād browght capyteynes warde kept holde kynges cōmaūdemēt englond tyme ye erle marchall capyteyne caleys anone aftyr commaūdemēt kīg fals coūceill commaunded capiteȳ put hȳ dethe ād anon̄ certeyne yomen te good duke kepyng toke hyr counceyl wold put hym vnto deth ād hir appoȳtemēt ſhold come vpō hȳ whā hys bedde ād ſlepe fethyr bedde ād anon̄ boū de hym foot ād honde ād charged hym lye ſtyll ād don̄ thus tokē two ſmale towailles made hī two rid knottes caſt towailles aboute duke nekke ād thā tokē fethir bedde lay vndyr hym caſt aboue thā drowen hyr towailles eche weyes ſome lay vpon fether bed vpō hym vnto tyme dede cauſe ſhold make noyſe ād thꝰ ſtrēgled worthy duke vnto deth who ſowle god hys hygh̄ pyte haue mercy amen whan kyng areſted worthy duke hys vncle ſent hym caleys came ayen̄ londō haſt wyt wonder grete peple ſone come ſent erle arūdell good erle warrewyk anon̄ came areſtyd hē hym ſelf ſir iohā cobhā ſir iohā cheyne knyghtes areſted hē hym ſelfe ye ſame maner tyll made parlemēt▪ anon̄ put hold ye erle arūdell went large vnto parlemēt tyme foūde ſufryſant ſurete abyde lauwe āſwere maner poȳtes kyng hys con̄ceyll wold put vpō hȳ xxi yere kȳg rychardes regne ordeyned parlemet weſtmynſter whyche kalled grete parlement thys parlement made iugge thys iij worthy lordes othir mo hē liſt tyme iuggemēt kyng let make haſt longe large hows tymbre which̄ kalled halle couered wyt tyles ouer ād opē aboute bothe ſides endes maner mē might ſee thurghout ād dome holden vpon theſe forſayd lordes ād iuggement yafe thys forſayd parlement come vnto thys parlement kyng ſente hys wryttes vnto euery lord baron knyght ſquyer euery ſhire throughoute englond euery lord gadre brynge hys retenue hym ſhort tyme beſt araye might gete mayntenyng ſtrenghtȳg king ayens hē ennemyes don̄ ī ha • come paine dethe king hȳ ſelue ſent cheſhire vnto cheuitais contre gadred brought grete hugh̄ multitude peple bothe knightes ſquyers principally yomē cheſtreſhire which̄ yomē archiers kȳg toke hys owne court yafe hem bouge court good wage kepers owne body both̄ night day aboue othir ꝑſones moſt loued bed truſt whiche ſone afterward turned ye kȳg grete loſſe ſhame hynderȳg hys vttyr vndoyng deſtruction ye ſhall ſone aftyr yt tyme came ſir hēry erle derby grete meyne men armes archiers erle ruttelād came ſtrōge power peple bothe men armes archiers ye erle kent browght grete power men armes archiers erle marchall came ſam̄ maner lord spencer ye ſame maner erle northūberland ſir hēry percy ſone ſir thomas percy hys brother theſe worthy lordes broughtē fayre meyne ſtronge power eche man beſt aray duke lācaſtre te duke yorke camen ſame maner wyth men armes archiers folowyng kyng ſir wylliam ſtrope treſorer englond came ſame maner thus thys aray camē worthy men thys land vnto king peple came londō one day ſomoche euery ſtrete lane ſubarbes full hem logged x xij myle aboute londō euery wey thees peple brought kyng weſtmynſtre wenten home ayen̄ hyr loggynyng bothe hors man mōday xvij day septēbre ꝑlement begā weſtmynſtre which̄ kalled grete ꝑlemēt fryday nex erle arū dell brought parlemest amōg lordes ſeynt mathews day apoſtell ād euangeliſt hewes iugget vnto deth halle made ye paleys weſtmynſtre iugement ſhold gon̄ foot wyth hys hondes bownde behynde hym place iuged ād ſo forth throughout ye cyte lōdō vnto ye toure hille ther hede ſmyten ſo don̄ dede ſame place vi ye grete lordes ſate hys iuggement riddē wyt vnto place ther don̄ vnto deth ſo ſee execucion done hir dome ād kynges cōmaūdemēt wyth hem wenten foot men armes ād archiers grete multitude cheſtre ſhire men ſtrengthyng lordes brought erle vnto deth drad leſt erle ſhold haue reſcued ād take hem whan came lōdō thus paſſed forth thurgh cyte vnto hys deth ād ther toke full pacientely who ſowle god haue mercy am̄ ¶and came freres auſtyns toke vp body hede good erle ād bare home vnto hir hous buried hȳ hyr quere morwe ſir rychard erle warrewyk brought ꝑlement erle arundel iuged yafe erle warrewyke ſame iugemēt ye forſaid erle ye lordes compaſſyon hym cauſe age
