men armes archiers ād thurghowte euery ward alſo king made v duke ducheſſe markeys foure erles fyrſt hē erle derby ād made duke hereford ſeconde erle rutteland made duke wemarle thridde erle kēt made duke furre fourthe erle huntyngdone ād made duke exceſtre v erle notynghā made duke northfolk erle somerſete made ye markeys dorſet lord ſpencer made erle glowceſtre ād lord neuill raby made erle weſtmerland ād ſir thomas percy made erle wurceſtre ſir williā ſcroppe treſorer englond made erle wylyſhire ſir iohan montagu erle salyſbury whan kȳg thus don̄ punctel helde parlemēt ryall feſt vnto hys lordes maner peple yt thyder came ſame yere deied ſir johā gaūt kynges vncle duke lācaſtre biſſhoppes ynnem holborn brought frō thēs ſeȳt poules ther ye king made ād helde entremēt well worthely wt lordes chyrch̄ ſeȳt poules lōdō buried beſide dame blaūce wyfe doughter heyre good henry yt duke lācaſtre ſame yere fyll diſcencyon debate bytwene duke hereford duke northfolk ſo moch̄ yt waged bataille ād kaſt downe hir gloues thā thei take vp enſeled ye bataill ioyned day ſet place aſſigned whā ſhold couētre thyder came kȳg wt lordes yt day ād ſette ī feld thā thees worthy lordes camē feld clene armed well arayed wt redy don̄ hir bataill place fyght vtteraunce kīg bad hē ceſe toke quarell hond forth wyt ryght p̄ſent exilled duke hereford terme x yere duke northfolke euermore ſir thomas arū dell erchebiſſhop caūterbury exilled ſam̄ time euer depoſed oute ſee malyce kȳg anon̄ theſe iij worthy lordes werē commaūded defended kynges reame ād anon̄ gate hē ſhippes dyuerſe hauenes wētē ouer ſee diuerſe lōdes ech̄ hys wey duke northfolk wēt venyce ād deyed who ſowle god haue mercy amē thā king rychard made clerke ſir rogier waldē erchebiſſhop caūterbury xxij yere kȳg richardes regne fals coūceill ymaginacyō couetous men yt werē aboute hȳ made ordeyne blāke chartres made hē ēſeled maner ryche mē thurghoute reame ſo moch̄ compelled diuerſe peple ſette ſeal therto done grete couetyſe wherfor good hertes reaume werē clene tur ned away frō hȳ kyng euer vttyr deſtructyō ende hȳ yt ſo hygh̄ excellēt prȳce king ād thurgh couetyſe fals coūceil falſeli betraied allas pite ſuche kyng myght ſee kȳg richard ſette kȳgdome ryall lōde englōd ferme vnto iiij perſones which̄ theſe ſir williā ſtroppe erle wylteſhire treſorer englōd ſir iohā buſſh hēri greue ſir iohan bagot knyghtes whyche turned hem meſchief deth̄ withī littell tyme ye ſhull fynde wrytē kyng rychard made grete ordenaūce wēte ouer ſee irland many grete lordes wt wt grete hoſtes ſtrēgth̄ hyr king men armes archiers moch̄ grete ſtuffe right good ordenaūce lōgeth werre paſſed ſee ordeyned made ſir edmōd lāgely vncle duke york lieutenaūt englōd abſēce wt gouernaūce coūceill theſe four knightes haddē takē englōd ferme king paſſed ſee came irlād well worthely receyued rebelles ben̄ kalled wilde iriſſhmē anon̄ hir cheuitains hir gouernours hir leders came doune vnto king yeldē hē vnto hȳ body goodes own̄ wylle ſwore liege men ther dydē homaae feaute ād good ſeruyce ād thꝰ cōquered moſte partye irland littel tyme yt king richard thus irlād ſir hē ry bolynbroke erle derby kȳg made duke hereford whyche duke kyng exilled oute thys land comen ayen̄ englond chalenge dukedome lancaſtre hys right trewe heritage came downe owte fraūce londe vnto caleys ther mete ſir thomas arūdel erchebiſſhop caūterbury yt exilled oute englond ād came erle arundel ſone heire which̄ warde kepyng ſir iohā ād ſheley knight ſomme tyme erle hūtyngdone ād duke exceſtre which̄ caſtell reigate ſouthſexe ther ſtale hȳ away ād came caleys ther kepte well ād worthely tyll theſe othir two lordes comē vnto caleys thā worthy duke erchebiſſhop caū terbury arōdell ſhiped hauen caleys ād drowe hir courſe northward aryued yorke ſhire raueneſporte faſte wydelyngtō ād came ād entred londe ād theſe two lordes wt hir meyne thā moch̄ peple reame herd hys comyng ād knowen wher anon̄ thei drewe vnto welcomed theſe lordes ād ſo coraged hē alle maner thing paſſed forth lande gadred moche peple whē kyng rychard herd wiſt theſe two forſaid lordes come ayene englond lōded thā kyng left ordenaūce irlād came englōd ward alle haſt might came vnto caſtell flynt abode take hys cownceill myght beſt done hȳ came none ſir thomas percy erle wurcheſtre yt kynges ſtyward wyſt knewe anone came halle among peple ād ther brake ye ryall kīges howſhold ād anone diſperkled euery man went way forſoke hir maiſter ād ſoueraigne lord left hym allone thus kyng rychard brought downe deſtroyed ād ſtode allone withoute comfort ſocour good coūceyll man allas pite ryall kyng anone came tydȳ ge ſir hēry holȳgbroke vp wonder ſtronge power peple ſherewes englōd reyſed vp ſhires ſtrengthyng hym ayēs kyng rychard • thus ſone come oute northcōtre bryſtowe mette ſir willyā ſcrope erle wildeſhire treſorer englōd wt ſir iohan buſſh ſir henry grene iohan bagot ſkaped hem wēt ouer ſee irland theſe iij knyghtes taken hyr hedes ſmytē thus deyed hir fals couetyſe thā kyng richard take brought vnto duke ād anone duke put hym faſt ward ſtrōge hold vnto hys comȳg london ther romer londō ſtronge noyſe kyng rychard came weſtmynſtre punctel ād peple londō ranne thyder wolde haue don̄ moch̄ harme ſkate hyr woodneſſe mayre alderman othir worthy men ſeced hem wyt fayre wordes turned hem home ayene london ther ſir iohā ſlake dekē kynges chappell weſtmynſtre take ād brought london put pryſon ludgate bagot take ī irland brought londō put pryſon newgate ther kepte abyde anſwere ſon̄ duke brought kyng rychard priuely vnto lōdō put towre vndyr ſure kepyng pryſoner thā came lordes reame wyt coūceyll vnto toure kyng rychard ſaidē hȳ miſgouernaūce extorciō done made ād ordeyned oppreſſe commune peple alſo reame wherfore cōmune peple hys reame wold haue hȳ depoſed hys kyngdome ād ſo depoſed tyme towre london lordes coū ceyll commune aſſent ye reame put frō toure vnto caſtell lede kēt ther kepte lad vnto caſtel poūfrete north cō tre kepte pryſon ſon̄ afterward right made ende whē kīg rychard depoſed reſygned croune hys kȳgdome kept faſt hald lordes reame cōmunes aſſent bi accord choſen worthy lord ſir hēry bolyngbroke erle derby duke hereford duke lācaſtre ryght line heritage rightfull manhode peple fonde hȳ othir choſen hym made kȳg englond amonges hem ¶of ſir hēry bolȳgbroke erle derby regned kīg rychard which̄ fourth̄ hēry aftyr conqueſt capitulo ccxliij kȳg rychard xj depoſed ād put owte hys kȳgdome lordes cōmunes wt own̄ aſſent othir worthy ye reame choſen ſir hēry bolȳgbroke erle derby ſone heyre iohan ye duke lācaſtre worthy māhode ofte tyme foūde ī hȳ dede p̄ ued vpō ſeynt edwardes day ye cōfeſſour crowned king englond weſtmȳſtre reames aſſent next depoſyng kyng rychard thā made biſhop lōdō tyme ſtode voyde made erles ſone arundell came ouer ſee caleys englond erle arūdell fadre ben̄ put poſceſſiō lode made feaute homage vnto liege lord ye kīg othir lordes • • tha anon̄ many yere deth whetyr lyue orde de forth helde hyr fals opynyons beleue men den moche peple whiche c • m̄ grete meſchief ād fowle deth ye ſhall afterward ¶and kyng henry wiſte knewe verrailly dede let ſere beſt maner cloſed fayre cheſte dyuerſe ſpeceries baumes cloſed hem ſynnē clothe ſaufe hys viſage ād lefte open men myght ſee hys perſone frō othir men ſo brought london wt torche lyght brēnyng vnto ſeȳt poules maſſe dirige wyt moch̄ reuerēce ſolēpnite ſeruyce whā don̄ browght ſeint poules abbeye weſtmynſtre hole ſeruyce ayen̄ frō weſtmȳ ſtre brought langely buryed who ſowle god haue mercy amē ¶and fyrſt yere kȳg hē rye regne helde hys criſtmaſſe caſtell wȳdeſore xij euen came duke wemarle vnto kīg told hī duke surre duke exceſtre erle salyſbury erle glouceſtre othir mo hir affinite accorded make mōmyng vnto kyng xij day night caſtē ſlee ye kȳg reuelȳg thꝰ duke wemarle warned kyng kyng came ſame nyght london pryuely haſt myght gete hȳ ſocour cōfort coūceill anone theſe wolde haue don̄ kynge dethe fleddē haſt thei might knewen well hir cownceyll bewreyed ¶and thā fledde duke ſurre erle salyſburye wyt hyr meyne vnto towne ciſſeſtre peple towne wold haue areſted hem wold ſtode hyr arreſte ſtode defence fawght manly laſt ouercome take ſmotē duke hede surre ād ye erles heed saliſbury many moo put quartres ſakkes ād hyr hedes pole borne high̄ ſo brought thurgh cyte lō vnto londō brygge hyr hedes ſette vpō hygh̄ hyr quartres werē ſente othir good tounes cite ſette vpon tree oxēford take bloute knyght benet cely knyght ād thomas vnto tyborne honged hys hede ſmyten ād ſir iohan ſhelley knight ſir iohā mawdelyn ād ſir williā fereby perſones drawe thurghoute london tiborne hanged hyr hedes ſmyten ſette londō brygge ¶and ſame yere kȳg hē ry iiij ſente quene iſabell home ayen̄ frawnce whiche kyng rychardes wedded wyfe yafe hir goold ſiluer ynow many othir ryche iewelles ſo ſhe diſcharged hir dower ſente owte englond ¶and ſecond yere regne kyng henry fourthe ſir rogier claryngdone knyght ād two men pryour launde viij frere menours ſomme maiſtres dyuinyte othyr treſon wrought ayenſt kyng drawen hanged tyborne xij perſones ther began grete diſcē ſion debate contre walys bytwen̄ lord grey ruthyn̄ owen glendere ſquyer walys owē arered grete nombre walſhmē kepte alle contre aboute right ſtronge moch̄ harme deſtroied kȳges townes lorſhippes thurghoute walys robbed ſlowe kynges peple bothe englyſſh walyſſh thys maner endured xij yere large toke ye forſaid lord greyruthyn̄ pryſoner kept hȳ faſt hold tyl raūſoned priſoners marche kepte longe time hold laſt made hȳ wedde one hys doughters kepte ther ſtyll wyt wyfe▪ ſone deyed thā king hēry knowȳg meſchief deſtruction treſon owen hadde wrought then̄e anone ordeyned ſtronge power mē armes archiers moche othir ſtuffe longed werre abate ād deſtroye malice fals walſſhmā thā king came vnto walys wyt power deſtroie thys owen othir rebelles falſe walſſh men anon̄ thei fledden moūtayns ther myght king done hem non̄ harme maner wyſe moūtaignes ſo king came englond ayene forleſyng mo hys peple thus ſped nought ſame yere grete ſcarcyte whete englond quarter whete xv ſhyllyng marchandyſe englōd ſente pruys whete anon̄ lade fregzt ſhippes ynowe came home ſaufte bleſſhed god alle yiftes iiij yere kyng hēries reigne ſterre ſeyne firmamēt ſhewed ſelfe thurgh alle world diuerſe tokenes yt ſhold befalle ſone which̄ ſterre named ād called clergye ſtella comata ſeint marye magdalene day next folewing ſame yere bataille ſhroweſbury thider came ſir henry percy erles ſone northumberland wt grete multitude mē armes archiers yafe bataille kyng henry iiij thurgh fals counceyll wykked rede ſir thomas percy vncle erle wurcheſtre ſir henry percy ſlaine mooſt partie meyne feld ād ſir thomas percy take kepte faſt holde two dayes tyll kȳg ſette reſte amonge hys peple bothe ſydes ſir thoās percy anone iuged dede drawe hōged hys hede ſmyten fals treſon ſhroweſbury ād hede brought london ſette londō brygge othir peple ther ſlayn̄ bothe party kīg let burye ther ſlaine kinges ſide bataill erle ſtafford ād ſir walter bloū te kynges cote armure vnder kinges baner many mo worthy men who ſowle god haue mercy amen iiij yere kyng henryes regne came emperour cōſtātynoble many grete lordes ād knightes moche othir peple cōtre englōd kyng henri wt hȳ ſpeke diſporte ſee good gouernaūce cō dicions peple knowe ye cōmodytees englōd kīg lordes goodly wurſhipfully hȳ receiued welcomed hȳ meyne camē wyt hym punctel dyd hȳ reuerēce ād wurſhip thei coude might anon̄ kȳg ꝯmaūded maner offyciers ſhold ſerued worthely ryally lōged vnto ſuch̄ worthy lord ād emperour owne coſte lōge emꝑour ēglōd men camen wyt hȳ ſame yere came dame iane ducheſſe britaigne englōd londed fallemouthe cornewaill frō then ſhe brought ye cyte wȳ cheſtre ther ſhe wedded vnto kȳg hēry iiij abbey ſeȳt ſwithynes wȳcheſtre wt ſolēnite might don̄ made ſone after· ſhe brought frō thēs lōdon mayre aldermē cōmunes ye cite londō ryddē ayēs hyr hir welcomed brought hir thurgh cyte londō weſtmȳſter ſhe crowned quene englōd ye kȳg made ryall ſolēpne feſte maner men thydder wold come ſame yere dame blaūche eldeſt dowghter kyng henry iiij ſent ouer ſee erle somerſete hyr vncle maiſtir richard clyfford biſſhop wurcheſtre many othir worthi lordes knightes lady worthy ſquiers longed ſuche worthy kynges doughter camen vnto coleyn thyder came duke ſone barre wyt faire meyne receyued thys worthy lady ye biſſhop wurceſtre wedded ſacred hem gedre holy chyrch̄ wold made ryall feſte grete iuſtes reuerence wurſhip hem alle peple thyder came ād mariage feſt done erle biſſhop hyr meyne token hir leue ye lord lady came hom̄ ayene englōd ſaufte thā ked god▪ ¶and v yere kȳg hēryes regne lord thoās ſone wente ouer ſee ād erle kent many othir lordes knightes wyt men armes archiers grete nōbre chaſtyze rebelles forne don̄ moch̄ harm̄ oure englyſſhmē marchaūts many townes porte englōd ye ſee coſtes lorde thomas kynges ſone came flaūdres fore towne kalled skluſe amonges ſhippes dyuerſe nacyōs werē ther ryddē wyt hyr ſhippes amēnge hem wentē londe ſported hem ij dayes camen ayene hyr ſhippes token brode ſee metten wyth iij carikkes iene lade dyuerſe marchaūdyſe well manned ād ther foughtē gedre longe tyme englyſſhmen ye victorye broughten carrykkes cābre wȳ chelſee canted thees goodes ād one carrikkes ſodenly brent lordes hyr peple turned hē hom̄ ayen̄ went ferther yt time ſame tyme serle yoman kyng rychard robbes came englond oute ſcotland told dyuerſe peple kȳg rychard lyue ſcotland ſo moch̄ peple beleued hys wordes wherfor grete parte peple reame werē grete errour ād gru • chyng ayēs kyng thurgh informacion lie ād fals leſing serle made moch̄ peple truſted beleued ſeyng laſt takē north cōtre lawe iugged ben̄ drawe thurgh euery cyte good burgh townes englōd ſo ſerued ād laſt brought london vnto gildhalle iuſtyce iuged brought ye toure londō tyborne ād honged punctel quartred hys hede ſmyten ſette lō brygge hys quartres ſente foure good tounes englōd punctel ſette vp ād thus endeth fals treſon ād diſceyt ¶and vj yere king hē rye regne ye iiij erle marre scotlād ſaufconduyt came englōd chalēge ſir edmond erle kēt certayne courſes werre horſebak ſo chalēge accepted graūted place taken ſmytfeld london erle marre ye scote came proudely feld chalenge aſked anon̄ came alſo erle kente rode vnto scote manfully rode gedre wyt ſharp ſperes diuerſe courſes erle kent feld gate hym moche wurſhyp thanke maner men hys manfull dedes ¶and vij yere kyng hēryes regne ye iiij syr rychard ſtroppe erchebiſſhop yorke ād lord erle marchall englond gadred vnto hē ſtronge power ayens kȳg henry kȳg herȳg therof haſt myght came power northward mette hē york thees two lordes take brought king anone iuges ſette thees ij lordes brought forth ād dāpned vnto deth both̄ hyr hedes ſmiten made hir ende who ſowles god pyte haue mercy amen whē done kȳg came londō ayene reſted hī anon̄ god grete goodneſſe wrought ſhewed many grete myracles worthi clerck erchebiſſhop york yt thꝰ don̄ vnto deth ye vij yere kȳg hēryes regne dame luce duke ſuſter mylane came englōd ſo lō ther ſhe wedded ſir edmōd holād erle kēt priorye ſeint marie ouereis ſouthwerk wt moch̄ ſolēpnite ād grete wurſhip kīg ſelfe yafe hir church̄ dore whē wedded ād maſſe don̄ kȳg owne perſone brought lad worthi lady ye biſſhoppes place wȳ cheſtre wōder grete feſt holdē maner peple ¶in ye ſame yere ſir robert knolles knight worthi werrour deied hys maner northfolk ād frō thēs brought lōdō vpō hors bare wt moch̄ torche lyght ſo brought vnto ye white freres fleetſtrete· done made hī ſolēpne feſte ryall enteremēt thaȳ thyder wolde come both̄ pore ryche lyeth beryed dame conſtaūce hys wyfe myddel body ye chyrche who ſowle god hys pyte haue mercy amē thꝰ ſame yere ſir thoās rāpſton knyght cōſtable toure lōdon dreynt lōdō brygge came weſtmȳ ſtre towardes towre barge thurgh lewdeneſſe ſame yere dame phelip yonger doughter king hē ry lad ouer ſee wyt ſir rychard duke brother yorke ſir edmond courteney biſſhop norwych many othir lordes knightes ſquiers ladyes gentyll womē apperteygned ſuche worthy kynges doughter camen dēmarke lordes kīg receyued worthy lady wyfe ād welcomed thees worthy lordes dyd hē moche reuerēce grete wurſhypp brought vnto town̄ kalled lō dō dēmarke worthy lady wedded ſacred ye kyng denmarke wyth moche ſolēpnyte ſhe crowned quene dēmarke norway swytē made ryall feſte whē feſte mariage done ended theſe lordes lady token hyr leue kȳg quene camē home ayen̄ englond haſt thanked god almyghty viij yere kȳg henry regne man kalled walſſh clerke appeled knight called ſir percheual ſowdone treſon· ād joyned fyght vnto vtteraūce withȳne liſtes day place tyme aſſigned lemyted don̄ ended ī ſmythfeld which̄ day perſones camē felde foughten ſore mightely gedres ye laſt knight ouer came clerke ād made hȳ yelde hȳ creaunt fals empeſchement ſaid hȳ thā deſpoilled armure drawe owte ye felde tiborne hōged ye knyght take grace ād good man ſame yere erle northūberlād ād lord bardolfe came owte scotlād preiudyce deſtructyō king hēry wherfor north contre aryſen vpō hē fought wt hem ſcōfy • ed hē tokē hē ſmiten hyr hedes ād quartred hyr body ſente heed ye erle quarter lord hardolfe london ſette vpō brigge fals treſon yt purpoſed ayēs kȳg ix yere kyng henryes regne ſir edmōd holād erle kente made admyrall englōd kepe ſee wente ſee many ryall ſhippes full wel arayed empareled enarmed many good men armes archiers good defence werre kȳges name englōd ſo londed laſt ye coſt britaigne ile bryak hys peple ād beſieged caſtell ſauted withſtode hym grete defence ſtrengthe anone leyed hys ordenaūce ye leyēg gonne· came quarell ſmote good erle edmōd hede caught dethes woū de yet left nought tyll yt gete caſtell alle therynne ād good lord deyed who ſowle god haue mercy amen thā thys meyne came home ayen̄ englōd erles body beryed amonges aūceſtres ryght worthely ſame yere grete froſt englond dured xv wekes ¶and x yere noble kyng henry fowrthe came senechall henaude othyr meyne ſeke auntres ād gete wurſhippes dedes armes bothe horſbake foot maner poyntes werre ſeneſchall chalēged erle somerſete erle delyured hym manfully alle hys chalenges ād put aduerſarie wers poītes wanne grete wurſhyp gre felde ye next day came felde othir man armes ye senechallis partie ayēs hȳ came ſir rychard arūdel knight henaude bettyr hym fote one pointe brought hȳ hys knee thrydde day came othir mā armes feld ayens came ſir johā cornewaill knight manly knightly quyte hī maner poȳtes ayēs aduerſarie better ī ye felde ye iiij day came man armes henaude felde ayens hȳ came ſir iohan cheynys ſone manly quyte hym ayens hys aduerſarie caſte hors man feld kȳg māhode tyme dubbed knight ye v day came othir mā armes henaudes partye feld hȳ came ſir iohan ſtyward knight māfully quyte maner poȳtes better vj day came othir henaude hȳ came willyā porter ſquyer mā fully quyte hym better felde kyng dubbed hī knyght ſame tyme vij day came othir henaude felde hym came iohan kandyſh ſquyer manfully quyte hȳ aduerſarye better felde kyng dubbed knight ſame day ſame day came othir henaude came ſquyer gaſcoygne proudely māly quite hys aduerſarye better anon̄ kȳg dubbed hī knight viij day came ye felde ij men armes henaude hem cam̄ ij ſoudyours caleys bretheren kalled burghes· well māly quyte hem hyr aduerſaries better felde thus ended chalenges moch̄ wurſhippes king reuerēce ſtraungiers made grete feſte yafe hem ryche yiftes· tokē hir leue ād went home hyr owne contre▪ xi yere kyng henry regne iiij grete bataille done ſmythfelde bitwene two ſquiers one kalled glouceſtre appellaūt arthur defendaūt well manfully fowghtē gedre longe tyme ād kyng manfullneſſe hys grace toke hyr quarell hys honde made hem go owte felde one ād ſo deuyded hir batailles ād kyng yafe hē grace ¶and xij yere kyng henry regne fourthe rys dye ſquier walys yt rebell aryſer ſupporter owē glēdore dyd moch̄ deſtructiō peple walys taken brought lōdō came fore iuſtices dā pned treſon leid hurdel ſo drawe forth vnto tyborne thurgh cyte hanged let downe ayene hede ſmytē ād hys body quartred ſente iiij tounes ād hede ſette london brygge xiij yere kyng hēryes regne tho deyde ſir iohā beauford erle ſomerſette capitayne caleys beried abbey tourehyll who ſowle god haue mercy amen ſame yere lord thomas kȳg hen ries ſone wedded counteſſe somerſette ſame yere came ēbaſſotours fraū ce englōd duke burgoygn̄ vnto prȳce englōd kȳg hēries ſone heyre helpe ſocour men armes archiers ayēs ye duke orliaūce tho wēte ouer ſee erle arūdell ſir guillebert vmfreuille erle kente lord cobham ſir iohā olde caſtell many othir good knightes worthy ſquiers men armes ād good archiers fraunce came paris duke burgoigne receyued wellcomed thees englyſſhmen lordes othir meyne thā don̄ wyt duke orliaunce comen ſemtclowe faſt paris wyth grete nombre men armes ād arbalaſtriers thyder wēte oure englyſmē foughten wyth hē gate brigge ſemtclowe ſlowe moch̄ peple frēſſhmen armynakes remanaūt fledde wold lēger abyde thā englyſſhmē came ayen̄ paris token hyr leue duke camen home ayen̄ englōd ſaufte duke yafe hem grete yiftes anone folewȳg duke orliaūce ſent enbaſſatours englōd kyng henry fowrthe beſechyng hym hys helpe ſocour ayens hys dedely enemye ye duke burgoygne kyng made thomas ſone duke clarēce othir ſone iohan duke bedford ſone humfrey duke glowceſtre ſir thomas beauford erle dorſet duke wamarle made duke yorke kyng ordeyned ſone ſir thomas duke clarence ſir thomas beauford erle dorſet ſir iohan cornewaylle wyth many othir lordes knyghtes squyers men armes archiers gon̄ ouer ye ſee fraūce helpȳg ſtrē gthyng duke orliaunce theſe worthy lordes wt hir retinue ſhipped hamptō ſailled ouer normādie londed hogges mette hem lord hambe hyr londyng wyt vij men armes frēſſhmē iij ſergeaunts armes hem ād put flyght tokē hē vijc men armes· cccc hors withoute thaȳ ſlayne felde ſo ryddē forth thurghoute fraūce tokē caſtelles townes ſlowen moche peple frēſſhmen withſtodē hē tokē many pryſoners riddē ſo paſſed forth tyll camē burdeux thei reſted hem ſette contre pee reſted tyll wyntage redy ſaille· thā ye duke wt hys meyne came home englōd ſaufte thāked god ſame yere kī ge coyne chāged thurghoute englōd ye kyng coūceill ſeye ye noble halfe ferthȳg gold ye xiiij yere kȳg hēries regne iiij let make galeys werre hoped haue paſſed grete ſee ād ſo forth iheruſalē haue ended hys lyfe god viſited hȳ ſo ſone wyt infirmites ād grete ſikeneſſe might well endure ſo feruētly take brought bed weſtmȳſtre fayre chambre lay hys bed aſked hys chamberlayne kalled chamber lay ynne āſweryd ſayd jheruſalē thā ſaid ye prophecye ſaid ſhold make ende deie jheruſalē thā made hȳ redy vnto god diſpoſed ſone deied caried watyr weſtmynſter barge vnto feuerſhā ▪ frō thēs vnto caūterbury lande wyth moche torche light brēnyng abbey crichurche entered ād buryed beſide ſeȳt thoās caūterbury ſhryne thus ended worthy king hēry aboute mydlēten ſonday ye yere lord mccccxiij who ſowle god haue mercy amē ¶of kyng hēry v kȳg hēryes ſone capitulo ccxliiij deth king hēry iiij regned king hēry hys ſone borne monmouth walys worthy kīg gracious man grete cōquerour ād ye fyrſt yere regne grete loue goodneſſe ſente freres lāgely hys fadre don̄ ē burye kȳg richard ſecōd let take body oute erthe ayen̄ dyd bring weſtmȳſter ryall chare couered wyth blak veluet baners dyuerſe armes aboute alle ye hors drowen chare trapped blake betē wt diuerſe armes many torche brēnyng wey till came weſtmȳſtre let make hȳ ryall ſolēpne enteremēt ād beryed hym quene anne hys wyfe hys owne deſire ferther ſide ſeīt edwardes ſhryne ye abbey ſeint peter weſtmynſter who ſowle god haue mercy amē ī ſame yere certayne lollardes takē fals heretikes purpoſed thurgh fals treſon haue ſlayne kyng haue deſtroied clergye ye reame yf myght haue hir fals purpoſe lord god wold ſuffre haſt kȳg warȳg therof hir fals ordinaūce came ſodēly wyt power ſeint iohānes wtoute ſmythfeld anone tokē certaine lollardes fals heretikes brought hē vnto kī ge preſence ād told alle hir fals purpoſe ordinaūce wold haue don̄ wrought myght haue regned ād hyr wille told whych̄ hir capitaȳs gouernours thā kȳg ꝯmaūded hē lad ye toure lōdō thā toke moo hē bothe withȳ ye cyte withoute ſent hē newgate bothe cōtrees thā brought examinaciō clergie kīges iuſtices ād cōvicted ye clergye hyr fals hereſie dāpned iuſtice hyr fals treſō hir iugemēt ſhold drawe frō towre lōdō vnto ſeynt gilles feld hōged brēt galewes alſo takē ſir rogier acton knyght hereſie eke treſon ayēs ye kȳg reame came fore clergye cōuicted hys hereſie brēd dāpned iuſtyces drawen frō towre lōdō thurgh cyte ſeint gilles felde honged brēt ſecōd yere kȳg hēries regne v helde coūceill lordes reame weſtmȳſter put hȳ demāde praied ād beſought hē hyr goodneſſe hyr good coūceill good wyll ſhewe touchȳg title right yt normādie gaſcoygne guihēne which̄ kȳg fraūce wyt helde wrōgfulli vnryghtfully which̄ aū ceſtres hȳ trewe tytle cōqueſte right herytage ye whych̄ normādie gaſcoign̄ guyhēne good kȳg edward wȳdeſore aūceſtres hȳ haddē hold hir life time hys lordes yafe hȳ coūceyll ſend ēbaſſatours vnto kȳg fraūce coūceill ſhold yeue vnto hȳ ryght herytage ſaye normādye gaſcoygne gwyhēne whiche predeceſſours haddē hold fore elles wold wȳ ne dynt ſwerd ſhort tyme wyth helpe almyghty god dolphyne fraūce anſwered embaſſatours ſaid ī maner kyng ouer yong tendre age make werre ayens hym lyke good werriour make ſuch̄ conqueſt thervpon ſomwhat ſcorne deſpyte ſent tonne full tenys balles becauſe ſholde haue ſō playe wyth hȳ lordes became hȳ better thā maynten werre anon̄ lordes embaſſatours tokē leue camē englōd ayene ād told kȳg coūceil ye vngoodly anſwere dolphyne preſente ye which̄ ſente vnto king whē king herde hir wordes anſwere dolphyn wonder ſore agreued right euell payed toward ye frēſſhmen toward kȳg ād dolphyn thought auenge vpon hem ſone god wold ſend grace myght ād anon̄ let make tenys balles ye dolphȳ ye haſt yt might made grete gōne ſtone dolphyne play wt anon̄ kȳg ſent hys lordes ād helde grete coūceille weſtmynſtre ād told vnto hem anſwere dolphyne worthy preſente ſente hym lordes pley ād kyng hys lordes werē accorded ſhold redy ī armes wyth hyr power ye beſt araye might done gete mē armes archiers yt might goten othir ſtuffe lō ged werre redy hir retenue mete sowthāpton lammaſſe next ſewȳg withoute delay wherfore ye kȳg ordeyned nauye ſhippes wt maner ſtuffe vitaille yt lō ged ſuch̄ werrour maner ordinaūce ye hauē ſouthampton nōbre ccc xx ſailles ¶and fyll grete diſeſe fowle meſchyef ther thre lordes whych̄ yt king truſt moſt moch̄ ād thurgh fals couetiſe thei purpoſed ymagined kīges deth thought haue ſlayne hym hys brotheren take ſee whyche named thus ſir rychard erle cābrygge brothyr ye duke york ſeconde lord ſcroppe treſorer englond ye thridde ſir thoās gray knight northcōtre theſe lordes fore ſayd lucre money made promiſſe frēſſhmen haue ſlayne kyng henry hys worthy bretheren bi fals trayne ſodenly ware al mighty god grete grace helde hys holy hōde ouer ſaued hē peryllous meyne ād haue done thys receyued frenſſhmen million gold opynly preued thys fals treſon thei iuged vnto deth̄ thys iugemet ſhold ladden thurgh hampton withoute northgate beheded thus ended hir lyfe hir fals couetyſe treſon anone don̄ kīg meyne made hem redy wenten ſhippe tokē ſailled forth xvc ſhippes arryued withyn ſeyne kyde cauſe vpon ladyes euen aſſumptyon jn normandye wyth ordenaūce ſo went hī forth hareflete beſieged towne aboute lond eke bi watyr ſent capiteyne towne charged delyuer towne capyteyne ſayd none delyured none wold yelde hym bad hȳ don̄ beſt thā kyng laid ordynaūce vnto ye towne ſaye gō ne engynes trypgetes ſhetē caſt walles eke vnto toune kaſt downe bothe toures toune layd hē vnto grownde ād played tenys harde gō ne ſtone withyn towne ſhold playe ſonge wel away ād allas euer ſuch̄ tenys balles made curſed thē werre begā tyme euer borne morwe kyng dyd crye euery gate towne euery man ſhold redy morwe erly make aſſaute vnto ye towne willyam bouchier iohan graūt xij othir worthy burgeys camē kyng ād beſought ryall pryncehode power withdrawe hys malyce deſtructyon vnto hem beſought hī viij dayes reſpyte trewes yf reſkue myght come vnto hē elles yelde vp towne vnto hē hir goodes thā kyng ſente capyteyne kept remenaūt ſtill wyt hym lord gaucorte capiteyne ye towne wēte forth rone haſt vnto dolphyne helpe ſocour non̄ ne man reſkue ye dolphȳ wold abyde thus capiteyne came ayene vnto kyng ād yolde vp towne delyuered keyes kalled hys vncle erle dorſet made hȳ capiteyne town̄ harflete delyuered keyes bad hym gone put oute frenſſh peple bothe men woman child ſtuffed toune harflete englyſſhmē kyng ſente englond ād dyd crye euery good towne englōd crafty man wolde come thyder inhabyte towne ſholde haue hows howſhold hȳ heires euer ſo thyder wente mani diuerſe marchaūts crafty men enhabyted hē ſtrēgth̄ ye toune werē welcome whē kȳg ſaw town̄ wele ſtufed bothe vitaille ād men worthy prȳce toke leue wente caleys ward bi londe ād frenſſhmen herde comȳg thought ſtoppe way ſhold paſſe way ye haſte might brekē brigges ther ani paſſage hors man ſo moche might man paſſe ouer riuers nothyr hors ne foot yf ſhold drowned therfor kyng peple wente ſought hys waye ferre vp paris ward ther ryall power fraū ce aſſembled redy yeue hȳ bataille deſtroye al peple almighti god gydde ſaued enemy power purpoſe thāked god ſaued ſo own̄ knight kȳg hys rightfull titell king beholdȳg ſeyng multitude nōbre enemy whiche wey yeue hym bataill thā king wyth meke herte ād good ſpirit left vp handes almyghty god beſought hȳ helpe ſocour daye ſaue hys trewe ſeruaunts ad owr kyng gadred lordes othyr peple aboute bad hem good cher̄ thei ſhold haue faire day gracyous victorie better hyr enemyes praid hē make hem redy vnto ye bataill wold rather dede day felde taken hys enemyes wolde neuer put noble reame englond rawnſone hys perſone worthy duke yorke fell hys knee beſought ye kyng aboue wold graunte hym day avauntward hys bataille· noble kyng graūted hym aſkȳg ſayd graūte mercy coſin yorke praied make redj thā bad euery man ordeyne ſtake tree ſharp both̄ endes ſtake might pight erthe ſloppe hyr enemyes ſhold ouer come hē horſebake▪ hyr falſe purpoſe araied hē ther ouer ryde meyne ſodē ly fyrſt comyng • fyrſt brownt night bataylle frēſhmen maden many grete fyres moch̄ reuell howtyng ſhowting pleyde kȳge lordes diſe ād archier blā ke hyr money wenden alle bene heires morne aroſe day began ſpryng ¶ kyng good auyſe let araye bataille wynges charged euery man kepe hem hole gedres prayed hem good chere whā redy aſked tyme day ād thei ſaid pryme ſayd king good time englōd praied forvs therfore good chere let v go oure iourney thā ſaid high̄ voys name almyghty god ſeint george avaūt baner ſeint george day thyne helpe thā frenſſhmen came prykyng doūe wold haue ouer ryden oure meyne good ād oure archiers made hem ſone ſtomble archiers ſhet neuer arowe amys periſſhed brought groūde man hors ſhotē day wager oure ſtakes made toppe ouer terne eche othir thei lay hepes two ſpere lēgthe heyghte king hys meyne men armes archiers tokked hem ſo thikke wyt arewes leyde tho ſtakes kyng owne handes faught manly thꝰ almyghty god ſeȳt george brought enemyes groūde ād yafe v day victorie ſlayne frenſſhmē day feld agyncourt moo than̄ xim pryſoners taken ther nō bred day frēſſhmē felde moo ſix ſocore thouſād englyſſhmē nat vijm god day fought v came tydinges kyng newe bataille frenſſhmē ordeyned redy ſtelle camē towardes hym anone oure kȳg let crie euery man ſhold ſlee hys priſoner take ād anone arayed bataylle ayen̄ redy fyght frenſſhmen ſawe mē kylled doūe hir pryſoners than̄e thei withdrowe hē brake hir bataill alle hir aray thus owr kȳg worthy cōquerour day victorie feld agyncourt pycardie thā kyng retourned ayen̄ yt bataill ſee peple dede englyſſhmē hurt yt myght holpē ther dede felde duke barry duke alaūſoū duke borban erle nauerne chief coneſtable fraūce viij othir erles ād erchebiſſhop saūce good barōs hondred moo worthy knightes grete aliaūce cote armures thowſād v hōdred engliſſhmē dede yt day good duke york erle southfolk alle othir engliſſhmē ther nat dede paſſyng xxvi bodyes thāked god bataill don̄ fryday which̄ criſpynie criſpynianes day moneth octobre ād anon̄ kȳg ꝯmaūded bery hem duke yorke caryed forth erle ſouthfolk priſoners duke orlyaūce duke burbone erle vēdome erle ewe erle richemōd ſir burſigaūt marchaūt fraūce many othir worthy lordes werē taken bataille agȳcourt brought vnto towne caleys ſo ouer ſee wyt kyng englōd londed douer kent hys pryſoners ſaufte thanked god almyghty ād ſo came caūterbury ād offred ſeynt thomas ſhrine ſo forth rode thurgh kēte next way eltham reſted tyll yt wold come londō thā mayre london aldermē ſherews wyth worthy communers craftes camen blakhethe well worthely arayed welcomed owr kyng wyth dyuerſe melody ād thāked almyghty god hys gracious victorie ſhewed hym ſo kyng ād hys priſoners paſſed forth hem til came ſeynt thomas wateryng mette hym relygyous proceſſiō welcomed hym ſo kyng came rydyng hys priſoners thurgh cyte londō ther ſhewed many faire ſight conduytes ād croſſe chepe heuenly array angeles archā geles▪ patriarch prophetes ād virgines dyuerſe melody ſenſyng ād ſyngyng welcome kyng alle cōduytes rennyng wyth wyne ¶and kyng paſſed forth vnto ſeynt powles mette wyth hym xiiij biſſhoppes reueſſed mytered ſenſers welcome kyng▪ ſongē hys hyghe gracious victorie te deum laudamus kȳg offred toke leue rode weſtmȳſter thā ye mayre toke leue kȳg rode home ayen̄ ye thridde yere kȳg hēryes regne v came emperour almaygne kȳg rome hūgarye englond ſo cyte london mayre aldermā wyt ſherews worthy craftys londō kynges cōmaū demēt mette hȳ blake hethe beſt aray thei cowde horſebak ād welcomed hȳ brought hȳ lō wyth moch̄ honour ād grete reuerence ſeȳt thomas wateryng mette wyt hȳ kyng wyth lordes good aray worthy mettyng bytwene emperour ād kȳg kyſſed gedres enbrached eche othir thā kyng toke emꝑour bi honde ſo camē rydyng thurgh cyte london vnto ſeȳt powles offred biſſhoppes ſtoden reueſſed wyth ſencers hōdes ſenſing than̄ tokē hyr hors rydden vnto weſtmȳſtre· kȳg logged emperour hys owne paleys reſted hym grete kinges coſte ſone came duke holand englond come ſee emperour ſpeke wyt hȳ kyng hēry englōd worthely receyued logged biſſhoppes ynne ely kȳges coſte whē emperour well reſted hym ſeyn lōd dyuerſe partyes knewe cōmodytes proceſſe tyme toke hys leue kīg yede made knyght gartier receyued wered lyuery thāked kyng hys worthy lordes kyng went ouer ſee vnto caleys abydē ther longe tyme haue āſwere frēſſh̄ kyng laſt came pleſed hȳ right nought emperour toke hys leue kȳg paſſed forth goddes name kȳg came ouer ayen̄ englond ye haſt myght yt ſeynt luke eue came lambythe ye mōday next came parlement weſtmynſter▪ ād thys ſame yere grete derthe corne englōd thanked god laſted longe ye fowrthe yere kȳg hēryes regne v helde hys parlement weſtmȳſter begynnyng ye moneth octobre laſted vnto puryfycacyō lady next ād graūted vnto kȳg maȳten̄ hys werre bothe ſpyrytualte temperalte hole taxe diſme thā anone kȳg praied hys lordes make hem redy ſtrength̄ hym hys ryght anon̄ let make newe retenue charged alle men redy hamptō withſon weke next withoute delay kyng made ye duke bedeford protectour ād defendour hys reame englond hys abſence ād charged hym kepe hys lawes maynten bothe ſpyrytualte tēperalte kyng thꝰ done ſette alle thyng hys kȳ de ſeīt markes day tyme hokketuyſ • ay toke hys hors weſtmynſtre came rydyng ſeint powles offred toke hys leue ſo rode forth thurgh cyte taking hys leue maner peple wel poure anon̄ ſent hys heraudes capitaine charged delyuer towne caſtell punctel elles wolde hem gete ſtrength̄ honde anſweryd ſayd toke hē none ne none wold delyuer vnto hym ād anon̄ layde hys ſiege vnto towne laid gonne euery ſide ād bette downe bothe walles towres ād ſlowe alſo moch̄ peple hir houſes eke ſtretes good duke clarē ce laid downe walles ſide vnto grounde ſo withȳ kyng hys coūceyll exceſtre wt fayre meyne mē armes archer tho cyte rone diſplaied hys baner ſent heraudes vnto towne bad hem yelde cyte vnto owr kyng hyr ſiege lord ſayd toke hē none kepe ne non̄ ſhold haue yf right engliſſhmē drofe hē ye town̄ ayen̄ laſt capitaine town̄ ſawe meſchief nat reſcued alſo ſcarcite vitayll ye peple ſo deyde defaute mete euery day many thouſandes alſo ſawe yonge childrē lye ſouke hir modres pappes werē dede anon̄ ſent vnto kȳg beſechyng hȳ grace ād mercy brought keyes town̄ vnto kyng delyuered ye toune hȳ ſoudiours voided towne wyt hyr hors ād harneys cōmunes ye toune abyde ſtyll towne yerly pay ſucceſſours maner cuſtomes ād fee fermes katherines thā kyng entred ye town̄ reſted hȳ caſtell tyll towne ſette ī rewle ī gouernaūce ¶how kyng englōd made heritier regēt fraūce wedded quen̄ katherine cap ccxlv anon̄ rone goten depe many othir townes baa normādye yaf thē ouer withoute ſtroke ſiege whā vndyrſtode kȳg gotē rone alſo thys ſame yere bene pee made ſworne bitwene duke burgoygn̄ ye dolphyne which̄ ſworne vpon lordes body ſhold aſſiſte eche othir ayenſt enemyes thys contrayt thys othe ye duke iohā burgoign̄ ſlayne pitouſly murthred preſence dolphyn wherfore frēſſhmen gretly deuided veray neceſſyte labouryd haue traittie wyth ye kȳg englōd kyng englond man dayely thē townes caſtelles fortreſſes alſo thys ſame yere quene iane areſted brought caſtell ledis kente one frere raudolfe doctor diuinite ꝯfeſſour which̄ afterward ſlayne keper towre fallyng wordes ād debate quene iane delyuered ¶in vij yere bothe kynges frawnce alſo englond accorded kyng henry made heyre renent fraūce wedded dame katheryne kynges doughter fraūce troyes champaigne trinite ſonday made bi ye mene phelyp newly made duke burgoigne which̄ ſworne king hēry tauēge fadres deth become englyſſh thā kȳg newe wyfe wēt paris well rially receyued thēs wt hys lordes ye duke burgoign̄ many othir lordes frawnce leid ſiege diuerſe townes caſtelles helde dolphin partie wā hē towne melun held longe theryn good defendours viij yere king quene camen ouer ſee lōded candelmaſſe day morwe douer xiiij day feuerer king came londō xxj day ſame moneth quen̄ came xxiiij day ſam̄ ſhe crowned weſtmȳſter alſo ſame yere anon̄ eſtre kȳg helde parlemēt weſt mynſter which̄ ꝑlemēt ordeyned ye gold ī englyſſh coyne ſhold weyed none receyued bi weyght anon̄ witſontide king ſailled caleys ād paſſed ſo forth fraūce marche xxij day yt king came ouer duke clarence ſlaine fraūce diuerſe lordes takē pryſoners erle hūtyngdon erle somerſette diuerſe othir lordes cauſe thei wold take wyt hem archer thought haue dō frēſſhmen thē ſelfe withowte hē yet whā ſlayn̄ archer came reſkued body duke whyche wold haue caryed hē god haue mercy ſowle • vaillaūt man ſame yere bytwene criſtmas cā delmas towne melū yolden kȳg ix yere ſeynt nycolas day decembre borne hēry kynges fyrſt begoten ſone wynde • ore who godfadres fōtſton̄ henry biſſhop wȳcheſtre ād iohan duke bedford ducheſſe holād godmoder hēry chicheley erchebiſſhop caūterbury godfadre ye cōfermȳg x yere ye cyte mewes brye gotē which̄ ben̄ longe beſeged ¶and ſame yere quene ſhypped hamptō ſailled ouer kyng fraunce ſhe wurſhipfully receyued king ād alſo kyng fraunce hyr fadre ād hyr modre thus kȳg hēry wan faſt fraūce helde grete aſtate ſate dyuer grette feſt parys crouned ād ye quen̄ alſo which̄ ben̄ ſeē fore ād peple reſorted vnto court kȳg fraū ce helde non̄ aſtate ne rule left almoſt allon̄ alſo yere wether coke ſette vpō poulus ſteple lōdon yere ī moneth auguſt king ſike boy de vȳ cēt whē ſaw yt ſhold deye made teſtamēt ordeined many thȳges nobly ſoule deuoutly receyued ryghtes holy chyrchh̄ ſo ferforth yt whē enoȳted ſayd ye ſeruyce wt preſte • vers pſalme miſerere meidens benigne fac dūe bona volūtate tua ſyō vt edificētur mur •• hrlm̄ tarie • ſayd thꝰ good lord thou knouweſt myne entēt ben̄ yet might lyue reedifie walles ihrlm̄ then̄e preeſt proceded forth made ende anon̄ mooſt noble prynce ād victorious king flour time criſtē chiualrye whō ye world doubtet yaf ſowle hōdes god deide made ende naturell lyfe ſaid bois de vincent beſide paris xxxi yere age who ſowle haue mercy am̄ then̄ ye body enbawmed chered leyd ryall chare ymage lyk vnto hī leide vpō ye corp opē wt dyuerſe baners horſe couered rychely wt armes englōd fraū ce alſo ye olde armes ſeȳt edwardes ſeȳt edmōd othir wt grete mltitude torchis wt whō wēte kȳg scotlād many othir lordes which̄ accōpanyd ye body till came vnto weſtmȳſt lōdō englōd euery town̄ ye way ſolēpnely hys dirige theuē maſſe ye morne moch̄ almeſſe yeuen poure peple bi way vij day nouēbre corp brought thurgh lōdō wyt grete reuerēce ſolempnite weſtmȳſter lyeth wurſhipfully buried leyd tōbe riall ymage lyke ſelfe ſyluer gylt made atte coſt quen̄ katherine thꝰ ended thꝰ ētered buried ye noble kȳg hēry v who ſowle criſtē ſowles god haue mercy amen ¶of ye lawde kȳg hēry ye v ordeyēd kȳg rychard hȳ ſelfe deth cap ccxlvi noted yt thys kȳg hēry fyffte noble prȳce kīg crowned fore yongthe ben̄ wylde recheles ſpared thyng luſtes ne deſires accompliſſhed aftyr thys likynge ſone crouned enoȳted ſacred anon̄ ſodēli chaūged newe mā ſette intent lyue vertuouſly maȳtenȳg holy chyrch̄ deſtroyng heretikes kepȳg iuſtice defendȳg reame ſubgettys aſmoch̄ fadre depoſed labour ye good kīg richard pitouſly made deye thefēce don̄ hī ayēſt ligeaūce ſent rom̄ aſſoilled therof whiche offēce ye pope holy fadre enioned hȳ make hȳ prayed fore ꝑpetuelly ād lyke don̄ takē frō hī naturel lyfe therfore ſhold foūde iiij taper brēne ꝑpetuelly body yt ye extīctōn hys bodely life ſoule may ever remēbred lyue heuē ſpirituel lyfe ād alſo yt ſhold euery weke ye day comith aboute deth haue ſolēpne maſſe requiē euē fore dirige wt ix leſōs dole poure alway ye day xi ſhīllīges viij pēs delyd peny mele on̄s yere āniuerſarie teremēt holdē ye moſt honeſte wiſe deled yt day xx poūde pēs poure peple ād euery mōke haue xx ſhillȳges which̄ theſe thȳges ꝑformed noble kȳg hys fadre kȳg hēry ye iiij ꝑformed durȳg hys lyfe whō ſayd god touchyd lepre deyde alſo then̄ noble prȳce lete kalle ye abbotys priours ſeȳt benettey ordre ī englōd bad thē ye chapytre hous weſtmȳſter reformaciō ordre wherȳ comynycacyō alſo ye biſſhoppes mē ſpiritualte ſo ferforth yt doubted ſore wold haue teporal tee oute hōdes wherfore thauys labour procurȳg ſpiritualte encoraged kȳg chalēge normādie right fraūce thēde ſet • e hȳ werke ther yt ſhold ſeke occaſiōs ētre ſuch̄ mater lyfe aftyr laboured ye werrys cōquerȳg grete parte ye reame france yt gremēt kȳg charles gouernaūce reame fraūce ꝓclamed regēt ād heir fraūce ſo wythſtādyng thys grete werre yet remembred ſoule alſo mortall muſt deye which̄ ordeyned bi hys lyfe place ſepulture nowe buryed euery day thre maſſes perpetuelly ſongen fayre chapell ouer ſepulture whiche mydylmaſſe fyrſt laſte maſſe ſhalbe aſſigned hym apperyth bi thyſe verſys folowyng heurici miſſe quinti ſunt hic tabulate que ſucceſſiue ſunt per monachos celebrate die dn̄icaprima ſit aſſumpte de feſto virginis alme poſcit poſternam chriſtꝰ de morte reſurgens feria ſcda prima ſalutare feſto virginis extat nunciat angelicis laudē poſtrema choris feria tcia eſſe deum natum de v er gine prima fatetur cōmemorat natam ſic vltima miſſa mariam feria q̄rtaprima celebretur ad honorem pneumatis almi vltima conceptam deun̄ciat eſſe mariam feria quta semper prima coli debet de corꝑe chriſti vltima ſit facta de virgine puriticata feria ſextacondecet vt prima celebretur de cruce ſancta que falutate fiet poſtremo marie sabbatoomnes alij ſanctos eſt prima colenda ſupernos vltima de requie pro defunctis petit eſſe semper erit medium de proprietate dei yet noble kyng hēry ye v fownded two howſes relygyō vne kalled syō beſyde braȳ ford ordre ſeynt brigitte bothe men woman othir ſyde ye ryuer thamyſe hows mōkes chartrehous which̄ two place continuelly prayd nyght ād day euer whā syō reſted chartrehous don̄ theyr ſeruyce lyke wyſe whā thei ye chartrehous reſte othir goon ād ryngȳg belly either place eche knoweth whan haue endyth theyr ſeruyce which̄ nobly ēdouwed doō dayly ther grete almeſſe dedes ye chartrehows certayne chyldren ben fownde ſcole ſyon certayne almeſſe gyuē dayly ¶and yet beſyde founde recluſe which̄ ſhalbe alway preeſt praye hȳ ye ſayd chartrehous whyche preeſt well ſuffyciētly endowed hym ſeruaūt lo may prince takē exāple noble prynce regnyng ſo lyttel tyme fully x yere dyd ſo many noble actes well ſowle perpetuelly remēbred prayed ī wordly conqueſtis beȳg mooſt luſty age deſpyſed eſchewyd ſynne vertuous grete iuſtiſer ſomoch̄ prȳces cryſtēdome drad ād alſo hethenes determined hȳ ſelf god wold haue ſpared wold haue werred agayn ſarazyns knowe moch̄ doubted drad cauſe grete conqueſt fadre alſo wyſedō guydyng vncles ye duke bedford ye duke glouceſtre thys yere xxi day octobre deide charles kȳg fraūce lieth buryed ſeȳt denis thā duke duke alaūſon̄ which̄ grete bataill duke bedford hys ſide wyt hȳ erle ſaliſbury montagu lord talbote power coude make normā dye garniſōs kepte alſo many capitaines wyt moch̄ peple duke burgoign̄ worde agayn̄ yt ſhold finde day ſwerd ſteell ſo ye bataille ioyned both̄ ſides fought lō ge yt ther wyſte mā ſhold haue better grete laſt god wolde victorie fyll vnto englyſſh partie· ther ſlayne vnto nombre xm moo ther takē priſoner ye duke alaūſon many lordes gentylls fraūce scottes yt day ſlayne down̄ right ſubſtaūce ¶in thridde yere kyng hē ry vj duke glowceſtre maried ducheſſe holand wente ouer ſee hir henaude take poſceſſiō wife encheritaūce honourabely receyued takē lord londe ſone faȳ retourne home ayen̄ lefte hys wyfe hys treſowr brought towne called mounſe henaude· ye whych̄ promyſed trewe hym notwithſtādyng delyured lady ye duke burgoygne which̄ ſent hyr gaūt punctel then ſhe eſcaped mannes araye came zelād towne owne called zierirce fro then ſhe wente towne holād called ghowde ſhe ſtrōge ynough withſtode ſayd duke burgoygne ſone duke glowceſtre ſente ouer zeland lord fytzwater certayne mē werre archiers helpe ād ſocour forſayd ducheſſe holand which̄ which̄ lyued onely bi myracle etyng ony mete thys ſame yere duke burgoign̄ began ordre lyle golden flyes ordeyned certeyne knyghtes ordre made ſtatutes ordinaūces moch̄ accordȳg vnto ordre garter alſo thys ſame yere frēſſhmen enterpryſed haue ſtolē caleys fiſſyng time many bootis fraūce ſaufcoūduytis come caleys take herȳg ſoudeours towne cuſtome come chyrch̄ leue ſtauis ſtādyng chyrche dore frēſſhmē whiche araied lyke fyſſhers purpoſed haue taken ſo theyr wepen ād wonne towne one lay wt comȳ womā ye nyght fore tolde hir coūceill ſhe morne told ye lieutenaūt which̄ forthwith commaūded euery mā ſhold kepe wepē honde ſakrȳg tyme othir whā apꝑceyued yt myſpoȳ ted ſailled ſtrayt depe ſtale ād toke towne newyers euē thei tokē harflete thus engliſſhmen began loſſe caſtell ix day juyll duke burgoign̄ ye power flaūdres moch̄ othir peple came caleys ſette hys ſiege aboute towne ād euery towne flaūdres tentes hē ſelfe ād ſiege endured thre wekes mene duke glowceſtre beyng protectour englōd wente ouer ſee caleys reſcue town̄ fight duke hys hooſt wold haue byden tyme london euery good towne englond ſente ouer ſee reſcouſe certaȳ peple well araied beſt choſē men werre ij day auguſt ſaid duke glouceſtre arriued caleys wt armye v hōdred ſhippes moo duke hys ooſt lay ſiege ſone eſpied ſailles ſee thei approched caleys hauē ſodēly mornȳg departed fro ſiege leuyng behynde thē moch̄ ſtuffe vitaille fledde flaūdres pycardie ād lyke wyſe dyde ſiege lay tofore guynes thei gwynes toke grete gonne braſſe kalled dygeon ād many othir grete gonne ſerpētynes then̄e whā duke glowceſtre arryued alle ooſt wē te flaūdres therinne xj dayes dyd lyttell harme except brente two fayr vyllages poperyng belle othir howſes whiche ſtrenghthe ād ſo beyng therī duke somerſette edmōd erle ſhrewſbury whiche apoȳtement left plegges ād loſte normādie came home duryng ſayd ꝑlemēt duke sutfolk areſted ſente toure ther moneth· kyng dyd fecche hym oute which̄ cauſe commune englōd grete rumour delyueraūce angeoy mayn loſing normādye· eſpicial deth̄ good duke glouceſtre ſo moch̄ yt ſome place men gadred gedres made hem capitaynes bleweberd othir which̄ afterward reſiſted taken juſtyce deide then̄ ſaid ꝑlement adiourned leyceſtre thyder king brought wt duke suthfolk whē ꝯmune hous vnderſtode yt oute toure camē thyder deſired haue execucyon cauſe delyuerāce normādie bē cauſe deth duke glowceſtre ſold gaſcoygne gwyan whiche named gylty duke ſutfolk chief lord ſaye biſſhop ſalyſbury daniell many moo peaſe cō mon duke ſuthfolke exylled oute englōd v yere ād ſo duryng parlement wē te northfolke ād toke ſhyppyng goo owte reame englōd fraunce yere ſaylled ſee ſhipp werre kalled nycholas tour mette ſhippe foūde hȳ therynne whō toke brought hym ſhippe tofore maiſtir capytayns examined atte laſt iugged deth ſo put hȳ cabon chapelayne ſhryue don̄ browght hȳ doner rode ād ſette hī boot ſmoten hede brought body lō de vpō ſondes ſette hede therby don̄ ye fyrſt day maye lo auaylled hym nowe delyuerance normandie c ye may howe rewarded ye deth ye duke glouceſtre thꝰ began ſorow vpō ſorow ād deth deth c ¶how yere thinſurrexion kente cōmunes iake kade iriſſh man capytayne ca cclv yere owre lord mccccl grete grace iubilee rome grete pardon ſo moche place criſtendome grete multitude peple reſorted thyder thys yere grete aſſemble gadryng gedre cōmuns kēte grete nō bre made inſurrexiō rebelled ayens king lawes ordeyned hȳ capitaȳ called iohan kade iriſſhman whyche named hym ſelfe mortymer coſȳ duke yorke capitaȳ helde theſe men gedre ād made ordenaūces among thē ād browght hē blakeheth made bill peticions kīg coūceyll ſhewed iniuries opp̄ſſyōs poure cō mȳs ſuffred ād vndyr colour come aboue grete multitude peple ye xvij day iuyn̄ kȳg wt mani lordes capitayns men werre wēte toward hȳ blakeheth whē capitaȳ kēte vnderſtode comȳg ye kȳg wt ſo grete puiſſaūce withdrewe hȳ wyt peple ſeuenoke littel village xxviij day iuyn̄ beyng withdrawē goon ye kȳg came wyt armie ſette ordre ād enbatailled blakheth aduis cownceyll ſent ſir v • nfrey ſtafford knight willyā ſtafford ſquier two valyaūt capitaȳs wt certaȳ peple fyght wt ye capitaȳ take hȳ bryng acceſſaries kȳg which̄ wente ſeuenoke ye capitaȳs mette wt hē fought ayenſt hem cōcluſiō ſlewe thē both̄ many abode wold yelde hȳ ner flee durȳg ſkarmuſſh fyll grete variaūce amō ge lordes men comȳ peple beyng ye blakeheth ayēſt theyr lordes capytayns ſayng plaȳly wold go capitaȳ kente aſſiſte helpe hī· yf might haue execucyō ye traitours beyng aboute kȳg wherto ye kȳg ſaid nay ſaid playnly lord ſaye treſorer englōd· biſſhop ſaliſbury baron duddely abbot gloucetua daniel treuilliā many mo traitours ād worthy ded herfor pleſe lordes meine alſo ſome ye kȳges hous lord ſaie areſted ſente tour lōdō then̄e kyng herȳg tidinges deth ouerthrowȳg ſtaffordes witdrewe hȳ lōdō fro thēs kyllȳgworth ye kȳg ne lordes durſt truſt owne howſhold meyne c then̄ yt capitayne victorie vpō theſe ſtaffordes anon̄ toke ſir vmfreys ſalade brigātins ſmitē full gylt nailles alſo gylt ſpores araied hȳ like lord capitaȳ reſorted wyt meyne alſo moo blakheth agaȳ whō came erchebiſſhop caūterbury duke bokȳghā ye blakheth ſpake wt hym ſaid thei fownde hȳ witty talking requeſte ſo departed thridde day iuyll came entred lōdō wyt peple dyde make cryes kȳges name name man ſholde robbe ne take mānes good payed came ridyng thurgh ye cite grete pride ſmote ſweerd vpon lōdō ſtone cāwykeſtrete beȳg cite ſente ye towre haue lord ſaye ſo fete hȳ brought hī guyld hall maire aldremē examined ſaid wold owght ben̄ iuged bi peres cō munes kēte toke hym force mayre officiers yt kepte hym ād toke preſte ſhriue er might halfe ben̄ ſhryuē thei brought hȳ standard chepe ſmote hys hede who ſoule almighty god haue pyte mercy amē thus deyde ye lorde ſaye treſorer englond ſet hede ſpere bare aboute ye cyte ſam̄ day aboute myle ende crowemer beheded day afternone capytaine wyt certayne meyne wēte phelipp malpas hous robbed toke way moch̄ good fro thēs wēt ſeȳt margrete patyns one gherſtys hous robbed hȳ toke away moche good alſo whych̄ robbȳg diuerſe mē lōdō neighbour toke part wt thē thys robbyng peples hertes fyll hym euery thryſty man ferd ſerued lyke wyſe ther many man london awayted wolde fayne haue ſeē cōmune robberie which̄ almyghty god forbede ſuppoſe yf robbed might haue goon fer er withſtonde kȳg alle lordes ye reame englōd departed except ye lord scale kepte ye towre lōdō fifte day iuyll dyde don̄ ſmite mānys hede ī ſoutwerke night aft ye maire lōdō aldremē ꝯmunes ye cite cōcluded driue away ye capitaȳ hooſt ſente lord ſcales tour ād mathew gogh capitaȳ normādie thei wold yt night aſſaille capitaȳ wyt thē kēte ſo dyd camē lōdon brygge ſouthwerke er ye capytaȳ knowlege therof fought wt thē kepte ye brygge ye kē tiſſhmen wēte harnoys cam̄ brygge ſhot fowght wyt hē gate brygge ād made thē londō flee ſlow many hē endured night fro tyll ix clocke ye morne atte laſt thei brēte drawe brugge many thē lō dō drowned which̄ night suttō alderman ſlayne rogier heyſant mathew gohe many othir chaūceler englōd ſēt capitaȳ pardone generall hī othir meyne then̄ deꝑted frō ſouthwerke eueri mā hom̄ hows whē thei deꝑted goon ther ꝓclamaciōs made kēte ſoutſex ī othir place mā cowde take capitaȳ quyke dede ſhulde haue mark one alyſawnder iden ſquier kente toke hȳ gardȳ ſouthſex ād takyng capytayn iohan cade ſlain̄ beheded ād heed ſet london brygge anon̄ then̄e kyng came kē te dyd iuſtices ſitte caunterbury enquered acceſſarees chyef cauſe thys inſurrexiō viij mē iugged deth one day othir place moo fro thēs king went ſoutſex weſtcontre lyttell ſlayne biſſhop salyſbury ſame yer̄ ſo many iugged deth xxiij hedes ſtode london brigge attones ¶of felde ye duke york toke brentheth kente byrthe prynce edward fyrſt bataill ſeȳt albōs duk ſomerſette ſlayne capi cclvi yere xxx duke yorke came oute marche walys wyt erle denenſhire lord cobham grete puiſſaunce reformaciō certaȳ jniuries wronges alſo haue juſtyce certayn lordes beyng aboute ye king ād toke feld brentheth beſide derthford kente whych̄ ſtronge feld which̄ cauſe kyng lordes ye lōde went vnto blakeheth wyth grete ſtrōge multitude peple armed ordeyned werre beſt wyſe whā muſteried blakeheth certayne lordes ſente hȳ trete make apoȳtemēt wt hȳ which̄ biſſhop ely biſſhop wyncheſtre erles ſaliſbury warrewyke cōcluded duke ſomerſette ſhold warde āſwere ſuch̄ article duke yorke ſhold put hȳ thā duke yorke ſhold breke feld come kȳg whiche ꝓmyſed bi kȳg ſo kīg cōmaūded duke somerſette ſhold ward then̄ duke york brake vp feld came kȳg whē come cōtrary ye ꝓmyſe fore made duke ſomerſete p̄ſent felde awaytȳg chief aboute kyng made duke yorke ryde fore priſoner thurgh lōdon aft thei wold haue put hī hold noyſe aroſe erle marche ſone comȳg wyt xm men lōdon ward wherof kȳg coūceille fered then̄ cōcluded duke york ſhold departe aboute tyme begā grete deuyſion ſorniſſe bitwen̄ grete maiſtir ye knightes duche ordre whiche lordes yt cōtre· cōmunes tounes rebelled ayēſt lordes ād made ſo grete werre laſt thei kalled kȳg pole lord which̄ kȳg came ād wurſhipfully receyued layde ſiege caſtell marienburgh which̄ chief caſtell ſtrē geſt lond wan ād drofe owte maiſtir danſke alle othir place land alſo bene lordes many yeres loſte lorſhyppes poſceſſions yere incarnacyō owre lord mccccliij ſeynt edwardes day quene margrete delyuered fayr prī ce whiche named edward ſame day iohan norman choſen bene mayre londō day ſhold take othe weſtmynſter wente thyder water wyth craftes fore tyme mayre aldremen craftes roode horſebake whych̄ neuer vſed ſyn tyme haue goon euer water barge ¶ye haue well vnderſtōde tofore cōtrarye promyof kyng alſo concluſions taken bytwene kyng ād noble duke yorke brentheth duke somerſete wē te nat warde abode aboute kyng grete rewle anone made capytayn towne caleys rewled kyng reame wolde wherfore ye grete lordes reame alſo commune pleſyd whyche cauſe duke yorke ye erles warrewyk saliſbury wyt many knightes ſquyers ād moch̄ peple came remeue ye ſayd duke somerſette othir fro kyng kȳg heryng comȳg thought coū ceyll haue goon weſtward mete hē wt hē duke somerſette duke bokynghā erle stafford erle northūberland lord clyfford many othir tyme duke york felawſhyp vnderſtode yt kyng departed wt theſe ſayd lordes frō londō anon̄ chaū ged way coſted cōtre ād came ſeȳt albōs xxiij day may mette ye kȳg whō kȳg ſente certaȳ lordes deſired hē kepe pee departed concluſiō while treated one ſide erle warrewyk wyt march̄ men othir entrid towne othir fowght ayēs ye kyng partie ſo began bataille fyghtȳg which̄ endured good concluſion duke yorke obteyned ād ye victorie iourney whyche bataill ſlayn̄ duke ſomerſete erle northūberland lord clifford many knightes ſquyers many moo hurt ād morne brought kyng grete aſtate londō whiche logged biſſhoppes paleys londō anon̄ grete parlement holdē which̄ parlemēt duke yorke made protectour englond erle warrewyk capitaȳ caleys ād erle saliſbury chaūceler englōd ſuch̄ ꝑſones rewle fore aboute kyng ſet part might rewle dyd fore ſame yere deyed pope nycholas ye fifte hȳ calixte ye iij thys calixte catalane olde mā whā choſen cōtynuelly ſeke wherfore yt myght parforme hys zele deſire ayēſt turke cōceiued cauſe lettyng therof age ſekenes thys calixte inſtitued ordeyned ye feſte tranſfiguracyon owr lord halowed ſeint ſixtes day auguſt becauſe ye grete victorie thei hūgary ayenſt turkes yt ſame day choſen pope ye yere lord mcccclv deied yer̄ mcccclviij ſam̄ day ordeined feſte trāſfiguracyon halowed ſam̄ yere fyll affraye londō ayens lumbardes cauſe begā yongeman toke dogger lūbard brake wherfor yongman morne ſēte fore come maire aldremē therefor offence cōmytted warde then̄e mayre deꝑted guyldhall goo home hys diner chepe yōgmē mercerye moſt part prētiſes helde ye mayre ſherews ſtill chepe wold ſuffre hȳ deꝑte vnto time theyr felawe which̄ commyted warde delyuered ſo bi force reſcued felaw frō priſon punctel doū mayre ſhereues deꝑted pryſoner deliuered which̄ yf put priſon ieoꝑdye lyfe began rumour cyte ayēſt lūbardes ſame euenȳg hād crafty peple towne aroſe run lūbardes howſes deſpoylled robbed dyuerſe hē wherfore mayre aldremen came honeſte peple towne drofe thē then ād ſente ſome thē ſtolen newgate yōgman yt reſcued bi felawes ſawe thys grete rumour afraye robery enſiwed firſt • ȳg ye lumbard deꝑted wēte weſtmȳſter ſaintuarie elles coſted hȳ lyfe punctel anone came downe oeyr determyne iuſtyce thē ſo rebelle • cite ayens lūbardes whiche ſate wyt maire tyme willyā marowe th̄e duke bokȳgham many othir lordes ſee excecucyon doū comyns cite ſecretly made thē redy dide arme thē theyr howſes purpoſe haue rongē comȳ belle whyche named bowe belle thei lette ſad men which̄ cam̄ knowlech̄ duke bokynghā othir lordes incōtinēt aroos thei durſt lēger abyde dowbted hole cite ſhold haue ariſen ayenſt thē yet neuertheles ij iij ye cite iuged deth thys robbery hāged tiborn̄ anone king quene othir lordes rode couētre withdrewe hē frō lōdon thiſe cauſe littell tofore duke yorke ſēte fore grenewich ād diſcharged ꝓtectourſhip lord ſaliſbury chaūcelerſhip ſent fore preuy ſeall come couētre thei almoſt deceyued ye erle warrewyk alſo ſhold haue ben̄ deſtroied thei ſeen well lord egremōd taken therle saliſburyes ſones robbyng ſandwhych capitu cclvij yere taken iiij grete fiſſhes bitwen̄ eerethe lōdō one kalled mors marine ſecōd aſwerd fiſſhe ye othir tweyne wer̄ wale thys ſame yere certayne affraye don̄ ye northcōtre bitwen̄ lord egremōd ye erle ſaliſbury ſones ſaid lord egremōd whō takē cōdāpned grete ſome money ſaid erle ſaliſbury therfor cōmyſed pryſō newgate lōdō wher whā certaȳ ſpace brak pryſō iij priſoners wt hȳ eſcaped wēt way alſo yere erle warrewyk wyfe wēte caleys wyt fayre felawſhyp toke poſceſſion hys office aboute time grete reformacion many monaſteries religion diuerſe party world which̄ reformed ye firſt inſtitucion continued many place alſo aboute time crafte enprȳtȳg firſt fōde magūte almaygne which̄ craft mltiplied multiplied thurgh ye world many place bokes ben̄ grete chepe grete nombre cauſe ye ſame craft ſam̄ yere grete bataill march bitwen̄ hūgerie turkye place kalled ſeptedrawe innumerable turkes ſlayn̄ myracle mānes hōde onely honde god ſmote thē ſeȳt johā capeſtrane p̄ſent prouoked ye criſten peple beyng then̄ aferd afterward purſiewe ye turkes infinite multitude ſlayn̄ ād deſtroied turkes ſaid yt grete nōbre armed mē folowed thē yt aferd turne agayn̄ holy angelis ſame yere priſoners newgate lōdō brake pryſons wē te vpō ye leedes fought ayēs thē cite kepte gate lōge laſt toun̄ gate pryſon thē thā thei put feteris yrōs ſore puniſſhed enſāple othir yere alſo grete erthequake napels ī ſomoch̄ yt ther ꝑiſſed xlm peple yt ſāke īto ye pier de brezey seneſhall normādie wt capitaȳ depe many othir capytaȳs men werre wente ſee wyt grete nauye came downes bi night ye morne erly day lōded came ſandwych both̄ lād bi watyr toke • ne ryfled deſpoilled ād tok • many pryſoners left toune bare which̄ riche place moche good theryn lad wt hem many riche pryſoners ſame yer̄ many place fraūce almaigne flaūdres holād zelād childrē gadred thē bi grete cōpanyes go pylgrymage ſeynt mycheles moūt normandie which̄ came fro fer cōtres wherof peple mervailled ād many ſuppoſed ſome wyked ſpiryte meved thē ſo doo▪ ēdured lōge becauſe longe way ād alſo lake vitayll wēte yere raynold pecok biſſhopp chicheſtre foundē heretike iij daye decēbre abiured lābhyte preſēce ye erchebiſſhop caunterbury many biſſhoppes doctours cōmiſſion ād wēte ouer ſee caleys sone thys erle saliſbury comyng lōdon encōtrid bloreheth lord awdely moch̄ othir peple ordeyned haue diſtreſſyd hȳ hauȳg knowleche ſhold mete accōpanied wyt ij ſones sir thomas ſir iohā neuyll grete felawſhip good men ſo mete ād fought gedres wher therle ſaliſbury wan felde lord awdely ſlain̄ many gentillmen cheſſhire moch̄ peple hurt therles ij ſones hurt ād goyng homward afterward takē punctel lad cheſtre ye quenes meyne calixte pius pope choſē yere mcccclviij called tofore eneas eloquent man poete laureate· enbaſſatour emperour afore tyme ād wrote connceill baſille noble traittye auctorite ſame alſo canoniſed ſeynt katherine ſenys pope ordeyned grete indulgēces pardō wold go werre ayēſt turke wrote epiſtle grete turke exortyng become mcccclxiiij xiiij day auguſt ¶how andrewe trollop ſowdyours caleys forſoke duke yorke maiſtir therle warrewyke weſtcōtre capit cclix duke yorke erles warrewyk saliſbury ſawe ye gouernaū ce reame ſtāde moſt bi quene hir coūceill grete prynces londe called counceill ſette parte onely ſo hit ſayd thurgh reame ſaid lordes ſhold deſtroyed vtterly opēly ſhewed atte bloreheth wold haue ſlayne erle saliſbury then̄ ſauaciō theyr lyues ād alſo cōmyn wele ye ream̄ thought remedie thiſe thȳges aſſēbled thē gedyr wt moch̄ peple tok felde weſtcōtre which̄ ye erle warrewyke came frō taleys wt many holde ſoudiours ādrew trollop othir ī who wiſedome werre moch̄ truſted whā thꝰ aſſēbled· made theyr felde kȳg ſent oute cōmiſſiōs preuy ſealys vnto alle lordes hys reame come ād awayte hȳ mooſt defenſable wyſe ſo euery men came ſuch̄ wyſe yt kȳg ſtrōger moch̄ peple thā duke york erles warrewyk ſaliſbury noted eueri lord 〈…〉 ſo deceyued toke coūcell ſhortely ye ſame night deꝑted thē god wolde then̄e king wēte ludlowe deſpoilled caſtell towne ſent duches yorke wyt hir childrē ladi bokȳghā hyr ſuſter ſhe kepte longe fortwith kyng ordeyned duke ſomerſette capytaȳ caleys theſe othir lordes ſo departed fore ſaid proclamed rebellis grete traitours then̄e duke ſomerſette toke hȳ ye ſowdiours deꝑted felde made redy haſt go caleys toke poſſeſſion hys offyce whā came fownde therle warrewyk therin capitayn therles marche ſaliſbury alſo then̄e lōded ſcales wēte gwyſnes receyued fortuned yt ſome ſhippes yt camē ouer wt camē caleys hauen fre wyll ſhipmē owght fauour ye erle warrewyke thā duke ſomerſete jn which̄ ſhippes takē diuerſe men ienyn finkhill iohan felaw kailles purſer which̄ beheded ſon̄ aft caleys aft thys dayly came men ouer ſee thiſe lordes caleys began wexe ſtrēger thei borowed moche good ſtaple yt othir ſide duke ſomerſette beyng gwyſnes gate peple hī whiche came oute ſcarmuſſhed wyt thē caleys thei caleys wt hē endured many day duryng thꝰ ſame ſcarmuſſhȳg moche peple dayly came ouer vnto theſe lordes then̄e tyme thauys counſeill lordes caleys ſente ouer maiſtir dēhā wt grete felawſhip ſādwhich toke towne therin lord riuers lord scaleys ſone toke many ſhippes ī hauen browght hē caleys which̄ ſhippes many marō ners fre came caleys ſerue ye erle warrewyke· erle warrewyke thauys lordes toke ſhippes māned thē well ſailled ſelf irlād ſpeke wt duke yorke take auys thei ſhold entre englōd agayn̄ whē ben̄ done hys eraudes retorned agayn̄ toward caleys brought moder cownteſſe ſaliſbury came weſtcontre vpō ſee▪ duke exceſtre admyrall englōd beȳg grace • e • accōpanied wyt many ſhippes werre mette therle warrewyke flete fought ſubſtaūce peple beȳg wt duke exceſtre ou •• better fauour therle warrewyk thā thei deꝑted came caleys ſaufte bleſſyd god thā ye kȳges coū ceill ſeȳg yt theſe lordes gotē ye ſhyppes frō ſādwhich takē lord riuers ſone ordeyned garnyſō ſādwhych kepe ye towne made one moūtfort capitayn town̄ mā ne vitaill ne marchaūt ſhold goo flaūdres ſhold goo caleys then̄e caleys ſeyng made oute maiſter denham many othir go ſandwhich̄ ſo dyd aſſailled towne water ād lōd gate brought moūtfort capitaȳ ouer ſee ryſebā ke ſmote hede dayely men came ouer oute party englōd ¶how erles marche warrewyke▪ ſaliſbury entred englōd felde northamptō dyuerſe lordes ſlayne capitulo cclxi ye ſaid erles marche warrewyke ſaliſbury came ouer douer wt moch peple ād lōded whō cōtrey drewe came londō armed ād late lordes kynges coū ceyl knowe trouth̄ alſo theyr entēt aſſembled thē tolde thē thei entended harme kynges perſone ſauf yt wold put fro hȳ ſuche ꝑſones aboute hȳ ſo deꝑted london grete puyſſaūce toward northamptō kyng accōpanyed wyt many lordes made ſtronge felde withoute ye toune bothe ꝑties mete fowghtē grete bataille which̄ batayll ſlayne ye duke bokȳghā erle ſhroweſburi vicōte beaumōd lord egremōd· many knightes ſquiers oth̄ir alſo kȳg hȳ ſelfe takē feld afterward brought lōdō anon̄ afterward ꝑlemēt weſtmīſter durȳg which̄ parlemēt duke yorke came oute irlād wt erle rutelād ridȳg wt grete felawſhip paleys weſtmȳſter toke ye kī ge paleys came ꝑlement chābre toke kȳges place claimed ye croune ꝓpre enheritaūce right caſt forth wrytyng title alſo yt rightfull heyr wherfore moche ꝯcluſiō appoynted cōcluded yt kȳg henry ſhold regne kȳg durīg natural life aſmoch̄ bē ſo lōg kȳg poceſſyd deth̄ duke york ſhold kȳg heires kȳges hȳ forthwith ſhold ꝓclaimed heir apꝑaūt ſhold alſo ꝓtectour englōd durȳg ye kȳges lyfe wt many othir thīges ordeyned ye ſam̄ parlemēt kīg hēry durīg lyfe wēte frō apoȳtemēt article ꝯcluded ſaid ꝑlement ſhold depoſed duke ſhold take ye crown̄ kīg which̄ thȳges wer̄ enacted bi auctorite ſaid ꝑlemēt whyche parlement cōmunes reame beȳg aſſēbled comō hous comonȳg treatyng vpō title ye ſaid duke york ſodēly fyll down̄ croune whiche henge then̄e myddes ſaid hous whiche fraytour abbey weſtmȳſter which̄ taken prodige tokē regne king hēry ended alſo croune whiche ſtode higheſt toure ye ſteple caſtell douer fylle downe ſame yere ¶how noble duke yorke ſlayn̄ felde wakelfeld ſecōd iourney ſeȳt albōs quene prynce ca cclxij then̄e aſmoch̄ quene wt prince north abſented frō kyng wold obeye ſuch̄ thȳges cō cluded ī ꝑlemēt w ordeyned duke york ꝓtectour ſhold goo northward bring quen̄ ſubdue ſuche wold obeye wyt whō wēte erle ſaliſburj ſir thoās neuyll ſone wt moche peple wakefeld criſtmas weke ouerthrowē ſlayne lordes quenes ꝑtie wete duke yorke ſlayn̄ ▪ erle rutlād ſir thomas neuill many moo erle ſaliſbuey takē lyue othir johā harow lōdō capitaȳ ye footmē hāſon hule which̄ brought poūfrete ther beheded hedes ſēte yorke ſette vpō yates thꝰ noble prȳce ſlain̄ duke york who ſoule criſtē ſowles god haue mercy thys tyme therle marche beyng ſhreweſbury hering deth fadre deſired aſſiſtence ayde town tauēge fadres deth frō thēs wēte walys • cādelmaſſe bataylle mortimes croſſe ayēſt therles pēbroke ād wilſhire therle marche victorie then̄ ye quen̄ lordes north diſtreſſed ſlayn ye duke yorke felawſhip came ſouthward wt grete multytude puiſſaūce peple come kȳg defete ſuch̄ cōcluſiōs ben̄ takē bi ye ꝑlement ayēs who comȳg ye duke nortfolk therle warrewyk wt moch peple ordinaūce wēte vnto ſeȳt albōs lad kīg hēry wt hē encōtred gedre jn ſuch̄ wiſe yt ye duke northfolk erle warrewyke wyth othir theyr partye fledde loſt iourney kyng henry taken wente wyth quene prynce hys ſone▪ whiche tho goten felde thēne quen̄ hyr partie beȳg aboue ſente anon̄ londō whych̄ aſſhwedneſday fyrſte day lente vytaylle whyche mayre ordeyned thauys aldremē yt certayne cartres laden wt vitaill ſhold ſente ſeȳt albons thē whā cartres camen crepelgate cōmunes cite kepte gate toke vitailles frō cartres ād wold ſuffre paſſe then̄ certaine aldremē cō munes appoīted go barnet ſpeke wt quenes coūceil entrete northeryn mē ſhold ſēte home theyr contrey ayen̄ cite lōdō dredde ſore robbed deſpoilled come thus durȳg traittie tydynges came ye erle warrewyke mette erle marche cotteſwold comyng oute walys grete meyne walſſhmē punctel both̄ comȳg londō ward anone theſe tydynges knowē trayttye brokē kȳg quene prynce othir lordes wyt departed ſeynt albōs northward wyt peple yet departed thēs beheded lord bonuille ſir thomas kriell which̄ takē iourney don̄ ſhrotewiſday thenne ducheſſe yorke beyng londō herȳg ye loſſe felde ſeynt albiōs ſente ouer ſee ij yōge ſones george rychard which̄ wēte vtrecht phelipp malpas ryche marchaūt london thoās vaghā ſquyer maiſtir willyā hatteclyf many othir ferȳg comȳg quene lōdō toke ſhyp andwarp haue goō zelād othir coſt takē one colūpne frēſſhmā ſhipp werre toke hē pryſoners brought hē fraūce payed grete good theyr raūſone ther moche good rycheſſe ſhipp ¶of depoſicyon kȳg hēry ſixthe kȳg edward ye fourthe toke poſceſſion ād bataille palmeſonday crowned capi cc▪lxiij thenne whan erle marche erle warrewyck mette gedre cotiſwold incōtinēt thei cōcluded goon londō ſēt word anon̄ mayre cyte ſhold come anone cyte glad comȳg hopyng relieued ſo came londō whē comen ſpokē wyt lordes eſtates then̄e beȳg cōcluded aſmoch̄ kīg hēry goon thē northward yt forfaited croune ought depoſed accordyng vnto actes maad paſſed laſt parlement ād ſo thaduyſe lordes ſpirituell temporell then̄e beȳg lōdō erle marche edward ye ḡce god oldeſt ſone richard duke york rightfull heyre next enheriteur fadre ye iiij day marche ye yere lord mcccclix • oke poſceſſiō reame englōd weſtmȳſtre grete halle chirche abbey offred king beryng ſeptre riall whō lordes bothe ſpirituell tēporell dide homage obeiſaunce ſoueraȳ liege ād lawefull lord king forthwith ꝓclamed thurgh cite kīg edward fourth̄ name anon̄ kȳg rode riall aſtate northward wt lordes ſubdue ſubgettes yt tyme beȳg north tauēge fadres deth palmeſō day grete bataill northcontre place kalled towton ferre fro york wyt helpe god gate felde victorye ſlayne aduerſaries xxxm men moo ſaid mē jn which̄ batayll ſlayne erle northūberland lord clifford punctel ſir iohā neuill erle weſtmerlādis brother· andrew trollop ād many othir knightes ſquiers thenne kȳg hēry yt king beyng wyt quen̄ prince yorke hering loſſe yt felde ſo moch̄ peple ſlayn ouerthrowē anon̄ forthwith departed thre wt duke ſomerſete lord roos othir toward ſcotlād next day kīg edward wyt hys armye ētred yorke ther proclamed king obeyed owght mayre aldremē cōmyns ſworn̄ liegemē whē taried north yt cōtre turned hȳ retorned ſouthward leuȳg erle warrewyke tho party kepe gouerne cō tre aboute midſomer aft yere lord mcccclx firſt yere regne crouned weſtmȳſter enoȳted kyng englōd hauyng hole poſceſſiō hole reame whō pray god ſaue kepe ſēde hī accōpliſſement remenaūt rightful enheritaūce beyōde ſee may regne thē pleſir almighty god helthe ſowle honour wurſhipp preſent lyfe well prouffyt ſubgets ther then̄ may veray fynall pee criſten reames infidel miſeraūts may withſtādē deſtroied faith enchaunced which̄ ī thiſe dayes ſore minuſſhed bi puiſſaunce turkes hethē men preſent ſhort lyfe may comē euerlaſting lyfe bliſſe heuen amen ¶here ben endyd cronycles reame englond apperteignaunces enprētyd duchye braband towne andewarpe yere owr lord mccccxciij maiſtir gerard de leew man grete wyſedom maner kūnyng whych̄ nowe come lyfe vnto deth which̄ grete harme many poure man who ſowle god almyghty hys hygh̄ grace hau • mercy amen
